 dvandvaḥ samāsaḥ pramāṇa ādīnām tatvam iti śaiṣikī ṣaṣṭhī tatvasya jñānam niḥśreyasasya adhigama iti ca karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhyau ta etāvantaḥ  vidyamāna arthāḥ eṣām aviparīta jñāna artham iha upadeśaḥ saḥ  ayam anavayavena tantra artha uddiṣṭaḥ  veditavyaḥ ātma ādeḥ khalu prameyasya tatva jñāna atriḥ śreyasa adhigamaḥ tad caiduttara sūtreṇa anūdyate heyam tasya nirvartakam hānam ātyantikam tasya upāyaḥ adhigantavya iti etāni khalu catvāri artha padāni samyak buddhvā niḥśreyasam adhigacchati tatra sa śaya ādīnām pṛthak vacanam arthakame saṃśayāt ayaḥ  hi yathāsambhavam pramāṇeṣu prameyeṣu ca antarbhavantaḥ  na vyatiraccinta iti satyam evam etad  imāḥ tu catastraḥ  vidyāḥ pṛthak prasthānāḥ prāṇabhṛtām anugrahāya upadiśyante yāsām caturrthāyamānvīkṣikī nyāya vidyā tasyāḥ pṛthak prasthānāḥ saṃśaya ādayaḥ padārthāḥ teṣā pṛthak vacanam antareṇa adhyātma vidyā mātram iyam syāt  yathā upaniṣadaḥ tasmāt  saṃśaya ādibhiḥ padārthaiḥ pṛthak  prasthāpyate tatra na anupalabdhe na niṇaute artheḥ pravarttate ki tarhi saṃśayite arthe tathā ca uktam vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣau nyāya pravṛttiḥ artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ tatva jñānam iti sa ca ayam kiṅkhit iti vastu vimarśa mātram anavadhāraṇam jñānam saṃśayaḥ sa ca prameye anta bhavan  evam artha pṛthak ucyate iti artha prayojanam yena prayuktaḥ pravartate tad  prayojanam yam artham abhopsan jihāsan vā karma ārabhate tena anena sarve prāṇinaḥ sarvāṇi karmāṇi sarvāḥ ca vidyā vyāptāḥ tad āśrayaḥ ca nyāyaḥ pravartate kaḥ nunarayam nyāyaḥ pramāṇaiḥ artha parīkṣaṇam pratyakṣa āgama āśritam ca anumanam sa anvīkṣā pratyakṣa āgamābhyām īkṣitasya arthasya anvīkṣaṇam anvīkṣā tayā pravartata iti ānvīkṣakī nyāya vidyā nyāya śāstram yad punar anumānam pratyakṣa āgama viruddha nyāya ābhāsaḥ sa iti tatra vāda jalpau sa prayojanau vitaṇḍā tu parikṣyate vitaṇḍayā pravatāmānaḥ  vaitaṇḍikaḥ sa prayojanam anuyuktaḥ  yadi pratipadyate saḥ  asya pakṣāḥ saḥ  asya siddhānta iti vaitaṇḍika tvam jahāti atha na pratipadyate na ayam laukikaḥ  na parīkṣaka iti āpadyate atha api para pakṣa pratiṣedha jñāpanam prayojanam bravīti etad api tādṛś eva yaḥ  jñāpayati yaḥ  jānāti yena jñāpayate yad ca jñāpyate etad ca pratipadyate cadi tadā vaitaṇḍika tvam jahāti atha na pratipadyate para pakṣa pratiṣedha jñāpanam prayojanam iti etad asya vākyam anarthakam bhavati vākya samūhaḥ ca sthāpanā hīnaḥ  vitaṇḍā tasya yadi abhidheyam pratipadhate saḥ  asya pakṣāḥ sthāpanīyaḥ  bhavati atha na pratipadyate pralāpa mātram anarthakam bhavati vitaṇḍa tvam nivartata iti atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ  arthaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ catra laukika parīkṣakāṇām darśanam na vayāhanyate sa ca prameyam tasya pṛthak vacanam ca tad āśrayau  anumāna āgamau tasmin sati syātām anumāna āgamau asati ca na syātām tad āśrayā nyāya pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhena ca para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ  vacanīyaḥ  bhavati dṛṣṭān samādhinā ca sva pakṣaḥ sthāpanīyaḥ  bhavati nāstikaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntam abhyupagacchan nāstika tvam jahāti anabhyupagacchan kiṃsādhanaḥ param upālabheta niruktena ca dṛṣṭāntena śakyam abhidhātum sādhya sādharmyāt  tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭāṃ  ta udāharaṇam tad viparyayāt  vā viparītam iti asti ayam iti abhyanujñāyamānaḥ  arthaḥ siddhāntaḥ sa ca prameyam tasya pṛthak vacanam satsu siddhānta bhedeṣu vāda jalpa vitaṇḍāḥ pravartante nātā anyathā iti sādhanīyasya arthasya yāvati śabda samūhe siddhiḥ parisamāpyate tasya pañca avayavāḥ pratijña ādayaḥ samūham apekṣya avayavā ucyante teṣu pramāṇa samavāyaḥ āgamaḥ pratijñā hetuḥ anumānam udāharaṇam pratyakṣame upamānam upanayaḥ sarveṣām ekārtha samavāye sāmarthya pradarśanam nigamanam iti tad āśrayā ca tatva vyavasthā te ca ete avayavāḥ śabda viśeṣāḥ santaḥ prameye anta mūtā evam artha puthagracyanta iti tarkaḥ  na pramāṇa saṃguhātaḥ  na pramāṇa antaram pramāṇānām anugrāhakastatva jñānāya kalpate tasya udāharam kim idam janma kṛtakena hetunā nirvartyate āhosvit akṛtakena atha akasmikam iti evam avijñāta tatve arthe kāraṇa upapatyā uhaḥ pravatāte yadi kṛtakena hetunā nirvartyate hetu u  chedāt upapannaḥ  ayam janma ucchadaḥ atha akṛtakena hetunā tatas  henu u  chedasya aśakya tvāt anupapannaḥ  janma ucchedaḥ atha akāsmikam atas  akasmāt nirvartyamānam na punar nirvartsyati iti nivṛtti kāraṇam na upapadyate tena janma anuccheda iti etasmin  tarka viṣaye karma nimitam janma iti pramāṇāni pravartamānāni tarkeṇa anugṛhyante tanu ajñāna viṣayasya ca vibhāgāt  tatu ajñānāya kalpate tarka iti saḥ  ayam ittham abhūtaḥ tarkaḥ pramāṇa sahitaḥ  vāde sādhanāya upālambhāya ca arthasya bhavati iti evam artha pṛthak ucyate prameya anta bhūtaḥ  api iti nirṇayaḥ tatva jñānam pramāṇānām phalam tad avasānaḥ  vādaḥ tasya pālana artha jalpa vitaṇḍe tau  etau tarka nirṇayau lokayātrām vahata iti saḥ  ayam nirṇayaḥ prameya antar bhūta  evam artha pṛthak uddiṣṭa iti vādaḥ khalu nānā pravaktṛkaḥ pratyadhikaraṇa sādhanaḥ  anyatara adhikaraṇa nirṇaya ā  āsānaḥ  vākya samūhaḥ pṛthak uddiṣṭa upalakṣaṇa artham upalakṣitena vyavahāraḥ tatva jñānāya bhavati iti tad viśeṣau jala vitaṇḍe tatvā adhyāvasāya saṃrakṣaṇa arthatam i ti aktam nigraha sthānabhyaḥ pṛthak uddiṣṭa hetvābhāsāḥ vāde ca odanīyā bhaviṣyanti iti jalpa vitaṇḍayoḥ tu nigraha sthānāni iti chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām pṛthak upadeśa upalakṣaṇa arthaḥ upalakṣitānām svāvakye parivarjanam chala ja ati nigraha sthānānām para vākye paryanuyogaḥ jāteḥ tu pareṇa pra yujyamāṇāyāḥ sulabhaḥ samādhiḥ svayam ca sukaraḥ prayoga iti sā iyam ānvīkṣikī pramāṇa ādibhiḥ padārthaiḥ vibhajyamānā pradīpaḥ sarva vidyānām upāyaḥ sarva karmaṇām āśrayaḥ sarva dharmāṇām vidyā uddeśe prakīrtitā iti tad idam tatva jñānam niḥśreyasa adhigamaḥ ca yathāvidyam vedatavyam iha tu adhyātma vidyāyām ātma ādi jñānam tatu jñānam niḥśreyasa adhigama apavarga prāptiḥ iti tad  khalu vai niḥśreyasam kim tattva jñāna anantaram eva bhavati na iti ucyate kim tarhi tattva jñānāt  tatra ātma ādi apavarga paryante prameye mithyājñānam aneka prakārakam vartate ātmani tāvat na asti iti anātmani ātmā iti duḥkhe sukham iti anitye nityam iti atrāṇe trāṇam iti sa bhaye nirbhayam iti jugupsite abhimatam iti hātavye apratihātavyam iti pravṛttau na asti karma na asti karma phalam iti doṣeṣu na ayam doṣa nimittaḥ saṃsāra iti pretyabhāve na asti jantuḥ jīvaḥ  vā sattva ātmā vā yaḥ preyāt  pretya ca bhavet iti anam ittam janma animittaḥ  janma uparama iti ādimān pretyabhāvaḥ  anantaḥ ca iti naimittikaḥ sanna karmaṃ nimittaḥ pretyabhāva iti deha indriya buddhi vedanā santāna uccheda pratisandhānābhyām nirātmakaḥ pretyabhāva iti apavarge bhīṣmaḥ khalu ayam sarva kārya uparamaḥ sarva viprayoge apavarge bahu bhadrakam lupyatam iti katham buddhimān sarva sukha ucchedam acaitanyam amum apavargam rocayet iti etasmāt mithyā jñānāt anukūleṣu rāgaḥ pratikūleṣu ca dveṣaḥ rāga dveṣa adhikārāt cāsatya īrṣyā asūyā māna lobhāt ayaḥ  doṣā bhavanti doṣaiḥ prayuktaḥ śarīreṇa pravartamānaḥ  hiṃsā steya pratiṣiddha maithunāni ācarati vācā anṛta parūṣa sūcanā sambaddhāni manasā para droham para dravya abhīpsām nāstikyam ca iti seyaṃpāpa ātmikā pravṛttiḥ adharmāya atha śubhā śarīreṇa dānam paritrāṇam para ciraṇam ca vācā satyam hitam priyam svādhyāyam ca iti manasā dayām aspṛhām śraddhām ca iti sā iyam dharmāya atra pravatti sādhanau dharma adharmaum pravṛtti śabdena uktau yathā anna sādhanāḥ prāṇāḥ annam vai prāṇinaḥ prāṇāḥ iti sā iyam pravṛttiḥ kutsitasya abhipūjitasya ca janmanaḥ kāraṇam janma punar  śarīra indriya buddhi vedanānām nikāya viśiṣṭaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ tasmin sati duḥkham tad punar  pratikūla vedanīyam bādhanā pīḍā tāpa iti ta hame mithyājñā nāt ayaḥ  duḥkhāntā dharmā avicchedena pravartamānāḥ saṃsāra iti yadā tu tattva jñānāt mithyājñānam apaiti tadā mithyājñānāye doṣā apayanti doṣa apāye pravṛttiḥ apaiti pravṛtti apāye janma apaiti janma apāye duḥkham apaiti duḥkha apāye ca ātyantikaḥ  apavargaḥ  niḥśreyasam iti tattva jñānam tu khalu mithyājñāna viparyayeṇa vyākhyātam ātmani tāvat  asti iti anātmani anātmā iti evam duḥkhe anitye atrāṇe sa bhaye jugupsite hātavye ca yathā viṣayam veditavyam pravṛttau asti karma asti karma phalam iti doṣeṣa doṣa nimittaḥ  ayam saṃsāra iti pretyabhāve khalu asti jantuḥ jovaḥ sattva ātmā vā yaḥ preyāt  pretya ca bhavet iti nimittavat janma nimittavān janma uparama iti anādiḥ pretyabhāvaḥ  apavarga anta iti naimittikaḥ san pretyabhāvaḥ pravṛtti nimittam iti sa ātmkaḥ san deha indriya buddhi vedanā santāna uccheda pratisandhānābhyām pravartata iti apavarge śāntaḥ khalu ayam sarva viprayogaḥ sarva uparamaḥ  apavargaḥ bahu ca kṛcchram ghora pāpakam lupyata iti katham buddhimān sarva duḥkha ucchedam sarva duḥkhā saṃvidam apavargam na rocayet iti tad  yathā madhu viṣa saṃpṛktam annam anādeyam iti evam sukham duḥkha anuṣaktam anādeyam iti trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ u uddeśaḥ  lakṣaṇam parīkṣā ca iti tatra nāmadheyena padārtha mātrasya abhidhānam uddeśaḥ tatra uddiṣṭasya atattva vyavaccheda kaḥ  dharmaḥ  lakṣaṇam lakṣitasya yathālakṣaṇam upapadyate na vā iti pramāṇaiḥ avadhāraṇam parīkṣā tatra uddiṣṭasya pravibhaktasya lakṣaṇam ucyate yathā pramāṇānām prameyasya ca uddiṣṭasya lakṣitasya ca vibhāga vacanam yathā chalasya vacana vighātaḥ  artha vikalpa upapattyā chalam [ ] tad  trividham [ ] iti atha uddiṣṭasya vibhāga vacanam akṣāsyākṣasya prativiṣayam vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam vṛttiḥ tu sannikarṣaḥ  jñānam vā yadā sannikarṣaḥ tadā jñānam pramitiḥ yadā jñānam tadā hāna upādāna upekṣa buddhayaḥ phalam mitena liṅgena liṅginaḥ  arthasya paścāt mānam anumānam upamānam sāmīpyamānam yathā gauḥ evam gavaya iti sāmīpyam tu sāmānya yogaḥ śabdaḥ śabdyate anena artha  iti abhidhīyate vijñāpyata iti upalabdhi sādhānāni pramāṇāni iti samākhyā nirvacana sāma arthyāt  boddhavyam pramīyate anena iti karaṇa artha abhidhānaḥ  hi pramāṇa śabdaḥ tad viśeṣa samākhyāyāḥ  api tathā eva vyākhyānam kim punar etāni pramāṇāni prameyam abhisaṃplavante atha pratiprameyam vyavatiṣṭhanta iti ubhayathā darśanam asti ātmā iti āpta upadeśāt pratīyate atra anumānam icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ  liṅgam [ ] iti pratyakṣam yuñjānasya yoga samādhi jam ātmāni ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga piśeṣāt ātmā pratyakṣaḥ [vai sū ] iti agniḥ āpta upadeśāt pratīyate amutra agniḥ iti pratyāsīdatā dhūma darśanena anumīyate pratyāsannena ca pratyakṣata upalabhyate vyavasthā punar  agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāmaḥ iti laukikasya svarge na liṅga darśanam na pratyakṣam stanayitnu śabde śrūyamāṇe śabda hetoḥ anumānam tatra na pratyakṣam na āgamaḥ pāṇau ca pratyakṣata upalabhyamāne na anumānam na āgama iti sā ca iyam pramitiḥ pratyakṣa parā jijñāsitam artham āpta upadeśāt pratipadyamānaḥ  liṅga darśanena api bubhutsate liṅga darśanena anumitam ca pratyakṣataḥ didṛkṣate pratyakṣata upalabdhe arthe jijñāsā nivartate pūrva uktam udāharaṇam agniḥ iti pramātuḥ pramātavye arthe pramāṇānām saṃkaraḥ  abhisaṃplavaḥ asakaraḥ  vyavasthā iti atha vibhaktānām lakṣaṇa vacanam iti indriyasya arthena sannikarṣāt utpadyate yad jñānam tad  pratyakṣam na tarhi idānīm idam bhavati ātmā manasā saṃyujyate mana indriyeṇa indriyam arthena iti na idam kāraṇa avadhāraṇam etāvat pratyakṣe kāraṇam iti kim tu viśiṣṭa kāraṇa vacanam iti yad pratyakṣa jñānasya viśiṣṭa kāraṇam tad ucyate yad tu samānam anumāna ādi jñānasya na tad nivartyata iti manasaḥ tarhi indriyeṇa saṃyogaḥ  vaktavyaḥ bhidyamānasya pratyakṣa śrajñānasya na ayam bhidyata iti samāna tvāt na ukta iti yāvadartham vai nāmadheya śabdāḥ taiḥ artha sampratyayaḥ artha saṃpratyayāt ca vyavahāraḥ tatra idam indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpannam artha jñāna rūpam iti vā rasa iti eva vā bhavati rūpa rasa śabdāḥ ca viṣaya nāmadheyam tena vyapadiśyate jñānam rūpam iti jānīte rasa iti jānīte nāmagheya śabdena vyapadiśyamānam sat  śābdam prasajyate ata āha avyapadeśyam iti yad idam anupayukte śabda artha sambandhe artha jñānam na tad  nāmadheya śabdena vyapadiśyate gṛhīte api ca śabda artha sambandhe asya arthasya ayam śabdaḥ  nāmadheyam iti yadā tu saḥ  arthaḥ  gṛhyate tadā tad pūrvasmāt artha jñānāt na viśiṣyate tad  artha vijñānam tādṛś eva bhavati tasya tu artha jñānasya anyaḥ samākhyā śabdaḥ  na asti yena pratīyamānam vyavahārāya kalpet  na ca apratīyamānena vyavahāraḥ tasmāt jñeyasya arthasya saṃjñā śabdena iti karaṇa yuktena nirddhiśyate rūpam iti jñānam rasa iti vā jñānam iti tad evam artha jñāna kāle sa na samākhyā śabdaḥ  vyāpriyate vyavahāra kāle tu vyāpriyate tasmāt aśa abdam artha jñānam indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam iti grīṣme marīcayaḥ bhaumena ūṣmaṇā saṃsṛṣṭāḥ spandamānā dūra sthasya cakṣuṣā sannikṛṣyante tatra indriya artha sannikarṣāt udakam iti jñānam utpadyate tad ca pratyakṣam prasajyate iti ata āha avyabhicāri iti yad etasmin  tadati tad vyabhicāri yad tu tasmin  tad iti tad avyabhicāri pratyakṣam iti dūrāt cakṣuṣā hi ayam artham paśyat nāvadhārayati dhūma iti vā reṇuḥ iti vā tad etad indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam anavadhāraṇa jñānam pratyakṣam prasajyata iti ata āha vyavasāya ātmakam iti na ca etad mantavyam ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa jam eva anavadhāraṇa jñānam iti kim tarhi cakṣuṣā hi ayam artham paśyat nāvadhārayati yathā ca indriyeṇa upalabdham artha manasā upalabhate evam indriyeṇa anavadhārayat manasā na avadhārayati yad ca tad indriya anavadhāraṇa pūrvakam manasā anavadhāraṇam tad viśeṣa apekṣam vimarśemātram saṃśayaḥ na pūrvam iti sarvatra ca pratyakṣa viṣaye jñātuḥ indriyeṇa vyavasāyaḥ paścāt manasā anuvyavasāyaḥ upahata indriyāṇām anuvyavasāya abhāvāt iti ātma ādiṣu sukha ādiṣu ca pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam vaktavyam anindriya artha sannikarṣa jam hi tad iti indriyasya vai sataḥ  manasa indriyebhyaḥ pṛthak upadeśaḥ  dharmaṃbhedāt  bhautikāni indriyāṇi niyata viṣayāṇi sa guṇānām ca eṣām indriya bhāva iti manaḥ tu abhautikam sarva viṣayam ca na asya sa guṇasya indriya bhāva iti sati ca indriya artha sannikarṣe sannidhim asannidhi ca asya yugapad jñāna anutpatti kāraṇam vakṣyāmaḥ iti manasaḥ ca indriya abhāvāt na vācyam lakṣaṇa antaram iti tantra antara samācārāt ca etad pratyetavyam iti paramatama pratiṣiddham anumatam iti hi tantra yuktiḥ vyākhyātam pratyakṣam tad pūrvakam iti anena liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandha darśanam liṅga darśanam ca abhisaṃbadhyate liṅga liṅginoḥ saṃbaddhayoḥ darśanena liṅga smṛtiḥ abhisaṃbadhyate smṛtyā liṅga darśanena ca apratyakṣaḥ  arthaḥ  anumīyate pūrvavat iti yatra kāraṇena kāryam anumīyate yathā medhā unnatyā bhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti śeṣavat tad yatra kāryeṇa kāraṇam anumīyate pūrva udaka viparītam udakam na ādyāḥ pūrṇa tvam śīghra tvam dṛṣṭhvā strotasaḥ  anumīyate bhūtā vṛṣṭiḥ iti sāmānyatodṛṣṭam vrajyā pūrvakam anyatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra darśanam iti tathā ca ādityasya tasmāt  asti apratyakṣā api ādityasya vrajyā iti atha vā pūrvavat iti yatra yathāpūrva pratyakṣa bhūtayoḥ anyatara darśanena anyatarasya apratyakṣasya anumānam yathā dhūmena agniḥ iti śeṣavat nāma pariśaṣaḥ sa ca prasakta pratiṣedhe anyatra aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe saṃpratyayaḥ yathā sat anityam evamādinā dravya guṇa karmaṇā ām aviśeṣeṇa sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyebhyaḥ  nirbhaktasya śabdasya tasmin dravya guṇa karma saṃśaye na dravyam eka dravya tvāt na karma śabda antara hetutvāt yaḥ tu śiṣyate saḥ  ayam iti śabdasya guṇatva pratipattiḥ sāmānyatodṛṣṭam nāma yatra apratyakṣe liṅga liṅginoḥ sambandhe kenacid arthena liṅgasya sāmānyāt apratyakṣaḥ  liṅgī gamyate yathā iccha ādibhiḥ ātmā icchā dayaḥ guṇāḥ guṇāḥ ca dravya saṃsthānāḥ tad yad eṣām sthānam sa ātmā iti vibhāga vacanāt eva trividham iti siddhe trividha vacanam mahataḥ  mahā viṣayasya nyāyasya laghīyasā sūtreṇa upadeśāt param vākya lāghavam manyamānasya anyasmin vākya lāghave anādaraḥ tathā ca ayam asya ittham bhūtena vākya vikalpena pravṛttaḥ siddhānte chale śabda ādiṣu ca bahulam samācāraḥ śāstra iti sat viṣayam ca pratyakṣam sat asat viṣayam ca anumānam kasmāt  traikālya grahaṇāt  tri kāla yuktā arthā anumānena gṛhyante bhaviṣyati iti anumīyate bhavati iti ca abhūt iti ca asat ca khlvatītam anāgatam ca iti atha upamānam prajñātena sāmānyāt prajñāpanīyasya prajñāpanam upamānam iti yathā gauḥ evam gavaya iti kim punar atra upamānena kriyate yadā khalu ayam gavā samāna dharmam pratidyate tadā pratyakṣataḥ tam artham pratipadyata iti samākhyā sambandha pratipattiḥ upamāna artham iti āha yathā gauḥ evam gavaya iti upamāne prayukte gavā samāna dharmāṇam artham indriya artha saṃnikarṣāt upalabhamānaḥ  asya gavaya śabdaḥ saṃjñā iti saṃjñā sajñi sambandham pratipadyata iti yathā mudgaḥ tathā mūdgaparṇī yathā bhāṣaḥ tathā māṣa paṇi iti upamāne prayukte upamānāt saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandham pratipadyamānaḥ tām oṣadhī bhaiṣajyāya āharati evam anyaḥ api upamānasya loke viṣayaḥ  bubhutsitavya iti atha śabdaḥ āptaḥ khalu sākṣātkṛta dharmā yathādṛṣṭasya arthasya cikhya apayiṣayā prayukta upadeṣṭā sākṣātkaraṇam arthasya āptiḥ tayā pravartata iti āptaḥ ṛṣyāri amla icchānām samānam lakṣaṇam tathā ca sarveṣām vyavahārāḥ pravartanta iti evam ebhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ deva manuṣya tiraścām vyavahārāḥ prakalpante na atas  anyathā iti yasya iha dṛśyate arthaḥ sa dṛṣṭa arthaḥ yasya amutra pratīyata saḥ  adṛṣṭa arthaḥ evam ṛṣi laukika vākyānām vibhāga iti kimartham punar idam ucyate sa na manyeta dṛṣṭa artham eva āpta upadeśaḥ pramāṇam arthasya avadhāraṇa āt ita adṛṣṭa arthaḥ  api pramāṇam arthasya anumānāt iti iti pramāṇa bhāṣyam kim punar anena pramāṇena artha jātam pramātavyam iti tad ucyate tatra ātmā sarvasya draṣṭā sarvasya bhoktā sarvajñaḥ sarva anubhāvī tasya bhoga āyatanam śarīram bhoga sādhanāni indriyāṇi bhoktavyā indriya arthāḥ bhogaḥ  buddhiḥ sarva artha upalabdhau na indriyāṇi prabhavanti iti sarva viṣayam antaḥkaraṇa manaḥ śarīra indriya artha buddhi sukha duḥkha saṃvedanānām nirvṛtti kāraṇam pravṛttiḥ doṣaḥ ca na asya idam śarīram apūrvam anuttaram ca pūrva śarīrāṇām ādiḥ na asti uttareṣām apavargaḥ  anta iti pretyabhāvaḥ samādhana sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ phalam duḥkham iti na idam anukūla vedanīyasya sukhasya pratīteḥ pratyākhyānam kim tarhi janmana eva idam sa sukha sādhanasya duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt  duḥkhena aviprayogāt vividha bādhana ayogāt  duḥkham iti samādhi bhāvanam upadiśyate samāhitaḥ  bhāvayati bhāvayat nirvidyate nirviṇṇasya vairāgyam viraktasya apavarga iti janma maraṇa prabandha ucchedaḥ sarva duḥkha prahāṇam apavarga iti asti anyat api dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyāḥ prameyam tad bhedena ca aparisaḍkhyeyam asya tu tattva jñānāt apavargaḥ  mithyājñānāt saṃsāra iti ata etad upadiṣṭam viśeṣeṇa iti tatra ātmā tāvat pratyakṣataḥ na gṛhyate sa kim āpta upadeśa mātrāt eva pratipadyata iti na iti ucte anumānāt ca pratipattavya iti katham yad jātīyasya arthasya sannikarṣāt sukham ātma apalabdhavān tad jātīyam eva artham paśyan  upādātum icchati sā iyam ādātum icchā ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisandhānāt bhavati liṅgam ātmanaḥ niyata viṣaye hi buddhi bheda mātre na saṃbhavati deha antaravat iti ekam ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisandhānāt  duḥkha hetau dveṣaḥ yad jātīyaḥ asya arthaḥ sukha hetuḥ prasiddhaḥ tad jātīyam artha paśyan ādātum prayatate saḥ  ayam prayatna ekam aneka artha darśinam darśana pratisandhātāram anteraṇa na syāt  niyata viṣaye hi buddhi bhedā mātre na saṃbhavati deha antaravat iti etena duḥkha hetau prayatnaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ sukha duḥkha smṛtyā ca ayam tad sādhanam ādadānaḥ sukham upalabhate duḥkham upalabhate suḥkha duḥkhe vedayate pūrva ukta eva hetuḥ bubhutsamānaḥ khalu ayam vimṛśati kim svid iti vimṛśan  ca jānīte idam iti tad idam jñānam bubhutsā vimarśābhyām abhinna kartṛkam gṛhyamāṇam ātmanaḥ  liṅgam pūrva ukta eva hetuḥ iti tatra deha antaravat iti vibhajyate yathā anātma vādinaḥ  deha antareṣu niyata viṣayā buddhi bhedā na pratisandhīyante tathā eka deha viṣayā api na pratisandhīyeran aviśeṣāt  saḥ  ayam eka sattvasya samācāraḥ svayan dṛṣṭasya smaraṇam na anya dṛṣṭasya na adṛṣṭasya iti evam khalu nānā sattvānām samācāraḥ  anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ na smarati iti tad etad ubhayam aśakyam anātma vādinā vyavasthāpayitum iti evam upapannam asti ātmā iti tasya bhoga adhiṣṭhānam katham ceṣṭā āśrayaḥ īpsitam jihāsitam vā artham adhikṛtya īpsā ajihāsā prayuktasya tad upāya anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇā samīhā ceṣṭā sa yatra vartate tad śarīram katham indriya āśrayaḥ yasya anugraheṇa anugṛhītāni upaghāte na ca upahatāni sva viṣayeṣu sādhu asādhuṣu pravartante sa eṣām āśrayaḥ tad śarīram katham artha āśrayaḥ yasmin  āyatane indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpannayoḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ pratisaṃvedanam pravartate sa eṣām āśrayaḥ tad śarīram iti bhoga sādhanāni punar  jighrati anena iti ghrāṇam gandham gṛhṇāti iti rasayati anena iti rasanam rasam gṛhṇāti iti caṣṭe anena iti cakṣū rūpam paśyati iti tvac sthānam indriyam tvac  tad upacāraḥ sthānāt iti śṛṇoti anena iti śrotram śabdam gṛhṇāti iti evam samākhyā nirvacana sāmarthyāt bodhyam sva viṣaya grahaṇa lakṣaṇāni indriyāṇi iti bhūtebhya iti nānā prakṛtīnām eṣām satām viṣaya niyamaḥ na eka prakṛtīnām sati ca viṣaya niyame sva vaṣiya grahaṇa lakṣaṇtvam bhavati iti kāni punar indriya kāraṇāni saṃjñā śabdaiḥ pṛthak upadeśaḥ  bhūtānām vibhaktānām su vacam kāryam bhaviṣyati iti ime tu khalu pṛthivī ādīnām yathā viniyogam guṇā indriyāṇām yathākramam arthā viṣayā iti acetanasya karaṇasya buddheḥ jānam vṛttiḥ cetanasya akartu rūpalabdhiḥ iti yukti viruddham artham pratyācakṣāṇaka iva idam āha na acetanasya karaṇasya buddheḥ jñānam bhavitum arhati tad hi cetanam syāt  ekaḥ ca ayam cetanaḥ deha indriya saṅghāta vyatirikta iti prameya lakṣaṇa arthasya vākyasya anya artha prakāśanam upapatti sāmarthyāt iti smṛti anumāna āgama saṃśaya pratibhāsvapna jñāna ūhāḥ sukha ādi pratyakṣam icchā ādayaḥ ca manasaḥ  liṅgāni teṣu satsu iyam api anindriya nimittāḥ smṛti ādayaḥ karaṇa antara nimittā bhavitum arhanti iti yugapad ca khalu ghrāṇa ādīnām gandha ādīnām ca sannikarṣeṣu satsu yugapad jñānāni na utpadyante tena anumīyate asti tad tad indriya saṃyogi sahakāri nimitta antaram avyāpi yasya āsannidheḥ na utpadyate jñānam sannidheḥ ca utpadyata iti manaḥ saṃyoga anapekṣasya hi indriya artha sannikarṣasya jñāna hetu tve yugapad utpadyeran jñānāni iti krama prāptā tu manaḥ  atra buddhiḥ iti abhipretam budhyate anena iti buddhiḥ saḥ  ayabhārambhaḥ śarīreṇa vācā manasā ca puṇyaḥ pāpaḥ ca daśavidhaḥ tad etad kṛta bhāṣyam dvitīya sūtra iti pravartanā pravṛtti hetu tvam jñātāram hi rāga ādayaḥ pravartayanti puṇye pāpe vā yatra mityā jñānam tatra rāga dveṣau  iti pratyātma vedanīyā hi ime doṣāḥ kasmāt lakṣaṇataḥ nidrdiśyanta iti karma lakṣaṇāḥ khalu rakta dviṣṭa mūḍhāḥ raktaḥ  hi tad karma kurute yena karmaṇā sukham duḥkham vā labhate tathā dviṣṭaḥ tathā mūḍha iti doṣā rāga dveṣa mohā iti ucyamāne bahu na uktam bhavati iti utpannasya kvacid sattva nikāye mṛtvā yā punar u utpattiḥ sa pretyabhāvaḥ utpannasya sambaddhasya sambandhaḥ tu deha indriya buddhi vedanābhiḥ punar u utpattiḥ punar deha ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ purariti abhyāsa abhidhānam yatra kvacid prāṇa bhṛt nikāye varttamānaḥ pūrva upāttān deha ādīn jahāti tad praiti yad  tatra anyatra vā deha ādīn anyān upādatte tad bhavati pretyabhāvaḥ mṛtvā punarjanma saḥ  ayam janma maraṇa prabandha abhyāsaḥ  anādiḥ apavarga antaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ  veditavya iti sukha duḥkha saṃvedanam phalam sukha vipākam karma duḥkha vipākam ca tad punar deha indriya viṣaya buddhiṣu satīṣu bhavati iti saha deha ādibhiḥ phalam abhipratam tathā hi pravṛtti doṣa janitaḥ  artha  phalam etad sarvam bhavati tad etad phalam upāttam upāttam heyam tyaktam tyaktam upādeyam iti na asya hāna upādānayoḥ niṣṭhā paryavasānam vā asti sa khalu ayam phalasya hāna upādāna srotatasā uhyate loka iti atha etad eva bādhanā pīḍā tāpa iti tayā anubaddha mana ṣaktam avinirbhāgena vartamānam duḥkha yogāt  duḥkham iti saḥ  ayam sarvam duḥkhena anubaddham iti paśyan duḥkham jihāsuḥ janmani duḥkha darśī nirvidyate nirviṇṇaḥ  virajyate viraktaḥ  vimucyate yatra tu niṣṭhā yatra tu paryavasānam saḥ  ayam tena duḥkhena janmanā atyantam vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ katham upāttasya janmanaḥ  hānam anyasya ca anupādānam etām avasthām aparyantām apavargam vedayante apavarga vidaḥ tad abhayam ajaram amṛtyu padam brahma kṣema prāpitar iti nityam sukham ātmanaḥ  mahat tvavat  tad tu mokṣe abhivyajyate tena abhivyaktena atyantam vimuktaḥ sukhī bhavati iti kecid  manyante teṣām pramāṇa abhāvāt anupapattiḥ na pratyakṣam na anumānam na āgamaḥ  vā vidyate nityam sukham ātmanaḥ  mahat tvavat  tad tu mokṣe abhivyajyata iti nityasya abhivyaktiḥ saṃvedanam tasya hetu vacanam nityasya sukhasya abhivyaktiḥ saṃvedanam jñānam iti tasya hetuḥ vācyaḥ  yatas tad utpadyata iti sukhavat nityam iti ced  saṃsāra sthasya muktena aviśeṣaḥ yathā muktaḥ sukhena tad saṃvedanena ca sannityena upapannaḥ tathā saṃsāra sthaḥ  api iti aviśeṣaḥ prasajyate ubhayasya nitya tvāt  abhyunujñāne ca dharma adharma phalena sāhacaryam yaugapadyam gṛhyate yad idam utpatti sthāneṣu dharma adharma phalam sukham duḥkham ca saṃvedyate paryāyeṇa tasya ca nitya saṃvedanasya ca sahabhāvaḥ  yaugapadyam gṛhyeta na sukha abhāvaḥ  na anabhivyaktiḥ asti ubhayasya nitya tvāt  anitya tve hetu vacanam atha mokṣe nityasya sukhasya sa vedanam anityam yatas tad utpadyate sa hetuḥ vācyaḥ ātma manaḥ saṃyogasya nimitta antara sahitasya hetu tvam tasya sahakāri nimitta antara vacanam ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ  hetuḥ iti ced  evam api tasya sahakāri nimitta antaram vacanīyam iti dharmasya kāraṇa vacanam yadi dharmaḥ  nimitta antaram tasya hetuḥ vācyaḥ  yata utpadyata iti yoga samādhi jasya kārya avasāya virodhāt prakṣaye saṃvedanenivṛttiḥ yadi yoga samādhi jaḥ  dharmaḥ  hetuḥ tasya kārya avasāya vipodhāt prakṣaye saṃvedanam amatyantam nivarteta asaṃvedane ca avidyamānena aviśeṣaḥ yadi dharma kṣayāt saṃvedana uparamaḥ  nityam sukham na saṃvedyate iti kim vidyamānam na saṃvedyate atha avidyamānam iti na anumānam viśiṣṭe asati iti aprakṣayaḥ ca dharmasya niranumānam utpatti dharmakasya anitya tvāt yoga samādhi jaḥ  dharmaḥ  na kṣīyata iti na asti anumānam utpatti dharmakam anityam iti viparyayasya tu anumānam yasya tu saṃvedana uparamaḥ  na asti tena saṃvedana hetuḥ nitya iti anujñeyam nitye ca mukta saṃsāra sthayoḥ aviśeṣa iti uktam yathā muktasya nityam sukham tad saṃvedana hetuḥ ca saṃvedanasya tu uparamaḥ  na asti kāraṇasya nitya tvāt  tathā saṃsāra sthasya api iti evam ca sati dharma adharma phalena sukha duḥkha saṃvedanena sāhacaryam gṛhyeta iti śarīra ādi sambandhaḥ pratibandha hetuḥ iti ced  na śarīra ādīnām upabhoga artha tvāt viparyayasya ca ananumānāt  syāt matam saṃsāra avasthasya śarīra ādi sambandhaḥ  nitya sukha saṃvedana hetoḥ pratibandhakaḥ tena aviśeṣaḥ  na asti iti etad ca ayuktam śarīra ādaya upabhoga arthāḥ te bhoga pratibandham kariṣyanti iti nupapannam na ca asti anumānam aśarīrasya ātmanaḥ  bhogaḥ kaścid asti iti iṣṭa adhigama arthā pravṛttiḥ iti ced  na aniṣṭa uparama artha tvāt idam anumānam iṣṭa adhigama arthaḥ  mokṣa upadeśaḥ pravṛttiḥ ca mumukṣūṇām na ubhayam anarthakam iti etad ca ayuktam aniṣṭa uparama arthaḥ  mokṣa upadeśaḥ pravṛttiḥ ca mumukṣūṇām iti na iṣṭam aniṣṭena ananubaddham sambhavati iti aniṣṭa anubandhāt  iṣṭam api aniṣṭa sampadyate aniṣṭa hānāya ca ghaṭamāna iṣṭam api jahāti viveka hānasya aśakya tvāt iti dṛṣṭa atikramaḥ ca deha ādiṣu tulyaḥ yathā dṛṣṭam anityam sukham parityajya nityam sukham kāmayate evam deha indriya buddhīḥ nityā dṛṣṭā anikramya muktasya nityā deha indriya buddhayaḥ kalpayitavyāḥ sādhīyaḥ ca evam muktasya ca aikātmyam kalpitam bhavati iti upapatti virūddham iti ced  samānam deha ādīnām nitya tvam pramāṇa virūddham kalpayayitum aśakyam iti samānam sukhasya api tarhi nitya tvam pramāṇa virūddham kalpayitum aśakyam iti ātyantike ca saṃsāra duḥkha abhāve sukha vacanāt āgame api satya virodhaḥ yadi api kaścid āgamaḥ syāt  muktasya ātyantikam sukham iti sukha śabda ātyantike duḥkha abhāve prayukta iti evam upapadyate dṛṣṭaḥ  hi duḥkha abhāve sukha śabda prayogaḥ  bahulaṃloke  iti nitya sukha rāgasya aprahāṇe mokṣa adhigama abhāvaḥ  rāgasya bandhana samājñānāt  yadi ayam mokṣe nityam sukham abhivyajyata iti nitya sukha rāgeṇa mokṣāya ghaṭamānā na mokṣam adhigacchet  na adhigantum arhati iti bandhana samājñātaḥ  hi rāgaḥ na ca bandhane sati api kaścid mukta iti upapadyata iti prahīṇa nitya sūkha rāgasya apratikūla tvam atha asya nitya sukha rāgaḥ prahīyate tasmin prahīṇe na asya nitya sukha ārāgaḥ pratikūlaḥ  bhavati yadi evam muktasya nityam sukham bhavati atha api na bhavati na asya ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ mokṣa adhigamaḥ  vikalpyata iti sthānavata etarhi saṃśayasya lakṣaṇam vācyam iti tad ucyate samāna dharma upapatteḥ viśeṣa apekṣaḥ  vimarśaḥ saṃśaya iti sthāṇu purūṣayoḥ samānam dharmam āroha pariṇāhau paśyan pūrva dṛṣṭam ca tayaḥ viśeṣam bubhutsamānaḥ kisvid iti anyataram na avadhārayati yad  tad anavadhāraṇa jñānam sa saṃśayaḥ samānam anayoḥ dharmam upalabhe viśeṣam anyatarasya na upalabha iti eṣā buddhiḥ apekṣā sā saṃśayasya pravarttikā varttate tena viśeṣa apekṣaḥ  vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ aneka dharma upapatteḥ iti samāna jāta uyama samāna jātīyam ca anekam tasya anekasya dharma upapatteḥ viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt  samāna jātīyebhyaḥ  asamāna jātīyebhyaḥ ca arthā viśiṣyante gandhavat tvāt pṛthivī avādibhyaḥ ca viśiṣyate guṇa karmabhyaḥ ca asti ca śabde vibhāga janya tvam viśeṣaḥ tasmin dravyam guṇaḥ karma vā iti sandehaḥ viśeṣasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt  kim dravyasya sataḥ  guṇakam abhyaḥ  viśeṣaḥ āhosvit aguṇasya sataḥ  dravya karmabhyaḥ atha karmaṇaḥ sataḥ  dravya guṇebhya iti viśeṣa apekṣā anyatamasya vyavasthāpakam dharmam na upalabha iti buddhiḥ iti vipratipatteḥ iti vyāhatam ekārtha darśanam vipratipattiḥ vyāghātaḥ virodhaḥ  asahabhāva iti asti ātmekam darśanam na asti ātmā iti aparam na ca sadbhāva asadbhāvau saha ekatra sambhavataḥ na ca anyatara sādhakaḥ  heturūpalabhyate tatra tattva anavadhāraṇam saṃśaya iti upalabdhi avyavthātaḥ khalu api sat ca udakam upalabhyate taḍāga ādiṣu marīciṣu ca avidyamānam udakam iti atas  kkacid upasabhyamāne tattva vyavasthāpakasya pramāṇasya anupalabdheḥ kim sat upalabhyate atha asat iti saṃśayaḥ  bhavati anupalabdhi avasthātaḥ ca sat ca na upalabhyate mūlakīlaka udaka ādi asat ca anutpannam nirūddham vā tatas  kkacid anupalabhyamāne kim sanna upalabhyate uta asat iti saṃśayaḥ  bhavati viśeṣa apekṣaḥ  pūrvavat  pūrvaḥ samānaḥ  anekaḥ ca dharmaḥ  jñeya sthaḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhī punar jñātṛ sthe etāvatā viśeṣeṇa punarvacanam samāna dharma adhigamāt samāna dharma upapatteḥ viśeṣa smṛti apekṣaḥ  vimarśa iti sthānavatām lakṣaṇa vacanam iti samānam yam artham āptavyam hātavyam vā vyavasāya tad āpti hāna upāyam anutiṣṭhati prayojanam tad veditavyam pravṛtti hetu tvāt  imam artham āpsyāmi hāsyāmi vā iti vyavasāyaḥ  arthasya adhikāraḥ evam vyavasīyamānaḥ  arthaḥ  adhikriyata iti loka sāmānyam anatītāḥ laukikāḥ naisargikam vainayikam buddhi atiśayam aprāptāḥ tad viparītāḥ parīkṣakāḥ tarkeṇa pramāṇaiḥ artham parīkṣitum arhanti iti yathā yam artham laukikā budhyatante tathā parīkṣakā api saḥ  arthaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhena hi pratipakṣāḥ pratiṣeddhavyā bhavanti iti dṛṣṭānta samādhitā na sva pakṣāḥ sthāpanīyā bhavanti iti avayaveṣu ca udāharaṇāya kalpata iti atha siddhāntaḥ idam ittham bhūtañcā iti abhyanujñāyamānam artha jātam siddham siddhasya saṃsthitiḥ siddhāntaḥ saṃsthitiḥ ittham bhāva vyavasthā dharma niyamaḥ sa khalu ayam tantra arthasa sthitiḥ tantra saṃsthitiḥ tantram itaretara abhisambaddhasya artha samūhasya upadeśaḥ śāstram adhikaraṇa anuṣakta artha saṃsthitiḥ adhi karaṇa saṃsthitiḥ abhyupagama saṃsthitiḥ anavadhārita artha parigrahaḥ tad viśeṣa parīkṣaṇāya abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ tantra bhedāt  tu khalu sa caturvidhaḥ tatra etāḥ catasraḥ saṃsthitayaḥ artha antara bhūtāḥ tāsām yathā ghrāṇa ādīni indriyāṇi gandhādaya indriya arthāḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni pramāṇaiḥ arthasya grahaṇam iti yathā na asata atma lābhaḥ na sata ātma hānam niratiśayāḥ cetanāḥ deha indriya manaḥ saṃ viṣayeṣu tad tad kāraṇeṣu ca viśeṣa iti sāṅkhcānām puruṣa karma ādi nimittaḥ  bhūta sargaḥ karma hetavaḥ  doṣāḥ pravṛttiḥ ca sva guṇa viśiṣṭāḥ cetanāḥ asat utpadyate utpannam nirudhyata iti yogānām yasya arthasya siddhau  anye arthā anuṣajyante na taiḥ vinā saḥ  arthaḥ sidhyati te arthā yad adhiṣṭhānāḥ saḥ  adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ yathā deha indriya vyatiriktaḥ  jñātā darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt iti atra anuṣaṅgiṇaḥ  arthā indriya nānā tvam niyata viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi sva viṣaya grahaṇa liṅgāni jñātuḥ jñāna sādhanāni gandha ādi guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam guṇa adhikaraṇam aniyata viṣayāḥ cetanā iti pūrva artha siddhau  ete arthāḥ sidhyanti na taiḥ vinā saḥ  arthaḥ sambhavati iti yatra kiṃcid artha jātam aparīkṣitam abhyupagamyate astu dravyam śabdaḥ sa tu nityaḥ  atha anitya iti dravyasya sataḥ  anitya tā nitya tā vā tad viśeṣaḥ parīkṣyate saḥ  abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ sva buddhi atiśaya cikhyā apayiṣayā para buddhi avajñānāya ca pravartata iti atha avayavāḥ daśa avayavān eke nauyayikā vākye sañcakṣate jijñāsā saṃśayaḥ śakya prāptiḥ prayojanam saṃśaya vyudāsa iti te kasmāt na ucyanta iti tatra apratīyamāne arthe pratyaya arthasya pravartikā jijñāsā apratīyamānam artham kasmāt jijñāsate tam tattvataḥ  jñātam hāsyāmi vā upādāsya upekṣiṣye vā iti tā etā hāna upādāna upekṣā buddhayaḥ tattva jñānasya arthaḥ tad artha mayam jijñāsate sā khalu i yamasādhanam arthasya iti jijñāsā adhi kaṣṭhānam saṃśayaḥ ca vyāhata dharma upasaṅghātāt tatu jñāne pratyāsannaḥ vyāhatoḥ hi dharmayoḥ anyatarat tattvam bhavitum arhati iti sa pṛthak upadiṣṭaḥ  api asādhanam arthasya iti pramātuḥ pramāṇāni prameya adhigama arthāni sā śakya prāptiḥ na sādhakasya vākyasya bhāgena yujyate pratijña ādivat iti prayojanam tattva avadhāraṇam artha sādhakasya vākyasya phalam na eka deśa iti saṃśaya vyudāsaḥ pratipakṣa upavarṇanam tad pratiṣedhena tattva jñāna abhyanujñāna artham na tvayam sādhaka vākya eka deśa iti prakaraṇe tu jijñādaya samarthā avadhāraṇīya artha upakārāt  tattva arntha sādhaka bhāvāt tu pratijña ādayaḥ sādhaka vāṅkyasya bhāgā eka deśā avayavā iti teṣām tu yathā vibhaktānām prajñā apanīyena dharmeṇa dharmiṇaḥ  viśiṣṭasya parigraha vacanam pratijñā sādhya nirdeśaḥ anityaḥ śabda iti udāharaṇena sāmānyāt sādhyasya dharmasya sādhanam prajñāpanam hetuḥ sādhye pratisandhāya dharmam udāharaṇe ca pratisandhāya tasya sādhana tā vacanam hetuḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti utpatti dharmakam anityam dṛṣṭam iti kim etāvat hetu lakṣaṇam iti na iti ucyate kim tarhi udāharaṇa vaidharmyāt ca sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ katham anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt  anutpatti dharmakam nityam dṛṣṭam ātma ādaya iti sādhyena sādharmyam samāna dharma tā sādhya sādharmyāt kāraṇāt tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭānta iti tasya dharmaḥ tad dharmaḥ tasya iti sādhyasya sādhyam ca dvividham dharmi viśiṣṭaḥ  vā dharmaḥ śabdasya anitya tvam dharma viśiṣṭaḥ  vā dharmī anityaḥ śabda iti iha uttaram tad grahaṇena gṛhyata iti kasmāt  pṛthak dharma vacanāt  tasya dharmaḥ tad dharmaḥ tad dharmasya bhāvaḥ tad dharma bhāvaḥ sa yasmin dṛṣṭānte vartate sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ tad dharma bhāvī yasmin dṛṣṭānte sādhya sādharmyāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt  sādhyasya dharmaḥ  anitya tvam bhavati sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya sādharmyāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt tad dharma bhāvī bhavati sa ca udāda haraṇam iṣyate sthālī ādi dravyam utpatti dharmakam anityam dṛṣṭām iti tatra yudat padyate tad utpatti dharmakam tad ca bhūtvā na bhavati ātmānam jahāti nirudhyata iti anityam evam utpatti dharmaka tvam sādhanam anitya tvam sādhyam saḥ  ayam ekasmin dvayoḥ dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ sādharmyāt  vyasthita upalabhyate tam dṛṣṭānta upalabhamānaḥ śabde api anuminoti śabdaḥ  api utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ sthālī ādivat iti udāhriyate anena dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva iti udāharaṇam dṛṣṭānta udāharaṇam iti prakṛtam sādhya vaidharmyāt atad dharma bhāvī ca dṛṣṭānta udāharaṇam iti anityaḥ śabda utpatti dharmaka tvāt  anutpatti dharmakam nityam ātma ādi saḥ  ayam ātma ādiḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya vaidharmyāt anutpatti dharmaka tvāt atad dharma bhāvī yaḥ  asau sādhyasya dharmaḥ  anitya tvam sa tasmin na bhavati iti atra ātma ādau dṛṣṭānta utpatti dharmaka tvasya abhāvāt anitya tvam na bhavati iti upalabhamānaḥ śabde vapiḥ yayam anuminoti utpatti dharmaka tvasya bhāvāt anityaḥ śabda iti sādharmya uktasya hetoḥ sādhya sādharmyāt  tad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭānta udāharaṇam vaidharmya uktasya hetoḥ sādhya vaidharmyāt atad dharma bhāvī dṛṣṭānta udāharaṇam pūrvasmin dṛṣṭānte yau tau dharmaum sādhya sādhana bhūtau paśyati sādhye api tayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvam anuminoti uttarasmin dṛṣṭānte yayoḥ dharmayoḥ ekasya abhāvāt itarasya abhāvam paśyati tayoḥ ekatarasya bhāvāditarasya bhāvam sādhye anuminoti iti tad etad hetvābhāseṣu na sambhavati iti ahetavaḥ  hetvābhāsāḥ tad idam hetu udāharaṇayoḥ sāmarthyam parama sūkṣmam duḥkha bodham paṇḍita rūpa vedanīyam iti udāharaṇa apekṣa udāharaṇa tantra udāharaṇa vaśaḥ vaśaḥ sāmarthyam sādhya sādharmya yukte udāharaṇe sthālī ādi dravyam utpatti dharmakam anityam dṛṣṭam tathā ca śabda utpatti dharmaka iti sādhyasya śabdasya utpatti dharmaka tvam ūpa saṃhriyate sādhya vaidharmya yuktam punar udāharaṇe ātma ādi dravyam anutpatti dharmakam nityam dṛṣṭam na ca tathā anutpatti dharmakaḥ śabda iti anutpatti dharmaka tvasya upasaṃhāra pratiṣedhena utpatti dharma kattvam upasaṃhriyate tad idam upasaṃhāradvetam udāharaṇa dvaitāt bhavati upasaṃhriyate anena iti ca upasaṃhāraḥ  veditavya iti dvividhasya punar heta udvividhasya ca udāharaṇasya upasaṃhāra dvaite ca samānam sādharmya ukte vā vaidharmya ukte vā yathā udāharaṇam upasaṃhriyate tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabda iti nigamanam nigamyante anena iti pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanayā ekatra iti nigamanam nigamyante samarthyante saṃbadhyante tatra sādharmya ukte tāvat vetau vākyam anityaḥ śabda iti pratijñā utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti hetuḥ utpatti dharmakam sthālī ādi dravyam anityam iti udāharaṇam tathā ca utpatti dharmakaḥ śabda iti upanayaḥ tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabda iti nigamanam vaidharmya ukte api anityaḥ śabdaḥ utpatti dharmaka tvāt  anatpatti dharmakam ātma ādi dravyam nityam dṛṣṭam na ca tathā anutpatti dharmakaḥ śabdaḥ kim tarhi utpatti dharmakaḥ tasmāt utpatti dharmaka tvāt anityaḥ śabda iti avayava samudāye ca vākye saṃbhūya itaretara abhisaṃbandhāt pramāṇāni artham sādhayanti iti saṃbhavaḥ tāvat  śabda viṣayā pratijñā āpta upadeśasya pratyakṣa anumānābhyām pratisandhānāt anṛṣeḥ ca svātantrya anupapatteḥ anumānam hetuḥ udāharaṇe saṃdṛśya pratipatteḥ tad ca udāharaṇa bhāṣye vyākhyātam pratyakṣa viṣayam udāharaṇam dṛṣṭena adṛṣṭa siddheḥ upamānam upanayaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhaarāt  na ca tathā iti ca upamāna dharma pratiṣedhe viparīta dharma upasaṃhaara siddheḥ sarveṣām eka artha pratipattau sāmarthya pradarśanam nigamanam iti itaretara abhisaṃbandhaḥ  api asatyām pratijñāyām anāśrayā hetvādayaḥ  na pravartteran asati hetau kasya sādhana bhāvaḥ pradarśyeta udāharaṇe sādhye ca kasya upasaṃhaaraḥ syāt  kasya ca apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam syāt  iti asati udāharaṇe kena sādharmyam vaidharmyam vā sādhya sādhanam upādīyeta kasya vā sādharmya vaśāt upasaṃhaaraḥ pravarteta upanayam ca antareṇa sādhye anupasaṃhṛtaḥ sādhakaḥ  dharmaḥ  na artham sādhayet  nigamana abhāve ca anabhivyakta saṃbandhānām pratijñā ādīnām eka arthena pravartanam tathā iti pratipādanam kasya iti atha avayava arthaḥ sādhyasya dharmasya dharmiṇā saṃbandha upapādanam pratijña arthaḥ udāharaṇena samānasya viparītasya vā sādhyasya dharmasya sādhaka bhāva vacanam hetu arthaḥ dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva pradarśanam ekatra udāharaṇa arthaḥ sādhana bhūtasya dharmasya sādhyena dharmeṇa sāmānādhikaraṇya upapādanam upanaya arthaḥ udāharaṇa sthayā ūḥ ddharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva upapattau sādhye viparīta prasaṅga pratiṣedha artham nigamanam na ca etasyām hetu udāharaṇa pariśuddhau satyām sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt jāti nigraha sthāna bahu tvam prakramate avyavasthāpya khalu dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvam udāharaṇe jāti vādī pratyavatiṣṭhate vyavasthitā iha khilu dharmayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāve dṛṣṭānta sthe gṛhyamāṇe sādhana bhūtasya dharmasya hetu tvena upādānam na sādharmya mātrasya na vairdharmya mātrasya vā iti ata ūrdhvam tarkaḥ  lakṣaṇīya iti atha idam ucyate avijñāyamāna tattve arthe jijñāsā tāvat jāyate jānīya imam artham iti atha jijñāsitasya vastunaḥ  vyāhatau dharmaum vibhāgena vimṛśati kim svid  ittthamāha usvit na ittham iti vimṛśyamānayoḥ dharmayoḥ ekataram kāraṇa upapattyā anujñānāti sambhavati asmin kāraṇam pramāṇam hetuḥ iti kāraṇa upapattyā syāt evam etad  na itarat iti tatra nidarśanam yaḥ  ayam jñātā jñātavyam artham jānīte tam tattvataḥ  jānīya iti jijñāsā sa kim utpatti dharmakaḥ anutpatti dharmakam iti vimarśaḥ vimṛśyamāne avijñāta tattve arthe yasya dharmasya abhyanujñā kāraṇam upapadyate tam anujānāti yadi ayam anutpatti dharmakaḥ tatas  sva kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalam anubhavati jñātā duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttaram uttaram pūrvasya pūrvasya kāraṇam uttara uttara apāye ca tad anantara abhāvāt apavarga iti syātām saṃsāra apavargaum utpatti dharmake jñātari punar na syātām utpannaḥ khalu jñātā deha indriya viṣaya buddhi vedanābhiḥ saṃbadhyata iti na asya idam sva kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phalam utpannaḥ ca bhūtvā na bhavati iti tasya avidyamānasya niruddhasya vā sva kṛta karmaṇaḥ phala upabhogaḥ  na asti tad evam ekasya aneka śarīra yogaḥ śarīra viyogaḥ ca atyantam na syāt iti yatra kāraṇam anupapadyamānam paśyati tad na anujānāti saḥ  ayam evaṃlakṣaṇa ūhaḥ tarka iti ucyate katham punar ayam tattva jñāna arthaḥ  na tattva jñānam eva iti anavadhāraṇāt  anujānātyayam ekataram dharmam kāraṇa upapattyā na tu avadhārayati na vyavasyati na niścinoti evam eva idam iti katham tattva jñāna artha iti tattva jñāna viṣaya abhyanujñā lakṣaṇādūhād bhāvitāt prasannāt anantaram pramāṇa sāmarthyāt  tattva jñānam utpadyata iti evam tattva jñāna artha iti saḥ  ayam tarkaḥ pramāṇāni pratisandadhānaḥ pramāṇa abhyanujñānāt pramāṇa sahitaḥ  vāde apadiṣṭa iti avijñāta tattve arthe iti yathā saḥ  arthaḥ  bhavati tasya tathā abhāvaḥ tattvam aviparyayaḥ yāthātathyam etasmiḥ ca tarka viṣaye sthāpanā sādhanam pratiṣedha upālambhaḥ tau sādhana upālambhau pakṣa pratipakṣa āśrayau vyatiṣaktau  anubandhena pravarttamānau pakṣa pratipakṣau  iti ucyete tayoḥ anyatarasya nivṛttiḥ ekatarasya avasthānam avarjanīyam avaśyambhāvi tvāt yasya avasthānam tasya artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ na idam pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam sambhavati iti ekaḥ  hi pratijñātam artham tam hetutaḥ sthāpayati pratiṣiddham ca uddharati dvitīyasya dvitīyena sthāpanā hetuḥ ca pratiṣidhyate tasya eva pratiṣedha hetuḥ ca uddhriyate sa nivarttate tasya nivṛttau yaḥ  avatiṣṭhate tena artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ ubhābhyām eva artha avadhāraṇam iti āha kayā yuktyā ekasya saṃbhavaḥ  dvitīyasya asambhavaḥ tau  etau sambhava asambhavau vimarśam saha nivarttayata ubhaya sambhave ubhayā sambhave tu anivṛttaḥ  nimarśa iti vimṛśya iti vimarśam kṛtvā saḥ  ayam vimarśaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣau  avadyotya nyāyam pravartayati iti upādīyata iti etad ca viruddhayoḥ eka dharmi sthayoḥ bodhavyam yatra tu dharmi sāmānya gatau viruddhau dharmaum hetutaḥ sambhavataḥ tatra samuccayaḥ hetutaḥ arthasya tathā abhāva upapatteḥ yathā kriyāvat  dravyam iti lakṣaṇa vacane yasya dravyasya kriyā yogaḥ  hetutaḥ saṃbhavati tad  kriyāvat  yasya na saṃbhavati tad akriyam iti eka dharmi sthāyoḥ ca viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ ayugapad bhāva vinoḥ kāla vikalpaḥ yathā tad eva dravyam kriyā yuktam kriyāvat  anutpanna uparata kriyam punar akriyam iti na ca ayam nirṇaye niyamaḥ vimṛśya eva pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇaya iti kim tarhi bhavati khalu indriya artha sannikarṣāt utpanna pratyakṣe artha avadhāraṇam nirṇaya iti parīkṣā viṣaye tu vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ śāstre vāde ca vimarśa varjam iti vātsyāyanīye nyāya bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya prathama āhnikam tisraḥ kathā bhavanti vādaḥ  jalpaḥ  vitaṇḍā ca iti tāsām eka adhikaraṇa sthau viruddhau dharmaum pakṣa pratipakṣau pratyanīka bhāvāt  asti ātmā na asti ātmā iti nānā adhikaraṇa sthau viruddhau  api na pakṣa pratipakṣau yathā nitya ātmā anityā buddhiḥ iti parigrahaḥ  abhyupagama vyavasthā sa udyayam pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ  vādaḥ tasya viśeṣaṇam pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhanaḥ pramāṇa tarka upālambhaḥ ca pramāṇaiḥ tarkaṇa ca sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin kriyata iti sādhanam sthāpanā upālambhaḥ pratiṣadhaḥ tau sādhana upālambhau ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ vyatiṣaktau  anubaddhau ca tāvat  yāvat ekaḥ  nivṛtta ekataraḥ vyavasthita iti nivṛttasya upālambhaḥ  vyavasthitasya sādhanam iti jalpe nigraha sthāna viniyogāt vāde tad pratiṣedhaḥ tad pratiṣedhe ca kasyacid abhyanujñāna artham siddhānta aviruddha iti vacanam siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddha iti viruddhasya hetvābhāsasya nigraha sthānasya abhyanujñā vāde pañca avayava upapanna iti hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūnam hetu dāharaṇa adhikam adhikam iti ca etayoḥ abhyanujñāna artham iti avayaveṣu pramāṇa tarka antarbhāve pṛthak  pramāṇa tarka grahaṇam sādhana upalambha vyatiṣaṅga jñāpana artham anyathā ubhau  api pakṣau sthāpanā hetunā pravṛttau vāda iti syāt  antareṇa api ca avayava saṃbandham pramāṇāni artham sādhayanti iti dṛṣṭam tena api kalpena sādhana upālambhau vāde bhavata iti jñāpayati chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambhaḥ  jalpa iti vacanāt vinigrahaḥ  jalpa iti mā vijñāyi chala ja ati nigraha sthāna sādhana upālambha eva jalpaḥ pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ  vāda eva iti sa mā vijñāyi iti evam artha pṛthak  pramāṇa tarka grahaṇam iti yathā ukta upapanna iti pramāṇa tarka sādhana upālambhaḥ siddhānta aviruddhaḥ pañca avayava upapannaḥ pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ chala jāti nigra sthāna sādhana upālambha iti chala ja ati nigraha sthānaiḥ sādhanam upālambhaḥ ca asmin kriyata iti evaṃviśeṣaṇaḥ  jalpaḥ na khalu vai chala ja ati nigraha sthānaiḥ sādhanam kasyacid arthasya sambhavati pratiṣedha artha tā eva eṣām sāmānya lakṣaṇe viśeṣa lakṣaṇe ca śrūyate vacana vighātaḥ  artha vikalpā upattyā chalam iti sādharmya vaigharmyābhyām pratyavasthānam jātiḥ vipratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ ca nigraha sthānam iti viśeṣa lakṣaṇeṣu api yathāsvam iti na ca etad vijānīyāt pratiṣedha artha tayā eva artham sādhayanti iti chala ja ati nigraha sathāna upālambhaḥ  jalpa iti evam api ucyamāne vijñāyata etad iti pramāṇaiḥ sādhana upālambheyīḥ chala jāti nigraha sthānānām aṅga bhāvaḥ sva pakṣa rakṣaṇa artha tvāt na sva tantrāṇām sādhana bhāvaḥ yad tad pramāṇaiḥ arthasya sādhanam tatra chala jāti nigra sthānānām aṅga abhāvaḥ  rakṣaṇa artha tvāt tāni hi prayujyamānāni para pakṣa vighāte sva pakṣam rakṣanti tathā ca uktam tattva adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa artham jalpa vitaṇḍe bīja praroha saṃha rakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhā āvaraṇavat iti yaḥ ca asau pramāṇaiḥ pratipakṣasya upālambhaḥ tasya ca etāni prayujyamānāni pratiṣedha bighātāt sahakārīṇi bhavanti tad evam aṅgībhūtānām chala ādīnām upādānam jalpe na sva tantraṇām sādhana bhāvaḥ upālambhe tu svātantrayam api asti iti sa jalpaḥ  vitaṇḍā bhavati kim viśeṣaṇaḥ pratipakṣa sthāpanayā hīnaḥ yau tau samāna adhikaraṇau viruddhau dharmaum pakṣa pratipakṣau  iti uktau tayoḥ ekataram vaitaṇḍikaḥ  na sthāpayati iti para pakṣa pratiṣedhena eva pravarttata iti astu tarhi sa pratipakṣa hīnaḥ  vitaṇḍā yad vai khalu tad para pratiṣedha lakṣaṇam vākyam sa vaitaṇḍikasya pakṣaḥ na tu asau sādhyam kaṃcid artham pratijñāya sthāpayati iti tasmāt yathā anyāsam eva astu iti hetu lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ahetavaḥ  hetu sāmānyāt vetuvat ābhāsamānāḥ ta ime teṣām vyabhicāra ekatra avyavasthitiḥ saha vyabhicāreṇa varttate iti savyabhicāraḥ nidarśanam nityaḥ śabdaḥ  asparśa tvāt  sparśavān kuṃmoḥ anityaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ na ca tathā sparśavān śabdaḥ tasmāt asparśa tvāt nityaḥ śabda iti dṛṣṭānte sparśavat tvam anitya tvam ca dharmaum na sādhya sādhana bhūtau gṛhyate sparśavān  cāṇuḥ nityaḥ ca iti ātma ādau ca dṛṣṭānte udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ nitya tvam vyabhicarati asparśā ca buddhiḥ anityā ca iti evam dvividhā api dṛṣṭānte vyabhicārāt sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ  na asti iti lakṣaṇa abhāvāt ahetuḥ iti nitya tvam api ekaḥ  antar  anitya tvam api ekaḥ  antar  ekasmin  ante vidyata iti aikāntikaḥ  viparyayāt anaikānitakaḥ ubhāya anta vyāpaka tvāt iti tam viruṇaddhi iti tad virodhī abhyupetam siddhāntam vyāhanti iti yathā saḥ  ayam vikāraḥ  vyakteḥ apaiti nityatva pratiṣedhāt  na nityaḥ  vikāra upapadyate apetaḥ  api vikāraḥ  asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt  saḥ  ayam nityatva pratiṣedhāt iti hetuḥ vyakteḥ apetaḥ  api vikāraḥ  asti iti anena sva siddhāntena virudhyate katham vyaktiḥ ātma lābhaḥ upāyaḥ pracyutiḥ yadi ātma lābhāt pracyutaḥ  vikāraḥ  asti nityatva pratiṣedhau na upapadyate yad vyakteḥ apetasya api vikārasya astitvam tad  khalu nitya tvam iti nityatva pratiṣedhaḥ  nāma vikārasya ātma lābhāt pracyuteḥ upapattiḥ yad ā ātma lābhāt pracyavate tad anityam dṛṣṭam yad asti na tad ātma lābhāt pracyavate astitvam ca ātma lābhā pracyutiḥ iti ca viruddhau  etau dhamau na saha sambhavata iti saḥ  ayam hetuḥ yam siddhāntam āśritya pravarttate tam eva vyāhanti iti vimarśa adhiṣṭhānau pakṣa pratipakṣau  ubhau  anavasitau prakaraṇam tasya cintā vimarśāt prabhṛti prāk nirṇayāt yad samīkṣaṇam sā jijñāsā yad kṛtā sa nirṇaya artham prayukta ubhaya pakṣa sāmyāt  prakaraṇam anativartamānaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ  nirṇayāya na prakalpate prajñāpanam tu anityaḥ śabdaḥ  nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ iti anupalabhyamāna nitya dharmakam anityam dṛṣṭam sthālī ādi yantra samānaḥ  dharmaḥ saṃśaya kāraṇam hetu tvena upādīyate sa saṃśaya samaḥ savyabhicāra eva yā tu vimarśasya viśeṣa apekṣitā ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ ca sā prakaraṇam pravartayati yathā śabde nitya dharmaḥ  na upalabhyate evam anitya dharmaḥ api sā iyam ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ prakaraṇa cintām pravartayati katham viparyaye hi prakaraṇa nivṛtteḥ yadi nitya dharmaḥ śabde gṛhyeta na syāt prakaraṇam yadi vā anitya dharmaḥ  gṛhyeta evam api nivartteta prakaraṇam saḥ  ayam hetuḥ ubhau pakṣau pravartayan  anyatarasya nirṇayāya na prakalpate dravyam chāyā iti sādhyam gatimat tvāt iti hetuḥ sādhyena aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhanīya tvāt  sādhya samaḥ ayam api asiddha tvāt sādhayavat prajñāpayitavyaḥ sādhyam tāvat etad  kim puruṣavat śāyā api gacchati āhaḥ svidāvaraka dravye saṃsarpati āvaraṇa santānāt asannidhi santānaḥ  ayam tejasaḥ  gṛhyata iti sarpatā khalu dravyeṇa yaḥ  yaḥ tejaḥ bhāga āvriyate tasya tasya asannidhiḥ eva avicchinnaḥ gṛhyata iti āvaraṇam tu prāpti pratiṣedhaḥ kāla atyayena yuktaḥ  yasya artha eka deśaḥ  apadiśyamānasya sa kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atīta iti ucyate nidarśanam nityaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt rūpavat  prāgūrddham ca vyakteḥ avasthitam rūpam pradīpa ghaṭa saṃyogena vyajyate tathā ca śabdaḥ  api avasthitaḥ  bherī daṇḍa saṃyogena vyajyate dāruparaśu saṃyogena vā tasmāt saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvāt nityaḥ śabda iti ayam ahetuḥ kāla atyaya apadeśāt vyañjakasya saṃyogasya kālam na vyaṅgyasya rūpasya vyaktiḥ atyeti sati pradīpa saṃyoge rūpasya grahaṇam bhavati na nivṛtte saṃyoge rūpam gṛhyate nivṛtte tu dāruparaśu saṃyoge dūra sthena śabdaḥ śrūyate vibhāga kāle sā iyam śabdasya vyaktiḥ saṃyoga kālam atyeti iti na saṃyoga nimittā bhavati kasmāt  kāraṇa abhāvāt hi kārya abhāva iti evam udāharaṇa sādharmi asya abhāvāt asādhana mayam hetuḥ hetvābhāsa iti avayava viparyāsa vacanam na sūtra arthaḥ kasmāt  yasya yena artha sambandhaḥ  dūra sthasya api tasya saḥ arthataḥ  hi asamarthānām ānantaryam akāraṇam iti etad vacanāt viparyāsena uktaḥ  hetuḥ udāharaṇa sādharmyāt tathā vaidharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetu lakṣaṇa na jahāti ajahat hetu lakṣaṇam na hetvābhāsaḥ  bhavati iti avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpata kālam iti ca nigraha sthānam uktam tad eva idam punar ucyate iti atas tad na sūtra arthaḥ atha chalam na sāmānya lakṣaṇe chalam śakyam udāhartum vibhāge tu udāharaṇāni vibhāgaḥ ca teṣām nava kambalaḥ  ayam māṇavaka iti prayogaḥ atra navaḥ kambalaḥ  asya iti vaktuḥ ābhiprāyaḥ vigrahe tu viśeṣaḥ  na samāse tatra ayam chalavādī vaktuḥ abhiprāyāt avivakṣitam anyam artham nava kambalā asya iti tāvat abhihitam bhavatā iti kalpayati kalpayitvā ca asambhavena pratiṣedhati ekaḥ  asya kambalaḥ kutaḥ nava kambalā iti tad idam sāmānya śabde vāci nimitte chalam vākchalam iti asya pratyavasthānam sāmānya śabdasya aneka artha tve anyatara abhidhāna kalpanāyām viśeṣa vacanam nava kambala iti aneka artha abhidhānam navaḥ kambalaḥ  asya iti nava kambalā asya iti ca etasmin prayukte yā iyam kalpanā nava kambalā asya iti etad  bhavatā abhihitam tad ca na sambhavati iti etasyām anyatara abhidhāna kalpanāyām viśeṣaḥ  vaktavyaḥ yasmāt viśeṣaḥ  artha viśeṣeṣu vijñāyate ayam arthaḥ  anena abhihita iti sa ca viśeṣaḥ  na asti tasmāt mithyā abhiyoga mātram etad iti prasaddhiḥ ca loke śabda artha sambandhaḥ  abhidhāna abhidheya niyama niyogaḥ asya abhidhānasya ayam arthaḥ  abhidhena iti samānaḥ sāmānya śabdasya viśeṣaḥ  viśiṣṭa śabdasya prayukta pūrvāḥ ca ime śabdā arthe prayujyante na aprayukta pūrvāḥ prayogaḥ ca artha sampratyaya arthaḥ artha pratyayāt ca vyavahāra iti tatra evam artha gati arthe śabda prayoge sāmarthyāt sāmānya śabdasya prayoga niyamaḥ ajām grāmam naya sarpiḥ ādara brāhmaṇam bhojaya iti sāmānya śabdāḥ santaḥ  artha avayaveṣu prayujyante sāmarthyāt  yatra artha kriyā deśanā sambhavati tatra pravartante na artha sāmānye kriyā deśanā sambhavāt  evam ayam sāmānya śabdaḥ  nava kambala iti yaḥ  arthaḥ sambhavati navaḥ kambalaḥ  asya iti tatra pravartate yasatu na sambhavati nava kambalā asya iti tatra na pravartate saḥ  ayam anupapadyamāna artha kalpanayā para vākya upālambhaḥ te na kalpata iti ahaḥ khala vasau brāhmaṇaḥ  vidyā caraṇa sampanna iti ukte kaścid āha sambhavati brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad iti asya vacanasya vidhātaḥ  artha vikalpa upapattyā asambhūta artha kalpanayā kriyate yadi brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad  sambhavati nanu vrātye api sambhavet  vrātyaḥ  api brāhmaṇaḥ saḥ  api astu vidyā caraṇa sampannaḥ yad vivakṣitam artham āpnoti ca atyeti ca tad atisāmānyam yathā brāhmaṇa tvam vidyā caraṇa sampadam kvacid āpnoti kvacid atyeti iti sāmānya nimittam chalam sāmānyacchalam iti asya ca pratyavasthānam avivakṣita hetukasya viṣaya anuvādaḥ praśaṃsā artha tvāt  vākyasya tad atra asaṃbhūta artha kalpanā anupapattiḥ yathā sambhavanti asmin kṣetre śālaya iti anirākṛtam avivakṣitam ca bīja janma pravṛtti viṣayaḥ tu kṣetram praśasyate saḥ  ayam kṣetra anuvādaḥ  na asmin śālayaḥ  vidhīyanta iti bījātam śāli nirvṛttiḥ satī na vivakṣitā evam sambhavati brāhmaṇe vidyā caraṇa sampad iti sampad viṣayaḥ  brāhmaṇa tvam na sampad hetuḥ na ca atra hetuḥ vivakṣitaḥ viṣaya anuvādaḥ tu ayam praśaṃsā artha tvāt  vākyasya sati brāhmaṇa tve sampad hetuḥ samartha iti viṣayam ca praśaṃsatā vākyena yathā hetutaḥ phala nirvṛttiḥ na pratyākhyāyate tad evam sati vacana vidhātaḥ  asambhūta artha kalpanayā na upapadyata iti abhidhānasya dharmaḥ  yathā artha prayogaḥ dharma vikalpaḥ  anyatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra prayogaḥ tasya nirdeśe dharma vikalpa nirdeśe yathā mañcāḥ krośanti iti artha sadbhāvaneva pratiṣedhaḥ mañca sthāḥ puruṣāḥ krośanti na tu mañcāḥ krośanti kā punar atra artha vikalpa upattiḥ anyathā prayuktasya anyathā artha kalpanam bhaktyā prayoge prādhānyena kalpanam upacāra viṣayam chalam upacāracchalam upacāraḥ  nīta arthaḥ sahacaraṇa ādi nimittena atadbhāve tadvat abhidhānam upacāra iti atra samādhiḥ prasiddhe prayoge vaktuḥ yathā abhiprāyam śabda arthayoḥ abhyanujñā pratiṣedhaḥ  vā na cchandataḥ pradhāna bhūtasya śabdasya bhāktasya ca guṇa bhūtasya prayoga ubhayoḥ loke siddhaḥ siddhe prayoge yathā vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ tathā śabda arthau  anujñeyau pratiṣedhyau vā na cchandataḥ yadi vaktā pradhāna śabdam prayuṅkte yathābhūtasya abhyanujñā pratiṣedhaḥ  vā na nchandataḥ atha guṇa bhūtam tadā guṇa bhūtasya yatra tu vaktā guṇa bhūtam śabdam prayuṅkte pradhāna bhūtam abhipretya paraḥ pratiṣedhati sva manīṣayā pratiṣedhaḥ  asau bhavati na para upālambha iti na vāc chalāt upacāra  chalam bhidyate tasya api artha antara kalpanāyā aviśeṣāt  iha api sthāni arthaḥ  guṇa śabdaḥ pradhāna śabdaḥ sathāna artha iti kalpayitvā pratiṣidhyata iti na vākchalam eva upacāra  chalam tasya artha sadbhāva pratiṣedhasya artha antara bhāvāt kutas  artha antara kalpanātaḥ anyā hi artha anta kalpanā anyaḥ  artha sadbhāva pratiṣedha iti chalasya dvi tvam abhyanujñāya tri tvam pratiṣidhyate kiṃcid sādharmyāt  yathā ca ayam hetuḥ trit tvam pratiṣedhati tathā dvi tvam api abhyanujñātam pratiṣedhati vidyate hi kiṃcid sādharmyāt na nivartate tri tvam api na nivartsyati iti ata ūddham prayukte hi hetau yaḥ prasaṅgaḥ  jāyate sā jātiḥ sa ca prasaṅgaḥ sādharmya vaidharmyābhyā pratyavasthānam upālambhaḥ pratiṣedha iti udāharaṇa sādharmyāt  sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti asya udāharaṇa vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam tathā udāharaṇa vaidharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti asya udāharaṇa sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam pratyanīka bhāvāt jāyamānaḥ  arthaḥ  jātiḥ ati viparītā vā kutsitā vā pratipattiḥ vipratipattiḥ vipratipadyamānaḥ parājayam prāpnoti nigraha sthānam khalu parājaya prāptiḥ apratipattiḥ tu ārambha viṣaye api anārambhaḥ pareṇa sthāpitam vā na pratiṣedhati pratiṣedham vā na uddharati asamāsāt ca na ete eva nigraha sthāne iti kim punar dṛṣṭāntavat jāti nigraha sthānayoḥ abhedaḥ  atha siddhāntavat bheda iti ata āha tasya sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt jāti bahu tvam tayoḥ ca vipratipatti apratipattyaḥ vikalpān nigraha sthāna bahuttvam nānā kalpaḥ  vikalpaḥ vividhaḥ  vā kalpaḥ  vikalpaḥ tatra ananubhāṣaṇam ajñānam apratibhā vikṣepaḥ  mata anujñā paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam iti apratipattiḥ nigraha sthānam śeṣaḥ tu vipratipattiḥ iti ta ime pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthā uddiṣṭā yathoddeśam ca lakṣitā yathālakṣaṇam ca parīkṣiṣyanta iti trividhā ca asya śāstrasya pravṛttiḥ veditavyā iti vātsyāyanīye nyāya bhāṣye prathama adhyāyasya dvitīya āhnikam samāptaḥ ca ayam prathamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ #################################################################### śrī śrī nivāsa svāmi śrī vināyaka svāmi śrī sarasvatī devī om atha saṭīke nyāya bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam ata ūrdhvam pramāṇa ādi parīkṣā sā ca vimṛśya pakṣa pratipakṣābhyām artha avadhāraṇam nirṇayaḥ iti agre vimarśa eva parīkṣyate samānasya dharmasya adhyavasāyāt  saṃśayaḥ  na dharma mātrāt atha vā asamānam anayoḥ dharmam upalabhe iti dharma dharmi grahaṇe saṃśaya abhāva iti atha vā samāna dharma adhyavasāyāt artha antara bhūte dharmiṇi saṃśayaḥ  anupapannaḥ na jātu rūpāsaya artha antara bhūtasya adhyavasāyāt artha antara bhūte sparśe saṃśaya iti atha vā na adhyavasāyāt artha avadhāraṇāt  anavadhāraṇa jñānam saṃśaya upapadyate kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya abhavāt iti etena aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt  iti vyākhyātam anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt ca saṃśayaḥ  na bhavati tatas  hi anyatara avadhāraṇam eva iti na vipratipatti mātrāt avyavasthā mātrāt vā saṃśayaḥ kim tarhi vipratipattim upalabhamānasya saṃśayaḥ evam avyavasthāyām api iti atha vā aasti ātmā iti eke anāsti ātmā iti apare manyante iti upalabdheḥ katham saṃśayaḥ syāt  iti tathā upalabdhiḥ avyavasthitā anupalabdhiḥ  ca avyavasthitā iti vibhāgena adhyavasite saṃśayaḥ  na upapadyate iti yām va vipratipattim bhavān saṃśaya hetum manyate sā saṃpratipattiḥ sā hi dvayoḥ pratyanīka dharma viṣayā tatra yadi viprattipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ saṃpratipatteḥ eva saṃśaya iti na saṃśayaḥ yadi tāvat iyam avyavasthā ātmani eva vyavasthitā vyavasthānāt avyavasthā na bhavati iti anupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ atha avyavasthā ātmani na vyavasthitā evam atādātmyāt avyavasthā na bhavati iti saṃśaya abhāva iti yena kalpena bhavān samāna dharma upapatteḥ saṃśaya iti manyate tena khalu  atyanta saṃśayaḥ prasajyate samāna dharma upapatteḥ anucchedāt saṃśaya anucchedaḥ na ayam atad dharmā dharmī vimṛśyamānaḥ  gṛhyate satatam tu tad dharmā bhavati iti asya pratiṣedha prapañcasya saṃkṣepeṇa uddhāraḥ na saṃśaya anutpattiḥ saṃśaya anucchedaḥ ca prasajyate katham yad tāvat asamāna dharma adhyavasāyaḥ saṃśaya hatuḥ na samāna dharma mātram iti evam etad  kasmāt evam na ucyate iti vaśeṣa apekṣiḥ iti vacanāt  tad siddheḥ viśeṣasya apekṣā ākāṅkṣā sā ca anupalabhyamāne vaśeṣe simarthā na ca uktam asamāna dharma apekṣaḥ iti samāne ca dharme katham ākāṅkṣā na bhavet  yadi ayam apratyakṣaḥ myāt  etena sāmarthyena vajñāyite asamāna dharma adhyavasāyāt iti upapatti vacanāt vā samāna dharma upapatteḥ iti ucyate na ca anyā sadbhāva saṃvedanāt ṛte samāna dharma upapattiḥ asti anupalabhyamāna sadbhāvaḥ  hi samānaḥ  dharmaḥ  avadyimānavat  bhavati iti vaṣiya śabdena vā vaṣiyiṇaḥ pratyayasya abhidhānam yathā loke adhūmena agniḥ anumīyate iti ukte adhūma darśanena agniḥ anumīyate iti jñāyate katham dṛṣṭvā hi dhūmam atha agnim anuminoti na adṛṣṭe na cam vākye darśana śabdaḥ śrūyate anujānāti ca vākyasya artha pratyāyaka tvam tena manyāmahe vaṣiya śabdena vaṣiyiṇaḥ pratyayasya abhidhānam boddha anujānāti evam iha api samāna dharma śabdena samāna dharma adhyavasāyamāha iti yad uktam asamānam anayaḥ dharmam upalabhe iti dharma dharmi grahaṇe saṃśaya abhāvaḥ iti pūrva dṛṣṭa viṣayam etatuyāvaham arthau pūrvam adrākṣam tayoḥ samānam dharmam upalabhe viśeṣam na upalabhe iti katham nu viśeṣam paśyeyam yena anyataram avadhārayeyam iti na ca etad  samāna dharma upalabdhau dharma dharmi grahaṇa mātreṇa nivartate iti yad ca uktam na artha antara adhyavasāyāt anyatra saṃśaya iti yaḥ  hi artha antara adhyavasāya mātram saṃśaya hetum upādadīta sa evam vācya iti yad punar etad  kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpya abhāvāt iti kāraṇasya bhāva abhāvayoḥ kāryasya bhāva abhāvau kārya kāraṇayoḥ sārūpyam uyasya utpādāt yad utpadyate yasya ca anutpādāt  yad na utpadyate tad  kāraṇam kāryam itarad ityet sārūpyam asti ca saṃśaya kāraṇe saṃśaye ca etad iti etena aneka dharma adhyavasāyāt iti pratiṣedhaḥ parihṛta iti yad punar etad uktam vipratipatti avyavasthā adhyavasāyāt ca na saṃśaya iti pṛthak pravādayoḥ vyāhatam artham upalabhe viśeṣam ca na jānāmiunā upalabhe yena anyataram avadhārayeyam tad kotra viśeṣaḥ syāt  yena ekataram avadhārayeyam iti saṃśayaḥ  vipratipatti jani toyam na śakyaḥ  vipratipatti saṃpratipatti mātreṇa nivartayitum iti evam upalabdhi anupalabdhi avyavasthā kṛte saṃśaye veditavyam iti yad punar etad  vipratipattau ca saṃpratipatteḥ iti vipratipatti śabdasya yorthaḥ tad adhyavasāyaḥ  viśeṣa apekṣaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ tasya ca samākhyā antareṇa na nivṛtti ḥusamāne adhikaraṇe vyāhata arthau pravādau vipratipatti śabdasya arthaḥ tad adhyavasāyaḥ ca viśeṣa apekṣaḥ saṃśaya hetuḥ na ca asya saṃpratipatti śabde samākhyā antare yojyamāne saṃśaya hetu tvam nivartate tad idam akṛtabuddhi saṃmohanam iti yad punar  avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt ca avyavasthāyāḥ iti saṃśaya hetoḥ arthasya apratiṣedhāt  avyavasthā abhyanujñānāt ca nimitta antareṇa śabda antara kalpanā vyarthā śabda antara kalpanā aavyavasthā khalu  avyavasthā na bhavati avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthita tvāt iti na anayoḥ upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ sat asat viṣaya tvam viśeṣa apekṣam saṃśaya hetuḥ na bhavati iti pratiṣidhyate yāvatā ca avyavasthā ātmani vyavasthitā na tāvatā ātmānam jahāti tāvatā hi anujñātā bhavati avyavasthā evam iyam kriyamāṇā api śabda antara kalpanā na artha antaram sādhayati iti yad punar etad  tathā atyanta saṃśayaḥ tad dharma sātatya upapatteḥ iti na ayam samāna dharma ādibhya eva saṃśayaḥ kim tarhi tad viṣaya adhyavasāyāt  viśeṣa smṛti sahitāt  iti atas  na atyanta saṃśaya iti anyatara dharma adhyavasāyāt vā na saṃśayaḥ iti tad na yuktam viśeṣa apekṣaḥ  vimarśaḥ saṃśayaḥ iti vacanāt  viśeṣaḥ ca anyatara dharmaḥ  na tasmin   adhyavasīyamāne viśeṣa apekṣā saṃbhavati iti yatra yatra saṃśaya pūrvikā parīkṣā śāstre kathāyām vā tatra tatra evam saṃśaye pareṇa pratiṣiddhe samādhiḥ vācya iti atas  sarva parīkṣā vyāpi tvāt prathamam saṃśayaḥ parīkṣita iti atha pramāṇa parīkṣā pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇyam na asti traikālya asiddheḥu pūrva apara sahabhāva anupapatteḥ iti atha sāmānya vacanasya artha vibhāgaḥ gandha ādi viṣayam jñānam pratyakṣam tad  yadi pūrvam paścāt  gandha ādīnām siddhiḥ na idam gandha ādi saṃnikarṣāt utpadyate iti asati pramāṇe kena pramīyamāṇaḥ  arthaḥ prameyaḥ syāt  pramāṇena khalu pramīyamāṇaḥ  arthaḥ prameyam iti etad  sidhyati yadi pramāṇam prameyam ca yugapad  bhavataḥ evam api gandha ādiṣu indriya artheṣu jñānāni pratyartha niyatāni yugapad  saṃbhavanti iti jñānānām pratyartha niyata tvāt  krama vṛttitva abhāva ḥuyā imā buddhayaḥ krameṇa artheṣu vartante tāsām krama vṛtti tvam na saṃbhavati iti vyāghātaḥ ca yugapad  jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ  liṅgam iti etāvān  ca pramāṇa prameyayoḥ sadbhāva viṣayaḥ sa ca anupapanna iti tasmāt  pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇa tvam na saṃbhavati iti asya samādhiḥ upalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāvā aniyamāt  yathādarśanam vibhāga vacanam kvacid upalabdhi hetuḥ pūrvam paścāt upalabdhi viṣayaḥ  yathā ādityasya prakāśaḥ utpadyamānānām kvacid  pūrvam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ paścāt upalabdhi hetuḥ yathā avasthitānām pradīpaḥ kvacid upalabdhi hetuḥ upalabdhi viṣayaḥ ca saha bhavataḥ  yathā dhūmena agneḥ grahaṇam iti upalabdhi hetuḥ ca pramāṇam prameyam tu upalabdhi viṣayaḥ evam pramāṇa prameyayoḥ pūrva apara sahabhāve aniyate yathārthaḥ  dṛśyate tathā vibhajya vacanīya iti tatra ekāntena pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ sāmānyena khalu vibhajya pratiṣedha ukta iti samākhyā heta usra ekālya yogāt tathābhūtā samākhyā yad punar idam apaścāt siddhauuasati pramāṇe prameyam na sidhyati pramāṇena pramīyamāṇaḥ  arthaḥ prameyam iti vijñāyate iti pramāṇam iti etasyāḥ samākhyāyā upalabdhi hetu tvam nimittam tasya traikālya yogaḥ aupalabdhim akārṣīt aupalabdhim karoti aupalabdhim kariṣyati iti samākhyā hetoḥ traikālya yogāt  samākhyā tathābhūtā pramitaḥ  anena arthaḥ pramīyate pramāsyate iti pramāṇam pramitam pramīyate pramāsyate iti ca prameyam evam sati bhaviṣyati asmin hetuta upalabdhiḥupramāsyate ayam arthaḥ prameyam idam iti etad sarvam bhavati iti traikālyān abhyanujñāne ca vyavahāra anupapa ttiḥ yaḥ ca evam na abhyanujānīyāt  tasya apācakam ānaya pakṣyati alāvakam ānaya laviṣyati iti vyavahāraḥ  na upapadyate iti pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam traikālya asiddheḥ iti evamādi vākyam pramāṇa pratiṣedhaḥ tatra ayam praṣṭavyaḥ atha anena pratiṣedhena bhavatā kim kriyate iti kim saṃbhavaḥ  nivartyate atha asaṃbhāvaḥ  jñāpyate iti tad  yadi saṃbhavaḥ  nivartyate sati saṃbhave pratyakṣa ādīnām pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ atha asaṃbhavaḥ  jñāpyate pramāṇa lakṣaṇam prāptaḥ tarhi pratiṣedhaḥ pramāṇa asaṃbhavasya upalabdhi hetu tvāt iti kim ca atas  asya tu vibhāgaḥ pūrvam hi pratiṣedha siddhau  asati pratiṣedhye kim anena pratiṣidhyate paścāt  siddhau pratiṣedha asiddhiḥ pratiṣedha abhāvāt iti yūgapad siddhau pratiṣedhya siddhi abhyanujñānāt anarthakaḥ pratiṣedha iti pratiṣedha lakṣaṇe ca vākye anupapadyamāne siddham pratyakṣa ādīnām pramāṇa tvam iti katham traikālya asiddheḥ iti asya hetoḥ yadyudāharaṇam upādīyate hetu arthasya sādhaka tvam dṛṣṭānte darśayitavyam iti na ca tarhi pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam atha pratyakṣa ādīnām aprāmāṇyam upādīyamānam api udāharaṇam na artham sādhayiṣyati iti soyam sarva pramāṇaiḥ vyāhataḥ  hetuḥ ahetuḥ siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhī viruddhaḥ iti vākya arthaḥ  hi asya siddhāntaḥ sa ca vākya arthaḥ apratyakṣa ādīni na artham sādhayanti iti idam ca avayavānām upādānam arthasya sādhanāya iti atha na upādīyate apradarśita hetu arthasya dṛṣṭānte na sādhaka tvam iti pratiṣedhaḥ  na upapadyate hetutva asiddheḥ iti pratiṣedha lakṣaṇe sva vākye teṣām avayava āśritānām pratyakṣa ādīnām prāmāṇye abhyanujñāyamāne para vākyepi avayava āśritānām prāmāṇyam prasajyate aviśeṣāt iti evam ca na sarvāṇi pramāṇāni pratiṣidhyante iti vipratiṣedhaḥ iti vi iti ayam upasargaḥ saṃpratipatti arthe navya āghāte artha abhāvāt iti kimartham punar idam ucyate pūrva ukta nibandhana artham yad tāvat pūrva uktam aupalabdhi hetoḥ upalabdhi viṣayasya ca arthasya pūrva apara sahabhāva aniyamād yathādarśanam vibhāga vacanam iti tad itas  samuttthānam yathā vijñāyeta aniyama darśī khalu ayam krṛṣiḥ niyamena pratiṣedham pratyācaṣṭe traikālyasya ca ayuktaḥ pratiṣedha iti tatra ekām vidhām udāharati śabdāt ātodya siddhivat iti yathā paścāt  siddhena śabdane pūrva siddham ātā udyam anumīyate sādhyam ca ātodyam sādhanam ca śabdaḥ antarhite hi ātodye svanataḥ  anumānam bhavati iti vīṇā vādyate veṇuḥ pūryate iti svana viśeṣeṇa ātodya viśeṣam pratipadyate tathā pūrva siddham upalabdhi viṣayam paścāt siddhena upalabdhi hetunā pratipadyate iti nidarśana artha tvāt ca asya śeṣayoḥ vidhayoḥ yathā uktam udāharaṇam veditavyam iti kasmāt  punar iha tad na ucyate pūrva uktam upapādyate iti sarvathā tāvat ayam arthaḥ prakāśayitavyaḥ sa iha vā prakāśyeta tatra vā na kaścid viśeṣa iti pramāṇam prameyam iti ca samākhyā samāveśena vartate samākhyā nimitta vaśāt  samākhyā nimittam tu upalabdhi sādhanam pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣayaḥ ca prameyam iti yadā ca upalabdhi viṣayaḥ kvacid upalabdhi sādhanam bhavati tadā pramāṇam prameyam iti ca ekaḥ arthaḥ  abhidhīyate asya arthasya avadyotana artham idam ucyate gurutva parimāṇa jñāna sādhanam tulā pramāṇam jñāna viṣayaḥ  guru dravyam suvarṇa ādi prameyam yadā ca suvarṇa ādinā tulā antaram vyavasthāpyate tadā tulā antara pratipattau suvarṇa ādi pramāṇam tulā antaram prameyam iti evam anavayavena tantra artha uddiṣṭaḥ  veditavyaḥ ātmā tāvat upalabidha viṣaya tvāt prameye paripaṭhitaḥ upalabdhau ca svātantryāt  pramātā buddhiḥ upalabdhi sādhana tvāt  pramāṇam upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt  prameyam ubhaya abhāvāt  pramitiḥ evam artha viśeṣe samākhyā samāveśaḥ  yojyaḥ tathā ca kāraka śabdā nimitta vaśāt  samāveśena vartante iti avṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati iti sva sthitau svātantryāt  kartā avṛkṣam paśyati iti darśanena āptum iṣyamāṇa tvāt  karma avṛkṣeṇa candramasam jñāpayati iti jñāpakasya sādhakatama tvāt  karaṇam avṛkṣāya udakam āsiñcati iti āsicyamānena udakena vṛkṣam abhipraiti iti saṃpradānam avṛkṣāt  parṇam patati iti dhruvam apāye apādānam iti apādānam avṛkṣe vayāṃsi santi iti ādhāraḥ  adhikaraṇam iti adhikaraṇam evam ca sati ca dravya mātram kārakam na vā kriyā mātram kim tarhi kriyā sādhanam kriyā viśeṣa yuktam kārakam yad  kriyā sādhanam svatantraḥ sa kartā na dravya mātram na kriyā mātram kriyayā vyāptum iṣyamāṇatamam karma na dravya mātram na kriyā mātram evam sādhakatama ādiṣu api evam ca kāraka an vā ākhyānam yathā eva upapattita evam lakṣaṇataḥ kāraka an vā ākhyānam api na dravya mātreṇa na kriyayā vā kim tarhi kriyā sādhane kriyā viśeṣa yukta iti kāparaka śabdaḥ ca ayam pramāṇam prameyam iti sa ca kāraka dharmam na hātum arhati asti bhaḥ kāraka śabdānām nimitta vaśāt  samāveśaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni ca pramāṇāni upalabdhi hetu tvāt  prameyam ca upalabdhi viṣaya tvāt  saṃvedyāni pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni ca apratyakṣeṇa upalabhe anumānena upalabhe upamānena upalabhe āgamena upalabhe pratyakṣam me jñānam ānumānikam me jñānam aupamānikam me jñānam āgamikam me jñānam iti viśeṣā gṛhyante lakṣaṇataḥ ca jñāpyamānāni jñāyante viśeṣeṇa aindriya artha saṃnikarṣa utpannam jñānam iti evamādinā sā iyam upalabdhiḥ pratyakṣa ādi viṣayā kim pramāṇa antarataḥ atha antareṇa pramāṇam asādhanā iti kaḥ ca atra viśeṣaḥ yadi pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇena upalabhyante yena pramāṇena upalabhyante tad  pramāṇa antaram astīni pramāṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ prasajyate iti anavasthām āha tasya api anyena tasya api anyena iti na ca anavasthā śakyā anujñātum anupapatteḥ iti yadi pratyakṣa ādi upalabdhau pramāṇa antaram nivartate ātmā iti upalabdhau  api pramāṇa antaram nivartsyati aviśeṣāt  evam ca sarva pramāṇa vilopa iti ata āha yathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ pratyakṣa aṅga tvāt  dṛśya darśane pramāṇam sa ca pratyakṣa antareṇa cakṣuṣaḥ saṃnikarṣeṇa gṛhyate pradīpa bhāva abhāvayoḥ darśanasya tathā abhāvāt  darśana hetuḥ anumīyate atamasi pradīpam upādadīthāḥ iti āpta upadeśena api pratipadyate evam pratyakṣa ādīnām yathādarśanam pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva upasabdhiḥ indriyāṇi tāvat  sva viṣaya grahaṇena eva anumīyante arthāḥ pratyakṣataḥ gṛhyante indriya artha saṃnikarṣāḥ tu āvaraṇena liṅgena anumīyante indriya artha saṃnikarṣa utpannam jñānam ātma manasoḥ saṃyoga viśeṣāt ātma samavāyāt ca sukha ādivat  gṛhyate evam pramāṇa viśeṣaḥ  vibhajya vacanīyaḥ yathā ca dṛśyaḥ san pradīpa prakāśaḥ  dṛśya antarāṇām darśana hetuḥ iti dṛśya darśana vyavasthām labhate evam prameyam sat  kiñcid artha jātam upalabdhi hetu tvāt pramāṇa prameya vyavasthām labhate sā iyam pratayakṣa ādibhiḥ eva pratyakṣa ādīnām yathādarśanam upalabdhiḥ na pramāṇa antarataḥ  na ca pramāṇa manteraṇa niḥsādhana iti tana eva tasya agrahaṇam iti ced  na artha bhedasya lakṣaṇa sāmānyāt  pratyakṣa ādīnām pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ eva grahaṇam iti ayuktam anyena hi anyasya grahaṇam dṛṣṭam iti na artha bhedasya lakṣaṇa sāmānyātu pratyakṣa lakṣaṇena anekorthaḥ saṃgṛhītaḥ tatra kena cit  kasyacid  grahaṇam iti adoṣaḥ evam anumāna ādiṣu api iti yathā uddhṛtena udakena āśaya sthasya grahaṇam iti jñātṛ manasoḥ ca darśanāt  aaham sukhī aham duḥkhī ca iti tena eva jñātrā tasya eva grahaṇam dṛśyate yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ  liṅgam iti ca tena eva manasā tasya eva anumānam dṛśyate jñātuḥ jñeyasya ca abhedaḥ  grahaṇasya grāhyasya ca abheda iti nimitta bhedaḥ  atra iti ced  samānam na nimitta antareṇa vinā jñāta ātmānam jānīte na ca nimitta antareṇa vinā manasā manaḥ  gṛhyate iti samānam etad  pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ pratyakṣa ādīnām grahaṇam iti atra api artha bhedaḥ  na gṛhyate iti pratyakṣa ādīnām ca aviṣayasya anupapatteḥ yadi syāt  kiñcid artha jātam pratyakṣa ādīnām aviṣayaḥ yad  pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ na śakyam grahītum tasya grahaṇāya pramāṇa antaram upādīyeta tad tu na śakyam kenacid upapādayatum iti pratayakṣa ādīnām yathādarśanam eva idam sat ca asat ca sarvam viṣaya iti kecid tu dṛṣṭāntam aparigṛhītam hetunā viśeṣa hetum antareṇa sādhya sādhanāya upādadate yathā pradīpa prakāśaḥ pradīpa antara prakāśam antareṇa gṛhyate tathā pramāṇāni pramāṇa antaram antareṇa gṛhyante iti sa ca ayam kva cit nivṛtti darśanāt anivṛtti darśanāt ca kva cit anekāntaḥ yathā ayam prasaṅgaḥ  nivṛtti darśanāt  pramāṇa sādhanāya upādīyate evam prameya sādhanāya api upādeyaḥ aviśeṣa hetu tvāt yathā sthālī ādi rūpa grahaṇe pradīpa prakāśaḥ prameya sādhanāya upādīyate evam pramāṇa sādhanāya api upādeyaḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt soyam viśeṣa hetu parigraham antareṇa dṛṣṭānta ekasmin pakṣe upādeyaḥ  na pratipakṣe iti anekāntaḥ ekasmin  ca pakṣe dṛṣṭānta iti anekāntaḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt iti viśeṣa hetu parigrahe sati upasaṃhāra abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ viśeṣa hetu parigṛhītaḥ tu dṛṣṭānta ekasmin pakṣe upasaṃhiyamāṇaḥ  na śakyaḥ  ananujñātum evam ca sati aanekāntaḥ iti ayam pratiṣedhaḥ  na bhavati pratyakṣa ādīnām pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ upalabdhau   anavasthā iticed  na saṃvid viṣaya nimittānām upalabdhyā vyavahāra upapa tteḥ pratyakṣeṇa artham upalabhe anumānena artham upalabhe upamānena artham upalabhe āgamena artham upalabhe iti pratyakṣam me jñānam ānumānikam me jñānam aupamānikam me jñānam āgamikam me jñānam iti saṃvid viṣayam saṃvid nimittam ca upalabhamānasya dharma artha sukha apavarga prayojanaḥ tad pratyanīka parivarjana prayojananaḥ ca vyavahāra upapadyate soyam tāvatyā eva nirvartate na ca asti vyavahāra antaram anavasthā sādhanīyam yena prayuktaḥ  anavasthām upādadīta iti sāmānyena pramāṇāni parīkṣya viśeṣeṇa parīkṣyante tatra ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ  hi kāraṇa antaram na uktam iti na ca asaṃyukte dravye saṃyoga janyasya guṇasya utpattiḥ iti jñāna utpatti darśanāt ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ kāraṇam manaḥ saṃnikarṣa anapekṣasya ca indrinaya artha saṃnikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tve yugapad utpadyeran buddhaya iti manaḥ saṃnikarṣa upi kāraṇam tad idam sūtram purastāt  kṛta bhāṣyam ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣa abhāve na utpadyate pratyakṣam indriya artha saṃnikarṣa abhāvavat iti sati ca indriya artha saṃnikarṣe jñāna utpatti darśanāt kāraṇa bhāvam bruvate diś ādiṣu satsu jñāna bhāvāt  tāni api kāraṇāni iti akāraṇa bhāvepi jñāna utpatteḥ diś ādi saṃnidhera varjanīya tvāt yadā api akāraṇam diś ādīni jñāna utpattau tadā api satsu diś ādiṣu jñānena bhavitavyam na hi diś ādīnām saṃnidhiḥ śakyaḥ parivarjayitum iti tatra kāraṇa bhāve hetu vacanam etasmāt  hetoḥ diś ādīni jñāna kāraṇāni iti ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ tarhi upasaṃkhyeya iti tatra idam ucyate jñānam ātma liṅgam tad guṇatavāt  na ca asaṃyukte dravye saṃyoga jasya guṇasya utpattiḥ asti iti anavarodha iti vartate yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ  liṅgam iti ucyamāne sidhyati eva manaḥ saṃnikārṣā apekṣa indriya artha saṃnikarṣaḥ  jñāna kāraṇam iti pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdānām nimittam ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ pratyakṣasya eva indriya artha saṃnikarṣa iti  asamānaḥ  asamāna tvāt  tasya grahaṇam indriya artha saṃnikarṣasya grahaṇam na ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣasya iti ekadā khalu ayam prabodha kālam praṇidhāya suptaḥ praṇidhāna vaśāt  prabudhyate yadā tu tīvrau dhvani sparśaum prabodha kāraṇam bhavataḥ tadā prasuptasya indriya artha saṃnikarṣa nimittam prabodha jñānam utpadyate tatra na jñātuḥ manasaḥ  ca saṃnikarṣasya prādhānyam bhavati kim tarhi indriya arthayoḥ saṃnikarṣasya na hi atmā jijñāsamānaḥ prayatnena manaḥ tadā prerayati iti ekadā khalu ayam viṣāya antara avyāsakta manāḥ saṃkalpa vaśāt  viṣaya antaram jijñāsamānaḥ prayatna preritena manasā indriyam saṃyojya yad  viṣaya antaram jānīte yadā tu khalu asya niḥsaṃkalpasya nirjijñāsasya ca vyāsakta manasaḥ  bāhya viṣaya upanipātanād jñānam utpadyate tadā indriya artha saṃnikarṣasya prādhānyam na hi atra asau jijñāsamānaḥ prayatnena manaḥ prerayati iti prādhānyāt ca indrinaya artha saṃnikarṣasya grahaṇam kāryam guṇa tvāt na ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣasya iti prādhānye ca hetu antaram taiḥ indriyaiḥ arthaiḥ ca vyapadiśyante jñāna viśeṣāḥ katham aghrāṇena jighrati acakṣuṣā paśyati arasanayā rasayati iti aghrāṇa vijñānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam rasana vijñānam agandha vijñānam rūpa vijñānam rasa vijñānam iti ca indriya viṣaya viśeṣāt ca pañcadhā buddhiḥ bhavati atas  prādhanyam indriya artha saṃnikarṣasya iti yad uktam aindriya artha saṃnikarṣa grahaṇam kāryam na ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣasya iti kasyāt  supta vyāsakta manasām indriya arthayoḥ saṃnikarṣasya jñāna nimitta tvāt iti soyam yadi tāvat  kvacid ātma manasoḥ sa nikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tvam na iṣyate tadā yugapad jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ  liṅgam iti vyāhanyeta na idānīm manasaḥ saṃnikarṣam indriya artha saṃnikarṣaḥ  apekṣate manaḥ saṃyoga anapekṣāyām ca yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅgaḥ atha mā bhūd vyāghāta iti sarva vijñānānām ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ kāraṇam iṣyate tad avastham eva idam bhavati ajñāna kāraṇa tvāt ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣasya grahaṇam kāryam iti na asti vyāghātaḥ na hi ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇa tvam vyabhicarati indriya artha saṃnikarṣasya prādhānyam upādīyate artha viśeṣa prābalyāt hi supta vyāsakta manasām jñāna utpattiḥ ekadā bhavati artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid eva indriya arthaḥ tasya prābalyam tīvra tā paṭute tad ca artha viśeṣa prābalyām indriya artha saṃnikarṣa viṣayam na ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣa viṣayam tasmāt indriya artha saṃnikarṣaḥ pradhānam iti asati praṇidhāne saṃkalpe ca asati supta vyāsakta manasām yad  indriya artha saṃnikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam tatra manaḥ saṃyoga upi kāraṇam iti manasi kriyā kāraṇam vācyam iti yathā eva jñātuḥ khalu ayam icchā janitaḥ prayatnaḥ  manasaḥ preraka ātma guṇa evam ātmani guṇa antaram sarvasya sādhakam pravṛtti doṣa janitam asti yena preritam mana indriyeṇa saṃbadhyate tena hi  apreryamāṇe manasi saṃyoga abhāvāt jñānātutpattau sarva artha tāsya nivartate eṣitavyam cāsaya guṇa antarasya dravya guṇa karma kāraka tvam anyathā hi caturvidhānām aṇūnām bhūta sūkṣmāṇām manasām ca tatas  anyasya kriyā hetoḥ asaṃbhavāt śarīra indriya viṣayāṇām anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ yad idam indriya artha saṃnikarṣāt utpadyate jñānam avṛkṣaḥ iti etad  kila pratyakṣam tad khalu anumānam eva kasmāt  eka deśa grahaṇāt  vṛkṣasya upalabdheḥ arvāc bhāga mayam gṛhītvā vṛkṣam upalabhate na ca eka deśaḥ  vṛkṣaḥ tatra yathā dhūmam gṛhītvā vahnim anuminoti tādṛś eva tad  bhavati kim punar gṛhyamāṇāt eka deśāt  artha antaram anumeyam manyase avayava samūha pakṣe avayava antarāṇi dravya utpatti pakṣe tāni ca avayavī ca iti avayava samūha pakṣe tāvat eka deśa grahaṇāt  vṛkṣa buddheḥ abhāvaḥ na hi  agṛhyamāṇam eka deśa antaram vṛkṣaḥ  gṛhyamāṇa eka deśavat iti atha eka deśa grahaṇāt eka deśa antara anumāne samudāya pratisaṃdhānāt  tatra vṛkṣa buddhiḥ na tarhi vṛkṣa buddhiḥ anumānam evam sati bhavitum arhati iti dravya antara utpatti pakṣe na avayavi  anumeyaḥ asya eka deśa saṃbaddhasya agrahaṇāt  grahaṇe ca aviśeṣāt anamumeyatva abhāvaḥ tasmāt  vṛkṣa buddhiḥ anumānam na bhavati eka deśa grahaṇam āśritya pratyakṣasya anumāna tvam upapādyate tad ca na pratyakṣam anumānam kasmāt  pratyakṣeṇa eva upalambhāt  yad  tad eka deśa grahaṇam āśrīyate pratyakṣeṇa asau  upalambhaḥ na ca upalambhaḥ  nirviṣayosti yāvat ca artha jātam tasya viṣayaḥ tāvat abhyanujñāyamānam pratyakṣa vyavasthāpakam bhavati kim punar tatas  anyat artha jām avayavī samudāyaḥ  vā na ca eva deśa grahaṇam anumānam bhāvayitum śakyam hetu abhāvāt iti anyathā api ca pratyakṣasya na anumānatva prasaṅgaḥ tad pūrvaka tvāt pratyakṣa pūrvakam anumānam saṃbaddhau  agni dhūmau pratyakṣataḥ dṛṣṭavataḥ  dhūma pratyakṣa darśanāt  agnau  anumānam bhavati yad ca saṃbaddhayoḥ liṅga liṅganoḥ pratyakṣam yad ca liṅmātra pratyakṣa grahaṇam na etad antareṇa anumānasya pravṛttiḥ
