asti na tu etad anumānam indriya artha saṃnikarṣa ja tvāt na ca anumeyasya indriyeṇa saṃnikarṣāt anumānam bhavati soyam pratkṣā anumānayoḥ lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ  mahān āśrayitavya iti na ca eka deśa upalabdhi mātram kim tarhi eka deśa upalabdhiḥ tad sahacarita avayavī upalabdhiḥ ca kasmāt  avayavi sadbhāvāt  asti hi ayam eka deśa vyatiriktaḥ  avayavī tasya avayava sthānasya upalabdhi kāraṇa prāptasya eka deśa upalabdhau anupalabdhiḥ anupapanna iti akṛtsna grahaṇāt iticed  na kāraṇataḥ anyasya eka deśasya abhāvāt na ca avayavāḥ kṛtsnā gṛhyante avayavaiḥ eva avayava antara vyavadhānāt  na avayavī kṛtsnaḥ  gṛhyate iti na ayam gṛhyamāṇeṣu avayaveṣu parisamāpta iti sā iyam eka deśa upalabdhiḥ anivṛttā eva iti kṛtsnam iti vai khalu aśeṣa tayām satyām bhavati akṛtsnam iti śeṣe sati tad ca etad  avayaveṣu bahuṣu asti avyavadhāne grahaṇāt  vyavadhāne ca agrahaṇāt iti aṅgam tu bhavān pṛṣṭaḥ  vyācaṣṭām gṛhyamāṇasya āvayavinaḥ kim agṛhītam manyase yena eka deśa upalabdhiḥ syāt iti na hi asya kāraṇebhyaḥ  anye eka deśā bhavanti iti tatra avayava vṛttam na upapadyate iti idam tasya vṛttam yeṣām indriya saṃnikarṣāt  grahaṇam avayavānām taiḥ saha gṛhyateyeṣām avayavānām vyavadhānāt agrahaṇam taiḥ saha na gṛhyate na ca etad kṛta usti bheda iti samudāya upyaśeṣa tā vā samudāyaḥ  vṛkṣaḥ syāt  tad prāptiḥ vā ubhayathā grahaṇa abhāvaḥ mūla skandha śākhā palāśa ādīnām aśeṣa tā vā samudāyaḥ  vṛkṣa iti syāt  prāptiḥ vā samudānayinām iti ubhayathā api samudāya bhūtasya vṛkṣasya grahaṇam na upapadyate iti avayavaiḥ tāvat avayava antarasya vyavadhānāt aśeṣa grahaṇam na upapadyate prāpti grahaṇam api na upapadyate prāptimatām agrahaṇāt  sā iyam eka deśa grahaṇa sahacaritā vṛkṣa buddhiḥ dravya antara utpattau kalpate na samudāya mātre iti avayavi sadbhāvāt  iti ayam ahetuḥ sādhya tvāt  sādhyam tāvat etad  kāraṇebhyaḥ  dravya antaram utpadyate iti anupapāditam etad  evam ca sati vipratipatti mātram bhavati vipratipatteḥ ca avayavini saṃśaya iti yadi avayavī na asti sarvasya grahaṇam na upapadyate kim tad  sarvam dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyāḥ katham kṛtvā paramāṇu samavasthānam tāvat  darśana viṣayaḥ  na bhavati atīndriya tvāt aṇūnām dravya antaram ca avaya vi bhūtam darśana viṣayaḥ  na asti darśana viṣayāḥ ca ime dravya ādayaḥ  gṛhyante te niradhiṣṭhānā na gṛhyeḥ anu gṛhyante tu akumbhoyam śyāma ekaḥ  mahān saṃyuktaḥ spandate asti mṛd mayaḥ ca iti santi ca ime guṇāt ayaḥ  dharmā iti tena sarvasya grahaṇāt  paśyāmaḥ  asti dravya antara bhūtaḥ  avayavi iti avayavi artha antara bhūta  iti saṃgraha kārite vai dhāraṇa ākarṣaṇe saṃgrahaḥ  nāma saṃyoga sahacaritam guṇa antaram sneha dravatva kāritam apām saṃyogāt āme kumbhe agni saṃyogāt  pakve yadi tu avayava kārite abhaviṣyatām pāṃśu rāśi prabhṛtiṣu api ajñāsyetām dravya antara anutpattau ca tṛṇa upala kāṣṭha ādiṣu jatu saṃgṛhīteṣu api na abhaviṣyatām iti atha avayavinam pratyācakṣāṇakaḥ amā bhūt  pratyakṣa lopaḥ iti aṇu sañcayam darśana viṣayam pratijānānaḥ kim anuyoktavyaḥ iti aekam idam dravyam iti ekabuddheḥ viṣayam paryanuyojyaḥ kim eka buddhiḥ abhinna artha viṣayā ahaḥ bhinna artha viṣayā iti abhinna artha viṣaya iti ced  artha antara anujñānāt avayavi siddhiḥ nānā artha viṣaya iti ced  bhinneṣu eka darśana anupapattiḥ anekasmin eka iti vyāhatā buddhiḥ na dṛśyate iti yathā senā aṅgeṣu vana aṅgeṣu ca dūrāt agṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu aekam iti upapadyate buddhiḥ evam aṇuṣu saṃciteṣu agṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktveṣu aekam iti upapadyate buddhiḥ iti yathā gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktvānām senā vana aṅgānām ārāt  kāraṇa antarataḥ pṛthaktvasya agrahaṇam yathā gṛhyamāṇa jātīnām palāśa iti vā khadira iti vā na arāj jāti grahaṇam bhavati yathā gṛhyamāṇa praspandānām nārāt  spanda grahaṇam gṛhyamāṇe ca artha jāte pṛthaktvasya agrahaṇāt  aekam iti bhāktaḥ pratyayaḥ bhavati na tu aṇūnām gṛhyamāṇa pṛthaktvānām kāraṇataḥ pṛthaktvasya agrahaṇāt  bhākta eka pratyayaḥ atīndriya tvāt aṇṛnām iti idam eva parīkṣyate kim eka pratyayaḥ aṇu saṃcaya viṣayaḥ āhaḥ svinna iti aṇu saṃcaya eva senā vana aṅgāni na ca parīkṣyamāṇam udāharaṇam iti yuktam sādhya tvāt iti dṛṣṭam iticed  na tad viṣayasya parīkṣā upapatteḥ yad api manyeta dṛṣṭam idam senā vana aṅgānām pṛthaktu asya agrahaṇāt abhedena aekam iti grahaṇam na ca dṛṣṭam śakyam pratyākhyātum iti tad ca na evam tad viṣayasya parīkṣā upapatteḥ darśana viṣaya eva ayam parīkṣyate yoyam ekam iti pratyayaḥ dṛśyate sa parīkṣyate kim dravya antara viṣayaḥ  vā atha aṇu saṃcaya viṣayaḥ iti atra darśanam anyatarasya sādhakam na bhavati nānābhāve ca aṇūnām pṛthaktu asya agrahaṇāt abhedena aekam iti grahaṇam atasmin  tad iti pratyayaḥ yathā sthāṇau puruṣa iti tatas  kim atasmin  tad iti pratyayasya pradhāna apekṣi tvāt pradhāna siddhiḥ sthāṇau puruṣa iti pratyayasya kim pradhānam yaḥ  asau puruṣe puruṣa pratyayaḥ tasmin sati puruṣa sāmānya grahaṇāt sthāṇau puruṣoyam iti evam nānā bhūteṣu aekam iti sāmānya grahaṇāt pradhāne sati bhavitum arhati pradhānam ca sarvasya agrahaṇāt  na upapadyate iti tasmāt abhinne eva ayam abheda pratyayaḥ aekam iti indriya antara viṣayeṣu abheda pratyayaḥ pradhānam iti ced  na viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt  dṛṣṭānta avyavasthā śrotra ādi viṣayeṣu śabda ādiṣu abhinneṣu eka pratyayaḥ pradhānam anekasmin   eka pratyayasya iti evam ca sati dṛṣṭānta upādānam na vyavatiṣṭhate viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt aṇuṣu saṃciteṣu eka pratyayaḥ kim atasmin  tad iti pratyayaḥ sthāṇau puruṣa pratyayavat  atha arthasya tathā abhāvāt tasmin  tad iti pratyayaḥ yathā śabdasya eka tvāt ekaḥ śabda iti viśeṣa hetu parigraham antareṇa dṛṣṭāntau saṃśayam āpādayata iti kumbhavat  saṃcaya mātram gandhādayā upi iti anudāha raṇam gandhādaya iti evam parimāṇa saṃyoga spanda jāti viśeṣa pratyayān api anuyoktavyaḥ teṣu ca evam prasaṅga iti ekatva buddhiḥ tasmin  tad iti pratyaya iti viśeṣa hetuḥ mahat iti pratyena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt aekam idam mahat ca iti eka viṣayau pratyayau samāna adhikaraṇau bhavataḥ tena vijñāyate yad mahat  tad ekam iti aṇu samūha atiśaya grahaṇam mahat pratyaya iti ced  saḥ  ayam amahatsu aṇuṣu mahat pratyayaḥ atasmin  tad iti pratyayaḥ bhavati iti kim ca atas  atasmin  tad iti pratyayasya pradhāna apekṣi tvāt pradhāna siddhiḥ iti ubhavitavyam mahati eva mahat pratyayena iti aṇuḥ śabdaḥ  mahān iti ca vyavasāyāt  pradhāna siddhiḥ iticed  na mandatīvra tā grahaṇam iyat tān avadhāraṇāt  yathā dravye aaṇuḥ śabdaḥ  alpaḥ  mandaḥ iti etasya grahaṇam amahān śabdaḥ paṭuḥ tīvraḥ iti etasya grahaṇam kasmāt  iyattā an avadhāraṇa atuna hi ayam amahān śabdaḥ iti vyavasyan aiyānayam iti avadhārayati yathā badara āmalaka bilva ādīni asaṃyukte ime iti ca dvitva samāna āśraya prāpti grahaṇam dvau samudāyau  āśrayaḥ saṃyogasya iticed  koyam samudāyaḥ prāptiḥ anekasya anekā vā prāptiḥ ekasya samudāya iti ced  prāpteḥ agrahaṇam prāpti āśritāyāḥ  asaṃyukte ime vastunī iti na atra dve prāptī saṃyukte gṛhyete aneka samūhaḥ sudāya iti ced  na dvi tvena sāmānādhikaraṇyasya grahaṇāt  advau  imau saṃyuktau  artha oma iti grahaṇe sati na aneka samūha āśrayaḥ saṃyogaḥ  gṛhyate na ca dvayoḥ aṇvoḥ grahaṇam asti tasmāt mahatī dvitva āśraya bhūte dravye saṃyogasya sthānam iti pratyāsattiḥ pratīghāta avasānā saṃyogaḥ  na artha antaram iticed  na artha antara hetu tvāt saṃyoga asya śabda rūpa ādi spandānām hetuḥ saṃyogaḥ na ca dravyayoḥ guṇa antara upajananam antareṇa śabde rūpa ādiṣu spande ca kāraṇa tvam gṛhyate tasmāt  guṇa antaram pratyaya viṣayaḥ ca artha antaram tad pratiṣedhaḥ  vā akuṇḍalī guruḥ akuṇḍalaḥ chātraḥ iti saṃyoga buddheḥ ca yadi artha antaraṃpa na viṣayaḥ artha antara pratiṣedhaḥ tarhi viṣayaḥ tatra pratiṣidhyamāna vacanam asaṃyukte dravye iti yad artha antaram anyatra dṛṣṭam iha pratiṣidhyate tad  vaktavyam iti dvayoḥ mahatoḥ āśritasya grahaṇāt  na aṇvāśraya iti jāti viśeṣasya pratyaya anuvṛtti liṅgasya apratyākhyānam pratyākhyāne vā pratyaya vyavasthā anupapattiḥ vyadhikaraṇasya anabhivyakteḥ adhikaraṇa vacanam aṇu samavasthānam viṣaya iti ced  prāpta aprāpta sāmarthya vacanam kim aprāpte aṇu samavasthāne tad āśrayaḥ  jāti viśeṣaḥ  gṛhyate atha prāpte iti aprāpte grahaṇam iticed  vyavahitasya aṇu samavasthānasya api upalabdhi prasaṅga ḥu vyavahite aṇu samavasthāne tad āśrayaḥ  jāti viśeṣaḥ  gṛhyeta prāpte grahaṇam iticed  madhya para bhāgayoḥ aprāptau anabhivyaktiḥ yāvat  prāptam bhavati tāvatī abhivyaktiḥ iti ced tāvataḥ  adhikaraṇa tvam aṇu samavasthānasya auyāvati prāpte jāti viśeṣaḥ  gṛhyate tāvat asya adhikaraṇam iti prāptam bhavati tatra eka samudāye pratīyamāne artha bhede evam ca sati yaḥ  aṇu samudāyaḥ  vṛkṣa iti pratīyate tatra vṛkṣa bahu tvam pratīyeta auyatra yatra hi aṇu samudāyasya bhāge vṛkṣa tvam gṛhyate sa sa vṛkṣa iti tasmāt  samudita aṇu samavasthānasya artha antarasya jāti viśeṣa abhivyakti viṣaya tvāt  avayavi artha antara bhūta  iti parīkṣitam pratyakṣam anumānam idānīm parīkṣate apramāṇam iti ekadā api arthasya na pratipādakam iti rodhāt api nadī pūrṇā gṛhyate tadā ca aupariṣṭhāt  vṛṣṭaḥ  devaḥ iti mithyā anumānam nīḍa upaghātāt api pipīlikā aṇḍa saṃcāra u bhavati tadā ca abhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti mithyā anumānam iti puruṣopi mayūra vāśitam anukaroti tadā api śabda sādṛśyāt  mithyā anumānam bhavati na ayam anumāna vyabhicāraḥ ananumāne tu khalu ayam anumāna abhimānaḥ katham na aviśiṣṭaḥ  liṅgam bhavitum arhati pūrva udaka viśiṣṭam khalu varṣa udakam śīghratara tvam srotasaḥ bahutara phena phala parṇa kāṣṭha ādi vahanam ca upalabhamānaḥ pūrṇa tvena nadyāḥ aupari vṛṣṭaḥ  devaḥ iti anuminoti na udaka vṛddhi mātreṇa pipīlikā prāyasya aṇḍa saṃcāre abhaviṣyati vṛṣṭiḥ iti anumīyate na kāsām cit iti anedam mayūra vāśitam tad sadṛśa uyam śabdaḥ iti viśeṣa aparijñānāt  mithyā anumānam iti yaḥ tu viśiṣṭāt śabdāt  viśiṣṭa mayūra vāśitam gṛhṇati tasya viśiṣṭaḥ  arthaḥ  gṛhyamāṇaḥ  liṅgam yathā sarpa ādīnām iti soyam anumā ātura parādhaḥ  na anumānasya yaḥ  artha viśeṣeṇa anumeyam artham aviśiṣṭa artha darśanena bubhutsate iti tri kāla viṣayam anumānam traikālya grahaṇāt iti uktam atra ca vṛntāt  pracyutasya phalasya bhūmau pratyāsīdataḥ  yad  ūrdhvam sa patitaḥ  adhvā tad saṃyuktaḥ patita kālaḥ yaḥ  adhasyāt  sa patitavyaḥ  adhvā tad saṃyuktaḥ kālaḥ patitavya kālaḥ na idānīm tṛtīyaḥ  adhvā vidyate yatra patati iti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ  gṛhyeta tasmāt  vartamānaḥ kālaḥ  na vidyate iti na adhva vyaṅgyaḥ kālaḥ kim tarhi kriyā vyaṅgyaḥ patati iti yadā patana kriyā vyuparatā bhavati sa kālaḥ patita kālaḥ yadā utpatsyate sa patitavya kālaḥ yadā dravye vartamānā kriyā gṛhyate sa vartamānaḥ kālaḥ yadi ca ayam dravye vartamānam patanam na gṛhṇāti kasya uparamam utpatsyamāna tām vā prativadyate patitaḥ kāla iti bhūtā kriyā patitavyaḥ kāla iti ca utpatsyamānā kriyā ubhayoḥ kālayoḥ kriyā hīnam dravyam adhas  pratati iti kriyā saṃbaddham soyam kriyā dravyayoḥ saṃbandham gṛhṇāti vartamānaḥ kālaḥ tad āśrayau ca itarau kālau tad abhāve na syātām iti yadi  atīta anāgatau itaretara apekṣau sidhyetām pratipadyemahi vartamāna vilopam na atīta apekṣā anāgata siddhiḥ na api anāgata apekṣā atīta siddhiḥ kayā yuktyā kena kalpena atītaḥ katham atīta apekṣā anāgata siddhiḥ kena ca kalpena anāgataḥ iti na etad śakyam nirvaktum avyākaraṇīyam etad  vartamāna lope iti yad ca manyeta hrasva dīrghayoḥ sthala nimnayoḥ chāyā tapayoḥ ca yathā itara itara apekṣayā siddhiḥ evam atīta anāgatayoḥ iti tad na upapadyate viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt dṛṣṭāntavat pratidṛṣṭānta upi prasajyate yathā rūpa sparśaum gandharasau na itaretara apekṣau sidhyataḥ evam atīta anāgatau  iti na itara itara apekṣā kasya cit  siddhiḥ iti yasmāt eka abhāve anyatara abhāvāt ubhaya abhāvaḥ yadi ekasya anyatara apekṣā siddhiḥ anyatarasya idānīm kim apekṣā yadi anyatarasya eka apekṣā siddhiḥ ekasya idānīm kim apekṣā evam ekasya abhāve anyatarat na sidhyati iti ubhaya abhāvaḥ prasajyate artha sadbhāva vyaṅgyaḥ ca ayam vartamānaḥ kālaḥ avidyate dravyam avidyate guṇaḥ avidyate karma iti yasnaya ca ayam na asti tasya pratyakṣam indriya artha saṃnikarṣa jam na ca avidyamānam asad indriyeṇa saṃnikṛṣyate na ca ayam vidyamānam sat  kiñcid anujānāti iti pratyakṣa nimittam pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ pratyakṣa jñānam sarvam na upapadyate pratyakṣa anupapattau tad pūrvaka tvāt  anumāna āgamayoḥ anupapattiḥ sarva pramāṇa vilope sarva grahaṇam na bhavati iti ubhayathā ca vartamānaḥ kālaḥ  gṛhyate kvacid artha sadbhāva vyaṅgyaḥ  yathā aasti dravyam iti kvacid  kriyā saṃtāna vyaṅgyaḥ  yathā apacati chinatti iti nānāvidhā ca eka arthā kriyā kriyā saṃtānaḥ kriyā abhyāsaḥ ca nānāvidhā ca eka arthā kriyā apacati iti sthālī adhiśrayaṇam udaka āsecanam taṇḍulā vapana medha upasarpaṇam agni abhijvālanam darvī ghaṭṭanam maṇḍa srāvaṇam adhovatāraṇam iti chinatti iti kriyā abhyāsaḥ udyabhya udyamya paraśum dāruṇi nipātayan chinatti iti ucyate yad ca idam pacyamānam chidyamānam ca tad  kriyamāṇam tasmin kriyamāṇe kriyā saṃtānaḥ  anārabdhaḥ cikīrpitaḥ  anāgataḥ kālaḥ apakṣyati iti prayojana avasānaḥ kriyā saṃtāna uparamaḥ  atītaḥ kālaḥ aapākṣīt iti ārabdha kriyā saṃtānaḥ  vartamānaḥ kālaḥ apacati iti tatra yā uparatā sā kṛta tā yā cikīrṣitā sā kartavyatā yā vidyamānā sā kriyamāṇa tā tad evam kriyā saṃtāna sthaḥ traikālya samāhāraḥ apacati pacyate iti vartamāna grahaṇena gṛhyate kriyā saṃtānasya hi atra avicchedaḥ  vidhīyate na ārambhaḥ  na uparam iti soyam ubhayathā vartamānām gṛhyate apavṛktaḥ  vyapavṛktaḥ ca atīta anāgatābhyām sthiti vyaṅgyaḥ avidyate dravyam iti kriyā saṃtāna āviccheda abhidhāyī ca traikālya anvitaḥ apacati chinatti iti anyaḥ ca pratyāsatti prabhṛteḥ rathasya vivakṣāyām tad abhidhāyī bahu prakāraḥ  lokeṣu utprekṣitavyaḥ tasmāt asti vartamānaḥ kāla iti atha upamāna parīkṣā atyanta sādharmyādu pāmanam na sidhyati na ca evam bhavati ayathā gauḥ evam gauḥ iti prāyas sādharmyāt upamānam na sidhyati na hi bhavati ayathā anaḍvān evam mahiṣaḥ iti eka deśa sādharmyāt upamānam na sidhyati na hi sarveṇa sarvam upamīyate iti na sādharmyasya kṛtsna prāya alpa bhāvam āśritya upamānam pravartate kim tarhi prasiddha sādharmyāt  sādhya sādhana bhāvam āśritya pravartate yatra ca etad asti na tatra upamānam pratiṣeddhum śakyam tasmāt  yathā ukta doṣaḥ  na upapadyate iti astu tarhi upamānam anumānam yathā dhūmena pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya vahneḥ grahaṇam anumānam evam gavā pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya gavayasya grahaṇam iti na idam anumānāt  viśiṣyate viśiṣyate iti āha kayā yuktyā yadā hi ayam upayukta upamānaḥ  godarśī gavā samānam artham paśyati tadā ayam gavaya iti asya saṃjñā śabdasya vyavasthām pratipadyate na ca evam anumānam iti para artham ca upamānam yasya hi upameyam aprasiddham tad artham prasiddha upameyena kriyate iti para artham upamānam iticet na svaya madhyavasāyāt  bhavati ca bhoḥ svaya madhyavasāyaḥ yathā gauḥ evam gavaya iti na adhyavasāyaḥ pratiṣidhyate upamānam tu tad na bhavati prasiddha sādharmyāt  sādhya sādhanam upamānam na ca yasya upameyam prasiddham tam prati sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ  vidyate iti atha api tathā iti samāna dharma upasaṃhārāt upamānam sidhyati na anumānam ayam ca anayoḥ viśeṣa iti atha śabda pramāṇa parīkṣā śabdaḥ  anumānam na pramāṇa antaram kasmāt  śabda arthasya anumeya tvāt katham anumeya tvam pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdheḥ yathā anupalabhyamānaḥ  liṅgī mitena liṅgena paścāt  mīyate iti anumānam evam mitena śabdena paścāt  mīyate arthaḥ  anupalabhyamāna iti anumānam śabdaḥ itas ca anumānam śabdaḥ pramāṇa antara bhāve dvi pravṛttiḥ upalabdhiḥ anyathā hi upalabdhiḥ anumāne anyathā upamāne tad  vyākhyātam śabda anumānayoḥ tu upalabdhiḥ at vipravṛttiḥ yathā anumāne pravartate tathā śabdepi viśeṣa abhāvāt anumānam śabda iti śabda unumānam iti vartate saṃbaddhayoḥ ca śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandha prasiddhau śabda upalabdheḥ artha grahaṇam yathā saṃbaddhayoḥ liṅga liṅginoḥ saṃbandha pratītau liṅga upalabdhau liṅgi grahaṇam iti yad tāvat aarthasya anumeya tvāt iti tad na asvargaḥ apsarasaḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ sapta dvīpāḥ samudraḥ  loka saṃniveśaḥ iti evamādeḥ apratyakṣasya arthasya na śabda mātrāt  pratyayaḥ kim tarhi aāptaiḥ aya muktaḥ śabdaḥ iti atas  saṃpratyayaḥ viparyayeṇa saṃpratyaya abhāvāt na tu evam anumānam iti yad  punar  upalabdheḥ advi pravṛtti tvāt iti ayam eva śabda anumānayoḥ upalabdheḥ pravṛtti bhedaḥ tatra viśeṣe satya hetuḥ aviśeṣa abhāvāt iti yad  punar idam saṃbandhāt ca iti asti ca śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ  anujñātaḥ asti ca pratiṣiddhaḥu aasya idam iti ṣaṣṭhī viśiṣṭasya vākyasya artha viśeṣaḥ  anujñātaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇaḥ tu śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ kasmāt  pramāṇatā unupalabdheḥu pratyakṣataḥ tāvat  śabda artha prāpteḥ na upalabdhiḥ atīndriya tvātuyena indriyeṇa gṛhyate śabdaḥ tasya viṣaya bhāvam ativṛttaḥ  arthaḥ  na gṛhyate asti ca ati indriya viṣaya bhūta upyarthaḥ samānena ca indriyeṇa gṛhyamāṇayoḥ prāptiḥ gṛhyate iti prāpti lakṣaṇe ca gṛhyamāṇe saṃbandhe śabda arthayoḥ śabda antike vā arthaḥ syāt  artha antike vā śabdaḥ syāt  ubhayam vā ubhayatra atha khalu ayam sthāna karaṇa abhāvāt iti ca arthaḥ na ca ayam anumāna topyupalabhyate śabda antike artha  iti etasmin pakṣe api  āsya sthāna karaṇa uccāraṇīyaḥ śabdaḥ tad antike artha  iti anna agni asi śabda uccāraṇe pūraṇa pradāha pāṭanāni gṛhyeran na ca gṛhyante agrahaṇāt na anumeyaḥ prāpti lakṣaṇḥ saṃbandhaḥ artha antike śabdam iti sthāna karaṇa asaṃbhavāt  anuccāraṇam sthānam kaṇṭha ādayaḥ karaṇam prayatna viśeṣaḥ tasya artha antike anupapattiḥ iti ubhaya pratiṣedhāt ca na ubhayam tasmāt na śabdena arthaḥ prāpta iti śabda artha pratyayasya vyavasthā darśanāt  anumīyate asti śabda artha saṃbandhaḥ  vyavasthā kāraṇam asaṃbandhe hi śabda mātrāt artha mātre pratyaya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt apratiṣedhaḥ saṃbandhasya iti atra samādhiḥ na saṃbandha kāritam śabda artha vyavasthānam kim tarhi samaya kāritam yad tad avocāma aasya idam iti ṣaṣṭhī viśiṣṭasya vākyasya artha viśeṣaḥ  anujñātaḥ śabda arthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ iti samayam tam avocāma iti kaḥ punar ayam samayaḥ aasya śabdasya idam artha jātam abhidheyam iti abhidhāna abhidhaiya niyama niyogaḥ tasmin  upayukte śabdāt artha saṃpratyayaḥ  bhavati viparyaye hi śabda śravaṇepi pratyaya abhāvaḥ saṃbandha vādinā api ca ayam avarjanīya iti prayujyamāna grahaṇāt ca laukikānām samaya pālana artham ca idam pada lakṣaṇāyāḥ  vācaḥ  anvākhyānam vyākaraṇam vyākya lakṣaṇāyāḥ  vācaḥ  artha lakṣaṇam pada samūhaḥ  vākyam artha parisamāptau  iti tad evam prāpti lakṣaṇasya śabda artha saṃbandhasya artha juṣaḥ  api  anumāna hetuḥ  na bhavati iti sāmayikaḥ śabda artha saṃpratyayaḥ  na svābhāvikaḥ ṛṣyāri amla icchānām yathākāmam śabda prayogaḥ  artha pratyāyanāya pravartate svābhāvike hi śabdasya artha pratyāyaka tve yathākāmam na syāt  yathā taijasasya prakāśasya rūpa pratyaya hetu tvam na jāti viśeṣam vyabhicarati iti putra kāma iṣṭi havana abhyāsepu tasya iti śabda viśeṣam eva adhikurute bhagavān ṛṣiḥ śabdasya pramāṇa tvam na saṃbhavati kasmāt  anṛta doṣāt  putra kāma iṣṭau putra kāmaḥ putra iṣṭyā yajeta iti na iṣṭau saṃsthitāyām putra janma dṛśyate dṛṣṭa arthasya vākyasya anṛta tvāt  adṛṣṭa artham api vākyam agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāmaḥ ityādi anṛtam iti jñāyate vihita vyāghāta doṣāt ca havane udite hotavyam anudite hotavyam samaya adhyuṣite hotavyam iti vidhāya vihitam vyāhanti śyāvaḥ  asya āhutim abhyavaharati ya udite juhoti śabalaḥ  asya āhutim abhyavaharati yaḥ  anudite juhoti śyāva śavalau vā asya āhutim abhyavaharataḥ  yaḥ samaya adhyuṣite juhoti iti vyāghātāt ca anyatara d mithyā iti punarukta doṣāt ca abhyāse deśyamāne tris  prathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti punarukta doṣaḥ  bhavati punarukta ca pramatta vākyam iti tasmāt apramāṇam śabdaḥ anṛta vyāghāta punarukta doṣebhya iti na anṛta doṣaḥ putra kāma iṣṭau kasmāt  karma kartṛ sādhana vaiguṇyāt  iṣṭyā pitarau saṃyujyamānau putram janayata iti iṣṭiḥ karaṇam sādhanam pitarau kartārau saṃyogaḥ karma trayāṇām guṇa yogāt  putra janma vaiguṇyāt  viparyayaḥ iṣṭi āśrayam tāvat  karma vaiguṇyam samīha abhreṣaḥ kartṛ vaiguṇyam avidvān prayoktā kapūya ācaraṇaḥ ca sādhana vaiguṇyam haviḥ asaṃskṛtam upahatam iti mantrā nyūna adhikāḥ svara varṇa hīnā iti dakṣiṇā durāgatā hīnā ninditā ca iti atha upajana āśrayam karma vaiguṇyam mithyā saṃprayogaḥ kartṛ vaiguṇyam yoni vyāpādaḥ  bīja upaghātaḥ ca iti sādhana vaiguṇyam iṣṭau  abhihitam loke ca aagni kāmaḥ  dāruṇī mathnīyāt iti vidhi vākyam tatra karma vaiguṇyam mithyā abhimanthānam kartṛ vaiguṇyam prajñā prayatna gataḥ pramādaḥ sādhana vaiguṇyam ārdram suṣiram dāru iti tatra phalam na niṣpadyate iti na anṛta doṣaḥ guṇa yogena phala niṣpatti darśanāt  na ca idam laukikāt  bhidyate putra kāmaḥ putra iṣṭyā yajeta iti ana vyāghātaḥ  havane iti anuvartate yaḥ  abhyupagatam havana kālam bhinatti tatas  anyatra juhoti tatra ayam abhyupagata kāla bhedaḥ  doṣa ucyate śyāvaḥ  asya āhutim abhyavaharati ca udite juhoti tad idam vidhi bhreṣe nindā vacanam iti apunarukta doṣaḥ  abhyāsena iti prakṛtam anartha kaḥ abhyāsaḥ punaruktaḥ arthavān abhyāsaḥ  anuvādaḥ yaḥ  ayam abhyāsaḥ tris  prathamām anvāha tris uttamām iti anuvāda upapadyate arthavat tvāt  tris vacanena hi prathama uttamayoḥ pañcadaśa tvam sāmadhenīnām bhavati tathā ca mantra abhivādaḥ idam aham bhrātṛvyam pañcadaśa āreṇa vāc vajreṇa bādhe yaḥ  asmān dveṣṭi yam ca vayam dviṣmaḥ iti pañcadaśa sāmidhenī vajram mantraḥ  abhivadati tad abhyāsam antareṇa na syāt iti pramāṇam śabdaḥ  yathā loke vibhāgaḥ ca brāhmaṇa vākyānām trividhaḥ tridhā khalu brāhmaṇa vākyāni viniyuktāni vidhivacanāni arthavāda vacanāni anuvāda vacanāni iti tatra yad  vākyam vidhāyakam ca udakam sa vidhiḥ vidhiḥ tu niyogaḥ  anujñā vā yathā agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāmaḥ ityādi vidheḥ phala vāda lakṣaṇā yā praśaṃsā sā stutiḥ saṃpratyaya arthā stūyamānam śraddadhīta iti pravartikā ca phala śravaṇāt  pravartate sarva jitaḥ  vai devāḥ sarvam ajayan sarvasya āptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam eva tena āpnoti sarvam jayati iti evamādi aniṣṭa phala vādaḥ  nindā varjana arthā ninditam na samācaret iti sa eṣa vā va prathamaḥ  yajñaḥ  yajñānām yad jyotiṣṭomaḥ  ya etena aniṣṭvā anyena yajate garte patati ayam eva etad  jīryate vā pramīyate vā iti evamādi anya kartṛkasya vyāhatasya vidheḥ vādaḥ parakṛtiḥ hutvā vapām eva agre abhidhārayanti atha pṛṣadājyam tad uha caraka adhvaryavaḥ pṛṣadājyam eva agre abhidhārayanti aagneḥ prāṇāḥ pṛṣadājyam stomam iti evam abhidadhati iti evamādi aitihya samācaritaḥ  vidhiḥ purā kalpa iti tasmāt vā etena brāhmaṇā bahiṣpavamānam sāma stoma maḥ tauṣan yone yajñam pratanavāmahe iti evamādi katham para kṛti purā kalpau arthavādau  iti stuti nindā vākyena abhisaṃbandhāt  vidhi āśrayasya kasyacid arthasya dyotanāt artha vāda iti vidhi anuvacanam ca anuvādaḥ  vihita anuvacanam ca pūrvaḥ śabda anuvādaḥ  aparaḥ  artha anuvādaḥ yathā punaruktam dvividham evam anuvāda upi kimartham punar vihitam anūdyate adhikāra artham vihitam adhikṛtya stutiḥ bodhyate nindā vā vidhi śeṣaḥ  vā abhidhiyate vihita anantara arthaḥ  api ca anuvādaḥ  bhavati evam anyat api utprekṣaṇīyam lokepi ca vidhiḥ artha vādaḥ  anuvāda iti ca trividham vākyam aodanam pacet iti vidhi vākyam arthavāda vākyam aāyuḥ varcaḥ  balam sukham pratibhānam ca anne pratiṣṭhitam anuvādaḥ apacatu pacatu bhavān iti abhyāsaḥ akṣi pram pacyatām iti vā aaṅga pacyatām iti vā adhyeṣaṇa artham apacyatām eva iti ca avadhāraṇa artham yathā laukike vākye vibhāgena artha grahaṇāt pramāṇa tvam evam veda vākyānām api vibhāgena artha grahaṇāt pramāṇa tvam bhavitum arhati iti apunaruktam asādhu sādhuḥ anuvādaḥ iti ayam viśeṣaḥ  na upapadyate kasmāt  ubhayatra hi pratīta arthaḥ śabdaḥ  abhyastate caritārthasya śabdasya abhyāsāt ubhayam asādhu iti na anuvāda punar uktayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ kasmāt  arthavataḥ  abhyāsasya anuvāda bhāvāt  samāne abhyāse punaruktam anarthakam arthavān abhyāsaḥ  anuvādaḥ śīghratara gamana upadeśavat aśīghram śīghram gamyatām iti kriyā atiśayaḥ  abhyāsena eva ucyate udāharaṇa artham ca idam evam anya upi abhyāsaḥ apacati pacati iti kriyā anuparamaḥ agrāmaḥ  grāmaḥ  ramaṇīyaḥ iti vyāptiḥ apari pari trigartebhyaḥ  vṛṣṭaḥ  devaḥ iti parivarjanam aadhya dhimaṇḍam niṣaṇṇam iti sāmīpyam atiktam tiktam iti prakāraḥ evam anuvādasya stuti nindā śeṣa vidhiṣu adhikāra artha tā vihita anantara artha tā ca iti kim punar  pratiṣedha hetu uddhārāt eva śabdasya pramāṇa tvam sidhyati na atas ca kim punar āyurvedasya prāmāṇyam yad tad āyurvedena upadiśyate aidam kṛtvā iṣṭam adhigacchati idam varjayitvā aniṣṭam jahāti iti tasya anuṣṭhīyamānasya tathā abhāvaḥ satya artha tā aviparyayaḥ mantra padānām ca viṣa bhūta aśani pratiṣedha arthānām prayoge arthasya tathā abhāvaḥ etad  prāmānaṇyam kiṅkṛtam etad  āpta prāmāṇya kṛtam kiṃpunar āptānām prāmāṇyam sākṣātkṛta dharmatā bhūta dayā yathābhūta artha cikhyā payiṣā iti āptāḥ khalu sākṣātkṛta dharmāṇaḥ aidam hātavyam idam asya hāni hetuḥ idam asya adhigatavyam idam asya adhigama hetuḥ iti bhūtāni anukampante teṣām khalu vai prāṇabhṛtām svayam anavabuddhyamānānām na anyat upadeśāt  avabodha kāraṇam asti na ca anavabodhe samīhā varjanam vā na ca akṛtvā svastibhāvaḥ na api  asya anya upakāra kopī asti hanta vayamebhyaḥ  yathādarśanam yathābhūtam upadiśāmaḥ te ime śrutvā pratipadyamānā heyam hāsyanti adhigantavyam eva adhigamiṣyanti iti evam āpta upadeśaḥ etena trividhena āpta prāmāṇyena parigṛhitaḥ  anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ  arthasya sādhakaḥ  bhavati evam āpta upadeśaḥ pramāṇam evam āptāḥ pramāṇam dṛṣṭa arthena āpta upadeśena āyurvedena adṛṣṭa arthaḥ  veda bhāgaḥ  anumātavyaḥ pramāṇam iti āpta prāmāṇyasya hetoḥ samāna tvāt iti asya api ca eka deśaḥ grāma kāmaḥ  yajeta iti evamādiḥ dṛṣṭa arthaḥ tena anumātavyam iti loke ca bhūyānupadeśa āśrayaḥ  vyavahāraḥ laukikasya api upadeṣṭuḥ upadeṣṭa vyāthejñānena para anujighṛkṣayā yathābhūta artha cikhyā apayiṣayā ca prāmāṇyam tad parigrahāt āpta upadeśaḥ pramāṇam iti draṣṭṛ pravaktṛ sāmānyāt ca anumānam ye eva āptā veda arthānām draṣṭāraḥ pravaktāraḥ cate eva āyurveda prabhṛtīnām iti āyurveda prāmāṇyavat  veda prāmāṇyam anumātavyam iti nitya tvāt veda vākyānām pramāṇa tve tad prāmāṇyam āpta prāmāṇyāt  iti ayuktam śabdasya vācaka tvāt artha pratipattau pramāṇa tvam nitya tve hi sarvasya sarveṇa vacanāt  śabda artha vyavasthā anupapattiḥ na anitya tve vācaka tvam iticed  na laukikeṣu artha darśanāt  tepi nityā iti ced  na anāpta upadeśāt artha visaṃvādaḥ  anupapannaḥ nitya tvāt hi śabdaḥ pramāṇam iti anityaḥ sa iti ced  aviśeṣa vacanam anāpta upadeśaḥ  laikikaḥ  na nitya iti kāraṇam vācyam iti yathā niyogam ca arthasya pratyāyanāt  nāmadheya śabdānām loke prāmāṇyam nitya tvāt  prāmāṇya anupapattiḥ yatra arthe nāmadheya śabdaḥ  niyujyate loke tasya niyoga sāmarthyāt  pratyāyakaḥ  bhavati na nitya tvāt  manvantara yuga antareṣu ca atīta anāgateṣu saṃpradāya abhyāsa prayoga aviccheda iti vedānām nitya tvam āpta prāmāṇyāt ca prāmāṇyam laukikeṣu śabdeṣu ca etad  samānam iti iti vātsyāyanīye nyāya bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam #################################################################### atha nyāya bhāṣya dvitīya adhyāyasya dvitīya mānhikam ayathārthaḥ pramāṇa uddeśa iti matvā āha na catvāri eva pramāṇāni kim tarhi aitihyam arthāpattiḥ saṃbhavaḥ  abhāva iti etāni api pramāṇāni tāni kasmāt na uktāni aiti ha ūcuḥ iti  anirdiṣṭa pravaktṛkam pravāda pāramparyam aitihyam arthādā pattiḥ arthāpattiḥ āpattiḥ prāptiḥ prasaṅgaḥ yatra abhidhīyamāne arthe yaḥ  anyaḥ  arthaḥ prasajyate saḥ  arthāpattiḥ yathā amegheṣu  asatsu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti kim atra prasajyate atatsu bhavati iti saṃbhavaḥ  nāma avinābhāvinaḥ  arthasya sattā grahaṇāt anyasya satta grahaṇam yathā droṇasya sattā grahaṇā dāḍhakasya sattā grahaṇam āḍhakasya grahaṇāt  prasthasya iti abhāvaḥ virodhī abhūtam bhūtasya avidyamānam varṣa karma vidyamānasya vāyu abhra saṃyogasya pratipādakam vidhārake hi vāyu abhra saṃyoge guru tvāt apām patana karma na bhavati iti satyam etāni pramāṇāni na tu pramāṇa antarāṇi pramāṇa antaram ca manyamānena pratiṣedha ucyate saḥ  ayam anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ katham aāpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti na ca śabda lakṣaṇam aitihyāt  vyāvartate soyam bhedaḥ sāmānyāt  saṃgṛhyate iti pratyakṣeṇa apratyakṣasya saṃbaddhasya prapittiḥ anumānam tathā ca arthāpatti saṃbhava abhāvāḥ vākya artha saṃpratyayena anabhihitasya arthasya pratyakanīka bhāvāt  grahaṇam arthāpattiḥ anumānam eva avinā abhāva vṛttyā ca saṃbaddhayoḥ samudāya samudāyinoḥ samudāyena itarasya grahaṇam saṃbhavaḥ tad api anumānam eva aasmin sati idam na upapadyate iti virodhi tve prasiddhe kārya anutpattyā kāraṇasya pratibandhakam anumīyate soyam yathārtha eva pramāṇa uddeśa iti asatyam etāni pramāṇāni na tu pramāṇa antarāṇi iti uktam atra arthāpatteḥ pramāṇa bhāva abhyanujñā na upapadyate tathā hi iyam asatsu megheṣu vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati iti satsu bhavati iti etadā arthāt āpadyate satsu api ca ekadā na bhavati sā iyam arthāpattiḥ apramāṇam iti na anaikāntika tvam arthāpatteḥ aasati kāraṇe kāryam na utpadyate iti vākyāt  pratyanīka bhūtaḥ  arthaḥ asati kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate iti arthāt āpadyate abhāvasya hi bhāvaḥ pratyanīka iti soyam kārya utpādaḥ sati kāraṇe arthāt āpadyamānaḥ  na kāraṇasya sattām vyabhicarati na khalu  asati kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate tasmāt  na anā ekāntikī yad tu asati kāraṇe nimitta pratibandhāt  kāryam na utpadyate iti kāraṇa dharmaḥ  asau na tu arthāpatteḥ prameyam kim tarhi asyāḥ prameyam sati kāraṇe kāryam upadyate iti yaḥ  asau kārya utpādaḥ kāraṇa sattām na vyabhicarati tad asyāḥ prameyam evam tu sati anartha āpattau arthāpatti abhimānam kṛtvā pratiṣedha ucyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca kāraṇa dharmaḥ  na śakyaḥ pratyākhyātum iti aarthāpattiḥ  na pramāṇam anaikāntika tvāt iti vākyam pratiṣedhaḥ tena anena arthāpatteḥ pramāṇa tvam pratiṣidhyate na sadbhāvaḥ evam anaikāntikaḥ  bhavati anaikāntika tvāt apramāṇena anena na kaścid arthaḥ pratiṣidhyate iti artha manyase niyata viṣayeṣu artheṣu sva viṣaye vyabhicāraḥ  bhavati na ca pratiṣedhasya sadbhāvaḥ  viṣayaḥ evam tarhi atha aṅpatteḥ api kārya utpādane kāraṇa sattāyā avyabhicāraḥ  viṣayaḥ na ca kāraṇa dharmaḥ  nimitta pratibandhāt  kāyāṅnutpādaka tvam iti abhāvasya tarhi pramāṇa bhāva abhyanujñā na upapadyate katham iti abhāvasya bhūyasi prameye loka siddhe vaiyātyāt ucyate na abhāva prāmāṇyam prameya asiddheḥ iti atha ayam artha bahu tvāt artha eka deśa udāhriyate tasya abhāvasya sidhyati prameyam katham lakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu anupādeyeṣu upādeyānām alakṣitānām alakṣaṇa lakṣita tvāt  lakṣaṇa abhāvena lakṣita tvāt iti ubhaya saṃnidhau alakṣitāni vāsāṃsi ānaya iti prayuktaḥ  yeṣu vāsaḥ satu lakṣaṇāni na bhavanti tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena pratipadyate pratipadya ca ānayati pratipatti hetuḥ ca pramāṇam iti yatra bhūtvā kiñcid na bhavati tatra tasya abhāva upapadyate na ca ālakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇāni bhūtvā na bhavanti tasmāt teṣu lakṣaṇa abhāvaḥ  anupapanna iti na anya lakṣaṇa upapatteḥ yathā ayam anyeṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣaṇānām upapattim paśyati na evam alakṣiteṣu soyam lakṣaṇa abhāvam paśyan abhāvena artham pratipadyate iti teṣu vāsaḥsu lakṣiteṣu siddhiḥ vidyamāna tā yeṣām bhavati na teṣām abhāvaḥ  lakṣaṇānām yāni ca lakṣiteṣu vidyante lakṣaṇāni teṣām alakṣiteṣu abhāva iti  ahetuḥ yāni khalu bhavanti teṣām abhāvaḥ  vyāhata iti na brūmaḥ  yāni lakṣaṇāni bhavanti teṣām abhāva iti kim tu keṣu cit lakṣaṇāni avasthitāni anavasthitāni keṣucid  apekṣamāṇaḥ  yeṣu lakṣaṇānām bhāvam na paśyati tāni lakṣaṇa abhāvena prapidyate iti abhāva dvaitam khalu bhavati prāk  ca utpatteḥ avidyamāna tā utpannasya ca ātmanaḥ  hānādavidyamāna tā tatra ālakṣiteṣu vāsaḥsu prāk utpatteḥ avidyamāna tā lakṣaṇaḥ  lakṣaṇānām abhāvaḥ  na itara iti āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti pramāṇa bhāve viśeṣaṇam bruvatā anānā prakāraḥ śabdaḥ iti jñāpyate tasmin sāmānyena vicāraḥ kim nityaḥ  atha anityaḥ iti vimarśa hetu anuyoge ca vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ aākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ  vibhuḥ nityaḥ  abhivyakti dharmakaḥ iti eke gandha ādi saha vṛttiḥ dravyeṣu saṃniviṣṭaḥ  gandha ādivat avasthitaḥ  abhivyakti dharmakaḥ iti apare aākāśa guṇaḥ śabda utpatti nirodha dharma kaḥ buddhivat iti apare amahābhūta saṃkṣobha jaḥ śabdaḥ  anāśrita utpatti dharmakaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ iti anye atas  saṃśayaḥ kim atra tattvam iti aanityaḥ śabdaḥ iti uttaram katham ādi ḥuyoniḥukāraṇam ādīyate asmāt iti kāraṇavat  anityam dṛṣṭam saṃyoga vibhāga jaḥ ca śabdaḥ kāraṇavat tvāt anitya iti kā punar iyam artha deśānā akāraṇavat tvāt iti utpatti dharma kattvāt anityaḥ śabda iti bhūtvā na bhavati vināśa dharmaka iti sāṃśayikam etad  kim utpatti kāraṇam saṃyoga vibhāgau śabdasya āhosvit abhivyakti kāraṇam iti ata āha aindriyaka tvāt  iti indriya pratyāsatti grāhya aindriyakaḥ kim ayam vyañjakena samāna deśaḥ  abhivyajyate rūpa ādivat  atha saṃyoga jāt śabdāt śabda saṃtāne sati śrotra pratyāsannaḥ  gṛhyate iti saṃyoga nivṛttau śabda grahaṇāt na vyañjakena samāna deśasya grahaṇam dāru vraścane dāruparaśu saṃyoga nivṛttau dūra sthena śabdaḥ  gṛhyate na ca vyañjaka abhāve vyaṅgya grahaṇam bhavati tasmāt na vyañjakaḥ saṃyogaḥ utpādake tu saṃyoge saṃyoga jāt śabdāt śabda santāne sati śrotra pratyāsannasya grahaṇam iti yuktam saṃyoga nivṛttau śabdasya grahaṇam iti itas caśabda utpadyate na abhivyajyate kṛtakavat upacārātu atīvram mandam iti kṛtakam upacaryate atīvram sukham mandam sukham tīvram duḥkham mandam duḥkham iti upacaryate ca atīvraḥ śabdaḥ  mandaḥ śabdaḥ iti vyañjakasya tathā abhāvāt  grahaṇasya tīvra manda tā rūpavat iti ced  na abhibhava upapatteḥ saṃyogasya vyañjakasya tīvra manda tayā śabda grahaṇasya tīvra manda tā bhavati na tu śabdaḥ  bhidyate yathā prakāśasya tīvra manda tayā rūpa grahaṇasya iti tad ca na evam abhibhava upapatteḥu tīvraḥ  bherī śabdaḥ  mandam tantrī śabdam abhibhavati na mandaḥ na ca śabda grahaṇam abhibhāvakam śabdaḥ ca na bhidyate iti śabde tu bhidyamāne yuktaḥ  abhibhavaḥ tasmāt utpadyate śabdaḥ  na abhivyajyate iti abhibhava anupapattiśyaca vyañjaka samāna deśasya abhivyaktau prāpti abhāvāt avyañjakena samāna deśaḥ  abhivyajyate śabdaḥ iti etasmin pakṣe na upapadyate abhibhavaḥ na hi bherī śabdena tantrī svanaḥ prāpta iti aprāpte abhibhava iti ced  śabda mātra abhibhava prasaṅgaḥ artha manyeta aasatyām prāptau  abhibhavaḥ  bhavati iti evam sati yathā bherī śabdaḥ kañcid  tantrī svanam abhibhavati evam antika stha upādānān iva davīyaḥ stha upādānān api tantrī svanān abhibhavet aprāpteḥ aviśeṣāt  tatra kvacid eva bheryā praṇāditāyām sarva lokeṣu samāna kālāḥ tantrī svanā na śrūyeran iti nānā bhūteṣu śabda santāneṣu satsu śrotra pratyāsatti bhāvena kasyacid śabdasya autīvreṇa mandasya abhibhavaḥ  yukta iti kaḥ punar ayam abhibhavaḥ  nāma grāhya samāna jātīya grahaṇa kṛtam agrahaṇam abhibhavaḥ yathā ulkā prakāśasya grahaṇa arhasya āditya prakāśena iti na khalu ādimat tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ kasmāt  vyabhicārāt  ādimataḥ khalu ghaṭa abhāvasya dṛṣṭam nitya tvam katham ādimān kāraṇa vibhāgebhyaḥ  hi ghaṭaḥ  na bhavati katham asya nitya tvam yaḥ  asau kāraṇa vibhāgebhyaḥ  na bhavati na tasya abhāvaḥ  bhāvena kadācid  nirvartyate iti yad api aindriyaka tvāt  iti tad api vyabhicarati aindriyakam ca sāmānyam nityam ca iti yad api kṛtakavat upacārāt iti etad api vyabhicarati nityeṣu anityavat upacāraḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  yathā hi bhavati avṛkṣasya pradeśaḥ kambalasya pradeśaḥ evam aākāśasya pradeśa ātmanaḥ pradeśaḥ iti bhavati iti nityam iti atra kim tāvat  tattvam artha antarasya anutpatti dharmakasya ātma hāna anupapattiḥ nitya tvam tad ca abhāve na upapadyate bhāktam tu bhavati yad tatra ātmāna mahāsītuyat  bhūtvā na bhavati na jātu tad  punar bhavati tatra nitya iva nityaḥ  ghaṭa abhāva iti ayam padārtha iti tatra yathājātīyakaḥ śabdaḥ  na tathājātīyakam kāryam kiñcid  nityam dṛśyate iti  avyabhicāraḥ yad api asāmānya nitya tvāt iti indriya pratyāsatti grāhyam aindriyakam iti anityeṣu avyabhicāraḥ iti prakṛtam na indriya grahaṇa sāmarthyāt  śabdasya anitya tvam kim tarhi indriya pratyāsatti grāhya tvāt saṃtāna anumānam tena anitya tvam iti yad api anityeṣu api anityavat upacārāt iti na aevam ākāśa pradeśaḥ ātma pradeśaḥ iti na atra ākāśa ātmanoḥ kāraṇa dravyam abhidhīyate yathā kṛtakasya katham hi avidyamānam abhidhīyate avidyamāna tā ca pramāṇataḥ  anupalabdheḥ kim tarhi tatra abhidhīyate saṃyogasya avyāpya vṛtti tvam uparicchinnena dravyeṇa ākāśa svaya saṃyogaḥ  na ākāśam vyāpnoti avyāpya vartate iti tad asya kṛtakena dravyeṇa sāmānyam na hi āmalakayoḥ saṃyoga āśrayam vyāpnoti sāmānya kṛtā ca bhaktiḥ aākāśasya pradeśaḥ iti anena ātma pradeśaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ saṃyogavat ca śabda buddhi ādīnām avyāpya vṛtti tvam iti parīkṣitā ca tīvra manda tā śabda tattvam na bhakti kṛta iti kasmāt  punar  sūtra kārasya asmin  arthe sūtram na śrūyate iti śīlam idam bhagavataḥ sūtrakārasya bahuṣu adhikaraṇeṣu dvau pakṣau na vyavasthāpayati tatra śāstra siddhāntāt tattva avadhāraṇam pratipattum arhati iti manyate śāstra siddhāntaḥ tu nyāya samākhyātam anumatam bahu śākham anumānam iti atha api khalu aidam asti idam na asti iti kuta etad  pratipattavyam iti pramāṇata upalabdheḥ anupalabdheḥ ca iti avidyamānaḥ tarhi śabdaḥ prāc uccāraṇāt nasti śabdaḥ kasmāt  anupalabdheḥ sataḥ  anupalabdhiḥ āvaraṇa ādibhya etad na upapadyate kasmāt  āvaraṇa ādīnām anupalabdhi kāraṇānāma grahaṇāt  anena āvṛtaḥ śabdaḥ  na upalabhyate asaṃnikṛṣṭaḥ ca indriya vyavadhānāt  iti evamādi anupalabdhi kāraṇam na gṛhyate iti saḥ  ayam anuccāritaḥ  na asti iti uccāraṇam asya vyañjakam tad abhāvāt prāc uccāraṇāt anupalabdhiḥ iti kim idam uccāraṇam nāma iti vivakṣā janitena prayatnena koṣṭhyasya vāyoḥ preritasya kaṇṭha tālu ādi pratighātāt  varṇa abhivyaktiḥ iti saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ  vai pratighātaḥ pratiṣiddham ca saṃyogasya vyañjaka tvam tasmāt na vyañjaka abhāvāt agrahaṇam api tu abhāvāt eva iti soyam uccāryamāṇaḥ śrūyate śrūyamāṇaḥ ca abhūtvā bhavati iti anumīyate ūrdhvañca uccāraṇān na śrūyate sa bhūtvā na bhavati abhāvāt na śrūyate iti katham āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ iti uktam tasmāt utpatti tirobhāva dharmakaḥ śabda iti evam ca sati tattvam pāṃśubhiḥ iva avākiran  idam āha yadi anupalambhāt āvaraṇam na asti āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api tarhi anupalambhāt na asti iti tasyāḥ  abhāvāt apratiṣiddham āvaraṇam iti katham punar jānīte bhavān na āvaraṇānupalabdhiḥ upalabhyate iti kim atra jñeyam pratyātma vedanīya tvāt  samānam ayam khalu āvaraṇam anupalabhamānaḥ pratyātmam eva saṃvedayate anāvaraṇam upalabhe iti yathā kuḍyena āvṛtasya āvaraṇam upalabhamānaḥ pratyātmam eva saṃvedayate sā iyam āvaraṇa upalabdhivat  āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api saṃvedyā eva iti evam ca sati apahṛta viṣayam uttara vākyam asti iti abhyanujñāvāt iva tu ucyate jāti vādinā yathā anupalabhyamānā api āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti evam anupalabhyamānam api āvaraṇam asti iti yadi abhyanujānāti bhavān anānupalīyamāna āvaraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asti iti abhyanujñāvaya ca vadati anāsti āvaraṇam anupalambhāt iti etad  etasmin  api abhyanujñā vāde pratipatti niyamaḥ  na upapadyate iti yudapalabhyate tad asti yad na upalabhyate tad na asti iti anupalambha ātmakam asat iti vyavasthitam upalabdhi abhāvaḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ iti sā iyam abhāva tvāt na upalabhyate sacaca khalvāvaraṇam tasya upalabdhyā bhavitavyam na na upalabhyate tasmāt na asti iti tatra yad uktam na āvaraṇa anupapattiḥ anupalambhāt  iti  ayuktam iti atha śabdasya nitya tvam pratijānānaḥ kasmāt  hetoḥ pratijānīte asparśam ākāśam nityam dṛṣṭam iti tathā ca śabda iti saḥ  ayam ubhayatas  savyabhicāraḥ sparśavān  cāṇuḥ nityaḥ asparśam ca karma anityam dṛṣṭam asparśa tvāt  iti etasya sādhya sādharmyeṇa udāharaṇam sādhya vaidharmyeṇa udāharaṇam ubhayasmin  udāharaṇe vyabhicārāt na hetuḥ ayam tarhi hetuḥ saṃpradīyamānam avasthitam dṛṣṭam saṃpradīyate ca śabda ācāryeṇa antevāsine tasmāt avasthita iti yena saṃpradīyate yasmai ca tayoḥ antarāle avasthānam asya kena liṅgena upalabhyate sa pradīyamānaḥ  hi avasthitaḥ saṃprādātuḥ paiti saṃpradānam ca prāpnoti iti avarjanīyam etad  adhyāpanam liṅgam asati saṃpradāne adhyāpanam na syāt iti samānam adhyāpanam ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ saṃśaya anivṛtteḥ kim ācārya sthaḥ śabdaḥ  astevāsinam āpadyate tad adhyāpanam āhaḥ svid  nṛtya upadeśavat  gṛhītasya anukaraṇam adhyāpanam iti evam adhyāpanam aliṅgam saṃpradānasya iti ayam tarhi hetuḥ abhyasyamānam avasthitam dṛṣṭam apañca kṛtvas  paśyati iti rūpam avasthitam punar  punar dṛśyate bhavati ca śabde abhyāsaḥ adaśa kṛtvā u adhītaḥ  anuvākaḥ viṃśati kṛtvā u adhītaḥ iti tasmāt avasthitasya punar  punar uccāraṇam abhyāsa iti anavasthānepi abhyāsasya abhidhānam bhavati advirnṛtyatu bhavān tris nṛtyatu bhavān iti adviranṛtyat tris anṛtyat adviragni hotram juhoti advirbhuṅkte iti evam vyabhicārāt  pratiṣiddha hetau anya śabdasya prayogaḥ pratiṣidhyate yad idam aanyat iti manyase tad  sva ātmanaḥ  ananya tvāt anyat na bhavati evam anyatāyā abhāvaḥ tatra yad uktam aanya tvepi abhyāsa upacārāt iti etad ayuktam iti śabda prayogam pratiṣedhataḥ śabda antara prayogaḥ pratiṣidhyate anyasmāt  anyatām upapādayati bhavān upapādya ca anyat  pratyācaṣṭe aananyat iti ca śabdam anujānāti prayuṅkte ca aananyat iti etad  samāsapadam anya śabda uyam pratiṣedhena saha samasyate yadi ca atra uttaram padam na asti kasya ayam pratiṣedhenana saha samāsaḥ tasmāt  tayoḥ anya ananya śabdayoḥ itaraḥ  ananya śabda itaram anya śabdam apekṣamāṇaḥ sidhyati iti tatra yad uktam aanyatāyā abhāvaḥ iti etad ayuktam iti astu tarhi dānīm śabdasya nitya tvam yad anityam tasya vināśaḥ kāraṇāt  bhavati yathā loṣṭasya kāraṇa dravya vibhāgāt śabdaḥ ced anityaḥ tasya vināśaḥ  yasmāt kāraṇāt  bhavati tad upalabhyeta na ca upalabhyate tasmāt nitya iti yathā vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ avināśa prasaṅgaḥ evam aśravaṇa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ satatam śravaṇa prasaṅgaḥ vyañjaka abhāvāt aśravaṇam iti ced  pratiṣiddham vyañjakam atha vidyamānasya nirnimittam aśravaṇam iti vidyamānasya nirnimittaḥ  vināśa iti samānaḥ ca dṛṣṭa virodhaḥ  nimittam antareṇa vināśe ca aśrivaṇe ca iti anumānāt ca upalabhyamāne śabdasya vināśa karaṇe abava nāśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ asattvāt iti anapadeśaḥ yathā ayasmāt viṣāṇī tasmāt aśvaḥ iti kim anumānam iti ced  saṃtāna upapattiḥ upapāditaḥ śabda saṃtānaḥ saṃyoga vibhāga jāt  śabdāt śabda antaram tata upi anyat tata upyanyat iti tatra kāryaḥ śabdaḥ kāraṇa śabdam viruṇaddhi pratighāti dravya saṃyogaḥ tu antyasya śabdasya nirodhakaḥ dṛṣṭam hi tiras pratikuḍyam antika sthena api aśravaṇam śabdasya śravaṇam dūra sthena api asati vyavadhāne iti ghaṇṭāyām abhihanyamānāyām tāraḥ tārataraḥ  mandaḥ mandatara iti śruti bhedāt  nānā śabda saṃtānaḥ  avicchedena śrūyate tatra nitye śabde ghaṇṭā stham anya gatam vā avasthitam saṃtāna vṛtti vā abhivyakti kāraṇam vācyam yena śruti saṃtānaḥ  bhavati iti śabda bhede ca asati śruti bheda upapādayitavya iti anitye tu śabde ghaṇṭā stham saṃtāna vṛtti saṃyoga sahakāri nimitta antaram saṃskāra bhūtam paṭu mandam anuvartate tasya anuvṛttyā śabda saṃtāna anuvṛttiḥ paṭu manda bhāvāt ca tīvra manda tā śabdasya tad kṛtaḥ ca śruti bheda iti na vai nirnimitta antaram saṃskāra upalabhyate anupalabdheḥ na asti iti pāṇikarmaṇā pāṇi ghaṇṭā praśleṣaḥ  bhavati tasmin  ca sati śabda saṃtānaḥ  na upalabhyate atas  śravaṇa anupapattiḥ tatra pratighāti dravya saṃyogaḥ śabdasya nimitta antaram saṃskāra bhūtam niruṇaddhi iti anumīyate tasya ca nirodhāt  śabda saṃtānaḥ  na utpadyate anutpanne ca śruti vicchedaḥ yathā pratighāti dravya saṃyoga ādiṣoḥ kriyā hetau saṃskāre niruddhe gamana abhāva iti kampa saṃtānasya sparśana indriya grāhyasya ca uparamaḥ kāṃsya pātra ādiṣu pāṇi saṃśleṣaḥ  liṅgam saṃskāra saṃtānasya iti tasmāt nimitta antarasya saṃskāra bhūtasya na anupalabdhiḥ iti yadi yasya vināśa kāraṇam na upalabhyate tad avatiṣṭhate avasthānāt ca tasya nitya tvam prasajyate evam yāni khalpimāni śabda śravaṇāni śabda abhivyaktaya iti matam na teṣām vināśa kāraṇam bhavatā upapādyate anupapādanāt avasthānam avasthānāt  teṣām nitya tvam prasajyate iti atha na evamḥ na tarhi vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ śabdasya avasthānāt nitya tvam iti kampa samāna āśrayasya ca anunādasya pāṇi praśleṣāt  kāraṇa uparamāt abhāvaḥ vaiyadhikaraṇye hi pratighāti dravya apraśleṣāt  samāna adhikaraṇasya eva uparamaḥ syāt iti yad idam anākāśa guṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratiṣidhyate ayam anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ asparśa tvāt  śabda āśrayasya rūpa ādi samāna deśasya agrahaṇe śabda saṃtāna upapatteḥ asparśa vyāpi dravya āśrayaḥ śabdaḥ iti jñāyate na ca kampa samāna āśraya iti pratidravyam rūpa ādibhiḥ saha saṃniviṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ samāna deśaḥ  vyajyate iti na upapadyate katham saṃtāna upapatteḥ ca iti ca arthaḥ tad  vyākhyātam yadi rūpa ādayaḥ śabdaḥ ca pratidravyam samasta aḥu samuditāḥ tasmin samāsa samudāye yaḥ  yathājātīyakaḥ saṃniviṣṭaḥ tasya tathā ajātīyasya eva grahaṇena bhavitavyam śabdasya rūpa ādivat  tatra yaḥ  ayam vibhāgaḥ eka dravye nānā rūpā bhinna śrutayaḥ vidharmāṇaḥ śabdaḥ abhivyajyamānāḥ yad ca vibhāga antaram sarūpāḥ samāna śrutayaḥ sadharmāṇaḥ śabdāḥ tīvra manda dharma tayā bhinnāḥ śrūyante tad ubhayam na upapadyate nānā bhūtānām utpadyamāna anām ayam dharmaḥ  na ekasya vyajyamānasya iti asti ca ayam vibhāgaḥ  vibhāga antaram ca tena vibhāga upapatteḥ manyāmahe na pratidravyam rūpa ādibhiḥ saha śabdaḥ saṃniviṣṭaḥ  vyajyate iti dvividhaḥ ca ayam śabdaḥ varṇa ātmakaḥ  dhvani mātraḥ ca tatra varṇa ātmani tāvat  adadhyatra iti kecid  ikāraḥ itvam hitvā yatvam āpadyate iti vikāram manyante kecid  ikārasya prayoge viṣaya kṛte yad  ikāraḥ sthānam jahāti tatra yakārasya prayogam bruvate saṃhitāyām viṣaye ikāraḥ  na prayujyate tasya sthāne yakāraḥ prayujyate sa ādeśa iti ubhayam idam upadiśyate tatra na jñāyate kim tattvam iti ādeśa upadeśaḥ tattvam vikāra upadeśe hi anvayasya agrahaṇāt  vikārān anumānam iti sati anvaye kiñcid  nivartate kiñcid upajāyate iti śakyeta vikāraḥ  anumātum na ca anvayaḥ  gṛhyate tasmāt  vikāraḥ  na asti iti bhinna karaṇayoḥ ca varṇayoḥ aprayoge prayoga upapattiḥ vivṛta karaṇa ikāraḥ īṣat spṛṣṭa karaṇaḥ  yakāraḥ tau  imau pṛthak  karaṇa ākhyena prayatnena uccāraṇīyau tayoḥ ekasya aprayoge anyasya prayoga upapanna iti avikāre ca aviśeṣaḥ yatra imau ikāraya kārau na vikāra bhūtau ayatate cachati prāyaṃmta iti aikāraḥ idam iti ca yatra ca vikāra bhūtau adṛṣṭyaḥ adadhyāhara iti ubhayatra prayoktuḥ aviśeṣaḥ  yatnaḥ śrotuḥ ca śrutiḥ ati ādeśa upipattiḥ prayujyamāna agrahaṇāt ca na khalu ikāraḥ prayujyamānaḥ  yakāra tām āpadyamānaḥ  gṛhyate kim tarhi ikārasya prayoge yakāraḥ prayujyate tasmāt avikāra iti avikāre ca na śabda anvā ākhyāna la upaḥ na vikriyante vaṇā iti na ca etasmin pakṣe śabda anvā ākhyānasya asaṃbhavaḥ  yena varṇa vikāram pratipadyemahi iti na khalu varṇasya varṇa antaram kāryam na hi ikārāt  yakāra utpadyate yakārāt vā ikāraḥ pṛthak sthāna prayatna utpādyā hi ime varṇāḥ teṣām anyaḥ anyasya sthāne prayujyate iti yuktam etāvat ca etad  paraṇāmaḥ  vikāraḥ syāt  kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ  vā ubhayam ca na asti tasmāt na santi varṇa vikāraḥ varṇa samudāya vikāra anupapattivat ca varṇa vikāra anupapa ttiḥ asteḥ bhūḥ bruvaḥ vaciḥ iti yathā varṇa samudāyasya dhātu lakṣaṇasya kvacid viṣaye varṇa antara samudāyaḥ  na paraṇāmaḥ  ni kāryam śabda antarasya sthāne śabda antaram prayujyate tathā varṇasya varṇa antaram iti itas ca na santi vikārāḥ prakṛti anuvidhānam vikāreṣu dṛṣṭam yakāre hasva dīrgha anuvidhānam na asti yena vikāra tvam anumīyata iti davya vikārā nyūnāḥ samā adhikāḥ ca gṛhyante tadvat ayam vikāraḥ  nyūnaḥ syāt iti dvividhasya api hetoḥ  abhāvāt  asādhanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ atra na udāharaṇa sādharmyāt  hetuḥ asti na vaidharmyāt  anupasaṃhṛtaḥ ca hetunā dṛṣṭāntaḥ  na sādhaka iti pratidṛṣṭānte ca aniyamaḥ prasajyeta yathā anaḍuhaḥ sthāne aśvaḥ vā uḍum niyuktaḥ  na tad vikāraḥ  bhavati evam ivaṛṇasya sthāne yakāraḥ prayuktaḥ  na vikāra iti na ca atra niyama hetuḥ asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhakaḥ  na pratidṛṣṭānta iti dravya vikāra udāharaṇam ca atulyānām dravyāṇām prakṛti bhāvaḥ  vikalpane vikāraḥ ca prakṛtīḥ anuvidhīyate na tu ivarṇam anuvidhīyate yakāraḥ tasmāt anudāharaṇam adravya vikāraḥ iti yathā dravya bhāvena tulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikāra vaiṣamyam evam varṇa bhāvena tulyāyāḥ prakṛteḥ vikāra vikalpa iti ayam vikāra dharmaḥ dravya sāmānye yad ātmakam dravyam mṛdvā suvarṇam vā tasya ātmanaḥ  anvaye pūrvaḥ vyūhaḥ  nivartate vyūha antaram ca upajāyate tam vikāram ācakṣate na varṇa sāmānye kaścid  śabda ātmā anvayī ya itvam jahāti yatvam ca āpadyate tatra yathā sati dravya bhāve vikāra vaiṣamye na anaḍuhaḥ  aśvaḥ vikāraḥ vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ evam ivaṛṇasya na yakāraḥ  vikāraḥ vikāra dharma anupapatteḥ iti itas ca na santi varṇa vikārāḥ anupapannā punar āpattiḥ katham punar āpatteḥ ananumānāt iti ikāraḥ  yakāra tvam āpannaḥ punar ikāraḥ  bhavati na punar ikā asya sthāne yakārasya prayoga iti atra anumānam na asti ananumānāt iti na idam hi anumānam suvarṇam kuṇḍala tvam hitvā rucaka tvam āpadyate rucaka tvam hitvā punar  kuṇḍala tvam āpadyate evam ikāraḥ  yaṇi yakāra tvam āpannaḥ punar ikāraḥ  bhavati iti vyabhicārāt ananumānam yathā payaḥ  dadhibhāvam āpannam punar  payaḥ  na bhavati kim evam varṇānām na punar āpattiḥ atha suvarṇavat punar āpattiḥ iti sūvarṇa udāharaṇa upapattiḥ ca avasthitam suvarṇam hīyamānena upajāyamānena ca dharmeṇa dharmi bhavati na evam kaścid  śabda ātmā hīyamānena itvena upajāyamānena yatvena ca dharmī gṛhyate tasmāt  suvarṇa udāharaṇam na upapadyate iti varṇa vikārā api varṇa tvam na vyabhicaranti yathā suvarṇa vikāraḥ suvarṇa tvam iti kuṇḍala rucakau suvarṇasya dharmaum na suvarṇa tvasya evam ikāraya kārau kasya varṇa ātmanaḥ  dharmaum varṇa tvam sāmānyam na tasya imau dharmaum bhavitum arhataḥ na ca nivartamānaḥ  dharma upajāyamānasya prakṛtiḥutatra nivartamāna ikāraḥ  na yakārasya upajāyamānasya prakṛtiḥ iti itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ anityā varṇāḥ iti etasmi n ṛ pakṣe ikāraya kārau varṇaum iti ubhayoḥ nitya tvāt  vikāra anupapattiḥ nitya tve avināśi tvāt  kaḥ kasya vikāra iti atha aanityā varṇāḥ iti pakṣaḥ evam api anavasthānam varṇānām kim idam anavasthānam varṇānām utpadya nirodhaḥ utpadya niruddhe ikāre yakāra utpadyate yakāre ca utpadya niruddhe ikāra utpadyate kaḥ kasya vikāraḥ tad etad  avagṛhya saṃdhāne saṃdhāya ca avagrahe veditavyam iti nitya pakṣe tu tāvat samādhiḥ anityā varṇā na vikriyante iti vipratiṣedhaḥ yathā nitya tve sati kiñcid atīndriyam kiñci dinrdiya grāhyam indriya grāhyāḥ ca varṇāḥ evam nitya tve sati kiñcinana vikriyate varṇāḥ tu vikriyante iti virodhāt ahetuḥ tad dharma vikalpaḥ nityam na upajāyate na apaiti anupajana apāya dharmakam nityam anityam punar upajana apāya yuktam na ca antareṇa upajana apāyau vikāraḥ saṃbhavati tad  yadi varṇā vikriyante nitya tvam eṣām nivartate atha nityāḥ vikāra dharma tvam eṣām nivartate soyam viruddhaḥ  hetvābhāsaḥ  dharma vikalpa iti anitya pakṣe samādhiḥ yathā anavasthāyinām varṇānām śravaṇam bhavati evam eṣām vikāraḥ  bhavati iti asaṃbandhāt asamarthā artha pratipādikā varṇa upalabdhiḥ na vikāreṇa saṃbandhāt asamarthā yā gṛhyamāṇā varṇa vikāram anumāpayet iti tatra yādṛś idam yathā gandha guṇā pṛthivī evam śabda sukha ādi guṇā api iti tādṛś etad  bhavati iti na ca varṇa upalabdhiḥ varṇa nivṛttau varṇa antara prayogasya nirvartikā yaḥ  ayami vaṛṇa nivṛttau yakārasya prayogaḥ yadi ayam i vaṛṇa upalabdhyā nirvartate tadā tatra upalabhyamāna ivarṇaḥ  yatvam āpadyate iti gṛhyeta tasmāt varṇa upalabdhiḥ ahetuḥ varṇa vikārasya iti tad dharma vikalpāt iti na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ na khalu vikāra dharmakam kiñcid  nityam upalabhyate iti varṇa upalabdhivat iti ca na yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ avagrahe hi adadhi atra iti prayujya ciram sthitvā tatas  saṃhitāyām prayuṅkte adadhyatra iti cira nivṛtte ca ayam i vaṛṇe yakāraḥ prayujyamānaḥ kasya vikāra iti pratīyate kāraṇa abhāvāt kārya abhāva iti una yogaḥ prasajyate iti itas ca varṇa vikāra anupapattiḥ ikāra sthāne yakāraḥ śrūyate yakāra sthāne khalvikāraḥ  vidhīyate vidhyati iti tad  yadi syāt  prakṛti vikāra bhāvaḥ  varṇānām tasya prakṛti niyamaḥ syāt  dṛṣṭaḥ  vikāra dharmi tve prakṛti niyama iti yoyam prakṛteḥ aniyama uktaḥ sa niyataḥ yathā viṣayam vyavasthitaḥ niyata tvāt niyama iti bhavati evam satya niyamaḥ  na asti tatra yad uktam prakṛti aniyamāt  iti etad ayuktam iti niyama iti atra artha abhyanujñā aniyama iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ anujñāta tiṣiddhayoḥ ca vyāghātāt anartha antara tvam na bhavati aniyamaḥ ca niyata tvāt  niyamaḥ  na bhavati iti na atra arthasya tathā abhāvaḥ pratiṣidhyate kim tarhi tathābhūtasya arthasya niyama śabdena abhidhīyamānasya niyata tvāt  niyama śabda eva upapadyate soyam niyamāt aniyame pratiṣedhaḥ  na bhavati iti na ca iyam varṇa vikāra upapattiḥ pariṇāmāt  kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā kim tarhi sthānyādeśa bhāvāt aprayoge prayogaḥ  vikāra śabda arthaḥ sa bhidyate guṇān atara āpattiḥ udāttasya anudatta iti evamādiḥ upamarde nāma eka rūpa nivṛttau rūpa antara upajanaḥ hrāsaḥ dīrghasya hrāsvaḥ vṛddhiḥ hrasvasya dīrghaḥ tayoḥ vā āplutaḥ leśaḥ lāghavam astaḥ iti asteḥ vikāraḥ śleṣaḥ āgamaḥ prakṛteḥ pratyayasya vā ete eva viśeṣāḥ vikārā iti ete eva ādeśāḥ ete ced vikārā upapadyante tarhi varṇa vikārā iti yathādarśanam vikṛtā varṇā vibhakti antāḥ pada saṃjñā bhavanti vibhaktiḥ dvayī nāmikī ākhyātikī ca abrāhmaṇaḥ apacati iti udāharaṇam upasarga nipātāḥ tarhi na pada saṃjñāḥ lakṣaṇa antaram vācyam iti śiṣyate ca khalu nāmikyā vibhakteḥ avyayāt lopaḥ tayoḥ pada saṃjñā artham iti padena artha saṃpratyaya iti prayojanam nāma padam ca adhikṛtya parīkṣā gauḥ iti nāma padam khalu idam udāharaṇam tad arthe avinā abhāva vṛttiḥ saṃnidhiḥ avinā abhāvena vartamānāsu vyakti ākṛti jātiṣu gauḥ iti prayujyate tatra na jñāyate kim anyatamaḥ padārthaḥ uta sarvaḥ iti śabdasya prayoga sāmarthyāt  padārtha avadhāraṇam tasmāt  vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt  yā śabda prabhṛtīnām vyaktau  upacārāt upacāraḥ prayogaḥ ayā gauḥ tiṣṭhati yā gauḥ niṣaṇṇā iti nu udam vākyam jāteḥ abhidhāyakam abhedāt  bhedāt tu dravya abhidhāyakam agavān samūhaḥ iti bhedāt  dravya abhidhānam na jāteḥ abhedāt  avaidyāya gām dadāti iti dravyasya tyāgaḥ  na jāteḥ amūrta tvāt  pratikrama anukrama anupapatteḥ ca parigrahaḥ sva tvena abhisaṃbandhaḥ akauṇḍinyasya gauḥ abrāhmaṇasya gauḥ iti dravya abhidhona dravya bhedāt  saṃbandha bheda iti upapannam abhinnā tu jātiḥ iti saṃkhyā adaśa gāvaḥ  viṃśatiḥ gāvaḥ iti bhinnam dravyam saṃkhyāyate na jātiḥ abhedāt iti vṛddhiḥ kāraṇavataḥ  dravyasya avayava upacayaḥ aavardhata gauḥ iti niravayavā tu jātiḥ iti etena apacayaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ varṇaḥ aśuklā gauḥ kapilā gauḥ iti dravyasya guṇa yogaḥ  na sāmānyasya samāsaḥ agohitam gosukham iti dravyasya sukha ādi yogaḥ  na jāteḥ iti anubandhaḥ sarūpa prajanana santānaḥ agauḥ gān janayati iti tad  utpatti dharma tvāt  dravye yuktam na jātau viparyayāt iti dravyam vyaktiḥ iti hi na artha antaram asya pratiṣedhaḥ na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt  anavasthānāt  yā śabda prabhṛtibhiḥ yaḥ viśeṣyate sa gaḥ śabda arthaḥ ayā gauḥ tiṣṭhati yā gauḥ niṣaṇṇā iti na dravya mātram aviśiṣṭam jātyā vinā abhidhīyate kim tarhi jāti viśiṣṭam tasmāt na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ evam samūha ādiṣu draṣṭavyam yadi na vyaktiḥ padārthaḥ katham tarhi vyaktau  upacāra iti nimittāt  atadbhāve api tad upacāraḥ  dṛśyate khalu atadbhāvepi tad upacāra iti atad śabdasya tena śabdena abhidhānam iti sahacaraṇāt  ayaṣṭikām bhojaya iti yaṣṭikā sahacaritaḥ  brāhmaṇaḥ  abhidhīyate iti sthānāt  amañcāḥ krāśanti iti mañca sthāḥ puruṣā abhidhīyante tādarthyāt  kaṭārtheṣu vīraṇeṣu vyūhyamāneṣu akaṭam karoti iti bhavati vṛttāt  ayamaḥ  rājā akuberaḥ  rājā iti tadvat vartate iti mānāt  āḍhakena mitāḥ saktavaḥ aāḍhakam saktavaḥ iti dhāraṇāt  tulayā dhṛtam candanam atulā candanam iti sāmīpyāt  agaṅgāyām gāvaḥ caranti iti deśaḥ  abhidhīyate saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ yogāt  kṛṣṇena rāgeṇa yuktaḥ śākaṭaḥ akṛṣṇaḥ iti abhidhīyate sādhanāt  aannam prāṇāḥ iti ādhipatyāt  aayam puruṣaḥ kulam aayam gotram iti tatra ayam sahacaraṇāt  yogāt  vā jāti śabdaḥ  vyaktau prayujyate iti yadi agauḥ iti asya padasya na vyaktiḥ arthaḥ astu tarhi ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt  padapekṣa tvāt  sattva vyavasthāna siddheḥ sattva avayavānām tad avayavānām ca niyataḥ  vyūha ākṛtiḥ tasyām gṛhyamāṇāyām sattva vyavasthānam sidhyati aayam gauḥ aayam aśvaḥ iti na agṛhyamāṇāyām yasya grahaṇāt  sattva vyavasthānam sidhyati tam śabdaḥ  abhidhātum arhati saḥ  asya artha iti na etad upapadyate yasya jātyā yogaḥ tad atra jāti viśiṣṭam abhidhīyate agauḥ iti na ca avayava vyūhasya jātyā yogaḥ kasya tarhi niyata avayava vyūhasya dravyasya tasmāt  na ākṛtiḥ padārthaḥ astu tarhi jātiḥ padārthaḥ jātiḥ padārthaḥ kasmāt  vyakti ākṛti yuktepi mṛdgavake prokṣaṇa ādīnām aprasaṅgāt iti agām prokṣaya agāmānaya agām dehi iti na etāni mṛdgavake prayujyante kasmāt  jāteḥ abhāvāt  asti hi tatra vyaktiḥ asti ākṛtiḥ yad abhāvāt  tatra asaṃpratyayaḥ sa padārtha iti jāteḥ abhivyaktiḥ ākṛti vyaktī apekṣate na agṛhyamāṇa āyām ākṛtau vyaktau ca jāti mātram śuddham gṛhyate tasmāt na jātiḥ padārtha iti na vai padārthena na bhavitum śakyam kaḥ khalu idānīm padārtha iti tuśabdaḥ  viśeṣaṇa arthaḥ kim viśiṣyate pradhāna aṅga bhāvasya aniyamena padārtha tvam iti yadā hi bheda vivakṣā viśeṣa gatiḥ ca tadā vyaktiḥ pradhānam aṅgam tu jāti ākṛtī yadā tu bhedaḥ  avivakṣitaḥ sāmānya gatiḥ ca tadā jātiḥ pradhānam aṅgam tu vyakti ākṛtī tad etad  bahulam prayogeṣu ākṛteḥ tu pradhāna bhāva utprekṣitavyaḥ katham punar jñāyate nānā vyakti ākṛti jātaya iti lakṣaṇa bhedāt  tatra tāvat  vyajyate iti vyaktiḥ indriya grāhya iti na sarvam dravyam vyaktiḥ yaḥ  guṇa viśeṣāṇām sparśa antānām gurutva dhanatva dravatva saṃskārāṇām avyāpinaḥ parimāṇasya āśrayaḥ  yathāsaṃbhavam tad dravyam mūrtiḥ mūrchita avayava tvāt iti yayā jātiḥ jāti liṅgāni ca prakhyāyante tām ākṛtim vidyāt  sā ca na anyā sattva avayavānām tad avayavānām ca niyatāt  vyūhāt iti niyata avayava vyūhāḥ khalu sattva avayavā jāti liṅgam śirasā pādena gām anum invanti niyate ca sattva avayavānām vyūhe sati gaḥ tvam prakhyāyate iti anākṛti vyaṅgyāyām jātau amṛt asuvarṇam arajatam iti evamādiṣu ākṛtiḥ nivartate jahāti padārtha tvam iti yā samānām buddhim prasūte bhinneṣu adhikaraṇeṣu yayā bahūni itaretaratas  na vyāvatente yaḥ  arthaḥ  anekatra pratyaya anuvṛtti nimittam tad  sāmānyam yad ca keṣāṃ cit abhedam keṣāñcid  bhedam karoti tad  sāmānya viśeṣaḥ  jātiḥ iti iti vātsyāyanīye nyāya bhāṣye dvitīya adhyāyasya dvitīyam āhnikam samāptam dvitīya adhyāyaḥ ca samāptaḥ #################################################################### atha saṭīke nyāya bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam parīkṣitāni pramāṇāni prameyam idānīm parīkṣyate tad ca ātmā ādi iti ātmā vivicyate kim deha indriya manaḥ buddhi vedanā saṃghāta mātram ātmā āhaḥ svid  tavdi atiriktaḥ iti kutas  saṃśayaḥ vyapadeśasya ubhayathā siddheḥ kriyā karaṇayoḥ kartrā saṃbandhasya abhidhānam vyapadeśaḥ sa dvividhaḥ avayavena samudāyasya amūlaiḥ vṛkṣaḥ tiṣṭhati astambhaiḥ prāsādaḥ  dhriyate iti anyena anyasya vyapadeśaḥ aparaśunā vṛścati apradīpena paśyati iti asti ca ayam vyapadeśaḥ acakṣuṣā paśyati amanasā vijānāti abuddhyā vicārayati aśarīreṇa sukha duḥkham anubhavati iti tatra na avadhāryate kim avayavena samudāyasya deha ādi saṃghātasya atha anyena anyasya tavdi atiriktasya iti anyena ayam anyasya vyapadeśaḥ kasmāt  darśanena yāvat arthaḥ  gṛhītaḥ sparśanena api saḥ  arthaḥ  gṛhyate ayam aham adrākṣam cakṣuṣā tam sparśanena api spṛśāmi iti ayam ca āspārkṣam sparśanena tam cakṣuṣā paśyāmi iti eka viṣayau cermā pratyayau eka kartṛkau pratisaṃdhīyete na ca saṃghāta kartṛkau na vā indriyeṇa eka kartṛkau tad  yaḥ  asau cakṣuṣā tvac indriyeṇa ca eka arthasya grahītā bhinna nimittau ananya kartṛkau pratyayau samāna viṣayau pratisaṃdadhāti saḥ  artha antara bhūta  ātmā katham punar na indriyeṇa eka kartṛkau indriyam khalu svam svam viṣaya grahaṇam ananya kartṛkam pratisaṃdhātum arhati na indriya antarasya viṣaya antara grahaṇam iti katham na saṃghāta kartṛkau ekaḥ khalu ayam bhinna nimittau sva ātma kartṛkau pratyayau pratisaṃhitau vedayate na saṃghātaḥ kasmāt  anivṛttam hi saṃghāte pratyekam viṣaya antara grahaṇasya apratisaṃdhānam indriya antareṇa iva iti na deha ādi saṃghātāt anyaḥ cetanaḥ kasmāt  viṣaya vyavasthānāt  vyavasthita viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi cakṣuṣy asati rūpam na gṛhyate sati ca gṛhyate yad ca yasmin   asati na bhavati sati ca bhavati tasya tad iti vijñāyate tasmāt  rūpa grahaṇam cakṣuṣaḥ cakṣū rūpam paśyati evam ghrāṇa ādiṣu api iti tāni indriyāṇi imāni sva sva viṣaya grahaṇāt cetanāni indriyāṇām bhāva abhāvayoḥ viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā abhāvāt evam sati kim anyena cetanena saṃdigdha tvāt ahetuḥ yaḥ  ayam indriyāṇām bhāva abhāvayoḥ viṣaya grahaṇasya tathā al̃āvaḥ sa kim cetana tvāt  āhosvit  cetana upakaraṇānām grahaṇa nimitta tvāt  iti saṃdihyate cetanā upakaraṇa tve api indriyāṇām grahaṇa nimitta tvāt  bhavitum arhati yad ca uktam viṣaya vyavasthānāt  iti yadi khalu ekam indriyam avyavasthita viṣayam sarvajñam sarva viṣaya grāhi cetanam syāt  kaḥ tatas  anyam cetanam anumātum śaknuyāt  yasmāt tu vyavasthita viṣayāṇi indri nayāṇi tasmāt  tebhyaḥ  anyaḥ cetanaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarva viṣaya grāhī viṣaya vyavasthitim atītaḥ  anumīyate tatra idam pratyabhijñānam apratyākhyeyam cetana vṛttam udāhriyate rūpa darśī khalu ayam rasam gandham vā pūrva gṛhītam anuminoti gandha prativedī ca rūpa rasau   anuminoti evam viṣaya śeṣepi vācyam rūpam dṛṣṭvā gandham jighrati ghrātvā ca gandha rūpam paśyati tad evam aniyata paryāyam sarva viṣaya grahaṇam eka cetanā adhikaraṇam ananya kartṛkam pratisaṃdhatte pratyakṣa anumāna āgama saṃśayān pratyayān  ca nānā viṣayān sva ātma kartṛkān pratisaṃdadhāti pratisaṃdhāya vedayate sarva artha viṣayam ca śāstram pratipadyate artham aviṣaya bhūtam śrotrasya krama bhāvinaḥ  varṇān śrutvā pada vākaya bhāvam pratisaṃdhāya śabda artha vyavasthām ca budhyamānaḥ  aneka viṣayam artha jātam agrahaṇīyam ekaikena indriyeṇa gṛhṇāti sā iyam sarvajñasya jñeya avyavasthā anupadam na śakyā parikramitum ākṛti mātram tu ūha āhṛtam tatra yad uktam aindriya caitanye sati kim anyena cetanena iti tad ayuktam bhavati itas ca deha ādi vyatirikta ātmā na deha ādi saṃghāta mātram śarīra grahaṇena śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā saṃghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ  gṛhyate prāṇi bhūtam śarīram dahataḥ prāṇi hiṃsā kṛta pāpam pātakam iti ucyate tasya abhāvaḥ tad phalena kartuḥ asaṃbandhāt  akartuḥ ca saṃbandhāt  śarīra indriya buddhi vedanā prabandhe khalu anyaḥ saṃghāta utpadyate anyaḥ  nirudhyate utpāda nirodha saṃtati bhūtaḥ prabandhaḥ  na anya tvam bādhate deha ādi saṃghātasya anyatva adhiṣṭhāna tvāt anyatva adhiṣṭhānaḥ  hi asau prakhyāyate iti evam sati yaḥ  deha ādi saṃghātaḥ prāṇi bhūtaḥ  hiṃsā karoti na asau hiṃsā phalena saṃbadhyate yaḥ ca saṃbadhyate na tena hiṃsā kṛtā tad evam sattva bhede kṛta hānam akṛta abhyāgamaḥ prasajyate sati ca sattva utpāde sattva nirodhe ca akarma nimittaḥ sattva sargaḥ prāpnoti tatra mukti arthaḥ  brahmacarya vāsaḥ  na syāt  tad  yadi deha ādi saṃghāta mātram sattvam syāt  śarīra dāhe pātakam na bhavet  aniṣṭam ca etad  tasmāt  deha ādi saṃghāta vyatirikta ātmā nitya iti yasya api nityena ātmanā sa ātmakam śarīram dahyate tasya api śarīra dāhe pātakam na bhavet  dagdhuḥ kasmāt  nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ na jātu kaścid  nityam hiṃsitum arhati atha hiṃsyate nitya tvam asya na bhavati sā iyam ekasmin pakṣe hiṃsā niṣphalā anyasmin  tu  anupapanna iti na brūmaḥ nityasya sattvasya vadhaḥ  hiṃsā api tu anucchiti dharmakasya sattvasya kārya āśrayasya śarīrasya sva viṣaya upalabdheḥ ca kartṝṇām indriyāṇām upaghātaḥ pīḍā vaikalya lakṣaṇaḥ prabandha ucchedaḥ  vā pramāpaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ  ca vadhaḥ  hiṃsā iti kāryam tu sukha duḥkha saṃvedanam tasya āyatanam adhiṣṭhānam āśrayaḥ śārīram kārya āśrayasya śarīrasya sva viṣaya upalabdheḥ ca kartṝṇām indriyāṇām vadhaḥ  hiṃsā na nityasya ātmanaḥ tatra yad uktam tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhepi tad nitya tvāt iti etad ayuktam yasya sattva ucchedaḥ  hiṃsā tasya kṛta hānam akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca iti doṣaḥ etāvat ca etad  syāt  sattva ucchedaḥ  vā hiṃsā anucchitti dharmakasya sattvasya kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhaḥ  vā na kalpa antaram asti sattva ucchedaḥ ca pratiṣiddhaḥ tatra kim anyat śeṣam yathābhūtam iti atha vā kārya āśraya kartṛ vadhāt iti kārya āśrayaḥ deha indriya buddhi saṃghātaḥ  nityasya ātmanaḥ tatra sukha duḥkha pratisaṃvedanam tasya adhiṣṭhānam āśrayaḥ utadāyatanam tad  bhavati na tatas  anyat iti sa eva kartā tad nimittā hi sukha duḥkha saṃvedanasya nirvṛttiḥ na tam antareṇa iti tasya vadhaḥ upaghātaḥ pīḍā pramāpaṇam vā hiṃsā na nitya tvena ātma ucchedaḥ tatra yad uktam tad abhāvaḥ sa ātmaka pradāhepi tad nitya tvāt iti etad na iti itas ca deha ādi vyatirikta ātmā pūrva parayoḥ vijñānayoḥ eka viṣaye pratisaṃdhi jñānam pratyabhijñānam atam eva etarhi paśyāmi yama jñāsiṣam asa eva ayam arthaḥ iti savyena cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭasya itareṇa api cakṣukṣā pratyaṃbhijñānāt  ayam adrākṣam tam eva etarhi paśyāmi iti indriya caitanye tu na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ pratyabhijānāti iti pratyabhijñāna anupapattiḥ asti tu idam pratyabhijñānam tasmāt indriya vyatiriktaḥ cetanaḥ ekam idam cakṣuḥ madhye nāsā asthi vyavahitam tasya antau gṛhyamāṇau dvitva abhimānam prayojayataḥ madhya vyavahitasya dīrghasya iva ekasmin  upahate ca uddhṛte vā vakṣuṣi dvitīyam avatiṣṭhate cakṣuḥ viṣaya grahaṇa liṅgam tasmāt ekasya vyavadhāna anupapattiḥ eka vinośe dvitīya avināśāt iti ahetuḥ kasmāt  vṛkṣasya hi kāsu cit chā ākhāsu cchinnāsu upalabhyate eva vṛkṣaḥ na kāraṇa dravya vibhāge kārya dravyam avatiṣṭhate nityatva prasaṅgāt  bahuṣu avayaviṣu yamya kāraṇāni vibhaktāni tasya vināśaḥ yeṣām kāraṇāni  avibhaktāni tāni  avatiṣṭhante atha vā dṛśyamāna artha virodhaḥ  dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ mṛtasya hi śaraḥ kapāle dvau   avaṭau nāsā asthi vyavahitau cakṣuṣaḥ sthāne bhedena gṛhyete na ca etad  ekasmin nāsā asthi vyavahite saṃbhavati atha ca eka vināśasya aniyamād dvau  imāva arthau tau ca pṛthak āvaraṇa upaghātau anumīyete vibhinnau  iti avapīḍanāt ca ekasya cakṣuṣaḥ  raśmi viṣaya saṃnikarṣasya bhedāt  dṛśya bheda ivava gṛhyate tad ca eka tve virudhyate avapīḍana nivṛttau ca abhinna pratisaṃdhānam iti tasmāt ekasya vyavadhāna anupapattiḥ anumīyate ca ayam deha ādi saṃghāta vyatiriktaḥ cetana iti kasyacid amla phalasya gṛhīta tad rasa sāhacarye rūpe gandhe vā kena cit indriyeṇa gṛhyamāṇe rasanasya indriya antarasya vikāraḥ  rasān usmṛtau rasa gardhi pravartitaḥ  danta udaka saṃplava bhūtaḥ  gṛhyate tasya indriya caitanye anupapattiḥ na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati smṛtiḥ nāma dharmaḥ  nimittāt utpadyate tasyāḥ smartavyaḥ  viṣayaḥ tad kṛta indriya antara vikāraḥ  na ātma kṛta iti tasyāḥ  ātma guṇa tve sati sadbhāvāt apratiṣedha ātmanaḥ yadi smṛtiḥ ātma guṇaḥ evam sati smṛtiḥ upapadyate na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati iti indriya caitanye tu nānā kartṛkāṇām viṣaya grahaṇānām apratisaṃdhānam pratisaṃdhāne vā viṣaya vyavasthā anupapattiḥ ekaḥ tu cetanaḥ aneka artha darśī bhinna nimittaḥ pūrva dṛṣṭam artham smarati iti ekasya aneka artha darśinaḥ darśana pratisaṃdhānāt  smṛteḥ ātma guṇa tve sati sadbhāvaḥ viparyaye ca anupapattiḥ smṛtyā śra nayāḥ prāṇabhṛtām sarve vyavahārāḥ ātma liṅgam udāharaṇa mātram indriya antara vikāra iti aparisaṃkhyāya ca smṛti viṣayam idam ucyate na smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt iti yā iyam smṛtiḥ agṛhyamāṇe arthe aajñāsiṣam aham amum artham iti etasyāḥ  jñātṛ jñāna viśiṣṭaḥ pūrva jñāta ūrthaḥ  viṣayaḥ  na artha mātram ajñātavān aham amum artham aasau  arthaḥ  mayā jñātaḥ aasmin    arthe mama jñānam abhūt  iti caturvidham etad vākyam smṛti viṣa ya jñāpakam samāna artham sarvatra khalu jñātā jñānam jñeyam ca gṛhyate atha pratyakṣe arthe yā smṛtiḥ tayā trīṇi jñānāni ekasmin  arthe pratisaṃdhīyante samāna kartṛkāṇi na nānā kartṛkāṇi na akartṛkāṇi kim tarhi eka kartṛkāṇi aadrākṣam amum artham yam eva etarhi paśyāmi adrākṣam iti darśanam darśana saṃvid ca na khalva saṃvidite svedarśane syāt etad  adrākṣam iti te khalu ete dve jñāne ayam eva etarhi paśyāmi iti tṛtīyam jñānam evam ekorthaḥ tribhiḥ jñānaiḥ yujyamānaḥ  na akartṛ kaḥ  na nānā kartṛkaḥ kim tarhi eka kartṛka iti saḥ  ayam smṛti viṣayaḥ  aparisaṃkhyāyamānaḥ  vidyamānaḥ prajñātaḥ  arthaḥ pratiṣidhyate anāsti ātmā smṛteḥ smartavya viṣaya tvāt iti na ca idam smṛti mātram smartavya mātra viṣayam vā idam khalu jñāna pratisaṃdhānavat smṛti pratisaṃdhānam ekasya sarva viṣaya tvāt ekaḥ  ayam jñātā sarva viṣayaḥ svāni jñānāni pratisaṃdhatte aamum arthan jñāsyāmi amum artham vijānāmi aamum artham ajñāsiṣam amum artham jijñāsamānaḥ ciram ajñātvā adhyavasyati aajñāsiṣam iti evam smṛtim api tri kāla viśiṣṭām su smūrṣā viśiṣṭām ca pratisaṃdhatte saṃskāra saṃtati mātre tu sattve utpadya utpadya saṃskārāḥ tirobhavanti sa na asti ekopi saṃskāraḥ  yaḥ tri kāla viśiṣṭam jñānam smṛtim ca anubhavet  na ca anubhavam antareṇa jñānasya smṛteḥ ca pratisaṃdhānam aham mama iti ca utpadyate deha antaravat atas  anumīyate asti ekaḥ sarva viṣayaḥ yaḥ prati deham sva jñāna prabandham smṛti prabandham ca pratisaṃdhatte iti yasya deha antareṣu vṛtteḥ abhāvāt na pratisaṃdhānam bhavati iti na deha ādi saṃghāta vyatirikta ātmā kasmāt  ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi saṃbhavāt  darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt iti evamādīnām ātma pratipādakānām hetūnām manasi saṃbhavacaḥ yatas  manaḥ  hi sarva viṣayam iti tasmāt na śarīra indriya manaḥ buddhi saṃghāta vyatirikta ātmā iti jñātuḥ khalu jñāna sādhanāni upapadyante acakṣuṣā paśyati aghrāṇena jighrati asparśanena spṛśati evam mantuḥ sarva viṣayasya mati sādhanam antaḥkaraṇa bhūtam sarva viṣayam vidyate yena ayam manyate iti evam sati jñātaryā ātma saṃjñā na mṛṣyate manaḥ saṃjñā abhyanujñāyate manasi ca manaḥ saṃjñā na mṛṣyate mati sādhana saṃjñā mṛṣyate tad idam saṃjñā bheda mātram na arthe vivāda iti pratyākhyāne vā sarva indriya vilopa prasaṅgaḥ atha mantuḥ sarva viṣayasya mati sādhanam sarva viṣayam pratyākhyāyate na asti ite evam rūpa ādi grahaṇa sādhanāni api na santi iti sarva indriya vilopaḥ prasajyate iti yaḥ  ayam niyama iṣyate rūpa ādi grahaṇa sādhanāni  asya santi mati sādhanam sarva viṣayam na asti iti ayam niyamaḥ  niranumānaḥ na atra anumānam asti yena niyamam pratipadyāmahe iti rūpa ādibhyaḥ ca viṣaya antaram sukha ādayaḥ tad upalabdhau karaṇa antara sadbhāvaḥ yathā cakṣuṣā gandhaḥ  na gṛhyate iti karaṇa antaram ghrāṇam evam cakṣuḥ ghrāṇābhyām rasaḥ  na gṛhyate iti karaṇa antaram rasanam evam śeṣeṣu api tathā cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ sukhādayaḥ  na gṛhyante iti karaṇa antareṇa bhavitavyam tad ca jñāna ayaugapadya liṅgam yad ca sukha ādi upalabdhau karaṇā tad ca jñāna ayaugapadya liṅgam tasya indriyam indriyam prati saṃnidhera saṃnidheḥ na yugapad  jñānāni utpadyante iti tatra yudaktam ātma pratipatti hetūnām manasi saṃbhavāt  iti tad ayuktam kim punar ayam deha ādi saṃghātāt anyaḥ  nityaḥ uta anityaḥ kutas  saṃśayaḥ ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt  saṃśayaḥ vidyamānam ubhayathā bhavati nityam anityam ca pratipādite ca ātma sadbhāve saṃśaya anivṛtteḥ iti ātma sadbhāva hetubhiḥ eva asya prāc deha bhedāt avasthānam siddham ūrdhvam api deha bhedāt avatiṣṭhate kutas  jātaḥ khalu ayam kumāraḥ  asmin janmani  agṛhīteṣu harṣa bhaya śoka hetuṣu harṣa bhaya śokān pratipadyate liṅga anumeyān te ca smṛti anubandhāt utpadyante na anyathā smṛti anubandhaḥ ca pūrva abhyāsam antareṇa na bhavati pūrva abhyāsaḥ ca pūrva janmani sati na anyathā iti sidhyati etad  avatiṣṭhate ayam ūrdhvam prāk  ca śarīra bhedāt iti yathā padma ādiṣu  anityeṣu prabodhaḥ saṃmīlanam ca vikāraḥ  bhavati evam anityasya ātmanaḥ  harṣa bhaya śoka saṃpratipattiḥ vikāraḥ syāt  hetu abhāvāt ayuktam anena hetunā padma ādiṣu prabodha saṃmīlana vikāravat  anityasya ātmanaḥ  harṣa ādi saṃpratipattiḥ iti na atra udāharaṇa sādharmyāt  sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ na vaidharmyāt asti hetu abhāvāt  asaṃbaddha arthakam apārthakam ucyate iti dṛṣṭāntāt ca harṣa ādi nimittasya anivṛttiḥ yā ca iyam āseviteṣu viṣayeṣu harṣa ādi saṃpratipattiḥ smṛti anubandha kṛtā pratyātmam gṛhyate sā iyam padma ādi saṃmīlana dṛṣṭāntena na nivartate yathā ca iyam na nivartate tathā jāta mātrasya api iti kriyājātaḥ ca parṇa vibhāga saṃyogaḥ prabodha saṃmīlane kriyā hetuḥ ca kriyā anumeyaḥ evam ca sati kim dṛṣṭāntena pratiṣidhyate atha nirnimittaḥ padma ādiṣu prabodha saṃmīlana vikāra iti matam evam ātmanā upi harṣa ādi saṃpratipattiḥ iti tad ca uṣṇa ādiṣu satsu bhāvāt  asat svabhāvāt  tad nimittāḥ pañcabhūta anugraheṇa nirvṛttānām padma ādīnām prabodha saṃmīlana vikārā iti nar nimittāḥ evam harṣāt ayopi vikārā nimittāt  bhavitum arhanti na nimittam antareṇa na ca anyat  pūrva abhyasta smṛti anubandhāt  nimittam asti iti na ca utpatti nirodha kāraṇa anumānam ātmanaḥ adṛṣṭāntāt  na harṣa ādīnām nimittam antareṇa utpattiḥ na uṣṇa ādivat  nimitta antara upādānam harṣa ādīnām dva tasmāt ayuktam etad  itas ca nitya ātmā jāta mātrasya vatsasya pravṛtti liṅgaḥ stanya abhilāṣaḥ  gṛhyate sa ca na antareṇa āhāra abhyāsam kayā yuktyā dṛśyate hi śarīriṇām kṣudhā pīḍyamānānām āhārābhyāṃsa kṛtāt  smaraṇa anubandhāt āhāra abhilāṣaḥ na ca pūrva śarīra abhyāsam antareṇa asau jāta mātrasya upapadyate tena anumīyatebhūta pūrvam śarīram yatra anena āhāraḥ  abhyasya iti sa khalu ayam ātmā pūrva śarīrāt  pretya śarīra antaram āpannaḥ kṣudh pīḍitaḥ pūrva abhyastam āhāram anusmaran stanyam abhilaghati tasmāt na deha bhedāt ātmā bhidyate ubhavati eva ūrdhvam deha bhedāt iti yathā khalu  ayaḥ  abhyāsam antareṇa ayaskā antam upasarpati evam āhāra abhyāsam antareṇa bālaḥ stanyam abhilaṣati kim idam ayasaḥ  ayaskānta abhigamanam nirnimittam artha nimittāt  iti nirnimittam tāvat  yadi nirnimittam loṣṭa ādaya upyayaskāntam upasarpayeyuḥ na jātu niyame kāraṇam asti iti atha nimittāt  tad  kena upalabhyate iti kriyā liṅgaḥ kriyā hetuḥ kriyā niyama liṅgaḥ ca kriyā niyama hetuḥ tena anyatra pravṛtti abhāvaḥ bālasya api niyatam upasarpaṇam kriyā upalabhyate na ca stanya abhilāṣa liṅgam anyat āhāra abhyāsa kṛtāt  smaraṇa anubandhāt nimittam dṛṣṭāntena upapādyate na ca asati nimitte kasya cit utpattiḥ na dṛṣṭāntaḥ  dṛṣṭam abhilāṣa hetum bādhate tasmāt ayasaḥ  askānta abhigamanam adṛṣṭānta iti ayasaḥ khalu api na anyatra pravṛttiḥ bhavati na jātvayaḥ  loṣṭam upasarpati kiṅkṛta usya niyamaḥ iti yadi kāraṇa niyamāt  sa ca kriyā niyama liṅgaḥ evam bālasya api niyata viṣayaḥ  abhilāṣaḥ kāraṇa niyamāt  bhavitum arhati tad ca kāraṇam abhyasta smaraṇam anyet vā iti dṛṣṭena viśiṣyate dṛṣṭaḥ  hi śarīriṇām abhyasta smaraṇāt āhāra abhilāṣa iti itas ca nitya ātmā kasmāt  sa rāgaḥ  jāyate iti arthāt āpadyate ayam jāyamānaḥ  rāga anuviddhaḥ  jāyate rāgasya pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintanam yoniḥ pūrva anubhavaḥ ca viṣayāṇām pūrvasmin janmani śarīram antareṇa na upapadyate soyam ātmā pūrva śarīra anubhūtān viṣayān anusmaran teṣu teṣu rajyate tathā ca ayam dvayoḥ janmanoḥ pratisandhiḥ evam pūrva śarīrasya pūrvatareṇa pūrvatara śarīrasya pūrvatamena ityādi nānādiḥ cetanasya śarīra yogaḥ anādiḥ ca rāga anubandha iti siddham nitya tvam iti katham punar jñāyate pūrva viṣaya anucintana janitaḥ  jātasya rāgaḥ na punar  yathā utpatti dharmakasya dravyasya guṇāḥ kāraṇata utpadyante tathā utpatti dharmakasya ātmanaḥ  rāgaḥ kutaścid utpadyate atra ayamudita anuvādaḥ  nidarśana arthaḥ na khalu sa guṇa dravya utpattivat  utpattiḥ ātmanaḥ  rāgasya ca kasmāt  saṃkalpa nimitta tvāt rāga ādīnām ayam khalu prāṇinām viṣayān āsevamānānām saṃkalpa janitaḥ  rogaḥ  gṛhyate saṃkalpaḥ ca pūrva anubhūta viṣaya anucintana yoniḥ tena anumīyate jātasya api pūrva anubhūta artha cintana kṛtaḥ  rāga iti ātma utpāda adhikaraṇāt tu rāga utpattiḥ bhavantī saṃkalpāt anyasmin rāga kāraṇe sati vācyā kārya dravya guṇavat na ca ātma utpādaḥ siddhaḥ na api saṃkalpāt anyat  rāga kāraṇam asti tasmāt ayuktam asa guṇa dravya utpattivat tayoḥ utpattiḥ iti atha api saṃkalpāt anyat  rāga kāraṇam dharma adharma lakṣaṇam adṛṣṭam upādīyate tathā api pūrva śarīra yogaḥ  apratyākhyeyaḥ tatra hi tasya nirvṛttiḥ na asmin janmani tad maya tvāt rāga iti viṣaya abhyāsaḥ khalu ayam bhāvanā hetuḥ tad maya tvam ucyate iti jāti viśeṣāt ca rāga viśeṣa iti karma khalu idam jāti viśeṣa nirvartakam tādātmyāt  tāt śabdyam vijñāyate tasmāt anupapannam saṃkalpāt anyat  rāga kāraṇam iti anādiḥ cetanasya śarīra yoga iti uktam sva kṛta karma nimittam ca āsyam śarīram sukha duḥkha adhiṣṭhāna tatṛ  parīkṣyate kim ghrāṇa ādivat eka prakṛtikam uta nānā prakṛtikam iti kutas  saṃśayaḥ vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni saṃkhyā vikalpena śarīra prakṛtiḥ iti pratijānata iti kim tatra tattvam tatra mānuṣam śarīram pārthivam kasmāt  guṇa antara upalabdheḥ gandhavatī pṛthivī gandhavat ca śarīram ap ādīnām agandha tvāt  tad prakṛti agandham syāt  na tu idam ap ādibhiḥ asaṃpṛktayā pṛthivī ārabdham ceṣṭa indriya artha āśraya bhāvena kalpate iti atas  pañcānām bhūtānām saṃyoge sati śarīram bhavati bhūta saṃyogaḥ  hi mithas  pañcānām na niṣiddha iti āpya taijasa vāyavyāni loka antare śarīrāṇi teṣu api bhūta saṃyogaḥ pūruṣa artha tantra iti atha ālyādi dravya niṣpattau  api niḥsaṃśayaḥ nāba ādi saṃyogam antareṇa niṣpattiḥ iti apārthiva āpya taijasam tad guṇa ulabdheḥ aniḥśvāsa ucchvāsa upalabdheḥ cāturbhauntikam agandha kleda pāka vyūha avakāśa dānebhyaḥ pāñcabhautikam te ime saṃdigdhā hetava iti upekṣitavān sūtra kāraḥ katham saṃdigdhāḥ sati ca prakṛti bhāve bhūtānām dharma upalabdhiḥ asati ca saṃyoga apratiṣedhāt saṃnihitānām iti yathā sthālyām udaka tejaḥ vāyu ākāśānām iti tad idam aneka bhūta prakṛti sat  śarīram agandham arasam arūpam asparśam ca prakṛti anuvidhānāt syāt  na tu idam ittham bhūtam tasmāt  pārthivam guṇa antara upalabdheḥ sūryam te cakṣuḥ gacchatām iti atra mantre pṛthivīm te śarīram iti śrūyate tad idam prakṛtau vikārasya pralaya abhidhānam iti sūryam te cakṣuḥ spṛṇomi iti atra mantra antare pṛthivīm te śarīram spṛṇomi iti śrūyate sā iyam kāraṇāt  vikārasya spṛttiḥ abhidhīyate iti sthālī ādiṣu ca tulya jātīyānām eka kārya ārambha darśanāt  bhinna jātīyānām eka kārya ārambha anupapattiḥ atha idānīm indriyāṇi prameya krameṇa vicāryante kim āvyaktikāni āhosvit  bhautikāni iti kṛtaḥ saṃśayaḥ kṛṣṇasāram bhautikam tasmin   anupahate rūpa upalabdhiḥ upahate ca anupalabdhiḥ iti vyatiricya kṛṣṇasāram avasthitasya viṣayasya upalambhaḥ  na kṛṣṇasāra prāptasya na ca aprāpya kāri tvam indriyāṇām tad idam abhautika tve vibhu tvāt  saṃbhavati evam ubhaya dharma upalabdheḥ saṃśayaḥ abhautikāni iti āha kasmāt  mahat iti mahattaram mahattamam ca upalabhyate yathā nyagrodha parvata ādi aṇu iti aṇutaram aṇutamam ca gṛhyate yathā nyagrodha dhāna ādi tad ubhayam upalabhyamānam cakṣuṣaḥ  bhautika tvam bādhate bhautikam hi yāvat  tāvat eva vyāpnoti abhautikam tu vibhu tvāt  sarva vyāpakam iti na mahat aṇu grahaṇa mātra āt abhautika tvam vibhu tvam ca indriyāṇām śakyam pratipattam idam khalu tayoḥ mahadaṇvoḥ grahaṇam cakṣūraśmeḥ arthasya ca saṃnikarṣa viśeṣāt  bhavati yathā pradīpa raśmeḥ arthasya ca iti raśmi artha saṃnikarṣaḥ ca āvaraṇa liṅgaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ  hi raśmiḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ āvṛtam artham na prakāśayati yathā pradīpa raśmiḥ iti āvaraṇa anumeya tve sati idam āha rūpa sparśavat hi tejaḥ mahat tvāt aneka dravyavat tvāt  rūpavat tvāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti pradīpavat  pratyakṣata upalabhyeta cākṣuṣaḥ  raśmiḥ yadi syāt iti saṃnikarṣa pratiṣedha arthena āvaraṇena liṅgena anumīyamānasya raśmeḥ yā pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ na asau  abhāvam pratipādayati yathā candramasaḥ para bhāgasya pṛthivyāḥ ca adhas bhāgasya bhinnaḥ khalu ayam dravya dharmaḥ  guṇa dharmaḥ ca mahat aneka dravyavat ca viṣakta avayavam āpyam dravyam pratyakṣataḥ na upalabhyate sparśaḥ tu śītaḥ  gṛhyate tasya dravyasya anubandhāt  hemanta śiśirau kalpete tathāvidham eva ca taijasam dravyam anudbhūta rūpam saha rūpeṇa na upalabhyate sparśaḥ tu  asya uṣṇa upalabhnapayate tasya dravyasya anubandhāt  grīṣma vasantau kalpete yatra tu eṣām bhavati yatra rūpam ca dravyam ca tad āśrayaḥ pratyakṣata upalabhyate rūpa viśeṣaḥ tu yad bhāvāt kvacid rūpa upalabdhiḥ yad abhāvāt ca dravyasya kvacid anupalabdhiḥ sa rūpa dharmoyam udbhava samākhyāta iti anudbhūta rūpaḥ ca ayam na ayanaḥ  raśmiḥ tasmāt  pratyakṣataḥ na upalabhyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca tejasaḥ  dharma bhedaḥ udbhūta rūpa sparśam pratyakṣam tejaḥ  yathā āditya raśmayaḥ udbhūta rūpam anudbhūta sparśam ca pratyakṣam tejaḥ yathā pradīpa raśmayaḥ udbhūta sparśam anudbhūta rūpam apratyakṣam yathā bādi saṃyuktam tejaḥ anudbhūta rūpa sparśaḥ  apratyakṣaḥ cākṣuṣaḥ  raśmiḥ iti yathā cetanasya arthaḥ  viṣaya upalabdhi bhūtaḥ sukha duḥkha upalabdhi bhūtaḥ ca kalpate tathā indriyāṇi vyūḍhāni viṣaya prāpti arthaḥ ca raśmeḥ cākṣuṣasya vyūhaḥ rūpa sparśānabhivyaktiḥ ca vyavahāra prakḷpti arthā dravya viśeṣe ca pratīghātāt āvaraṇa upapattiḥ vyavahāra arthā sarva dravyāṇām viśvarūpaḥ  vyūha indriyavat  karma kāritaḥ puruṣa artha tantraḥ karma tu dharma adharma bhūtam cetanasya upabhoga artham iti yaḥ ca āvaraṇa upalambhāt indriyasya dravya viśeṣe pratighātaḥ sa bhautika dharmaḥ na bhūtāni vyabhicarati nābhautikam pratighāta dharmakam dṛṣṭam iti apratighātaḥ tu vyabhicārī bhautikā bhautikayoḥ samāna tvāt iti yad api manyate pratighātāt  bhautikāni indriyāṇi apratighātāt abhautikāni iti prāptam dṛṣṭaḥ ca apratighātaḥ kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdheḥ tad na yuktam kasmāt  yasmāt  bhautikam api na pratihanyate kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita prakāśāt  pradīpa raśmīnām sthālī ādiṣu pācakasya tejasaḥ  apratighātaḥ upapadyate ca anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa bhedāt  yathā aneka dravyeṇa samavāyāt rūpa viśeṣāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti sati upalabdhi kāraṇe madhyandina ulkā prakāśaḥ  na upalabhyate āditya prakāśena abhibhūtaḥ evam mahat aneka dravyavat tvāt  rūpa viśeṣāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti sati upalabdhi kāraṇe cākṣuṣaḥ  raśmiḥ na upalabhyate nimitta antarataḥ tad ca vyākhyātam anudbhūta rūpa
