sparśasya dravyasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ iti atyanta anupalabdhiḥ ca abhāva kāraṇam yaḥ  hi bravīti loṣṭa prakāśaḥ  madhyandine āditya prakāśa abhibhavāt na upalabhyate iti tasya etaḥ syāt api  anumānataḥ  anupalabdheḥ iti ekam atyanta anupalabdheḥ loṣṭa prakāśaḥ  na asti na tu evam cākṣuṣaḥ  raśmiḥ iti upapanna rūpā ca iyam bāhyena prakāśena anugṛhītam cakṣuḥ viṣaya grāhakam tad abhāve anupalabdhiḥ sati ca prakāśa anugrahe rūpa sparśa upalabdhau ca satyām tad āśrayasya dravyasya cakṣuṣā grahaṇam rūpasya anudbhūta tvāt sā iyam rūpa anabhivyaktitaḥ  rūpa āśrayasya dravyasya anupalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭā tatra yad uktam tad anupalabdheḥ ahetuḥ iti etad ayuktam kasmāt  punar abhibhavaḥ  anupalabdhi kāraṇam cākṣuṣasya raśmeḥ na ucyate iti bāhya prakāśa anugraha nirapekṣatāyām ca iti ca arthaḥ yad  rūpam abhivyaktam udbhūtam bāhya prakāśa anugraham ca na apekṣate tad viṣayaḥ  abhibhavaḥ viparyaye abhibhava abhāvāt  anudbhūta rūpa tvāt ca anupalabhyamānam bāhya prakāśa anugrahāt ca upalabhyamānam na abhibhūyate iti evam upapannam asti cākṣuṣaḥ  raśmiḥ iti dṛśyate hi naktam nayana raśmayaḥ  naktañcarāṇām vṛṣadaṃśa prabhṛtīnām tena śeṣasya anumānam iti jāti bhedavat indriya bheda iti ced  dharma bheda mātram ca anupapannam āvaraṇasya prāpti pratiṣedha arthasya darśanāt iti indriya artha saṃnikarṣasya jñāna kāraṇatva anupapattiḥ kasmāt  tṛṇa ādi sarpad dravyam kāce abhra paṭale vā pratihatam dṛṣṭam avyavahitena saṃnikṛṣyate vyāhanyate vai prāptiḥ vyavadhānena iti yadi ca raśmi artha saṃnikarṣaḥ  grahaṇa hetuḥ syāt  na vyavahitasya saṃnikarṣa iti  agrahaṇam syāt  asti ca iyam kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdhaḥ sā jñāpiyati aprāpya kārīṇi indriyāṇi iti ata eva abhautikāni prāpya kāri tvam hi bhautika dharma iti na aprāpya kāri tve sati indriyaṇām kuḍya antaritasya anupalabdhiḥ  na syāt  prāpya kāri tve api tu kāca abhra paṭala sphaṭika antarita upalabdhiḥ na syāt  na ca kācaḥ  abhra paṭalam vā na ayana raśmim viṣṭabhnāti saḥ  apratihanyamānaḥ saṃnikṛṣyate iti yaḥ ca manyate na bhaitikasya apratighāta iti tad na aāditya raśmeḥ avighātāt asphaṭika antaritepi vighātāt adāhye avighātāt avighātāt iti ca pada abhisaṃbandhāt  vākya bheda iti yathā vākyam ca artha bheda iti āditya raśmiḥ kumbha ādiṣu na pratihanyate avighātāt  kumbha stham udakam tapati prāptau hi dravya antara guṇasya uṣṇasya sparśasya grahaṇam tena ca śīta sparśa abhibhava iti sphaṭika antaritepi prakāśanīye pradīpa raśmīnām apratighātaḥ apratighātāt  prāptasya grahaṇam iti bharjana kapāla ādi stham ca dravyam āgneyena tejasā dahyate tatra avighātāt prāptiḥ prāptau tu dāhaḥ na aprāpya kāri teja iti avighātāt  iti ca kevalam padam upādīyate koyam avighātaḥ  nāma avyūhyamāna avayavena vyavadhāyakena dravyeṇa sarvatas  dravyasya aviṣṛmbhaḥ kriyā hetoḥ apratibandhaḥ prāpteḥ apratiṣedha iti dṛṣṭam hi kalaśa niṣaktānām apām bahis  śīta sparśa grahaṇam na ca indri nayeṇa asaṃnikṛṣṭasya dravyasya sparśa upalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭau ca praspanda parisravau tatra kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ na ayana raśmeḥ pratighātāt  vibhidya arthena saha saṃnikarṣāt upapannam grahaṇam iti kāca abhra paṭala ādivat vā kuḍya ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ kuḍya ādivat vā kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ pratīghāta iti prasajyate niyame kāraṇam vācyam iti ādarśa udakayoḥ prasādaḥ rūpa viśeṣaḥ svar  dharmaḥ niyama darśanāt  prasādasya vā svar  dharmaḥ  rūpa upalambhanam yathā ādarśa pratihatasya parāvṛttasya nayana raśmeḥ svena mukhena saṃnikarṣe sati sva mukha upalambhanam pratibimba grahaṇa ākhyam ādarśa rūpa anugrahāt tad nimittam bhavati ādarśa rūpa upaghāte tad abhāvāt kuḍya ādiṣu ca pratibimba grahaṇam na bhavati evam kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ avighātaḥ cakṣūraśmeḥ kuḍya ādibhiḥ ca pratighātaḥ dravya svabhāva niyamāt iti pramāṇasya tattva viṣaya tvāt na khalu bhoḥ parīkṣamāṇena dṛṣṭa anumitā arthāḥ śakyā niyoktum aevam bhavata iti na api pratiṣeddhum aevam na bhavata iti na hi idam upapadyate arūpavat  gandhopi cākṣuṣaḥ  bhavatu iti agandhavat vā rūpam cākṣuṣam mā bhūta iti aagni pratipattivat  dhūmena udaka pratipattiḥ api bhavatu iti audaka apratipattivat vā dhūmena agni pratipattiḥ api mā bhūt iti kim kāraṇam yathā khalu arthā bhavanti ya eṣām svar  bhāvaḥ svar  dharma iti tathābhūtāḥ pramāṇena pratipadyante iti tathābhūta viṣayakam hi pramāṇathmati imau khalu niyoga pratiṣedhau bhavatā deśitau kāca abhra paṭala ādivat vā kuḍya ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ  bhavatu kuḍya ādivat vā kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ apratighātaḥ  mā bhūt  iti na dṛṣṭa anumitāḥ khalu ime dravya dharmāḥ pratighāta apratighātayoḥ hi upalabdhi anupalabdhī vyavasthāpike vyavahita anupalabdhyā anumīyate kuḍya ādibhiḥ pratighātaḥ vyavahita upalabdhyā anumīyate kāca abhra paṭala ādibhiḥ apratighāta iti atha api khalu ekam indriyam bahūni indriyāṇi vā kutas  saṃśayaḥ bahūni dravyāṇi nānā sthānāni dṛśyante nānā sthānaḥ ca san  ekaḥ  avayavī ca iti tena indriyeṣu bhinna sthāneṣu saṃśaya iti ekam indriyam atvac ekam indriyam iti āha kasmāt  avyatirekāt  na tvacā kiñcid indriya adhiṣṭhānam na prāptam na ca asatyām tvaci kiñcid viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati yayā sarva indriya sthānāni vyāptāni yasyām ca satyām viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati sā tvac ekam indriyam iti na indriya antara artha anupalabdheḥ sparśa upalabdhi lakṣaṇāyām satyām tvaci gṛhyamāṇe ca tvac indriyeṇe sparśe indriya antara arthā rūpādayaḥ  na gṛhyante andha ādibhiḥ na sparśa grāhakāt indriyāt  indriya antaram asti iti sparśavat  andhādibhiḥ gṛhyeran rūpa ādayaḥ na ca gṛhyante tasmāt na ekam indriyam tvak iti tvac avayava viśeṣeṇa dhūma upalabdhivat tad upalabdhiḥ yathā tvacaḥ  avayava viśeṣaḥ kaścid  cakṣuṣi saṃnikṛṣṭaḥ  dhūma sparśam gṛhṇāti na anya evam tvacaḥ  avayava viśeṣā rūpa ādi grāhakāḥ teṣām upaghātāt andhādibhiḥ na gṛhyante rūpa ādaya iti vyāhata tvāt ahetuḥ atvac avyatirekāt ekam indriyam iti uktvā atva gakyava viśeṣeṇa dhūma upalabdhivat  rūpa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti ucyate evam ca sati nānā bhūtāni viṣaya grāhakāṇi viṣaya vyavasthānāt  tad bhāve viṣaya grahaṇasya bhāvāt  tad upaghāte ca abhāvāt  tathā ca pūrvaḥ vāda uttareṇa vādena vyāhanyate iti saṃdigdhaḥ ca avyatirekaḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ api bhūtaiḥ indriya adhiṣṭhānāni vyāptāni na ca teṣu asatsu viṣaya grahaṇam bhavati iti tasmāt na tvac  anyat vā sarva viṣayam ekam indriyam iti ātmā manasā saṃbadhyate mana indriyeṇa indriyam sarva arthaiḥ saṃnikṛṣṭam iti ātma indriya manaḥ  artha saṃnikarṣebhyaḥ  yugapad  grahaṇāni syuḥ na ca yugapad  rūpādayaḥ  gṛhyante tasmāt na ekam indriyam sarva viṣayam asti iti asāhacaryāt ca viṣaya grahaṇānām na ekam indriyam sarva viṣayakam sāhacarye hi viṣaya grahaṇānām andha ādi anupapattiḥ iti na khalu tvac ekam indriyam vyāghātāt  tvacā rūpāṇi  aprāptāni gṛhyante iti aprāpya kāri tve sparśa ādiṣu api evam prasaṅgaḥ sparśa ādīnām ca prāptānām grahaṇāt  rūpa ādīnām api prāptānām grahaṇam iti prāptam prāpya aprāpya kāri tvam iticet āvaraṇa anupapatteḥ viṣaya mātrasya grahaṇam atha api manyeta prāptāḥ sparśa ādayaḥ tvacā gṛhyante rūpāṇi tu  aprāptāni iti evam sati na asti āvaraṇam āvaraṇa anupapatteḥ ca rūpa mātrasya grahaṇam vyavahitasya ca avyahitasya ca iti dūra antika anuvidhānam ca rūpa upalabdhi anupalabdhyoḥ na syāt  aprāptam tvacā gṛhyate rūpam iti dūre rūpasya agrahaṇam antike ca grahaṇam iti etad  na syāt iti ekatva pratiṣedhāt ca nānātva siddhau sthāna ahetuḥ api upādīyate arthaḥ prayojanam tad  pañcavidham indriyāṇām usparśanena indriyeṇa sparśa grahaṇe sati na tena eva rūpam gṛhyate iti rūpa grahaṇa prayojanam cakṣuḥ anumīyate sparśa rūpa grahaṇe ca tābhyām eva na gandhaḥ  gṛhyate iti gandha grahaṇa prayojanam ghrāṇam anumīyate trayāṇām grahaṇe na taiḥ eva rasaḥ  gṛhyate iti rasa grahaṇa prayojanam rasanam anumīyate na caturṇām grahaṇe taiḥ eva śabdaḥ śrūyate iti śabda grahaṇa prayojanam śrotram anumīyate evam indriya prayojanasya anitaretara sādhana sādhya tvāt  pañca eva indriyāṇi na khalu aindriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti sidhyati kasmāt  teṣām arthānām bahu tvāt  bahavaḥ khalu ime indriya arthāḥ sparśāḥ tāvat  śīta uṣṇa anuṣṇāśītā iti rūpāṇi śukla harita ādīni gandhā iṣṭa aniṣṭa upekṣaṇīyāḥ rasāḥ kaṭuka ādayaḥ śabdā varṇa ātmanaḥ  dhvani mātrāḥ ca bhinnāḥ tad  yasya indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi tasya indriya artha bahu tvāt  bahūni indriyāṇi prasajyante iti gandhatva ādibhiḥ sva samānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthānām gandha ādīnām yāni gandha ādi grahaṇāni tāni  asamāna sādhana sādhya tvāt  grāhaka antarāṇi na prayojayanti artha samūhaḥ  anumāna muktaḥ  na artha eka deśaḥ artha eka deśam ca āśritya viṣaya pañcatva mātram bhavān pratiṣedhati tasmāt ayuktoyam pratiṣedha iti katham punar gandhatva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthā gandha ādayaḥ iti sparśaḥ khalu ayam trividhaḥ śīta uṣṇaḥ  anuṣṇa aśītaḥ ca sparśa tvena sva sāmānyena saṃgṛhītaḥ gṛhyamāṇe ca śīta sparśe na uṣṇasya anuṣṇa aśītasya vā sparśasya grahaṇam grāhaka antaram prayojayati sparśa bhedānām eka sādhana sādhya tvāt  uyena eva śīta sparśaḥ  gṛhyate tena eva itarau  api iti evam gandha tvena gandhānām rūpa tvena rūpāṇām rasa tvena rasānām śabda tvena śabdānām iti gandha ādi grahaṇāni punar asamāna sādhana sādhyatva anna grāhaka antarāṇām prayojakāni tasmāt upapannam indriya artha pañcatvāt pañca indriyāṇi iti yadi sāmānyam saṃgrāhakam prāptam indriyāṇām viṣaya tvena hi sāmānyena gandha ādayaḥ saṃgṛhītā iti na khalu viṣaya tvena sāmānyena kṛta vyavasthā viṣayā grāhaka antara nirapekṣāḥ eka sādhana grāhya anumīyante anumīyante ca pañca gandhādayaḥ  gandhatva ādibhiḥ sva sāmānyaiḥ kṛta vyavasthāḥ indriya antara grāhyaḥ tasmāt asaṃbaddham etad  ayam eva ca arthaḥ  anūdyate abuddhi lakṣaṇa pañcatvāt iti buddhaya eva lakṣaṇāni viṣaya grahaṇa liṅga tvāt indriyāṇām tad etad indriya artha pañcatvāt iti etasmin sūtre kṛta bhāṣyam iti tasmāt  buddhi lakṣaṇa pañcatvāt  pañca indriyāṇi adhiṣṭhānāni api khalu pañca indriyāṇām sarva śarīra adhiṣṭhānam sparśanam sparśa grahaṇa liṅgam kṛṣṇa tārā adhiṣṭhānam cakṣuḥ bahis nismṛtam rūpa grahaṇa liṅgam nāsā adhiṣṭhānam ghrāṇam jihādhiṣṭhānam rasanam karṇa  chidra adhiṣṭhānam śrotram gandha rasa rūpa sparśa śabda grahaṇa liṅga tvāt iti gati medāt api indriya bhedaḥ kṛṣṇasāra upanibaddham cakṣuḥ bahis niḥsṛtya rūpa adhikaraṇāni dravyāṇi prāpnoti sparśana ādīni tu indriyāṇi viṣayā eva āśraya upasarpaṇāt pratyāsīdanti santāna vṛttyā śabdasya śrotra prattyāsattiḥ iti ākṛti khalu parimāṇam iyattā sā pañcadhā sva sthāna mātrāṇi ghrāṇa rasana sparśanāni viṣaya avyāpinā anumeyāni cakṣuḥ kṛṣṇasāra āśrayam bahis niḥsṛtam viṣaya vyāpi śrotram na anyat ākāśāt  tad ca vibhu śabda mātra anubhava anumeyam puruṣa saṃskāra upagrahāt ca adhiṣṭhāna niyamena śabdasya vyañjakam iti jātiḥ iti yonim pracakṣate pañca khalu indri naya yonayaḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni tasmāt  prakṛti pañcatvāt api pañca indriyāṇāti siddham katham punar jñāyate bhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi na avyakta prakṛtīni iti dṛṣṭaḥ  hi vāyu ādīnām bhūtānām guṇa viśeṣa abhivyakti niyamaḥ uvāyuḥ sparśa vyañjakaḥ āpaḥ  rasa vyañjikāḥ tejaḥ  rūpa vyañjakam pārthivam kiñcid  dravyam kasyacid  dravyasya grandha vyañjakam adva asti ca ayam indriyāṇām bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdhi niyamaḥ tena bhūta guṇa viśeṣa upalabdheḥ manyā mahebhūta prakṛtīni indriyāṇi na avyakta prakṛtīn iti atha artha vivecanam gandha ādayaḥ pṛthivī ādi guṇā iti uddiṣṭam uddeśaḥ ca pṛthivī ādīnām eka guṇa tve ca aneka guṇa tve samāna  iti ata āha sparśa paryantānām iti vibhakti vipariṇāmaḥ ākāśasya uttaraḥ uśabdaḥ sparśa paryantebhya iti katham tarhi tarapnirdeśaḥ svatantra viniyoga sāmarthyāt  tena uttara śabdasya para artha abhidhānam vijñāyate uddeśa sūtre hi sparśapayantebhyaḥ paraḥ śabda iti tantram vā sparśasya vivakṣita tvāt  sparśa paryanteṣu niyukteṣu yaḥ  anyaḥ tad uttaraḥ śabda iti na ayam guṇa niyogaḥ sādhuḥ kasmāt  yasya bhūtasya ye guṇā na te tad ātmakena indriyeṇa sarve upalabhyante pārthivena hi ghrāṇena sparśa paryantā na gṛhyante gandha eva ekaḥ  gṛhyate evam śeṣeṣu api iti katham tarhi ime guṇā viniyoktavyāḥ iti gandha ādīnām ekaikaḥ  yathākramam pṛthivī ādīnām ekaikasya guṇaḥ atas tad anupalabdhiḥ teṣām tayoḥ tasya ca anupalabdhiḥ ghrāṇena rasa rūpa sparśānām rasanena rūpa sparśayoḥ cakṣukṣā sparśasya iti katham tarhi aneka guṇāni bhūtāni gṛhyante iti ap ādi saṃsargāt ca pṛthivyām rasādayaḥ  gṛhyante evam śeṣeṣu api iti niyamaḥ tarhi na prāpnoti saṃsargasya aniyamāt  acaturguṇā pṛthivī atriguṇā āpaḥ adviguṇam tejaḥ aeka guṇa u vāyuḥ iti niyamaḥ ca upapadyate katham pṛthivī ādīnām pūrva pūrvam uttareṇa uttareṇa viṣṭam atas  na saṃsarga aniyama iti tad ca etad  bhūta sṛṣṭau veditavyam na etarhi iti na iti tri sūtrīm pratyācaṣṭe kasmāt  pārthivasya dravyasya api  asya ca pratyakṣa tvāt  mahattva aneka dravya tvāt rūpāt ca upalabdhiḥ iti taijasam eva dravyam pratyakṣam syāt  na pārthivam āpyam vā rūpa abhāvāt taijasavat tu pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  na saṃsargāt aneka guṇa grahaṇam bhūtānām iti bhūta antara rūpa kṛtam ca pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvam bruvataḥ pratyakṣaḥ  vāyuḥ prasajyate niyame vā kāraṇam ucyatām iti rasayoḥ vā pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  pārthivaḥ  rasaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ āpyaḥ  madhura eva na ca etad  saṃsargāt  bhavitum arhati rūpayoḥ vā pārthiva āpyayoḥ prata yakṣa tvāt  taijasa rūpa anugṛhītayoḥ saṃsarge hi vyañjakam eva rūpam na vyaṅgyam asti iti eka anekavidha tve ca pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  rūpayoḥ pārthivam harita lohita pīta ādi anekavidham rūpam āpyam tu śuklam aprakāśakam na ca etad eka guṇānām saṃsarge sati upalabhyate iti udāharaṇa mātram ca etad  atas  param prapañcaḥ sparśayoḥ vā pārthiva taijasayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  pārthivaḥ  anuṣṇa aśītaḥ sparśaḥ uṣṇaḥ taijasaḥ pratnayakṣaḥ na ca etad eka guṇānām anuṣṇa aśīta sparśena vāyunā saṃsargeṇa upapadyate iti atha vā pārthiva āpyayoḥ dravyayoḥ vyavasthita guṇayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  caturguṇam pārthivam dravyam triguṇam āpyam pratyakṣam tena tad kāraṇam anumīyate tathābhūtam iti tasya kāryam liṅm kāraṇa bhāvāt hi kārya bhāva iti evam taijasa vāyavyayoḥ davyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  guṇa vyavasthāyāḥ tad kāraṇe dravye vyavasthā anumānam iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca vivekaḥ pārthiva āpyayoḥ pratyakṣa tvāt  pārthivam dravyam abādibhiḥ viyuktam pratyakṣataḥ gṛhyate āpyam ca parābhyām taijasam ca vāyunā na ca ekaika guṇam gṛhyate iti niranumānam tu viṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa iti etad iti na atra liṅgam anumāpakam gṛhyate iti yena etad evam pratipadyemahi yad ca uktam aviṣṭam hi aparam pareṇa iti bhūta sṛṣṭau veditavyam na sāṃpratam iti niyama kāraṇa abhāvāt ayuktam dṛṣṭam ca sāṃpratam aaparam pareṇa viṣṭam iti vāyunā ca viṣṭam teja iti viṣṭa tvam saṃyogaḥ sa ca dvayoḥ samānaḥ vāyunā ca viṣṭa tvāt  sparśavat  tejaḥ na tu tejasā viṣṭa tvāt  rūpavān vāyuḥ iti niyama kāraṇam na asti iti dṛṣṭam ca taijasena sparśena vāyavyasya sparśasya abhibhavāt agrahaṇam iti na ca tena eva tasya abhibhava iti tad evam nyāya averuddham pravādam pratiṣidhya na sarva guṇa anupalabdheḥ iti coditam samādhīyate tasmāt na sarva guṇa upalabdhiḥ ghrāṇa ādīnām pūrvam pūrvam gandha ādeḥ guṇasya utkarṣāt tad tad pradhānam kā pradhāna tā viṣaya grāhaka tvam kaḥ  guṇa utkarṣaḥ abhivyaktau samartha tvam yathā bāhyānām pārthiva āpya taijasānām dravyāṇām caturguṇa triguṇa dviguṇānām na sarva guṇa vyañjaka tvam gandha rasa rūpa utkarṣāt tu yathākramam gandha rasa rūpa vyañjaka tvam evam ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuṣām caturguṇa triguṇa dviguṇānām na sarva guṇa grāhaka tvam gandha rasa rūpa utkarṣāt tu yathākramam gandha rasa rūpa grāhaka tvam tasmāt  ghrāṇa ādībhiḥ na sarveṣām guṇānām upalabdhiḥ iti yaḥ tu pratijānīte gandha guṇa tvāt  ghrāṇam gandhasya grāhakam evam rasanā ādiṣu api iti tasya yathā guṇa yogam ghrāṇa ādibhiḥ guṇa grahaṇam prasajyate iti kiṅkṛtam punar vyavasthānam kiñcid  pārthivam indriyam na sarvāṇi kānicid  āpya taijasa vāyavyāni indriyāṇi na sarvāṇi iti artha nirvṛtti samarthasya pravibhaktasya dravyasya saṃsargaḥ puruṣa saṃskāra kāritaḥ  bhūyas tvam dṛṣṭaḥ  hi prakarṣe bhūyastva śabdaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ  yathā viṣayaḥ abhūyān iti ucyate yathā pṛthak artha kriyā samarthāni puruṣa saṃskāra vaśāt  viṣa oṣadhi maṇi prabhṛtīni dravyāṇi nirvartyante na sarvam sarva artham evam pṛthak viṣaya grahaṇa samarthāni ghrāṇa ādīni nirvartyante na sarva viṣaya grahaṇa samarthāni iti sva guṇān na upalabhante indriyāṇi kasmāt iticed  svān gandha ādīn na upalabhante ghrāṇa ādīni kena kāraṇena iticed  sva guṇaiḥ saha ghrāṇa ādīnām indriya bhāvāt ghrāṇam svena gandhena samāna artha kāriṇā saha bāhyam gandham gṛhṇāti tasya sva gandha grahaṇam saha kāri vaikalyāt na bhavati evam śeṣāṇām api yadi punar gandhaḥ sahakārī ca syāt  ghrāṇasya grāhyaḥ ca syāt eva iti ata āha na guṇa upalabdhiḥ indriyāṇām yaḥ  brūte yathā bāhyam dravyam cakṣuṣām gṛhyate tathā tena eva cakṣuṣā tad eva cakṣuḥ gṛhyatām iti tādṛś idam tulyaḥ  hi ubhayatra pratipatti hetu abhāva iti asvaguṇān na upalabhante indriyāṇi iti etad na bhavati upalabhyate hi sva guṇaḥ śabdaḥ śrotreṇa iti na śabdena guṇena sa guṇam ākāśam indriyam bhavati na śabdaḥ śabdasya vyañjakaḥ na ca ghrāṇa ādīnām sva guṇa grahaṇam pratyakṣam na api anumīyate anumīyate tu śrotreṇa ākāśena śabdasya grahaṇam śabda guṇa tvam ca ākāśasya iti pariśeṣaḥ ca anumānam veditavyam ātmā tāvat  śrotā na karaṇam manasaḥ śrotra tve badhiratva abhāvaḥ pṛthivī ādīnām ghrāṇa ādi bhāve sāmarthyam śrotra bhāve ca asāmarthyam asti ca idam śrotram ākāśam ca śiṣyate pariśeṣāt ākāśam śrotram iti iti vātsyāyana viracite nyāya bhāṣye tṛtīya adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam #################################################################### atha nyāya bhāṣya tṛtīya adhyāyasya dvitīyam āhnikam parīkṣitāni indriyāṇi arthāḥ ca buddheḥ idānīm parīkṣā kramaḥ sā kim anityā nityā vā iti kutas  saṃśayaḥ asparśavat tvam tābhyām samānaḥ  dharma upalabhyate buddhau viśeṣaḥ ca upajana apāya dharmavat tvam viparyayaḥ ca yathāsvam anitya nityayoḥ tasyām buddhau na upalabhyate tena saṃśaya iti anupapannaḥ khalu ayam saṃśayaḥ sarva śarīriṇām hi pratyātma vedanīyā anityā buddhiḥ sukha ādivat  bhavati ca saṃvittiḥ ajñāsyāmi ajānāmi aajñāsiṣam iti na ca upajana apāyau  antareṇa traikālya vyaktiḥ tatas ca traikālya vyakteḥ aanityā buddhiḥ iti etad  siddham pramāṇa siddham ca idam śāstrepi uktam indriya artha saṃnikarṣa utpannam yugapad  jñāna anutpattiḥ manasaḥ  liṅgam iti evamādi tasmāt saṃśaya prakriyā anupapattiḥ iti dṛṣṭi pravāda upālambha artham tu prakaraṇam evam hi paśyantaḥ pravadanti sāṃkhyāḥ apuruṣasya antaḥkaraṇa bhūtā nityā buddhiḥ iti sādhanam ca pracakṣate kim punar idam pratyabhijñānam apūrvam ajñāsiṣam artham tam imam jānāmi iti jñānayoḥ samāne arthe pratisandhi jñānam pratyabhijñānam etad ca avasthitāyāḥ  buddheḥ upapannam nānātve tu buddhi bhedeṣu utpanna apavargiṣu pratyabhijñāna anupapattiḥ na anya jñātam anyaḥ pratyabhijānāti iti yathā khalu nitya tvam buddheḥ sādhyam evam pratyabhijñānam api iti kim kāraṇam cetana dharmasya karaṇe anupapattiḥ puruṣa dharmaḥ khalu ayam jñānam darśanam upalabdhiḥ bodhaḥ pratyayaḥ adhyavasāya iti cetanaḥ hi pūrva jñātam artham pratyabhijānāti tasya etasmāt  hetoḥ nitya tvam yuktam iti karaṇa caitanya abhyupagame tu cetana svarūpam vacanīyam na anirdiṣṭa svarūpam ātma antaram śakyam asti iti pratipattum jñānam ced  buddheḥ antaḥkaraṇasya abhyupagamyate cetanasya idānīm kim svarūpam kaḥ  dharmaḥ kim tattvam jñānena ca buddhau vartamānena ayam cetanaḥ kim karori iti cetayate iti ced  na jñānāt artha antara vacanam puruṣaḥ cetayate buddhiḥ jānāti iti na idam jñānāt artha antaram ucyate yetayate jānīte paśyati upalabhate iti ekoyam artha iti buddhiḥ jñāpayati iti ced  addhā jānīte puruṣaḥ  buddhiḥ jñāpayati iti satyam etad  evam ca abhyupagame ajñānam puruṣasya iti siddham bhavati na buddheḥ antaḥkaraṇasya iti prati puruṣam ca śabda antara vyavasthā pratijñāne pratiṣedha hetu vacanam yaḥ ca pratijānīte kaścid  puruṣaḥ cetayate kaścid  budhyate kaścid upalabhate kaścid  paśyati iti puruṣānatarāṇi khalu imāni cetanaḥ boddhā upalabdhā draṣṭā iti na ekasya iti dharmā iti atra kaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ iti arthasya abheda iti ced  samānam abhinna arthā ete śabdā iti tatra vyavasthā anupapattiḥ iti evam ced  manyase samānam bhavati puruṣaḥ cetayate buddhiḥ jānīte iti atatra api arthaḥ  na bhidyate tatra ubhayoḥ cetana tvāt anyatarala upa iti yadi punar budhyate anayā iti bodhanam buddhiḥ mana eva ucyate tad ca nityam astu etad evam na tu manasaḥ  viṣaya pratyabhijñānāt  nitya tvam dṛṣṭam hi karaṇa bhede jñātuḥ eka tvāt  pratyabhijñānam savya dṛṣṭasya itareṇa pratyabhijñānāt iti cakṣuḥvat  pradīpavat ca pradīpa antara dṛṣṭasya pradīpa antareṇa pratyabhijñānam iti tasmāt  jñātuḥ ayam nitya tve hetuḥ iti yad ca manyate buddheḥ  avasthitāyā yathā viṣayam vṛttayaḥ jñānāni niścaranti vṛttiḥ ca vṛttimataḥ  na anyā iti tad ca vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ ananya tve vṛttimataḥ  avasthānāt  vṛttīnām avasthānam iti yāni imāni viṣaya grahaṇāni tāni avatiṣṭhante iti yugapad  viṣayāṇām grahaṇam prasajyate iti atīte ca pratyabhijñāne vṛttimān api atīta iti antaḥkaraṇasya vināśaḥ prasajyate viparyaye na nānātvam iti avibhu caikram manaḥ paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyujyate iti indriya arthānām vṛtti vṛttimatoḥ nānātvam iti ekatve ca prādurbhāva tirobhāvayoḥ abhāva iti apratyabhijñānam anupalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca kasya cit arthasya viṣaya antara vyāsakte manasi upapadyate vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ nānātvāt  ekatve hi anartha kaḥ vyāsaṅga iti vibhu tve ca antaḥkaraṇasya paryāyeṇa indriyaiḥ saṃyogaḥ prāptāni indriyāṇi antaḥkaraṇena iti prāpti arthasya gamanasya abhāvaḥ tatra krama vṛttitva abhāvāt ayugapad grahaṇa anupapattiḥ iti gati abhāvāt ca pratiṣiddham vibhunaḥ  antaḥkaraṇasya ayugapad grahaṇam na liṅga antareṇa anumīyate iti yathā cakṣuṣaḥ  gatiḥ pratiṣiddhā saṃnikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ tulya kāla grahaṇāt pāṇi candramasoḥ vyavadhānena pratīghāte sā anumīyate iti saḥ  ayam na antaḥkaraṇe vivādaḥ  na ca tasya nitya tve siddham hi manaḥ  antaḥkaraṇam nityam ca iti kva tarhi vivādaḥ tasya vibhu tve tad ca pramāṇataḥ  anupalabdhaḥ pratiṣiddham iti ekam ca antaḥkaraṇam nānā ca etāḥ  jñāna ātmikā vṛttayaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānam ghrāṇa vijñānam rūpa vijñānam gandha vijñānam etad ca vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ eka tve anupapannam iti puruṣaḥ  jānīte na antaḥkaraṇam iti etena viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ viṣaya antara grahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ  viṣaya antara vyāsaṅgaḥ puruṣasya na antaḥkaraṇasya iti kena cit indriyeṇa saṃnidhiḥ kena cit  asaṃnidhiḥ iti ayam tu vyāsaṅgaḥ  anujñāyate manasa iti ekam antaḥkaraṇam nānā vṛttaya iti satyabhede vṛtteḥ idam ucyate tasyām vṛttau nānātva abhimānām yathā dravya antara upahite sphaṭike anyatva abhimānaḥ  anīlaḥ alohitaḥ iti evam viṣaya antara upadhānāt iti na hetu abhāvāt  sphaṭika anyatva abhimānavat ayam jñāneṣu nānātva abhimānaḥ  gauṇaḥ na punar gandha ādi anyatva abhimānavat iti hetuḥ na asti hetu abhāvāt anupapanna iti samānaḥ  hetu abhāvaḥ iti ced  na jñānānām krameṇa upajana apāya darśanātu krameṇa hi indriyārtheṣu jñānāni upajāyante cāpayanti ca iti dṛśyate tasmāt  gandha ādi anyatva abhimānavat ayam jñāneṣu nānātva abhimāna iti sphaṭika anyatva abhimānavat iti etad amṛṣyamāṇaḥ kṣaṇika va ādi āha asphaṭikasya abhedena avasthitasya upadhāna bhedāt nānātva abhimānaḥ iti ayam avidyamāna hetukaḥ pakṣaḥ kasmāt  sphaṭikepya para apara utpatteḥ usphaṭike api  anyā vyaktaya utpadyante anyā nirudhyante iti katham kṣaṇika tvāt  vyaktīnām kṣaṇaḥ ca alpīyān kālaḥ kṣaṇa sthitikāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ katham punar gamyate kṣaṇikā vyaktayaḥ iti upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanāt śarīra ādiṣu upakti nirvṛttasya āhāra rasasya śarīre rudhira ādi bhāvena upacayaḥ  apacayaḥ ca prabandhena pravartate upacayāt  vyaktīnām utpādaḥ apacayāt  vyakti nirodhaḥ evam ca sati vayava pariṇāma bhedena vṛddhiḥ śarīrasya kāla antare gṛhyate iti soyam vyakti viśeṣa dharmaḥ  vyakti mātre veditavya iti sarvāsam vyaktiṣu upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ śarīravat iti na ayam niyamaḥ kasmāt  hetu abhāvāt  na atra pratyakṣam anumānam vā pratipādakam asti iti tasmāt  yathādarśanam abhyanujñā yatra yatra upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ  dṛśyate tatra tatra vyaktīnām apara apara utpattiḥ upacaya apacaya prabandha darśanena abhyanujñāyate yathā śarīra ādiṣu yatra yatra na dṛśyate tatra tatra pratyākhyāyate yathā grāva prabhṛtiṣu sphaṭikepi upacaya apacaya prabandhaḥ  na dṛśyate tasmāt ayuktam asphaṭike api  apara apara utpattiḥ iti yathā ca arkasya kaṭukimnā sarva dravyāṇām kaṭu ki mānam āpadayet  tādṛś etad iti yaḥ ca aśeṣa nirodhena apūrva utpādam niranvayam dravya saṃtāne kṣaṇikatām manyate tasya etad utpatti kāraṇam tāvat upalabhyate avayava upacayaḥ  valmīka ādīnām vināśa kāraṇam ca upalabhyate ghaṭa ādīnām avayava vibhāgaḥ yasya tu  anapacita avayavam nirudhyate anupacita avayavam ca utpadyate tasya aśeṣa nirodhe niranvaye vāpūrva utpāde na kāraṇam ubhayatra api upalabhyate iti yathā anupalabhyamānam kṣīra vināśa kāraṇam dadhi utpatti kāraṇam ca abhyanujñāyate tathā sphaṭike parāparāsu vyaktiṣu vināśa kāraṇam utpatti kāraṇam ca abhyanujñeyam iti kṣīra vināśa liṅgam kṣīra vināśa kāraṇam dadhyutapatti liṅgam dadhi utpatti kāraṇam ca gṛhyate atas  na anupalabdhiḥ viparyayaḥ tu sphaṭika ādiṣu dravyeṣu apara apara utpattīnām na liṅgam asti iti anuvṛttiḥ eva iti atra kaścid  parihāram āha apayasaḥ parimāṇaḥ  na vināśaḥ iti eka āha pariṇāmaḥ ca avasthitasya dravyasya pūrva dharma nivṛttau dharma antara utpattiḥ iti aguṇa antara prādurbhāvaḥ iti apara āha sataḥ  dravyasya pūrva guṇa nivṛttau guṇa antaram utpadyate iti sa khalu eka pakṣībhāva iva atra tu pratidheṣaḥ saṃmūrchana lakṣaṇāt avayava vyūhāt  dravya antare dadhni utpanne gṛhyamāṇe pūrvam payaḥ dravyam avayava vibhāgebhyaḥ  nivṛttam iti anumīyate yathā mṛd avayavānām vyūha antarāt  dravya antare sthālyām utpannāyām pūrvam mṛd piṇḍa dravyam mṛdavayava vibhāgebhyaḥ  nivartate iti mṛdvat ca avayava anvayaḥ payaḥ dadhnoḥ na aśeṣa nirodhe niranvayaḥ  dravya antara utpādaḥ  ghaṭate iti abhyanujñāya na niṣkāraṇam kṣīra vināśam dadhi utpādam ca pratiṣedha ucyate iti kṣīra dadhivat niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika vyaktīnām iti na ayam ekānta iti kasmāt  hetu abhāvāt  na atra hetuḥ asti akāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām kṣīra dadhivat  na punar yathā vināśa kāraṇa bhāvāt  kumbhasya vināśa utpatti kāraṇa bhāvāt ca utpattiḥ evam sphaṭika ādi vyaktīnām vināśa utpatti kāraṇa bhāvāt vināśa utpatti bhāva iti niradhiṣṭhānam ca dṛṣṭānta vacanam gṛhyamāṇayoḥ vināśa utpādayoḥ sphaṭika ādiṣu syāt ayam āśrayavān dṛṣṭāntaḥ kṣīra vināśa kāraṇa anupalabdhivat  dadhi utpatti kāraṇa anupalabdhivat ca iti tau tu na gṛhyete tasmāt niradhiṣṭhānoyam dṛṣṭānta iti abhyanujñāya ca sphaṭikasya utpāda vināśau yotra sādhakaḥ tasya abhyanujñānāt apratiṣedhaḥ kumbhavat na niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau sphaṭika ādīnām iti abhyanujñeyaḥ  ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ pratiṣeddhum aśakyatvāt  kṣīra dadhivat tu niṣkāraṇau vināśa utpādau  iti śakyoyam pratiṣeddhum kāraṇataḥ vināśa utpatti darśanāt  kṣīra dadhnoḥ vināśa utpattī paśyatā tad kāraṇam anumeyam kārya liṅgam hi kāraṇam iti upapannam anityā buddhiḥ iti idam tu cintyate kasya iyam buddhiḥ ātma indriya manaḥ  arthānām guṇa iti prasiddhopi khalu ayam arthaḥ aparīkṣā śeṣam pravartayāmi iti prakriyate soyam buddhau saṃnikarṣa utpatteḥ saṃśayaḥ viśeṣasya agrahaṇāt iti tatra anayam viśeṣaḥ na indriyāṇām arthānām vā guṇa u jñānam teṣām vināśe api jñānasya bhāvāt  bhavati khalu idam indriye arthe ca vinaṣṭe jñānam aadrākṣam iti na ca jñātari vinaṣṭe jñānam bhavitum arhati anyat  khalu vai tad  indriya artha saṃnikarṣa jam jñānam yad  indriya artha vināśe na bhavati idam anyat ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣa jam tasya yuktaḥ  bhāva iti usmṛtiḥ khalu iyam aadrākṣam iti pūrva dṛṣṭa viṣayā na ca vijñātari naṣṭe pūrva upalabdheḥ smaraṇam yuktam na ca anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati na ca manasi jñātari abhyupagamyamāne śakyam indriya arthayoḥ jñātṛ tvam pratipādayitum astu tarhi manaḥ guṇaḥ jñānam yugapad jñeya anupalabdhiḥ antaḥkaraṇasya liṅgam tatra yugapad jñeya anupalabdhyā yad anumīyate anta karaṇam na tasya guṇa u jñānam kasya tarhi jñasya vaśitvāt  uvaśī jñātā vaśyam karaṇam jñāna guṇa tve vā karaṇa bhāva nivṛttiḥ ghrāṇa ādi sādhanasya ca jñātuḥ gandha ādi jñāna bhāvāt anumīyate antaḥkaraṇa sādhanasya sukha ādi jñānam smṛtiḥ ca iti tatra yad  jñāna guṇam manaḥ sa ātmā yad tu sukha ādi upalabdhi sādhanam antaḥkaraṇam manaḥ tad iti saṃjñā bheda mātram na artha bheda iti yugapad jñeya anupalabdheḥ ca ayogina iti ca arthaḥ yogī khalu ṛddhau prādurbhūtāyām vikaraṇa dharmā nirmāya sa indriyāṇi śarīra antarāṇi teṣu teṣu yugapaj jñeyāni upalabhate tad ca etad  vibhau jñātari upapadyate na aṇau manasi iti vibhu tve vā manasaḥ  jñānasya na ātma guṇatva pratiṣedhaḥ vibhu ca manaḥ tad antaḥkaraṇa bhūtam iti tasya sarva indriyaiḥ yugapad  saṃyogāt  yugapaj jñānāni utpadyeran  iti vibhuḥ ātmā sarva indriyaiḥ saṃyukta iti yugapad jñāna utpatti prasaṅga  iti gandha ādi upalabdheḥ indriya artha saṃnikarṣavat  indriya manaḥ saṃnikarṣoti kāraṇam tasya ca ayaugapadyam aṇu tvāt manasaḥ ayaugapadyāt anutpattiḥ yugapad jñānānām ātma guṇa tvepi iti yadi punar ātma indriya artha saṃnikarṣa mātrāt  gandha ādi jñānam utpadyate ātma indriya saṃnikarṣa mātrāt  gandha ādi jñānam utpadyate iti na atra utpatti kāraṇam apadiśyate yena etad  pratipadyemahi iti tad ātma guṇa tvepi tulyam iti etad anena samuccīyate dvividhaḥ  hi guṇa nāśa hetuḥ guṇānām āśraya abhāvaḥ  virodhī ca guṇaḥ nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ  anupapannaḥ pūrvaḥ virodhī ca buddheḥ guṇa u na gṛhyate tasmāt ātma guṇa tve sati buddheḥ nityatva prasaṅgaḥ anityā buddhiḥ iti sarva śarīriṇām pratyātma vedanīyam etad  gṛhyate ca buddhi saṃtānaḥ tatra buddheḥ buddhi antaram virodhī guṇa iti anumīyate yathā śabda saṃtāne śabdaḥ śabda antara virodhi iti asaṃkhyeyeṣu jñāna kāriteṣu saṃskāreṣu smṛti hetuṣu ātma samaveteṣu ātma manasoḥ ca saṃnikarṣe samāne smṛti hetau sati na kāraṇasya ayaugapadyam asti iti yugapad smṛtayaḥ prādurbhaveyuḥ yadi buddhiḥ ātma guṇaḥ syāt iti tatra kaścid  saṃnikarṣasya ayaugapadyam upapādayiṣyan  āha jñāna sādhanaḥ saṃskāraḥ  jñānam iti ucyate jñāna saṃskṛtaiḥ ātma pradeśaiḥ paryāyeṇa manaḥ saṃnikṛṣyate ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣāt  smṛtayopi paryāyeṇa bhavanti iti sa dehasya ātmanaḥ  manasā saṃyogaḥ  vipacyamāna karma āśaya sahitaḥ  jīvanam iṣyate tatra asya prāk  prāyaṇāt antar śarīre vartamānasya manasaḥ śarīrāt  bahis jñāna saṃskṛtaiḥ ātma pradeśaiḥ saṃyogaḥ  na upapadyate iti vipacyamāna karma āśaya mātram jīvanam evam ca sati sādhyam antar śarīra vṛtti tvam manasa iti su smūrṣayā khalu ayam manaḥ praṇidadhānaḥ cirāt api kam cit artham smarati smarataḥ ca śarīra dhāraṇam dṛśyate ātma manaḥ saṃnikarṣa jaḥ ca prayatnaḥ  dvividhaḥ dhārakaḥ prerakaḥ ca niḥsṛte ca śarīrāt bahis manasi dhārakasya prayatnasya abhāvāt  guru tvāt patanam syāt  śarīrasya ātmavata iti āśugati manaḥ tasya bahis  śarīrāt ātma pradeśena jñāna saṃskṛtena saṃnikarṣaḥ pratyāgatasya ca prayatna utpādanam ubhayam yujyate iti utpādya vā dhārakam prayatnam śarīrāt niḥsaraṇam manasaḥ  atas tatra upapannam dhāraṇam iti kiñcid  kṣipram smaryate kiñcid cireṇa yadā cireṇa tadā su smūrṣayā manasi dhāryamāṇe cintā prabandhe sati kasya cit arthasya liṅga bhūtasya cintanam ārādhitam smṛti hetuḥ bhavati tatra etad  cira niścarite manasi na upapadyate iti śarīra saṃyoga anapekṣaḥ ca ātma manaḥ saṃyogaḥ  na smṛti hetuḥ śarīrasya upabhoga āyatana tvāt  upabhoga āyatanam puruṣasya jñātuḥ śarīram na tatas  niścaritasya manasa ātma saṃyoga mātram jñāna sukha ādīnām utpattau kalpate kḷptau vā śarīra vaiyarthyam iti ātma preraṇena vā manasaḥ  bahis  śarīrāt  saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ syāt  yadṛcchayā vā ākasmika tayā jñatayā vā manasaḥ sarvathā ca anupapattiḥ katham smartavya tvāt  icchatāḥ smaraṇa jñāna asaṃbhavāt ca yadi tāvat ātmā aamuṣya arthasya smṛti hetuḥ saṃskāraḥ  amuṣmin  ātma pradeśe samavetaḥ tena manaḥ saṃyujyatām iti manaḥ prerayati tadā smṛta eva asau  arthaḥ  bhavati na smartavyaḥ na ca ātma pratyakṣa ātma pradeśaḥ saṃskāraḥ  vā tatra anupapanna ātma pratyakṣeṇa saṃvittiḥ iti su smūrṣayā ca ayam manaḥ praṇidadhānaḥ cirāt api kañcid artham smarati na akasmāt  jña tvam ca manasaḥ  na asti jñāna pratiṣedhāt iti etad ca yadā khalu ayam vyāsakta manāḥ kvacid  deśe śarkarayā kaṇṭakena vā pāda vyathanam āpnoti tad ātma manaḥ saṃyoga viśeṣa eṣitavyaḥ dṛṣṭam hi duḥkham duḥkha vedanam ca iti tatra ayam samānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yadṛcchayā tu na viśā eṣaḥ na ākasmikī kriyā na akasmikaḥ saṃyoga iti karma adṛṣṭam upabhoga artham kriyā hetuḥ iti ced  samānam karma adṛṣṭam puruṣa stham puruṣa upabhoga artham manasi kriyā hetuḥ evam duḥkham duḥkha saṃvedanam na sidhyati ca iti evam ced manyase samānam smṛti hetau  api saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ  bhavitum arhati tatra yad uktam ātma preraṇa yadṛcchā jña tābhiḥ ca na saṃyoga viśeṣaḥ iti ayam apratiṣedha iti pūrvaḥ tu pratiṣedhaḥ na antar śarīra  vṛtti tvāt manasaḥ iti kaḥ khalu idānīm kāraṇa yaugapadi asadbhāve yugapada smaraṇasya hetuḥ iti yathā khalu ātma manasoḥ saṃnikarṣaḥ saṃskāraḥ ca smṛti hetuḥ evam praṇidhānam liṅga ādi jñānāni tāni ca na yugapad  bhavanti tad kṛtā smṛtīnām yugapad anutpattiḥ iti yad  khalu idam prātibham iva jñānam praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣam smārtam utpadyate kadācid  tasya yugapad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ hetu abhāvāt  sataḥ smṛti hetoḥ asaṃvedanāt  prātibheda samāna abhimānaḥ bahu artha viṣaye vai cintā prabandhe kaścid eva arthaḥ kasyacid  smṛti hetuḥ tasya anucintanāt tasya smṛtiḥ bhavati na ca ayam smartā sarvam smṛti hetum saṃvedayate aevam me smṛtiḥ utpanna iti asaṃvedanāt  prātibham iva jñānam idam smārtam iti abhimanyate na tu asti praṇidhāna ādi anapekṣa smārtam iti prātibhe katham iticed  puruṣa karma viśeṣāt upabhogavat niyamaḥ prātibhām idānīm jñānam yugapad  kasmāt na utpadyate yathā upabhoga artham karma yugapad upabhogam na karoti evam puruṣa karma viśeṣaḥ pratibhā hetuḥ na yugapad anekam prātibham jñānam utpādayati hetu abhāvāt ayuktam iticed  na karaṇasya pratyaya paryāye samārthyāt  aupabhogavat niyamaḥ iti asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ  hetuḥ na asti iti ced manyase na karaṇasya pratyaya paryāye sāmarthyāt  na ekasmin jñeye yugapad anekam jñānam utpadyate na ca anekasmin tad idam dṛṣṭena pratyaya paryāyeṇa anumeyam karaṇa sāmarthyam iti ambhūtam iti na jñātuḥ vikaraṇa dharmiṇaḥ  deha nānā tve pratyaya yaugapadyāt iti ayam ca dvitīyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ vyavasthita śarīrasya ca aneka jñāna samavāyāt eka pradeśe yugapad aneka artha smaraṇam syāt  kvacid  deśe avasthita śarīrasya jñātuḥ indriya artha prabandhena jñānam ekasmin  ātma pradeśe samavaiti tā ena yadā manaḥ saṃyujyate tadā jñāta pūrvasya anekasya yugapad  smaraṇam prasajyate pradeśa saṃyoga paryāya abhāvāt iti ātma pradeśānām adravya antara tvāt ekārtha samavāyasya aviśeṣe smṛti yaugapadya pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ śabda saṃtāne tu śrotra adhiṣṭhāna pratyāsattyā śabda śravaṇavat  saṃskāra pratyāsattyā manasaḥ smṛti utpatteḥ na yugapad utpatti prasaṅgaḥ pūrva eva tu pratiṣedhaḥ na aneka jñāna samavāyāt eka pradeśe yugapad  smṛti prasaṅga iti yad  apuruṣa dharmaḥ  jñānam antaḥkaraṇasya icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkhāni dharmāḥ iti kasyacid  darśanam tad  pratiṣidhyate ayam khalu jānīte tāvat  aidam me sukha sādhanam idam me duḥkha sādhanam iti jñātam svasya sukha sādhanam āptum icchati duḥkha sādhanam hātum icchati prāptum icchā yuktasya asya sukha sādhana avāptaye samīha aviśeṣa ārambhaḥ jihāsā prayuktasya duḥkha sādhana parivarjanam nivṛttiḥ evam jñāna icchā prayatna dveṣa sukha duḥkhānām ekena abhisaṃbandhaḥ eka kartṛ tvam jñāna icchā pravṛttīnām samāna śraya tvam ca tasmāt  jñasya icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkhāni dharmā na acetanasya iti ārambha nivṛttyoḥ ca pratyagātmani dṛṣṭa tvāt  paratra anumānam veditavyam iti atra bhūta caitanika āha ārambha nivṛtti liṅgauvicchā dveṣau  iti yasya ārambha nivṛttī tasya icchā dveṣau tasya jñānam iti prāptam pārthiva apya taijasavāyavīnām śarīrāṇām ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa jñānaiḥ yoga iti caitanyam śarīra caitanya nivṛttiḥ ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa jñānaiḥ yoga iti prāptam paraśu ādeḥ karaṇasya ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt caitanyam iti atha śarīrasya icchā ādibhiḥ yogaḥ para śu ādeḥ tu karaṇasya ārambha nivṛttī vyabhicarataḥ na tarhi ayam hetuḥ apārthiva apya taijasavāyavīnām śarīrāṇām ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa jñānaiḥ yogaḥ iti ayam tarhi anyaḥ arthaḥ tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ pṛthivī ādīnām bhūtānām ārambhaḥ tāvat  trasa viśarāru sthā vara śarīreṣu tad avayava vyūha liṅgaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ loṣṭa ādiṣu liṅga abhāvāt pravṛtti viśeṣa abhāvaḥ  nivṛttiḥ ārambha nivṛtti liṅgauvicchā dveṣau  iti pārthiva ādyeṣu aṇuṣu tad darśanāt icchā dveṣayoḥ tad yogāt  jñāna yoga iti siddham bhūta caitanyam iti kumbha ādi mṛd ava yavānām vyūha liṅgaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣa ārambhaḥ sikata ādiṣu pravṛtti viśeṣa abhāvaḥ  nivṛttiḥ na ca mṛtsikatānām ārambha nivṛtti darśanāt icchā dveṣa prayatna jñānaiḥ yogaḥ tasmāt  tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣa yaḥ iti ahetuḥ iti tayoḥ icchā dveṣayoḥ niyama aniyamau viśeṣakau bhedakau jñasya icchā dveṣa nimitte pravṛtti nivṛttī na sva āśraye kim tarhi prayojya āśraye tatra prayujyamāneṣu bhūteṣu pravṛtti nivṛttī staḥ na sarveṣu iti  aniyama upapattiḥ yasya tu jña tvāt  bhūtānām icchā dveṣa nimitte ārambha nivṛttī sva āśraye tasya niyamaḥna syāt  yathā bhūtānām guṇa antara nimittā pravṛttiḥ guṇa pratibandhāt ca nivṛttiḥ bhūtamātre bhavati niyamena eva bhūtamātre jñāna icchā dveṣa nimitte pravṛtti nivṛttī sva āśraye syātām na tu bhavataḥ tasmāt  prayojaka āśritā jñāna icchā dveṣi prayatnāḥ prayojya āśraye tu pravṛtti nivṛttī iti siddham eka śarīre jñātṛ bahu tvam niranumānam bhūta caitanikasya eka śarīre bahūni bhūtāni jñāna icchā dveṣa prayatna guṇāni iti jñātṛ bahu tvam prāptam om iti bruvataḥ pramāṇam na asti yathā nānā śarīreṣu nānā jñātāraḥ  pratyaya vyavasthānāt  evam eka śarīrepi pratyaya vyavasthā anumānam syāt  jñātṛ bahutvasya iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca anya guṇa nimittaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ  bhūtānām sonu mānam anyatra api dṛṣṭaḥ karaṇa lakṣaṇeṣu bhūteṣu paraśu ādiṣu upādāna lakṣaṇeṣu ca mṛd prabhṛtiṣu anya guṇa nimittaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ sonu mānam anyatra api sa trasa sthāvara śarīreṣu tad avayava vyūha liṅgaḥ pravṛtti viśeṣaḥ  bhūtānām anya guṇa nimitta iti sa ca guṇaḥ prayatna samāna āśrayaḥ saṃskāraḥ  dharma adharma samākhyātaḥ sarva arthaḥ puruṣa artha ārādhanāya prayojakaḥ  bhūtānām prayatnavat iti ātmā astitva hetubhiḥ ātma nityatva hetumiḥ ca bhūta caitanya pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ  veditavyaḥ na indriya arthayoḥ tad vināśepi jñāna avasthānāt iti ca samānaḥ pratiṣedha iti kriyā mātram kriyā uparama mātram ca ārambha nivṛttī iti abhipretya uktam tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ iti anyathā tu ime ārambha nivṛttī ākhyāte na ca tathāvidhe pṛthivī ādiṣu dṛśyete tasmāt ayuktam tad liṅga tvāt icchā dveṣayoḥ pārthiva ādyeṣu apratiṣedhaḥ iti bhūta indriya manasām samānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  manaḥ tu udāharaṇa mātram icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha jñānāni ātmanaḥ  liṅgam iti atas  prabhṛti yathā uktam saṃgṛhyate tena bhūta indriya manasām caitanya pratiṣedhaḥ pāratantryāt  upara tantrāṇi bhūta indriya manāṃsi dhāraṇa preraṇa vyūhana kriyāsu prayatna vaśāt  pravartante caitanye punar  svatantrāṇi syuḥ iti akṛta abhyāgamāt ca pravṛttiḥ uvāc buddhi śarīra ārambha iti caitanye bhūta indriya manasām para kṛtam karma puruṣeṇa upabhujte iti syāt  acaitanye tu tad sādhanasya sva kṛta karma phala upabhogaḥ puruṣasya iti upapadyate iti atha ayam siddha upasaṃgrahaḥ aātma guṇa u jñānam iti prakṛtam pariśeṣaḥ  nāma prasakta pratiṣedhe anyatra aprasaṅgāt śiṣyamāṇe saṃpratyayaḥ bhūta indriya manasām pratiṣedhe dravya antaram na prasajyate śiṣyate ca ātmā tasya guṇa u jñānam iti jñāyate yathā ukta hetu upapatteḥ ca iti darśana sparśanābhyām ekārtha grahaṇāt iti evamādīnām ātma pratipatti hetūnām apratiṣedhāt iti pariśeṣa jñāpana artham prakṛta sthāpana ādi jñāna artham ca yathā ukta hetu upapatti vacanam iti atha vā upapatteḥ ca iti hetu antaram eva idam nityaḥ khalu ayam ātmā yasmāt ekasmin śarīre dharmam caritvā kāya bhedāt  svarge deveṣu upapadyate adharmam caritvā dehabhedāt  narakeṣu upapadyate iti upapattiḥ śarīra antara prāpti lakṣaṇā sā sati sattve nitye ca āśrayavatī buddhi prabandha mātre tu nirātmake nirāśrayā na upapadyate iti eka sattva adhiṣṭhānaḥ ca aneka śarīra yogaḥ saṃsāra upapadyate śarīra prabandha udaḥ ca apavargaḥ  muktiḥ iti upapadyate buddhi saṃtati mātre tu eka sattva anupapatteḥ na kaścid  dīrgham adhvānam saṃdhāvati na kaścid  śarīra prabandhāt vimucyata iti saṃsāra apavarga anupapattiḥ iti buddhi saṃtati mātre ca sattva bhedāt  sarvam idam prāṇi vyavahāra jātam apratisaṃhitam avyāvṛttam apariniṣṭhitam ca syāt  tatas  smaraṇa abhāvāt na anya dṛṣṭam anyaḥ smarati iti smaraṇam ca khalu pūrva jñātasya samānena jñātrā grahaṇam aajñāsiṣam amum artham jñeyam iti soyam ekaḥ  jñātā pūrva jñātam artham gṛhṇāti tad ca asya grahaṇam smaraṇam iti tad  buddhi prabandha mātre nirātmake na upapadyate upapadyate iti ātmana eva smaraṇam na buddhi saṃtati mātrasya iti tuśabdaḥ  avadhāraṇe katham jña svābhāvyāt  jña iti asya svabhāvaḥ usvaḥ  dharmaḥ ayam khalu ajñāsyati jānāti ajñāsīt iti tri kāla viṣayeṇa anekena jñānena saṃbadhyate tad ca asya tri kāla viṣayam jñānam pratyātma vedanīyam ajñāsyāmi jānāmi ajñāsiṣam iti vartate tad  yasya ayam svar  dharmaḥ tasya smaraṇam na buddhi prabandha mātrasya nirātmakasya iti smṛti hetūnām ayaugapadyāt  yugapada smaraṇam iti uktam atha kebhyaḥ smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti smṛtiḥ khalu su smūrṣayā manasaḥ  dhāraṇam praṇidhānam su smūrṣita liṅga cintanam ca artha smṛti kāraṇam nibandhaḥ khalu eka grantha upayama ūrthānām eka grantha upayatāḥ khalu arthā anyonya smṛti hetavaḥ ānupūrvyeṇa itarathā vā bhavanti iti dhāraṇā śāstra kṛtaḥ  vā prajñāteṣu vastuṣu smartavyānām upanikṣepaḥ  nibandha iti abhyāsaḥ tu samāne viṣaye jñānānām abhyāvṛttiḥ abhyāsa janitaḥ saṃskāra ātma guṇaḥ abhyāsa śabdena ucyate sa ca smṛti hetuḥ samāna  iti liṅgam punar  saṃyogi samavāyi eka artha samavāyi virodhi ca iti saṃyogi yathā dhūmaḥ  agneḥ goḥ viṣaṇam pāṇiḥ pādasya rūpam sparśasya abhūtam bhūtasya iti lakṣaṇam paśu avayava stham gotrasya smṛti hetuḥ vidānām idam gargāṇām idam iti sādṛśyam citra gatam pratirūpakam devadattasya iti evamādi parigrahāt  svena vā svāmī svāminā vā svam smaryate āśrayāt  grāmaṇyā tad adhīnam smarati āśritāt  tad adhīnena grāmaṇyam iti saṃbandhāt  antevāsinā yuktam gurum smarati ṛtvijā yājyam iti ānantaryāt  itikagṇīyeṣu artheṣu viyogāt  yena viprayujyate tad viyoga pratisaṃvedī bhṛśam smarati eka kāryāt  kartṛ antara darśanāt  kartṛ antare smṛtiḥ virodhāt  vijigīṣamāṇayoḥ anyatara darśanāt anyataraḥ smaryate atiśayāt  yena atiśaya utpāditaḥ prāpteḥ yatas  yena kiñcid  prāptam āptavyam vā bhavati tam abhīkṣṇam smarati vyavadhānāt  kośa ādibhiḥ asi bhṛtīni smaryante sukha duḥkhābhyām tad hetuḥ smaryate icchā dveṣābhyām yam icchati yam ca dveṣṭi tam smarati bhayāt  yatas  bibheti arthi tvāt  yena arthī bhojanen ācchādanena vā kriyayā rathena rathakāram smarati rāgāt  yasyām striyām raktaḥ  bhavati tām abhīkṣṇam smarati dharmāt  jāti antara smaraṇam iha ca adhīta śruta avadhāraṇam iti adharmāt  prāk anubhūta duḥkha sādhanam smarati na ca eteṣu nimitteṣu yugapad saṃvedanāni bhavanti iti yugapada smaraṇam iti nidarśanam ca idam smṛti hetūnām na parisaṃkhyānam iti anityāyām ca buddhau utpanna apavargi tvāt  kāla antara avasthānāt ca anityānām saṃśayaḥ kim utpanna apavargiṇī buddhiḥ śabdavat  ahaḥ svid  kāla antara avasthāyinī kumbhavan iti utpavya apavargiṇī iti pakṣaḥ parigṛhyate kasmāt  karmaṇaḥ  anavasthāyinaḥ grahaṇāt iti kṣiptasya īṣoḥ āpatanāt  kriyā saṃtānaḥ  gṛhyate gati artha niyamāt ca buddhīnām kriyā saṃtānavat  buddhi saṃtāna upapattiḥ iti avasthita grahaṇe ca vyavadhīyamānasya pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ avasthite ca kumbhe gṛhyamāṇe saṃtānena eva buddhiḥ vartate prāk  vyavadhānāt  tena vyavahite pratyakṣam jñānam nivartate kāla antara avasthāne tu buddheḥ dṛśya vyavadhānepi pratyakṣam avatiṣṭheta iti smṛtiḥ ca āliṅgam buddhi avasthāne saṃskārasya buddhi jasya smṛti hetu tvāt  yaḥ ca manyeta avatiṣṭhate buddhiḥ dṛṣṭā hi buddhi viṣaye smṛtiḥ sā ca buddhau  anityāyām kāraṇa abhāvāt na syāt iti tad idam aliṅgam kasmāt  buddhi jaḥ  hi saṃskāraḥ  guṇa antaram smṛti hetuḥ na buddhiḥ iti hetu abhāvāt ayuktam iticed  buddhi avasthānāt pratyakṣa tve smṛtyabhāvaḥ yāvat avatiṣṭhate buddhiḥ tāvat asau boddhavya arthaḥ pratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣe ca smṛtiḥ anupapanna iti yadi utpannā vargiṇīm buddhiḥ prāptam avyaktam boddhavyasya grahaṇam yathā vidyut saṃpāte vaidyutasya prakāśasya anavasthānāt avyaktam rūpa grahaṇam iti vyaktam tu dravyaṇām grahaṇam tasmāt ayuktam etad iti autpanna apavargiṇī buddhiḥ iti pratiṣeddhavyam tad eva abhyanujñāyate vidyut saṃpāte rūpa avyakta grahaṇavat iti yatra avyakta grahaṇam tatra utpanna apavargiṇī buddhiḥ iti grahaṇa hetu vikalpāt  grahaṇa vikalpaḥ  na buddhi vikalpāt  yad idam kvacid avyaktam kvacid  vyaktam grahaṇam ayam vikalpaḥ  grahaṇa hetu vikalpāt  uyatra anavasthitaḥ  grahaṇa hetuḥ tatra avyaktam grahaṇam yatra avasthitaḥ tatra vyaktam na tu buddheḥ  avasthāna anavasthānābhyām iti kasmāt  artha grahaṇam hi buddhiḥ yad  tad artha grahaṇam avyaktam vyaktam vā buddhiḥ sā iti viśeṣa agrahaṇe ca sāmānya grahaṇam avyakta grahaṇam tatra viṣaya antare buddhi antara anutpattiḥ nimitta abhāvāt yatra sāmānya dharma yuktaḥ ca dharmī gṛhyate viśeṣa dharma yuktaḥ ca tad  vyaktam grahaṇam tatra tu viśeṣe agṛhyamāṇe sāmānya grahaṇa mātram tad avyaktam grahaṇam sāmānya dharma yogāt ca viśiṣṭa dharma yogaḥ  viṣaya antaram tatra yad  grahaṇam na bhavati tad  grahaṇa nimitta abhāvāt  na nu buddheḥ anavasthānāt iti yathā viṣayam ca grahaṇa vyaktam eva pratyartha niyata tvāt ca buddhīnām sāmānya viṣayam ca grahaṇam sva viṣayam prati vyaktam viśeṣa viṣayam ca grahaṇam sva viṣayam prati vyaktam pratyartha niyatā hi buddhayaḥ tad idam avyakta grahaṇam deśitam kva viṣaye buddhi anavasthāna kāritam syāt iti dharmiṇaḥ tu dharma bhede buddhi nānātvasya bhāva abhāvābhyām tad upapattiḥ dharmiṇaḥ khalu arthasya samānāḥ ca dharmā viśiṣṭāḥ ca teṣu pratyartha niyatāḥ nānā buddhayaḥ tā ubhayyaḥ  yadi dharmiṇi vartante tadā vyaktam grahaṇam dharmiṇam abhipretya yadā tu sāmānya grahaṇa mātram tadā avyaktam grahaṇam iti evam dharmiṇam abhipretya vyakta avyaktayoḥ grahaṇayoḥ upapattiḥ iti na ca idam avyaktam grahaṇam buddheḥ boddhavyasya vā anavasthāyi tvāt upapadyate iti idam hi anavasthāyitvepi buddheḥ teṣām dravyāṇām grahaṇam vyaktam pratipattavyam katham pradīpa arciḥ saṃtati abhivyakta grahaṇavat  upradīpa arciṣām saṃtatyā vartamānānām grahaṇa anavasthānam grāhya anavasthānam ca pratyartha niyata tvāt vā buddhīnām yāvanti pradīpa arcīṣi tāvatyaḥ  buddhaya iti dṛśyate ca atra vyaktam pradīpa arciṣām grahaṇam iti cetanā śarīra guṇaḥ sati śarīre bhāvāt asati ca abhāvāt iti sāṃśayikaḥ sati bhāvaḥ sva guṇa u apsu drava tvam upalabhyate para guṇaḥ ca uṣṇa tā tena ayam saṃśayaḥ kim śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīre gṛhyate atha dravya antara guṇaḥ iti na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā kasmāt  na rūpa ādi hīnam śarīram gṛhyate cetanā hīnam tu gṛhyate yathā uṣṇatā hīnā āpaḥ tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti saṃskāravat iti ced  na kāraṇa anucchedāt  yathāvidhe dravye saṃkāraḥ tathāvidhe eva uparamaḥ na tatra kāraṇa ucchedāt atyantam saṃskāra anupattiḥ bhavati yathāvidhe śarīre cetanā gṛhyate tathāvidhe eva atyanta uparamaḥ cetanāyāḥ  gṛhyate tasmāt  asaṃskāravat iti asamaḥ samādhiḥ atha api śarīra stham cetana utpatti kāraṇam syāt  dravya antara stham vā ubhaya stham vā tad na niyama hetu abhāvāt uśarīra sthena kadācid  cetanā utpadyate kadācid na iti niyame hetuḥ na asti iti dravya antara sthena ca śarīre eva cetanā utpadyate na loṣṭa ādiṣu iti atra niyama hetuḥ na asti iti ubhaya sthasya nimitta tve śarīra samāna jātīya dravye cetanā na utpadyate śarīre eva ca utpadyate iti niyame hetuḥ na asti iti yad ca manyeta sati śyāma ādi guṇe dravye śyāma ādi uparamaḥ  dṛṣṭa evam cetanā uparamaḥ syāt iti na atyanta rūpa uparamaḥ dravyasya śyāme rūpe nivṛtte pāka jam guṇa antaram uraktam rūpam utpadyate śarīre tu cetanā mātra uparamaḥ  atyantam iti atha api yāvat su dravyeṣu pūrva guṇa pratidvandvi siddhiḥ tāvat su pākaja utpattiḥ dṛśyate pūrva guṇaiḥ saha pāka jānām avasthānasya agrahaṇāt  na ca śarīre cetanā pratidvandvi saha anavasthāyi guṇa antaram gṛhyate yena anumīyeta tena cetanāyāḥ  virodhaḥ tasmāt apratiṣaddhā cetanā yāvat śarīram varteta na tu vartate tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā śarīram śarīra avayavāḥ ca sarve cetana utpattyā vyāptā iti na kvacid anutpattiḥ cetanāyāḥ śarīravat  śarīra avayavāḥ cetanā iti prāptam cetana bahu tvam tatra yathā pratiśarīram cetana bahu tve sukha duḥkha jñānānām vyavasthā liṅgam evam eka śarīrepi syāt  na tu bhavati tasmāt na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā iti yad uktam na kvacid śarīra avayave cetanāyāḥ  anutpattiḥ iti sā na keśeṣu nakha ādiṣu ca anutpattiḥ cetanāyāḥ  iti anupapannam śarīra vyāpi tvam iti indriya āśraya tvam śarīra lakṣaṇam tvac paryantam jīva manaḥ sukha duḥkha saṃvitti āyatana bhūtam śarīram tasmāt na keśa ādiṣu cetanā utpadyate artha kāritaḥ tu śarīra upanibandhaḥ keśa ādīnām iti itas ca na śarīra guṇaḥ cetanā dvividhaḥ śarīra guṇaḥ apratyakṣam ca guru tvam indriya grāhyam ca rūpa ādi vidha antaram tu cetanā na apratyakṣā saṃvedya tvāt  na indriya grāhyā manaḥ viṣaya tvāt tasmāt  dravya antara guṇa iti yathā itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ  rūpādayaḥ  na śarīra guṇa tvam jahati evam rūpa ādi vaidharmya ārt cetanā śarīra guṇa tvam na hāsyati iti apratyakṣa tvāt ca iti yathā itaretara vidharmāṇaḥ  rūpādayaḥ  na dvaividhyam ativartante tathā rūpa ādi vaidharmyāt  cetanā na dvaividhyam ativarteta yadi śarīra guṇaḥ syāt iti ativarttate tu tasmāt na śarīra guṇa iti bhūta indriya manasām jñāna pratiṣedhāt  siddhe satya ārambhaḥ  viśeṣa jñāpana arthaḥ bahudhā parīkṣyamāṇam tattvam su niścitataram bhavati iti parīkṣitā buddhiḥ manasa idānīm parīkṣā kramaḥ tad  kim pratiśarīram ekam anekam iti vicāre asti khalu vai jñāna ayaugapadyam ekaikasya indriyasya yathā viṣayam karaṇasya eka pratyaya nirvṛttau sāmarthyāt  na tad ekatve manasaḥ  liṅgam yad tu khalu indriya antarāṇām viṣaya antareṣu jñāna ayaugapadyam iti tad liṅgam kasmāt  saṃbhavati khalu vai bahuṣu manaḥsu indriya manaḥ saṃyoga yaugapadyam iti jñāna yaugapadyam syāt  na tu bhavati tasmāt  viṣaye pratyaya paryāyāt ekam manaḥ  bhavati iti ayam khalu adhyāpakaḥ  adhīte vrajati kamaṇḍalum dhārayati panthānam paśyati śṛṇoti āraṇya jān śabdān bibheti vyāla liṅgāni bubhutsate smarati ca gantavyam sthānīyam iti kramasya agrahaṇāt  yugapad etāḥ kriyā iti prāptam manasaḥ  bahutvam iti āśu saṃcārāt alāta cakrasya bhramataḥ  vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ  na gṛhyate kramasya agrahaṇāt  aviccheda buddhyā cakravat  buddhiḥ bhavati tathā buddhīnām kriyāṇām ca āśu vṛtti tvāt  vidyamānaḥ kramaḥ  na gṛhyate kramasya agrahaṇāt  yugapad  kriyā bhavanati iti abhimānaḥ  bhavati kim punar  kramasya agrahaṇāt  yugapad  kriyā abhimānaḥ atha yugapad bhāvāt eva yugapad aneka kriyā upalabdhiḥ iti na atra viśeṣa pratipatteḥ kāraṇam ucyate uktam indriya antarāṇām viṣaya antareṣu paryāyeṇa buddhayaḥ  bhavanti iti tad ca apratyākhyeyam ātma pratyakṣa tvāt  atha api dṛṣṭa śrutān arthān  cintayataḥ krameṇa buddhayaḥ  vartante na yugapad  anena anumātavyam iti varṇa pada vākya buddhīnām tad artha buddhīnām ca āśu vṛtti tvāt kramasya agrahaṇam katham vākya stheṣu khalu varṇeṣu uccaratsu prativarṇam tāvat śravaṇam bhavati śrutam varṇam ekam anekam vā pada bhāvena pratisaṃdhatte pratisaṃdhāya padam vyavasyati pada vyavasāyena smṛtyā padārtham pratipadyate pada samūha pratisaṃdhānāt ca vākyam vyavasyati saṃbaddhān  ca padārthāna gṛhītvā vākya artham pratipadyate na ca āsām krameṇa vartamānānām buddhīnām āśu vṛtti tvāt  kramaḥ  gṛhyate tad etad anumānam anyatra buddhi kriyā yaugapadya abhimānasya iti na ca asti mukta saṃśayā yugapad utpattiḥ buddhīnām yayā manasaḥ  bahu tvam eka śarīre anumīyate iti aṇu mana ekam ca iti dharma samuccayaḥ jñāna ayaugapadyāt mahat tve manasaḥ sarva indriya saṃyogāt  yugapad  viṣaya grahaṇam syāt iti manasaḥ khalu bhoḥ sa indriyasya śarīre vṛtti lābhaḥ  na anyatra śarīrāt  jñātuḥ ca puruṣasya śarīra āyatanā buddhi ādayaḥ  viṣaya upabhogaḥ  jihāsita hānam īpsita avāptiḥ ca sarve ca śarīra āśrayā vyavahārāḥ tatra khalu vipratipatteḥ saṃśayaḥ kim ayam puruṣa karma nimittaḥ śarīra sargaḥ atha vā bhūta mātrāt akarma nimittaḥ iti śrūyate khalu atra vipratipattiḥ iti tatra idam tattvam pūrva śarīre yā pravṛttiḥ vāc buddhi śarīra ārambha lakṣaṇā tad  pūrva kṛtam karma uktam tasya phalam tad janitau dharma adharmaum tad phalasya anubandhaḥ ātma samavetasya avasthānam tena prayuktebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ tasya śarīrasya utpattiḥ na svatantrebhyaḥ  iti yad adhiṣṭhānoyam ātmā aayam aham itimanyamānaḥ  yatra abhiyuktaḥ  yatra upabhoga tṛṣṇayā viṣayānupalabhamānaḥ  dharma adharmaum saṃskaroti tad asya śarīram tena saṃskāreṇa dharma adharma lakṣaṇena bhūta sahitena patite asmin śarīre śarīra antaram niṣpadyate niṣpannasya ca tasya pūrva śarīravat  puruṣa artha kriyā puruṣasya ca pūrva śarīravat pravṛttiḥ iti karma apekṣebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ śarīra sargesati etad upapadyate iti dṛṣṭā ca puruṣa guṇena prayatnena prayuktebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ puruṣa artha kriyā samarthānām dravyāṇām ratha prabhṛtīnām utpattiḥ tayā anumātavyam aśarīram api puruṣa artha kriyā samartham utpadyamānam puruṣasya guṇa antara apekṣebhyaḥ  bhūtebhya utpadyate iti atra nāstika āha yathā karma nirapekṣebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ  nirvṛttā mūrtayaḥ usikatā śarkarā pāṣāṇa gairika añjana prabhṛtayaḥ puruṣa artha kāri tvāt upādīyante tathā karma nirapekṣebhyaḥ  bhūtebhyaḥ śarīm utpannam puruṣa artha kāri tvāt upādīyate iti yathā śarīra utpattiḥ akarma nimittā sādhyā tathā sikatā śarkarā pāṣāṇa gairika añjana prabhṛtīnām api  akarma nimittaḥ sargaḥ sādhyaḥ sādhya sama tvāda sādhanam iti bhūtebhyaḥ  mūrti upādānavat iti ca anena sādhyam viṣamaḥ ca ayam upanyāsaḥ kasmāt  nirbījā imā mūrtaya utpadyante bījapūrvikā tu śarīra utpattiḥ mātā pitṛ śabdena lohita retasī bīja bhūte gṛhyete tatra sattva svaya garbha vāsa anubhavanīyam karma pitroḥ ca putrula anubhavanīye karmaṇī mātuḥ garbha āśraye śarīra utpattim bhūtebhyaḥ prayojayanti iti upapannam bīja anuvidhānam iti utpatti nimitta tvāt  iti prakṛtam bhuktam pītam āhāraḥ tasya pakti nirvṛttam rasa dravyam mātṛ śarīre ca upacīyate bīje garbhāśaya sthe bīja samāna pākam mātrayā ca upacayaḥ bīje yāvat  vyūha samarthaḥ saṃcaya iti saṃcitam ca arbuda māṃsa peśī kalaka kaṇḍara śiraḥ pāṇi ādinā ca vyūhena indriya adhiṣṭhāna bhedena vyūhyate vyūhe ca garbha ganāḍya avatāritam rasa dravyam upacīyate yāvat  prasava samartham iti na ca ayam anna pānasya sthālī ādi gatasya kalpate iti etasmāt  kāraṇāt  karma nimitta tvam śarīrasya vijñāyate iti na sarvaḥ  dampatyoḥ saṃyogaḥ  garbhādhāna hetuḥ dṛśyate tatra asati karmaṇi na bhavati sati ca bhavati iti upapannaḥ  niyama abhāva iti karma nirapekṣeṣu bhūteṣu śarīra utpatti hetuṣu niyamaḥ syāt  na hi atra kāraṇa abhāva iti atha api yathā khalu idam śarīram dhātu prāṇa saṃvāhinīnām nāḍīnām śukra antānām dhātūnām ca snāyu tvac asthi śirā peśī kalala kaṇḍarāṇām ca śiraḥ bāhu udarāṇām sakthnām ca koṣṭha gānām vāta pitta kaphānām ca mukha kaṇṭha hṛdaya āmāśaya pakvāśaya adhas strotasām ca parama duḥkha saṃpādanīyena saṃniveśena vyūhitam aśakyam pṛthivī ādibhiḥ karma nirapekṣaiḥ utpādayitum iti karma nimittā śarīra utpattiḥ iti vijñāyate evam ca pratyātma niyatasya nimittasya abhāvāt  niratiśayaiḥ ātmabhiḥ saṃbandhāt  sarva ātmanām na samānaiḥ pṛthivī ādibhiḥ utpāditam śarīram pṛthivī ādi gatasya ca niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt  sarva ātmanām sukha duḥkha saṃvitti sādhanam samānam prāptam yad tu pratyātmam vyavatiṣṭhate tatra śarīra utpatti nimittam karma vyavasthā hetuḥ iti vijñāyate paripacyamānaḥ  hi pratyātma niyataḥ karma āśayaḥ  yasmin  ātmani vartate tasya eva upabhoga āyatanam śarīram utpādya vyavasthāpayati tad evam śarīra utpatti nimittavat  saṃyoga nimittam karma iti vijñāyate pratyātma vyavasthānam tu śarīrasya ātmanā saṃyogam pracakṣmahe iti yaḥ  ayam akarma nimitte śarīra sarge sati niyama iti ucyate ayam śarīra utpatti nimittavat  saṃyoga utpatti nimittam karma iti anena pratyuktaḥ kaḥ tāvat ayam niyamaḥ yathā ekasya ātmanaḥ śarīram tathā sarveṣām iti niyamaḥ anyasya anyathā anyasya anyathā iti  aniyamaḥ bhedaḥ uvyāvṛtti viśeṣa iti dṛṣṭā ca janma vyāvṛttiḥ ucca abhijanaḥ  nikṛṣṭa abhijana iti praśastam ninditam iti vyādhi bahulam arogam iti samagram vikalam iti pīḍā bahulam sukha bahulam iti puruṣa atiśaya lakṣaṇa upapannam viparītam iti praśasta lakṣaṇam nindita lakṣaṇam iti paṭu indriyam mṛd u indriyam iti sūkṣmaḥ ca bhedaḥ  aparimeyaḥ soyam janma bhedaḥ pratyātma niyatāt  karma bhedāt upapadyate asati karma bhede pratyātma niyate niratiśaya tvāt ātmanām samāna tvāt ca pṛthivī ādīnām pṛthivī ādi gatasya niyama hetoḥ abhāvāt  sarvam sarva ātmanām prasajyeta na tu idam ittham bhūtam janma tasmāt  na akarma nimittā śarīra utpattiḥ iti karma nimitte śarīra sarge tena śarīreṇa ātmanaḥ  viyoga upapannaḥ kasmāt  karma kṣaya upapatteḥ upapadyate khalu karma kṣayaḥ samyak darśanāt  prakṣīṇe mohe vīta rāgaḥ punarbhava hetu karma kāya vāc manobhiḥ na karoti iti uttarasya anupacayaḥ pūrva upacitasya vipāka pratisaṃvedanāt  prakṣayaḥ evam prasava hetoḥ abhāvāt  patite asmin śarīre punar  śarīra antara anutpatteḥ apratisaṃdhiḥ akarma nimitte tu śarīra sarge bhūta kṣaya anupapatteḥ tad viyoga anupapattiḥ iti adarśanam khalu adṛṣṭam iti ucyate adṛṣṭa kāri tā bhūtebhyaḥ śarīra utpattiḥ na jātu  anutpanne śarīre draṣṭā nirāyatanaḥ  dṛśyam paśyati tad ca asya dṛśyam dvividham viṣayaḥ ca nānā tvam ca avyakta ātmanoḥ tad arthaḥ śarīra sargaḥ tasmin   avasite caritārthāni bhūtāni na śarīram utpādayanti iti upapannaḥ śarīra viyoga iti evam ced manyase punar tad prasaṅgaḥ  apavarge punar  śarīra utpattiḥ prasajyate iti yā ca anutpanne śarīre darśana anutpattiḥ adarśana abhimatā yā ca apavarge śarīra nivṛttau darśana anutpattiḥ adarśana bhūtāḥ  na etayoḥ adarśanayoḥ kvacid  viśeṣaitya darśanasya anivṛtteḥ apavarge punar  śarīra utpatti prasaṅga  iti caritārtha tā viśeṣa iti ced  na karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ ārambha darśanāt caritārthāni bhūtāni darśana avasānāt  na śarīra antaram ārabhante iti ayam viśeṣaḥ evam ced ucyate na karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ ārambha darśanāt carita arthānām bhūtānām viṣaya upalabdhi karaṇāt punar  punar  śarīra ārambhaḥ  dṛśyate prakṛti puruṣayoḥ nānātva darśanasya akaraṇāt  nirarthakaḥ śarīra ārambhaḥ punar  punar dṛśyate tasmāt akarma nimittāyām bhūta sṛṣṭau na darśana arthā śarīra utpattiḥ yuktā yuktā tu karma nimitte sarge darśana arthā śarīra utpattiḥ karma viṣāka saṃvedanam darśanam iti tad adṛṣṭa kāritam iti ca kasyacid  darśanam adṛṣṭam nāma paramāṇūnām guṇa viśeṣaḥ kriyā hetuḥ tena preritāḥ paramāṇavaḥ saṃmūrcchitāḥ śarīram utpādayanti iti tad  manaḥ samāviśati sva guṇena adṛṣṭena preritam samanaske śarīre draṣṭuḥ upalabdhiḥ bhavati iti etasmin vai darśane guṇa an ucchedāt punar tad prasaṅga apavarge apavarge śarīra utpattiḥ paramāṇu guṇasya adṛṣṭasya anucchedyanvāt iti manaḥ guṇena adṛṣṭena samāveśite manasi saṃyoga vyucchedaḥ  na syāt  tatra kiṅkṛtam śarīrāt apasarpaṇam manasa iti karma āśaya kṣaye tu karma āśaya antarāt  vipacyamānāt apasarpaṇa upapattiḥ iti adṛṣṭāt eva apasa praṇamiti ced  yaḥ  adṛṣṭaḥ śarīra upasarpaṇa hetuḥ sa eva apasarpaṇa hetuḥ api iti na ekasya jīvana prāyaṇa hetutva anupapatteḥ evam ca sati ekam adṛṣṭam jīvana prāyaṇayoḥ hetuḥ iti prāptam na etad upapadyate vipāka saṃvedanāt  karma āśaya kṣaye śarīra pātaḥ prāyaṇam karma āśaya antarāt ca punarjanma bhūtamātrāt tu karma nirapekṣāt  śarīra utpattau kasya kṣayāt  śarīra pātaḥ prāyaṇam iti prāyaṇa anupapatteḥ khalu vai nityatva prasaṅgam vidmaḥ yādṛcchike tu prāyaṇe prāyaṇa bheda anupapattiḥ iti punar tad prasaṅgaḥ  apavarge etad sasādhitsurāha yathā aṇoḥ śyāma tā nityā agni saṃyogena pratibaddhā na punar utpadyate evam adṛṣṭa kāritam śarīram apavarge punar na utpadyate iti na ayam asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ kasmāt  akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt  akṛtam pramāṇataḥ  anupapannam tasya abhyāgamaḥ abhyupapattiḥ uvyaya sāyaḥ etad śraddadhānena pramāṇataḥ  anupapannam mantavyam tasmāt na ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ na pratayakṣam na ca anumānam kiñcid ucyate iti tad idan dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya sama tvam abhidhīyate iti atha vā na akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgāt  aṇu śyāma tā dṛṣṭāntena akarma nimittām śarīra utpattim samādadhānasya akṛta abhyāgama prasaṅgaḥ akṛte sukha duḥkha uhetau karmaṇi puruṣasya sukham duḥkham abhyāgacchati iti prasajyeta omiti brahavataḥ pratyakṣa anumāna āgama virodhaḥ pratyakṣa virodhaḥ tāvat  bhinnam idam sukha duḥkham pratyātma vedanīya tvāt  pratyakṣam sarva śarīriṇām kaḥ  bhedaḥ tīvram mandam ciram āśu nānā prakāram eka prakāram iti evamādiḥ viśeṣaḥ na ca asti pratyātma niyataḥ sukha duḥkha hetu viśeṣaḥ na ca asati hetu viśeṣe phala viśeṣaḥ  dṛśyate karma nimitte tu sukha duḥkha yoge karmaṇām tīvra manda tā upapatteḥ karma saṃcayānām ca utkarṣa apakarṣa bhāvāt  nānāvidha ekavidha bhāvāt ca karmaṇām sukha duḥkha bheda upapattiḥ soyam hetu bheda abhāvāt  dṛṣṭaḥ sukha duḥkha bhedaḥ  na syāt iti pratyakṣa virodhaḥ tathā anumāna virodhaḥ dṛṣṭam hi puruṣa guṇa vyavasthānāt  sukha duḥkha vyavasthānam uyaḥ khalu cetanāvān sādhana nirvartanīyam sukham buddhvā tad īpsan sādhana avāptaye yatate sa sukhena yujyate na viparītaḥ yaḥ ca sādhana nirvartanīyam duḥkham buddhvā tad jihāsuḥ sādhana pari varjanāya yatate sa duḥkhena tyajyate na viparītaḥ na asti ca idam yatnam antareṇa cetanānām sukha duḥkha vyavasthānam tena api cetana guṇa antara vyavasthā kṛtena bhavitavyam iti anumānam tad etad  akarma nimitte sukha duḥkha yoge virudhyate iti tad ca guṇa antaram asaṃvedya tvāt adṛṣṭam vipāka kāla aniyamāt ca avyavasthitam buddhi ādayaḥ tu saṃvedyāḥ ca apavargiṇaḥ ca iti atha āgama virodhaḥ bahu khalu ida bhārṣam ṛṣīṇām upadeśa jātam anuṣṭhāna pari varjana āśrayam upadeśa phalam ca śarīriṇām varṇa āśrama vibhāgena anuṣṭhāna lakṣaṇā pravṛttiḥ parivarjana lakṣaṇā nivṛttiḥ tad ca ubhayam etasyām dṛṣṭau anāsti karma su caritam duścaritam vā akarma nimittaḥ puruṣāṇām sukha duḥkha yogaḥ itiviruddhyate sā iyam pāpiṣṭhānām mithyādṛṣṭiḥ aakarma nimittā śarīra sṛṣṭiḥ akarma nimittaḥ sukha duḥkha yogaḥ iti iti vātsyāyanīye nyāya bhāṣye tṛtīyā adhyāya dvitīyam āhnikam samāptam tṛtīya adhyāyaḥ ca samāptaḥ #################################################################### atha saṭīke nyāya bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam manasaḥ  anantaram pravṛttiḥ parīkṣitavyā tatra khalu yāvat  dharma adharma āśraya śarīra ādi parīkṣitam sarvā sā pravṛtteḥ parīkṣā iti āha tathā parīkṣitā iti pravṛtti anantarāḥ tarhi doṣāḥ parīkṣyantām ityata āha parīkṣitā iti buddhi samāna āśraya tvāt ātma guṇāḥ pravṛtti hetu tvāt  punarbhava pratisaṃdhāna sāmarthyāt ca saṃsāra hetavaḥ saṃsārasya anādi tvādanādinā prabandhena pravartante mithyājñāna nivṛttiḥ tattva jñānāt tad nivṛttau rāga dveṣa prabandha ucchede apavarga iti prādurbhāva ti rodhāna dharmakā iti evamādi uktam doṣāṇām iti pravartanā lakṣaṇā doṣāḥ iti uktam tathā ca ime māna īrṣyā asūyā vicikitsā matsara ādayaḥ te kasmāt na upasaṃkhyāyante iti ata āha teṣām doṣāṇām trayaḥ  rāśayaḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ rāga pakṣaḥ kāmaḥ  matsaraḥ spṛhā tṛṣṇā lobha iti dveṣapakṣaḥ krodha īrṣyā asūyā drohaḥ  amarṣa iti mohapakṣaḥ mithyājñānam vicikitsā mānaḥ pramāda iti trairāśyāt na upasaṃkhyāyante iti lakṣaṇasya tarhi  abhedāt  tri tvam anupapannam na anupapannam rāga dveṣa moha artha antara bhāvāt āsakti lakṣaṇaḥ  rāgaḥ amarṣa lakṣaṇaḥ  dveṣaḥ mithyā pratipatti lakṣaṇaḥ  moha iti etad  pratayā ātma vedanīyam sarva śarīriṇām vijānāti ayam śarīrī rāgam utpannam aasti me adhyātmam rāga dharmaḥ iti virāgam ca vijānāti anāsti me adhyātmam rāga dharmaḥ iti evam itarayoḥ api iti māna īrṣyā asūyā prabhṛtayaḥ tu trairāśyam anupatitā iti na upasaṃkhyāyante na artha antaram rāga ādayaḥ kasmāt  eka pratyanīka bhāvāt  tattva jñānam samyak matiḥ ārya prajñā saṃbodha iti emam idam pratyanīkam trayāṇām iti eka pratyanīkāḥ pṛthivyām śyāmādayaḥ  agni saṃyogena ekena eka yonayaḥ ca pāka jā iti sati ca artha antara bhāve mohaḥ pāpaḥ pāpa taraḥ  vā dvau  abhipretya uktam kasmāt  na amūḍhasya itara utpatteḥ amūḍhasya rāga dveṣau na utpadyete mūḍhasya tu yathāsaṃkalpam utpattiḥ viṣayeṣu rañjanīyāḥ saṃkalpā rāga hetavaḥ kopanīyāḥ saṃkalpā dveṣa hetavaḥ ubhaye ca saṃkalpā na mithyā pratipatti lakṣaṇa tvāt  mohāt anye tau  imau moha yonī rāga dveṣau  iti tattva jñānāt ca moha nivṛttau rāga dveṣa anutpattiḥ iti eka pratyanīka bhāva upapattiḥ evam ca kṛtvā tattva jñānāt duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣam iti ājñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantarā pāyāt apavargaḥ iti vyākhyātam iti prāptaḥ tarhi anyat hi nimittam anyat ca naimittakam iti doṣa nimitta tvāt adoṣaḥ  moha iti pravartanā lakṣaṇā doṣaḥ iti anena doṣa lakṣaṇena avarudhyate doṣeṣu moha iti dravyāṇām guṇānām vā anekavidha vikalpaḥ  nimitta naimittaka bhāvaḥ  tulya jātīyānām dṛṣṭa iti doṣān antaram pretyabhāvaḥ tasya asiddhiḥ ātmanaḥ  nitya tvāt  na khalu nityam kiñcid  jāyate mriyate vā iti janma maraṇayoḥ nitya tvāt ātmanaḥ  anupapattiḥ ubhayam ca pretyabhāva iti tatra ayam siddha anuvādaḥ nityoyam ātmā praiti pūrva śarīram jahāti mriyate iti pretya ca pūrva śarīram hitvā bhavati jāyate śarīra antaram upādatte iti tad ca etad ubhayam punar utpattiḥ pretyabhāva iti tad ca etad  nitya tve saṃbhavati iti yasya tu sattva utpādaḥ sattva nirodhaḥ pretyabhāvaḥ tasya kṛta hānam akṛta abhyāgamaḥ ca doṣaḥ uccheda hetu vāde ṛṣi upadeśāḥ ca anarthakā iti katham utpattiḥ iticed  kena prakāreṇa kindharmakāt  kāraṇāt  vyaktam śarīram utpadyate iti vyaktāt  bhūta samākhyātāt  pṛthivī āditaḥ parama sūkṣmāt  nityāt  vyaktam śarīra indriya viṣaya upakaraṇa ādhāram prajñātam dravyam utpadyate vyaktam ca khalu indriya grāhyam tad sāmānyāt kāraṇam api vyaktam kim sāmānyam rūpa ādi guṇa yogaḥ rūpa ādi guṇa yuktebhyaḥ pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ  nityebhyaḥ  rūpa ādi guṇa yuktam śarīra ādi utpadyate pratyakṣa prāmāṇyāt  dṛṣṭaḥ  hi rūpa ādi guṇa yuktebhyaḥ  mṛd prabhṛtibhyaḥ tathābhūtasya dravyasya utpādaḥ tena ca adṛṣṭasya anumānam iti rūpa ādīnām anvaya darśanāt  prakṛti vikārayoḥ pṛthivī ādīnām nityānām atīndriyāṇām kāraṇa bhāva u anumīyate iti idam api pratyakṣam na khalu vyaktāt  ghaṭāt  vyaktaḥ  ghaṭa utpadyamānaḥ  dṛśyate iti vyaktāt  vyaktasya anutpatti darśanāt na vyaktam kāraṇam iti na brūmaḥ sarvam sarvasya kāraṇam iti kim tu yad utpadyate vyaktam dravyam tad  tathābhūtāt eva utpadyate iti vyaktam ca tad  mṛd dravyam kapāla saṃjñakam yatas  ghaṭa utpadyate na ca etad  nihnuvānaḥ kvacid abhyanujñām labdhum arhati iti tad etad tattvam atas  param prāvādukānām dṛṣṭayaḥ pradarśyante asataḥ sat utpadyate iti ayam pakṣaḥ kasmāt  upamṛdya prādurbhāvāt  upamṛdya bījam aṅkura utpadyate na anupamṛdya na ced  bīja upamarde aṅkura kāraṇam anupamardepi bījasya aṅkura utpattiḥ syāt iti atra abhidhīyate aupamṛdya prādurbhāvāt iti ayuktaḥ prayogaḥ vyāghātāt  yad upamṛdnāti na tad upamṛdya prādurbhavitum arhati vidyamāna tvāt  yad ca prādurbhavati na tena aprādurbhūtena avidyamānena upamarda iti ati iti ca anāgate ca avidyamāne kāraka śabdaḥ prayujyante putraḥ  janiṣyate janiṣyamāṇam putram abhinandati putrasya janiṣyamāṇasya nāma karoti abhūt  kumbhaḥ  bhinnam kumbham anuśocati bhinnasya kumbhasya kapālāni ajātāḥ putrāḥ pitaram tāpayanti iti bahulam bhāktāḥ prayogā dṛśyante kā punar iyam bhaktiḥ ānantarya bhaktiḥ ānantarya sāmarthyāt upamṛdya prādurbhāva arthaḥ prādurbhaviṣyan  aṅkura upamṛdgāti iti bhāktam kartṛ tvam iti na vinaṣṭāt  bījāt aṅkura utpadyate iti tasmāt na abhāvāt  bhāva utpattiḥ iti uṣamarda prādurbhāvayoḥ paurvāparya niyamaḥ kramaḥ sa khalva bhāvāt  bhāva utpatteḥ hetuḥ nirdiśyate sa ca na pratiṣidhyate iti vyāhata vyūhānām avayavānām pūrva vyūha nivṛttau vyūha antarāt  dravya niṣpattiḥ na abhāvāt  bīja avayavāḥ kutaścid nimittāt  prādurbhūta akriyāḥ pūrva vyūham jahati vyūha antaram ca āpadyante vyūha antarāt aṅkura utpadyate dṛśyante khalu avayavāḥ tad saṃyogāḥ ca aṅkura utpatti hetavaḥ na ca anivṛtte pūrva vyūhe bīja avayavānām śakyam vyūha antareṇa bhavitum iti upamarda prādurbhāvayoḥ paurvāparya niyamaḥ kramaḥ tasmāt na abhāvāt  bhāva utpattiḥ iti na ca anyat  bīja avayavebhyaḥ  aṅkura utpatti kāraṇam iti upapadyate bīja upādāna niyama iti atha apara āha puruṣoyam samīhamānaḥ  na avaśyam samīhā phalam prāpnoti tena anumīyate para adhīnām puruṣasya karma phala ārādhanam iti yad adhīnam sa īśvaraḥ tasmāt īśvaraḥ kāraṇam iti īśvara adhīnā ced  phala niṣpattiḥ syāt  api tarhi puruṣasya samīhām antareṇa phalam niṣpadyeta iti puruṣakāram īśvaraḥ  anugṛhṇāti phalāya puruṣasya yatamānasya īśvaraḥ phalam saṃpādayati iti yadā na saṃpādayati tadā puruṣa karma aphalam bhavati iti tasmāt  īśvara kārita tvāt  ahetuḥ puruṣa karma abhāve phala aniṣpatteḥ iti guṇa viśiṣṭam ātma antaram īśvaraḥ tasya ātma kalpāt  kalpa antara anupapattiḥ adharma mithyā jñāna pramāda hānyā dharma jñāna samādhi saṃpadā ca viśiṣṭam ātma antaram īśvaraḥ tasya ca dharma samādhi phalam aṇima ādi aṣṭavidham aiśvaryam saṃkalpa anuvidhāyī ca asya dharmaḥ pratyātma vṛttīn dharma adharma saṃcayān pṛthivī ādīni ca bhūtāni pravartayati evam ca sva kṛta abhyāgamasya ālopena nirmāṇa prāka ambham īśvarasya sva kṛta karma phalam veditavyam āpta kalpaḥ ca ayam uyathā pitā apatyānām tathā pitṛ bhūta īśvaraḥ  bhūtānām na ca ātma kalpāt anyaḥ kalpaḥ saṃbhavati na tāvat asya buddhim vinā kaścid  dharmaḥ  liṅga bhūtaḥ śakya upapādayitum āgamāt ca draṣṭā boddhā sarvajñātā īśvara iti buddhi ādibhiḥ ca ātma liṅgaiḥ nirupākhyam īśvaram pratyakṣa anumāna āgama viṣaya atītam kaḥ rakta upapādayitum sva kṛta abhyāgama lopena ca pravartamānasya asya yad uktam pratiṣedha jātam akarma nimitte śarīra sarge tad sarvam prasajyate iti apara idānīm āha animittā śarīra ādi upattiḥ kaṇṭaka taikṣṇya ādi darśanāt  kaṇṭakasya taikṣṇyam parvata dhātūnām citra tā grāvṇām ślakṣṇa tā ninirmittam ca upādānam dṛṣṭam tathā śarīra sarga upī iti animittatas  bhāva utpattiḥ iti ucyate yatas ca utpadyate tad nimittam animittasya nimitta tvāt  na animittā bhāva utpattiḥ iti anyat hi nimittam anyat ca nimitta pratyākhyānam na ca pratyākhyānam eva pratyākhyeyam yathā aanudakaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ iti na udaka pratiṣedha udakam bhavati iti sa khalu ayam vādaḥ aakarma nimittaḥ śarīra ādi sargaḥ iti etasmāt na bhidyate abhedāt  tad pratiṣedhena eva pratiṣiddhaḥ  veditavya iti anye tu manyante kim anityam nāma yasya kadācid  bhāvaḥ tad anityam utpatti dharmakam anutpannam na asti vināśa dharmakam ca avinaṣṭam na asti kim punar  sarvam bhautikam ca śarīra ādi abhautikam ca buddhi ādi tad ubhayam utpatti vināśa dharmakam vijñāyate tasmāt tad sarvam anityam iti yadi tāvat  sarvasya anitya tā nityā tad nitya tvāt  na sarvam anityam atha anityā tasyām avidyamānāyām sarvam nityam iti tasyāḥ  anitya tāyāḥ  api anitya tvam katham yathā agniḥ dāhyam vināśya anuvinaśyati evam sarvasya anitya tā sarvam vināśya anuvinaśyati iti ayam khalu vādaḥ  nityam pratyācaṣṭe nityasya ca pratyākhyānam anupapannam kasmāt  yathā upalabdhi vyavasthānāt  yasya utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam upalabhyate pramāṇataḥ tad anityam yasya na upalabhyate tad  viparītam na ca parama sūkṣmāṇām bhūtānām ākāśa kāla diś ātma manasām tad guṇānām ca keṣāñcid  sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām ca utpatti vināśa dharmaka tvam pramāṇata upalabhyate tasmāt  nityāni etāni iti ayam anya ekāntaḥ bhūtamātram idam sarvam tāni ca nityāni bhūta uccheda anupapatteḥ iti utpatti kāraṇam ca upalabhyate vināśa kāraṇam ca tad  sarva nitya tve vyāhanyate iti yasya utpatti vināśa kāraṇam upalabhyate iti manyase na tad  bhūta lakṣaṇa hīnam artha antaram gṛhyate bhūta lakṣaṇa avarodhāt  bhūtamātram idam iti  ayuktaḥ  ayam pratiṣedha iti kāraṇa samāna guṇasya utpattiḥ kāraṇam ca upalabhyate na ca etad ubhayam nitya viṣayam na ca utpatti tad kāraṇa upalabdhiḥ śakyā pratyākhyātum na ca āviṣayā kācid upalabdhiḥ upalabdhi sāmarthyāt  kāraṇena samāna guṇam kāryam utpadyate iti anumīyate sa khalu upalabdheḥ viṣaya iti evam ca tad lakṣaṇa avarodha upapatitiḥ iti utpatti vināśa kāraṇa prayuktasya jñātuḥ prayatnaḥ  dṛṣṭa iti prasiddhaḥ ca avayavī tad dharmā utpatti vināśa dharmā ca avayavī siddha iti śabda karma buddhi ādīnām ca avyāptiḥ pañcabhūta nitya tvāt  tad lakṣaṇa ārodhāt ca iti anena śabda karma buddhi sukha duḥkha icchā udvaṣa prayatnāḥ ca na vyāptāḥ tasmāt anekāntaḥ svapna viṣaya abhimānavat  mithyā upalabdhiḥ iticed  bhūta aupalabdhau tulyam yathā svapne viṣaya abhimāna evam utpatti kāraṇa abhimāna iti evam ca etad  bhūta upalabdhau tulyam upṛthivī ādi upalabdhiḥ api svapna viṣaya abhimānavat prasajyate pṛthivī ādi abhāve sarva vyavahāra vilopa iti ced  tad itaratra samānam utpatti vināśa kāraṇa upalabdhi viṣayasya api abhāve sarva vyavahāra vilopa iti soyam nityānām atīndriya tvāt aviṣaya tvāt ca utpatti vināśayoḥ asvapna viṣaya abhimānavat iti ahetuḥ iti avasthitasya upādānasya dharma mātram nivartate dharma mātram upajāyate sa khalu utpatti vināśayoḥ viṣayaḥ yad ca upajāyate tad  prāk api upajananāt asti yad ca nivartate tad  nivṛttam api asti iti evam ca sarvasya nitya tvam iti ayam upajana iyam nivṛttiḥ iti vyavasthā na upapadyate upajāta nivṛttayoḥ vidyamāna tvāt  ayam dharma upajātaḥ  ayam nivṛtta iti sadbhāvā viśeṣāt avyavasthā idānīm upajana nivṛttī na idānīm iti kāla vyavasthā na upapadyate sarvadā vidyamāna tvāt  asya dharmasya upajana nivṛttī na asya iti vyavasthā anupapattiḥ ubhayoḥ aviśeṣāt  anāgataḥ  atīta iti ca kāla vyavasthā anupapattiḥ vartamānasya sadbhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt avidyamānasya ātma lābha upajanaḥ  vidyamānasya ātma hānam nivṛttiḥ iti etasmin sati na ete doṣāḥ tasmāt  yad uktam aprāk api upajananāt asti nivṛttam ca asti iti tad ayuktam iti ayam anya ekāntaḥ sarvam nānā na kaścid ekaḥ bhāvaḥ vidyate kasmāt  bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthaktvāt  ubhau  asya lakṣaṇam abhidhānam yena lakṣyate bhāvaḥ sa samākhyā śabdaḥ tasya pṛthak viṣaya tvāt  sarvobhāva samākhyā śabdaḥ samūha vācī akumbhaḥ iti saṃjñā śabdaḥ  gandha rasa rūpa sparśa samūhe badhna pārśva grīvā ādi samūhe ca vartate nidarśana mātram ca idam iti aanekavidha lakṣaṇaiḥ iti madhyama pada lopī samāsaḥ gandha ādibhiḥ ca guṇaiḥ budhnā ādibhiḥ ca avayavaiḥ saṃbaddha ekaḥ  bhāvaḥ niṣpadyate guṇa vyatiriktam ca dravyam avayava atiriktaḥ ca avayavi iti vibhakta nyāyam ca etad ubhayam iti ana kaścid ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti ayuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt  lakṣaṇa vyavasthānāt eva yad iha lakṣaṇam bhāvasya saṃjñā śabda bhūtam tad ekasmin vyavasthitam ayam kumbham adrākṣam tam spṛśāmi ayam eva asprākṣam tam paśyāmi iti na aṇu samūhaḥ  gṛhyate iti aṇu samūhe ca āgṛhyamāṇe yad  gṛhyate tad ekam eva iti atha api etad anūktam na asti ekaḥ  bhāvaḥ yasmāt samudāyaḥ eka anupapatteḥ na asti eva samūhaḥ na asti ekaḥ  bhāvaḥ yasmāt  samūhe bhāva śabda prayogaḥ ekasya ca anupapatteḥ samūhaḥ  na upapadyate eka samuccayaḥ  hi samūha iti vyāhata tvāt anupapannam anāsti ekaḥ  bhāvaḥ iti yasya pratiṣedhaḥ pratijñāyate asamūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti hetum bruvatā sa eva abhyunujñāyate eka samuccayaḥ  hi samūha iti samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti ca samūham āśritya pratyekam samūhi pratiṣedhaḥ na asti ekaḥ  bhāva iti soyam ubhayatas  vyāghātāt  yad kiñcana vāda iti ayam apara ekāntaḥ yāvat  bhāva jātam tad sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt  bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ aasan gauraśva ātmanā aanaśvaḥ  gauḥ aasan   aśvaḥ  gavā ātmanā aagaurava śvaḥ iti  asat pratyayasya pratiṣedhasya ca bhāva śabdena sāmānādhikaraṇyāt sarvam abhāva iti pratijñā vākye padayoḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ ca vyāghātāt ayuktam anekasya aśeṣa tā sarva śabdasya arthaḥ bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ ca abhāva śabdasya arthaḥ pūrvam sa upākhyam uttaram nirupākhyam tatra samupākhyāyamānam katham nirupākhyam abhāvaḥ syāt iti na jātu abhāvaḥ  nirupākhyaḥ  aneka tayā aśeṣa tayā śakyaḥ pratijñātum iti sarvam etad abhāva iti ced  yad idam sarvam iti manyase tad bhāva iti evam ced  anivṛttaḥ  vyāghātaḥ anekam aśeṣam ca iti na abhāva pratyayena śakyam bhavitum asti ca ayam pratyayaḥ sarvam iti tasmāt na abhāva iti pratijñā hetvoḥ ca vyāghātaḥ asarvam abhāvaḥ iti bhāva pratiṣedhaḥ pratijñā abhāveṣu itaretara abhāva siddheḥ itihetuḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāvam anujñāya āśritya ca itaretarābhāva siddhau sarvam abhāva iti ucyate yadi sarvam abhāvaḥ bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddheḥ iti na upapadyate atha bhāveṣu itaretarābhāva siddhi sarvam abhāva iti na upapadyate sūtreṇa ca abhisaṃbandhaḥ na sarvam abhāvaḥ kasmāt  svena bhāvena sadbhāvāt  bhāvānām svena dharmeṇa bhāvā bhavanti iti pratijñāyate kaḥ ca svar  dharmaḥ  bhāvānām dravya guṇa karmaṇām sadādi sāmānyam dravyāṇām kriyāvat iti evamādiḥ viśeṣaḥ sparśa paryantāḥ pṛthivyāḥ  iti ca pratyekam ca anantaḥ  bhedaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa samavāyānām ca viśiṣṭā dharmā gṛhyante soyam abhāvasya nirupākhya tvāt  saṃpratyāyakaḥ  artha bhedaḥ  na syāt  asti tvayam tasmāt na sarvam abhāva iti atha vā na svabhāva siddheḥ bhāvānām iti svarūpa siddheḥ iti gauriti prayujyamāne śabde jāti viśiṣṭam dravyam gṛhyate na abhāva mātram yadi ca sarvam abhāvaḥ gauriti abhāvaḥ pratīyeta gaḥ śabdena ca abhāva ucyeta yasmāt tu gaḥ śabda prayoge dravya viśeṣaḥ pratīyate na abhāvaḥ tasmāt ayuktam iti atha vā na svabhāva siddheḥ iti aasan gauraśva ātmanā iti gavā ātmanā kasmāt na ucyate avacanāt  agava ātmanā gaurasti iti svabhāva siddhiḥ aanaśvaḥ  aśvaḥ iti vā agauragauḥ iti vā kasmāt na ucyate avacanāt  svena rūpeṇa vidyamāna tā dravyasya itivijñāyate avyatireka pratiṣedhe ca bhāvānām asat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyam saṃyoga ādi saṃbandhaḥ  vyatirekaḥ atra avyatirekaḥ  abheda ākhya saṃbandhaḥ tad pratiṣedhe ca asat pratyaya sāmānādhikaraṇyam yathā ana santi kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti aasan gauraśva ātmanā aanaśvaḥ gauḥ iti ca gavā śvayoḥ avyatirekaḥ pratiṣidhyate gavā śvayoḥ eka tvam na asti iti tasmin pratiṣidhyamāne bhāvena gavā sāma ādhi karaṇyam asat pratyayasya aasan gauraśva ātmanā iti yathā ana santi kuṇḍe badarāṇi iti kuṇḍe badara saṃyoge pratiṣidhyamāne sadbhiḥ asat pratyayasya sāma ādhikaraṇyam iti apekṣā akṛtam āpekṣikam hrasva apekṣā kṛtam dīrgham dīrgha apekṣā kṛtam hrasvam na svena ātmanā avasthitam kiñcid  kasmāt  apekṣā sāmarthyāt  tasmāt na svabhāva siddhiḥ bhāvānām iti yadi hrasva apekṣā kṛtam dīrgham kim idānīm apekṣya ahrasvam iti gṛhyate atha dīrgha apekṣā kṛtam hrasvam dīrgham anāpekṣikam evam itaretara āśrayayoḥ eka abhāve anyatara abhāvāt ubhaya abhāva iti apekṣā vyavasthā anupapannā svabhāva siddhau   asatyām samayoḥ parimaṇḍalayoḥ vā dravyayoḥ āpekṣike dīrghatva hrasva tve kasmāt na bhavataḥ apekṣāyām anapekṣāyām ca dravyayoḥ abhedaḥ yāvatī dravye apekṣamāṇe tāvatī eva anapekṣamāṇe na anyataratra bhedaḥ āpekṣika tve tu sati  anyataratra viśeṣa upajanaḥ syāt iti kim apekṣā sāmarthyam iticed  dvayoḥ grahaṇe atiśya grahaṇa upapattiḥ dve dravye paśyan ekatra vidyamānam atiśayam gṛhṇāti tad  dīrgham iti vyavasyati yad ca hīnam gṛhṇāti tad  hrasvam iti vyavasyati iti etad ca apekṣā sāmarthyam iti atha ime saṃkhyā ekāntāḥ sarvam ekam sat  aviśeṣāt  sarvam dvedhā nitya anityabhedāt  sarvam tredhā jñātā jñānam jñeyam iti sarvam caturdhā pramātā pramāṇam prameyam pramitiḥ iti evam yathā saṃbhavam anye api iti tatra parīkṣā yadi sādhya sādhānayoḥ nānātvam ekāntaḥ  na sidhyati vyatirekāt  atha sādhya sādhanayoḥ abhedaḥ evam api ekāntaḥ  na sidhyati sādhana abhāvāt  na hi tam antareṇa kasyacid  siddhiḥ iti na saṃkhyā ekāntānām asiddhiḥ kasmāt  kāraṇasya avayava bhāvāt  avayasavaḥ kaścid  sādhana bhūta  iti  avyatirekaḥ evam dvaita ādīnām api iti kāraṇasya avayava bhāvāt  iti ahetuḥ kasmāt  asarvam ekam iti anapavargeṇa pratijñāya kasyacid eka tvam ucyate tatra vyapavṛktaḥ  avayavaḥ sādhana bhūtaḥ  na upapadyate evam dvaita ādiṣu api iti te khalu ime saṃkhyā ekāntā yadi viśeṣa kāritasya artha bheda vistarasya pratyākhyānena vartante pratyākṣa anumāna āgama virodhāt  mithyāvādā bhavanti atha abhyanujñānena vartante samāna dharma kāritaḥ  artha saṃgrahaḥ  viśeṣa kāritaḥ ca artha bheda iti evam ekānta tvam jahati iti te khalu ete tattva jñāna praviveka artham ekāntāḥ parīkṣitā iti pretyabhāva anantaram phalam tasmin apacati dogdhi iti sadyas  phalam odana payasī akarṣati vapati iti kāla antare phalam śasya adhigama iti asti ca iyam kriyā agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāmaḥ iti etasyāḥ phale saṃśayaḥ svargaḥ phalam śrūyate tad ca bhinne asmin deha bhedāt utpadyate iti na sadyas  grāma ādi kāmānām ārambha phalam iti dhvastāyām pravṛttau pravṛtteḥ phalam na kāraṇam antareṇa utpattam arhati na khalu vai vinaṣṭāt  kāraṇāt  kiñcid utpadyate iti yathā phala arthinā vṛkṣa mūle seka ādi parikarma kriyate taṃmin  ca pradhvaste pṛthivī dhātuḥ ap dhātunā saṃgṛhīte āntareṇa tejasā pacyamānaḥ  rasa dravyam nirvartayati sa dravya bhūtaḥ  rasaḥ  vṛkṣa anugataḥ pāka viśiṣṭaḥ  vyūha viśeṣeṇa saṃniviśamānaḥ parṇa ādi phalam nirvartayati evam pariṣeka ādi karma cā arthavat  na ca vinaṣṭāt  phala niṣpattiḥ tathā pravṛttyā saṃskāraḥ  dharma adharma lakṣaṇaḥ  janyate sa jātaḥ  nimitta antara anugṛhītaḥ kāla antare phalam niṣpādayati iti uktam ca etad  pūrva kṛta phala anubandhāt tad utpattiḥ iti tad idam prāṅ niṣpatteḥ niṣpadyamānam prāk niṣpatteḥ niṣpatti dharmakam na asat  upādāna
