niyamāt  kasyacid utpattaye kiñcid upādeyam na sarvam sarvasya iti  asadbhāve niyamaḥ  na upapadyate iti na sat  prāk utpatteḥ vidyamānasya utpattiḥ anupapanna iti na sat asat sat asatoḥ vaidharmyāt  asat iti artha abhyanujñā aasat iti artha pratiṣedhaḥ etayoḥ vyāghātaḥ  vaidharmyam vyāghātāt avyatireka anupapattiḥ iti yad punaruktam aprāk utpatteḥ kāryam na asat  upādāna niyamāt iti idam asya utpattaye samartham na sarvam iti prāk utpatteḥ niyata kāraṇam kāryam buddhyā siddham utpatti niyama darśanāt  tasmāt upādāna niyamasya upapattiḥ sati tu kārye prāk utpatteḥ utpattiḥ eva na asti iti mūla seka ādi parikarma phalam ca ubhayam vṛkṣa āśrayam karma ca iha śarīre phalam ca amutra iti āśraya vyatirekāt ahetuḥ iti prītiḥ ātma pratyakṣa tvāt ātma āśrayā tad āśrayam eva karma dharma saṃjñitam dharmasya ātma guṇa tvāt  tasmāt āśraya vyatireka anupapattiḥ iti putra ādi phalam nirdiśyate na prītiḥ grāma kāmaḥ  yajeta putra kāmaḥ  yajeta iti tatra yad uktam aprītiḥ phalam iti etad ayuktam putra ādi saṃbandhāt phalam prīti lakṣaṇam utpadyate iti putra ādiṣu phalavat upacāraḥ  yathā anne prāṇa śabdaḥ annam vai prāṇāḥ iti phala anantaram duḥkham uddiṣṭa m uktam ca bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti tad  kim idam pratyātma vedanīyasya sarva jantu pratyakṣasya sukhasya pratyākhyānam āhosvit anyaḥ kalpaḥ iti anya iti āha katham na vai sarva loka sākṣikam sukham śakyam pratyākhyātum ayam tu janma maraṇa prabandha anubhava nimittāt  duḥkhāt  nirviṇṇasya duḥkham jihāsataḥ  duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanā upadeśaḥ  duḥkha hāna artha iti kayā yuktyā sarve khalu sattva nikāyāḥ sarvāṇi utpatti sthānāni sarvaḥ punarbhavaḥ  bādhana anuṣaktaḥ  duḥkha sāhacaryāt  bādhanā lakṣaṇam duḥkham iti uktam ṛṣibhiḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate atra ca hetuḥ upādīyate janma jāyate iti śarīra indriya buddhayaḥ śarīra ādīnām saṃsthāna viśiṣṭānām prādurbhāva utpattiḥ vividhā ca bādhanā hīnā madhyamā utkṛṣṭā ca iti utkṛṣṭā nārakiṇām tiraścām tu madhyamā manuṣya apām hīnāḥ devānām hīnatarā vīta rāgāṇām ca evam sarvam utpatti sthānam vividha bādhana anuṣaktam paśyataḥ sukhe tad sādhaneṣu ca śarīra indriya buddhiṣu duḥkha saṃjñā vyavatiṣṭhate duḥkha saṃjñā vyavasthānāt sarva lokeṣu  anabhirati saṃjñā bhavati anabhirati saṃjñām upāsīnasya sarva loka viṣaya atṛṣṇā vicchidyate tṛṣṇā prahāṇāt  sarva duḥkhāt  vimucyate iti yathā viṣa yogāt  payaḥ  viṣayam iti budhyamānaḥ  na upādatte anupādadānaḥ  maraṇa duḥkham na āpnoti duḥkha uddeśaḥ tu na sukhasya pratyākhyānam kasmāt  khalu ayam duḥkha uddeśaḥ sukhasya pratyākhyānam kasmāt  sukhasya antarāla niṣpateḥ niṣpadyate khalu bādhana antarāleṣu sukham pratyātma vedanīyam śarīriṇām tad aśakyam pratyākhyātum iti atha api sukhasya duḥkha uddeśena iti prakaraṇāt  paryeṣaṇam prārthanā viṣaya arjana tṛṣṇā paryeṣaṇasya doṣaḥ  yad ayam vedayamānaḥ prārthayate tad ca asya prārthitam na saṃpadyate saṃpadya vā vipadyate nyūnam vā saṃpadyate bahu pratyanīkam vā saṃpadyate iti etasmāt  paryeṣaṇa doṣāt  nānāvidhaḥ  mānasaḥ saṃtāpaḥ  bhavati evam vedayataḥ paryeṣaṇa doṣāt  bādhanāyā anavṛttiḥ bādhanā nivṛtteḥ duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam uddiśyate anena kāraṇena duḥkham janma na tu sukhasya abhāvāt iti atha api etad anūktam kāmam kāmayamānasya yadā kāmaḥ samṛdhyate atha enam aparaḥ kāmaḥ kṣipram eva prabādhate api ced udanemi samantāt  bhūmim ālabhate sa gava aśvān na sa tena dhanena dhana eṣī tṛpyati kim nu sukham dhana kāme iti duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanā upadeśaḥ kriyate ayam khalu sukha saṃvedane vyavasthitaḥ sukham parama puruṣa artham manyate na sukhāt anyat  niḥśreyasam asti sukhe prāpte caritārthaḥ kṛta karaṇīyaḥ bhavati mithyā saṃkalpāt  mukhe tad sādhaneṣu ca viṣayeṣu saṃrajyate saṃraktaḥ sukhāya ghaṭate ghaṭamānasya asya janma jarā vyādhi prāyaṇa aniṣṭa saṃyoga iṣṭa viyoga prārthita anupapatti nimittam anekavidham yāvat  duḥkham utpadyate tam duḥkha vikalpam sukham iti abhimanyate sukha aṅga bhūtam duḥkham na duḥkham anāsādya śakyam sukham avāptum tādarthyāt  sukham eva idam iti sukha saṃjñā upahata prajñaḥ ajāyasya mriyasva saṃghāva iti saṃsāram na ativartate tad asyāḥ sukha saṃjñā anayāḥ pratipakṣaḥ  duḥkha saṃjñā bhāvanam upadiśyate duḥkha anuṣaṅgāt  duḥkham janma iti na sukhasya abhāvāt  yadi evam kasmāt  aduḥkham janma iti na ucyate soyam evam vācye yad evakā āha duḥkham eva janma iti tena sukha abhāvam jñāpayati iti janma vinigraha arthīyaḥ  vai khalu ayam eva śabdaḥ katham na duḥkham janma svarūpataḥ kim tu duḥkha upacārāt evam sukham api iti etad  anena eva nivartyate na tu duḥkham eva janma iti duḥkha upadeśa anantaram apavargaḥ sa pratyākhyāyate ṛṇa anubandhāt na asti apavargaḥ jāyamānaḥ  ha vai brāhmaṇaḥ tribhiḥ ṛṇaiḥ ṛṇavān jāyate brahmacaryeṇa ṛṣibhyaḥ  yajñena devebhyaḥ prajāyā pitṛbhyaḥ iti ṛṇāni teṣām anubandhaḥ sva karmabhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ karma saṃbandha vacanāt  jarā marya vā etad satram yad agni hotram darśa pūrṇamāsau ca iti ujarayā ha eṣa tasmāt  satrāt vimucyate mṛtyunā ha vā iti ṛṇa anubandhāt apavarga anuṣṭhāna kālaḥ  na asti iti  apavarga abhāvaḥ kleśa anubandhāt nasti apavargaḥ kleśa anubaddha eva ayam mriyate kleśa anubaddhaḥ ca jāyate na asya kleśa anubandha vicchedaḥ  gṛhyate pravṛtti anubandhāt na asti apavargaḥ janma prabhṛti  ayam yāvat prāyaṇam vāc buddhi śarīra ārambheṇa avimuktaḥ  gṛhyate tatra yad uktam duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantarā pāyāt apavargaḥ iti tad anupapannam iti atra abhidhīyate yad tāvat aṛṇa anubandhāt iti ṛṇaiḥ iva ṛṇaiḥ iti ṛṇaiḥ iti na ayam pradhāna śabdaḥ yatra khalu ekaḥ pratyādeyam dadāti dvitīyaḥ ca pratideyam gṛhṇāti tatra asya dṛṣṭa tvāt  pradhānam ṛṇa śabdaḥ na ca etad iha upapadyate pradhāna śabda anupapatteḥ guṇa śabdena ayam anuvādaḥ ṛṇaiḥ iva ṛṇaiḥ iti prayukta upamam ca etad  yathā agniḥ māṇavakaḥ iti anyatra dṛṣṭaḥ ca ayam ṛṇa śabda iha prayujyate yathā agni śabdaḥ  māṇavake katham guṇa śabdena anuvādaḥ nindā prasaṃsā upapatteḥ karma lope ṛṇī iva ṛṇa ādānāt  nindyate karma anuṣṭhāne ca ṛṇī iva ṛṇa dānāt  praśasyate sa eva upama artha iti jāyamānaḥ iti guṇa śabdaḥ viparyaye anadhikārāt  jāyamānaḥ  ha vai brāhmaṇaḥ iti ca śabdaḥ  gṛhasthaḥ saṃpadyamānaḥ jāyamāna iti uyadāyam gṛhasthaḥ  jāyate tadā karmabhiḥ adhikriyate mātṛtaḥ  jāyamānasya anadhikārāt  uyadā tu mātṛtaḥ  jāyate kumāraḥ  na tadā karmabhiḥ adhikriyate arthinaḥ śaktasya ca adhikārāt  arthinaḥ karmabhiḥ adhikāraḥ karma vidhau kāma saṃyoga smṛteḥ agni hotram juhuyāt  svarga kāmaḥ iti evamādi śaktasya ca pravṛtti saṃbhavāt  uśaktasya karmabhiḥ adhikāraḥ pravṛtti saṃbhavāt  uśaktaḥ khalu vihite karmaṇi pravartate na itara iti ubhaya abhāvaḥ tu pradhāna śabda arthe mātṛtaḥ  jāyamāne kumāre ubhayam arthitā śaktiḥ ca na bhavati iti na bhidyate laukikāt  vākyāt  vaidikam vākyam prekṣā pūrva kāri puruṣa praṇīta tvena tatra laukikaḥ tāvat aparīkṣa kopi na jāta mātram kumāram evam brūyāt  aadhīṣva yajasva brahmacaryam cara iti kuta eṣa ṛṣiḥ upapannānavadya vādī upadeśa arthena prayukta upadiśati na khalu vai nartaka undheṣu pravartate na gāyanaḥ  badhireṣu iti upadiṣṭa artha vijñānam ca upadeśa viṣayaḥ yaḥ ca upadiṣṭam artham vijānāti tam pratyupadeśaḥ kriyate na ca etad asti jāyamāna kumārake iti gārhasthya liṅgam ca mantra brāhmaṇam karma abhivadati yad ca mantra brāhmaṇam karma abhivadati tad  patnī saṃbandha ādinā gārhasthya liṅgena upapannam tasmāt  gṛhastha uyam jāyamānaḥ  abhidhīyate iti arthi tvasya ca avipariṇāme jarā maryavāda upapattiḥ yāvat ca asya phalena arthi tvam na vipariṇamate na nivartate tāvat anena karma anuṣṭheyam iti upapadyate jarā maryavādaḥ tam prati iti jarayā ha vā iti āyuṣaḥ turīyasya caturthasya pravrajyā yuktasya vacanam jarayā ha vā eṣa etasmāt vimucyate iti āyuṣaḥ turīyam caturthaṃpravrajyā yuktam jarā iti ucyate tatra hi pravrajyā vidhīyate atyanta jarā saṃyoge jarayā ha vā iti anarthakam aaśaktaḥ  vimucyate iti etad api na upapadyate svayam aśaktasya bāhyām śaktim āha antevāsī vā juhuyāt  brahmaṇā sa parikrītaḥ kṣīra hotā vā juhuyāt  dhanena sa parikrītaḥ iti atha api vihitam vānūdyeta kāmāt vā arthaḥ parikalpyeta vihita anuvacanam nyāyyam iti ṛṇavān iva asvatantraḥ  gṛhya sthaḥ karmasu pravartate iti upapannam vākyasya sāmarthyam phalasya hi sādhanāni prayatna viṣayaḥ  na phalam tāni saṃpannāni phalāya kalpante vihitam ca jāyamānam vidhīyate ca jāyamānam tena yaḥ saṃbadhyate soyam jāyamāna iti pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt iti ced  na pratiṣedhasya api pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt iti pratyakṣataḥ vidhīyate gārhasthyam brāhmaṇena yadi ca aṃśrama antaram abhaviṣyat tad api vyadhāsyat  pratyakṣataḥ pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt na asti āśrama antaram iti na pratiṣedhasya api pratyakṣa vidhāna abhāvāt na pratiṣedha upi vai brāhmaṇena pratyakṣataḥ vidhīyate ana santi āśrama antarāṇi eka eva gṛhastha āśramaḥ iti pratiṣedhasya pratyakṣataḥ aśravaṇāt ayuktam etad iti adhikārāt ca vidhānam vidyā antaravat  yathā śāstra antarāṇi sve sve adhikāre pratyakṣataḥ vidhāyakāni na artha antara abhāvāt  evam idam brāhmaṇam gṛhastha śāstram sve adhikāre pratyakṣataḥ vidhāyakam na āśrama antarāṇām abhāvāt iti ṛc brāhmaṇam ca apavarga abhidhāyy abhidhīyate ṛcaḥ ca brāhmaṇāni cāpa varga abhivādīna bhivanti ṛvaḥ ca tāvat  karmabhiḥ mṛtyum ṛṣayaḥ  niṣeduḥ prajāvantaḥ  draviṇam icchamānāḥ atha apare ṛṣayaḥ  manīṣiṇaḥ param karmabhyaḥ  amṛtatva mānaśuḥ na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena eke amṛtatva mānaśuḥ pareṇa nākam nihitam guhāyām vibhrājate tad  yatayaḥ  viśanti veda aham etaṃpuruṣam mahāntam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt  tam eva viditvā atimṛtyum eti na anyaḥ panthā vidyate ayanāya atha brāhmaṇāni trayaḥ  dharma skandhāḥ yajñaḥ  adhyayanam dānam iti prathamaḥ tapa eva dvitīyaḥ  brahmacārī ācārya kula vāsī iti tṛtīyaḥ  atyantam ātmānam ācārya kule avasādayan sarve eva ete puṇya lokā bhavanti brahma saṃsthaḥ  amṛta tvam eti etam eva pravrājinaḥ  lokam abhīpsantaḥ pravrajanti iti athaḥ khalu āhuḥ kāma maya eva ayam puruṣa iti sa yathākāmaḥ  bhavati tathā akratuḥ bhavati yathākratuḥ bhavati tad karma kurute yad karma kurute tad abhisaṃpadyate iti karmabhiḥ saṃsaraṇam uktvā prakṛtam anyat upadiśanti iti tu kāmayamānaḥ  atha akāmayamānaḥ  yaḥ  akāmaḥ  niṣkām ātma kāma āpta kāmaḥ  bhavati na tasya prāṇā utkrāmanti iha eva samavalīyante brahmā eva san brahmā apyeti iti tatra yad uktam aṛṇa anubandhāt apavarga abhāvaḥ iti etad ayuktam iti yecatvāraḥ pathayaḥ  deva yānāḥ iti ca cātu gaśramya śruteḥ aika āśramya anupapattiḥ phala arthinaḥ ca idam brāhmaṇam jarā maryam vā etad satram yad agrihotram darśa pūrṇamāsau ca iti katham prājāpattyām iṣṭim nirupya nasyām sarva vedasam hutvā ātmani agnīn samāropya brāhmaṇaḥ pravrajet  iti śrūyate tena vijānīmaḥ prajā vitta loka eṣaṇābhyaḥ  vyutthitasya nivṛtte phala arthi tve samāropaṇam vidhīyate iti evam ca brāhmaṇāni saḥ  anyat  vratam upākariṣyamāṇaḥ  yājñavalkyaḥ  maitreyīm itihā uvāca pravrajiṣyan vā are aham asmāt  sthānāt asmi hanta te anayā kātyāyanyā sahāntam karavāṇi iti atha api ukta anuśāsanā asi maitreyi etāvat are khalu amṛta tvam iti ha uktvā yājñavalkyaḥ pravavrāja iti jarā marye ca karmaṇi  aviśeṣeṇa kalpyamāne sarvasya pātra caya antāni karmāṇi iti prasajyate tatra eṣaṇā vyutthānam na śrūyeta etad ha sma vai tad pūrve brāhmaṇā anūcānā vidvāṃsaḥ prajām na kāmayante kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ  yeṣām na uyam ātma ayam loka iti te ha sma putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti iti eṣaṇābhyaḥ ca vyutthitasya pātra caya antāni karmāṇi na upapadyante iti na aviśeṣeṇa kartuḥ prayojakam phalam bhavati iti cāturāśramya vidhānāt cetihāsa purāṇa dharma śāstreṣu aikāśramyā anupapattiḥ tad apramāṇam iticet na pramāṇena prāmāṇya abhyanujñānāt pramāṇena khalu brāhmaṇena itihāsa purāṇasya prāmāṇyam abhyanujñāyate te vā khalu ete atharva aṅgirasa etad itihāsa purāṇam abhyavadan itihāsa purāṇam pañcamam vedānām vedaḥ iti tasmāt  ayuktam etad  aprāmāṇyam iti aprāmāṇye ca dharma śāstrasya prāṇabhṛtām vyavahāra lopāt  loka uccheda prasaṅgaḥ draṣṭṛ pravaktṛ sāmānyāt ca aprāmāṇya anupapattiḥ ye eva mantra brāhmaṇasya draṣṭāraḥ pravaktāraḥ ca te khalu itihāsa purāṇasya dharma śāstrasya ca iti viṣaya vyavasthānāt ca yathā viṣayam prāmāṇyam anyaḥ  mantra brāhmaṇasya viṣayaḥ  anyaḥ ca itihāsa purāṇa dharma śāstraṇām iti yajñaḥ  mantra brāhmaṇasya loka vṛttam itihāsa purāṇasaya loka vyavahāra vyavasthānam dharma śāstrasya viṣayaḥ tatra ekena na sarvam vyavasthāpyate iti yathā viṣayam etāni pramāṇāni indriya ādivat iti yad punar etad  kleśa anubandhasya avicchedāt iti yathā suṣuptasya khalu svapna adarśane rāga anubandhaḥ sukha duḥkha anubandhaḥ ca vicchidyate tathā apavargepi iti etad ca brahma vidaḥ  muktasya ātmanaḥ  rūpam udāharanti iti yad api pravṛtti anubandhāt iti prakṣīṇeṣu rāga dveṣā moheṣu pravṛttiḥ na pratisaṃdhānāya pratisaṃdhiḥ tu pūrva janma nivṛttau punarjanma tad ca adṛṣṭa kāritam tasyām prahīṇāyām janma antara abhāvaḥ apratisaṃdhānam apavargaḥ karma vaiphalya prasaṅga iti ced  na karma vipāka pratisaṃvedanasya apratyākhyānāt pūrva janma nivṛttau punarjanma na bhavati iti ucyate na tu karma vipāka pratisaṃvedanam pratyākhyāyate sarvāṇi pūrva karmāṇi hi ante janmani vipacyante iti na upapadyate kleśa anubandha vicchedaḥ kasmāt  kleśa saṃtateḥ svābhāvika tvāt anādiḥ iyam kleśa saṃtatiḥ na ca anādiḥ śakya ucchettum iti atra kaścid  parīhāram āha yathā anādiḥ prāk utpatteḥ abhāva utpannena bhāvena nivartyate evam svābhāvikī kleśa saṃtatiḥ anityā iti apara āha yathā anādiraṇu śyāma tā atha ca agni saṃyogāt anityā tathā kleśa saṃtatiḥ api iti sataḥ khalu dharmaḥ  nitya tvam anitya tvam ca tattvam bhāve abhāve bhāktam iti aanādiraṇu śyāma tā iti hetu abhāvāt ayuktam anutpatti dharmakam anityam iti na atra hetuḥ asti iti ayam tu samādhiḥ akarma nimitta tvāt i taretara nimitta tvāt ca iti samuccayaḥ mithyā saṃkalpebhyaḥ  rañjanīya kopanīya mohanīyebhyaḥ  rāga dveṣa mohā utpadyante karma ca kattva nikāya nirvartakam naiyamikān rāga dveṣa mohān nirvartayati niyama darśanāt  dṛśyate hi kaścid sattva nikāyaḥ  rāga bahulaḥ kaścid  dveṣa bahulaḥ kaścid  moha bahulaḥ iti itaretara nimittā ca rāga ādīnām utpattiḥ umūḍhaḥ  rajyati mūḍhaḥ kupyati raktaḥ  muhyati kupitaḥ  muhyati sarva mithyā saṃkalpānām tattva jñānāt anutpattiḥ kāraṇa anutpattau ca kārya anutpatteḥ iti rāga ādīnām atyantam anutpattiḥ iti aanādiḥ ca kleśa saṃtatiḥ iti  ayuktam sarve ime khalu ādhyātmikā bhāvā anādinā prabandhena pravartante śarīrādayaḥ  na jātu atra kaścid anutpanna pūrvaḥ prathamata utpadyate anyatra tattva jñānāt na ca evam sati  anutpatti dharmakam kiñcid  vyaya dharmakam pratijñāyate iti karma ca sattva nikāya nirvartakam tattva jñāna kṛtāt  mithyā saṃkalpa vighātān na rāga ādi utpatti nimittam bhavati sukha duḥkha saṃvitti phalam tu bhavati iti iti vātsyāyana viracite nyāya bhāṣye caturtha adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam samāptam utpadyate atha kvacid utpadyate iti kaḥ ca atra viśeṣaḥ na tāvat eka ekatra yāvat viṣayam utpadyate jñeyānām ānantyāt  na api kvacid utpadyate tatra na utpadyate tatra anivṛttaḥ  moha iti moha śeṣa prasaṅgaḥ na ca anya viṣayeṇa tattva jñānena anya viṣayaḥ  mohaḥ śakyaḥ pratiṣeddhum iti mithyājñānam vai khalu mohaḥ  na tattva jñānasya anutpatti mātram tad ca mithyājñānam yatra viṣaye pravartamānam saṃsāra bījam bhavati sa viṣayaḥ tattvataḥ  jñeya iti kim punar tad mithyā jñānam anātmani ātma grahaḥ aham asmi iti mohaḥ  ahaṅkāra iti anātmānam khalu aham asmi iti paśyataḥ  dṛṣṭiḥ ahaṅkāra iti kim punar tad artha jātam yad viṣayaḥ  ahaṅkāraḥ śarīra indriya manaḥ vedanā buddhayaḥ katham tad viṣayaḥ  ahaṅkāraḥ saṃsāra bījam bhavati ayam khalu śarīra ādi artha jātam aham asmi iti vyavasitaḥ tad ucchedena ātma ucchedam manyamānaḥ  anuccheda tṛṣṇā pariplutaḥ punar  punar tad upādatte tad upādadānaḥ  janma maraṇāya yatate tena aviyogāt  na atyantam duḥkhāt vimucyate iti yaḥ tu duḥkham duḥkha āyatanam duḥkha anuṣaktam sukham ca sarvam idam duḥkham iti paśyati sa duḥkham parijānāti parijñātam ca duḥkham prahīṇam bhavati anupādānāt  sa viṣān navat evam doṣān karma ca duḥkha hetuḥ iti paśyati na ca aprahīṇeṣu doṣeṣu duḥkha prabandha ucchedena śakyam bhavitum iti doṣān jahāti prahīṇeṣu ca doṣeṣu na pravṛttiḥ pratisaṃdhānāya iti uktam pretyabhāva phala duḥkhāni ca jñeyāni vyavasthāpayati karma ca doṣān  ca praheyān apavargaḥ  adhigantavyaḥ tasya adhigama upāyaḥ tattva jñānam evam catasṛbhiḥ vidhābhiḥ prameyam vibhaktam āsevamānasya abhyasyataḥ bhāvayataḥ samyak darśanam yathābhūta avabodhaḥ tattva jñānam utpadyate evam ca śarīra ādi duḥkhāntam prameyam doṣa nimittam tad viṣaya tvāt mithyājñānasya tad idam tattva jñānam tad viṣayam utpannam ahaṅkāram nivartayati samāna viṣaye tayoḥ virodhāt  evam tattva jñānāt duḥkha janma pravṛtti doṣa mithyā jñānānām uttarottara apāye tad anantara abhāvāt apavarga iti sa ca ayam śāstra artha saṃgrahaḥ  anūdyate na apūrvaḥ  vidhīyate iti prasakhyān ānupūrvyā tu khalu kāma viṣayā indriya arthā iti rūpa ādaya ucyante te mityā saṃkalpyamānā rāga dveṣa mohān pravartayanti tān pūrvam prasaṃcakṣīta tān  ca prasaṃcakṣāṇasya rūpa ādi viṣayaḥ  mithyā saṃkalpaḥ  nivartate tad nivṛttau adhyātmam śarīra ādi prasaṃcakṣīta tad prasaṃkhyānāt adhyātma viṣayaḥ  ahaṅkāraḥ  nivartate soyam adhyātmam bahis ca vivikta cittaḥ  viharan mukta iti ucyate atas  param kācid  saṃjñā heyā kācid  bhāvayitavyā iti upadiśyate na artha nirākaraṇam artha upādānam vā katham iti teṣām doṣāṇām nimittam tu  avayavi abhimānaḥ sā ca khalu strī saṃjñā sa pariṣkārā puruṣasya puruṣa saṃjñā ca striyāḥ pariṣkāraḥ ca nimitta saṃjñā anuvyañjana saṃjñā ca nimitta saṃjñā rasanā śrotram dantoṣṭham cakṣuḥ nāsikam anuvyañjana saṃjñā ittham dantau ittham oṣṭhau  iti sā iyam saṃjñā kāmam vardhayati tad anuṣaktān  ca doṣān vivarjanīyān varjanam tu asyāḥ  bhedena avayava saṃjñā keśa loma māṃsa śoṇita asthi snāyu śirā kapha pitta uccāra ādi saṃjñā tām aśubha saṃjñā iti ācakṣate tām asya bhāvayataḥ kāma rāgaḥ prahīyate sati eva ca dvividhe viṣaye kācid  saṃjñā bhāvanīyā kācid  parivarjanīya iti upadiśyate yathā viṣa saṃpṛkte anne anna saṃjñā upādānāyāḥ  viṣa saṃjñā prahāṇāya iti atha idānīm artha nirākariṣyata avayavinī upapādyate sat asatoḥ upalambhāt  vidyā dvividhā sat asatoḥ anupalambhāt  avidyapi dvividhā upalabhyamāne avayavini vidyāt vaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ anupalabhyamāne ca avidyāt vaividhyāt saṃśayaḥ saḥ  ayam avayavī yadi upalabhyate atha api na upalabhyate na kathañcana saṃśayāt  mucyate iti tasmin   anupapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ kasmāt  pūrva ukta hetūnām apratiṣedhāt asti dravya antara ārambha iti vṛtti anupapatteḥ api tarhi saṃśaya anupapattiḥ na asti avayavi iti tad vibhajate ekaikaḥ  avayavaḥ  na tāvat  kṛtsne avaya vi nirvatate tayoḥ parimāṇa bhedāt  avayava antara saṃbandha abhāva prasaṅgāt ca na api avaya vi eka deśe na hi asya anye avayavā eka deśa bhūtāḥ santi iti atha avayaveṣu avayavī vartate na tāvat  pratyavayavam vartate tayoḥ parimāṇa bhedāt  dravyasya ca eka dravyatva prasaṅgāt  na api eka deśe sarveṣu anya avayava abhāvāt tad evam na yuktaḥ saṃśayaḥ na asti avayavi iti pṛthak  ca avayavebhyaḥ dharmibhyaḥ  dharmasya agrahaṇāt iti samānam kim pratyavayavam kṛtsnaḥ  avayavī vartate atha eka deśena iti na upapadyate praśnaḥ kasmāt  ekasmin bheda abhāvāt  bheda śabda prayoga anupapatteḥ akṛtsnam iti anekasya aśeṣa abhidhānam aeka deśaḥ iti nānātve kasyacid abhidhānam tau  imau kṛsna eka deśa śabdau bheda viṣayau na ekasmin   avayavinī upapadyete bheda abhāvāt iti anya avayava abhāvāt  na eka deśena vartate iti ahetuḥ avayava antara abhāvāt iti yadi api eka deśaḥ  avayava antara bhūtaḥ syāt  tathā api avayave avayava antaram varteta na avayavi iti anyaḥ  avayavi iti anya avayava bhāvepya vṛtteḥ aavayavinaḥ  na eka deśena vṛttiḥ anya avayava abhāvāt iti ahetuḥ vṛttiḥ katham iticed  ekasya anekatra āśraya āśrita saṃbandha lakṣaṇā prāptiḥ āśraya āśrita bhāvaḥ katham iticed  yasya yatas  anyatra ātma lābha anupapattiḥ sa āśrayaḥ na kāraṇa dravyebhyaḥ  anyatra kārya dravyam ātmānam labhate viparyayaḥ tu kāraṇa dravyeṣu iti nityeṣu katham iticed  anityeṣu darśanāt  siddham nityeṣu dravyeṣu katham āśraya āśrayi bhāva iti ced  anityeṣu dravya guṇeṣu darśanāt āśraya āśrayi bhāvasya nityeṣu siddhiḥ iti tasmāt avayavi abhimānaḥ pratiṣidhyate niḥśreyasa kāmasya na avayavī yathā rūpa ādiṣu mityāsaṃkalpaḥ  na rūpa ādaya iti sarva agrahaṇam avayavi siddheḥ iti pratyavasthita upyetat āha yathā ekaikaḥ keśaḥ taimirikeṇa na upalabhyate keśa samūhaḥ tu upalabhyate tathā ekaikaḥ  aṇuḥ na upalabhyate aṇu saṃcayaḥ tu upalabhyate tad idam aṇu samūha viṣayam grahaṇam iti yathā viṣayam indriyāṇām paṭu manda bhāvāt  viṣaya grahaṇānām paṭu manda bhāvaḥ  bhavati cakṣuḥ khalu prakṛṣyamāṇam na aviṣayam gandham gṛhṇāti nikṛṣyamāṇam ca na sva viṣayāt  pracyavate soyam taimirikaḥ kaścid cakṣuḥ viṣayam keśam na gṛhṇāti gṛhṇāti ca keśa samūham ubhayam hi  ataimirikeṇa cakṣuṣā gṛhyate paramāṇavaḥ tu  atīndriyāḥ indriya aviṣaya bhūtā kenacid indriyeṇa gṛhyante samuditāḥ tu gṛhyante iti aviṣaye pravṛttiḥ indriyasya prasajyeta na jātu artha antaram aṇubhyaḥ  gṛhyate iti te khalu ime paramāṇavaḥ saṃhatā gṛhyamāṇā atīndriya tvam jahati viyuktāḥ ca āgṛhyamāṇā indriya viṣaya tvam na labhante iti soyam dravya antara anutpattau  ati mahān vyāghāta iti upapadyate dravya antaram yad  grahaṇasya viṣaya iti saṃcaya mātram viṣaya iti ced  na saṃcayasya saṃyoga bhāvāt tasya ca atīndriyasya agrahaṇāt ayuktam saṃcayaḥ khalu anekasya saṃyogaḥ sa ca gahyamāṇa āśrayaḥ  gṛhyate na ati indriya āśrayaḥ bhavati hi idam anena saṃyuktam iti tasmāt ayuktam etad iti gṛhyamāṇasya ca indriyeṇa viṣayasya āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhi kāraṇam upalabhyate tasmāt na indriya daurbalyāt anupalabdhiḥ aṇūnām yathā na indriya daurbalyā cakṣuṣā anupalabdhiḥ gandha ādīnām iti yaḥ khalu vayavinaḥ  avayaveṣu vṛtti pratiṣedhāt abhāvaḥ soyam avayavasya avayaveṣu prasajyamānaḥ sarva pralayāya vā kalpeta niravayavāt vā nivarteta ubhayathā ca upalabdhi viṣayasya abhāvaḥ tad abhāvāt upalabdhi abhāvaḥ upalabdhi āśrayaḥ ca ayam vṛtti pratiṣedhaḥ sa āśrayam vyāghnan ātma ghātāya kalpate iti atha api avayava vibhāgam āśritya vṛtti pratiṣedhāt abhāvaḥ prasajyamānaḥ  niravayavāt  paramāṇoḥ nivartate na sarva pralayāya kalpate niravayava tvam khalu paramāṇoḥ vibhāgaiḥ alpatara prasaṅgasya abhāvāt  yatas  na alpīyaḥ tatra avasthānāt loṣṭasya khalu pravibhajyamāna avayavasya alpataram alpatamam uttaram uttaram bhavati sa ca ācamalpatara prasaṅgaḥ yasmāt nalpataram asti yaḥ paramaḥ  alpaḥ tatra nivartate yatas ca na alpīyosti tam pṛramāṇum pracakṣmahe iti avayava vibhāgasya anavasthānāt  dravyāṇām asaṃkhyeya tvāt  truṭitva nivṛttiḥ iti atha idānīmānupalambhikaḥ sarva na asti iti manyamāna āha tasya aṇoḥ niravayavasya nityasya anupapattiḥ kasmāt  ākāśa vyatibhedāt  antar bahis ca aṇuḥ ākāśena samāviṣṭaḥ vyatibhinnaḥ vyatibhedāt  sa avayavaḥ sa avayava tvāt anitya iti atha etad neṣyate paramāṇoḥ antar na asti ākāśam iti asarva gata tvam prasajyate iti aantaḥ iti pihitam kāraṇa antaraiḥ kāraṇam ucyate abahiḥ iti ca vyavadhāyakam avyavahitam kāraṇam eva ucyate tad etad kārya dravyasya saṃbhavati na aṇoḥ akārya tvāt  akārye hi paramāṇau   antar bahis iti asya abhāvaḥ yatra ca asya bhāvaḥ aṇu kāryam tad  na paramāṇuḥ yatas  hi na alpataram asti sa paramāṇuḥ iti yatra kvacid utpannāḥ śabdā vibhavanti ākāśe tad āśrayā bhavanti manobhiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ tad kāryaiḥ ca saṃyogā bhavanti ākāśe na asaṃyuktam ākāśena kiñcid mūrta dravyam upalabhyate tasmāt na asarva gatam iti saṃsapatā pratighātinā dravyeṇa na vyūhyate tathā kāṣṭhena udakam kasmāt  niravayavatu ārt sa pad ca pratighāti dravyam na viṣṭabhnāti na asya kriyā hetum guṇam pratibadhnāti kasmāt  asparśa tvāt  viparyaye hi viṣṭambhaḥ  dṛṣṭa iti sa avayave sparśavati dravye dṛṣṭam dharmam viparīte na āśaṅkitum arhati aṇu avayavasya aṇutaratva prasaṅgāt aṇu kārya pratiṣedhaḥ sāvayava tve cāṇoḥ aṇu avayavaḥ  aṇutara iti prasajyate kasmāt  kārya kāraṇa dravyayoḥ parimāṇa bheda darśanāt  tasmāt aṇu avayavasya aṇutara tvam yaḥ tu sa avayavaḥ aṇu kāryam tad iti tasmāt aṇu kāryam idam pratiṣidhyate iti kāraṇa vibhāgāt ca kāryasya anitya tvam na ākāśa vyatibhedāt  loṣṭasya avayava vibhāgāt anitya tvam na ākāśa samāveśāt iti paricchinnānām hi sparśavatām saṃsthānam trikoṇam catur asram samam parimaṇḍalam iti upapadyate yad tad saṃsthānam saḥ  avayava saṃniveśaḥ parimaṇḍalāḥ ca aṇavaḥ tasmāt  sa avayavā iti madhye san   aṇuḥ pūrva aparābhyām aṇubhyām saṃyuktaḥ tayoḥ vyavadhānam kurute vyavadhānena anunamīyate pūrva bhāgena pūrveṇa aṇunā saṃyujyate para bhāgena pareṇa aṇunā saṃyujyate yau tau pūrva aparau bhāgau tau   asya avayavau evam sarvatas  saṃyujyamānasya sarvatas  bhāgā avayavā iti yad tāvat mūrtimatām saṃsthāna upapatteḥ avayava sadbhāvaḥ iti atra uktam kim uktam avibhāga alpatara prasaṅgasya yatas  na alpīyaḥ tatra nivṛtteḥ aṇu avayavasya cāṇutaratva prasaṅgāt aṇu kārya pratiṣedhaḥ iti yad punar etad  saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca iti sparśavat tvāt  vyavadhānam āśrayasya ca avyāptyā bhāga bhaktiḥ uktam ca atra sparśavān aṇuḥ sparśavatoraṇvoḥ pratighātāt  vyavadhāyakaḥ  na sāvayava tvāt sparśavat tvāt ca vyavadhāne sati  aṇu saṃyogaḥ  na āśrayam vyāpnoti iti bhāga bhaktiḥ bhavati bhāgavān iva ayam iti uktam na atra avibhāge ālpatara prasaṅgasya yatas  na alpīyaḥ tatra avasthānāt tad avayavasya cāṇutaratva prasaṅgāt aṇu kārya pratiṣedhaḥ iti mūrtimatām ca saṃsthāna upapatteḥ saṃyoga upapatteḥ ca paramāṇūnām sāvayavat tvam itihetvoḥ yāvat  mūrtimat  yāvat ca saṃyujyate tad  sarvam sāvayavam iti anavasthā kāriṇau  imau hetū sāca anavasthā na upapadyate satyām anavasthāyām satyau hetū syātām tasmāt apratiṣedha uyam niravayavatvasya iti vibhāgaḥ ca vibhajyamāna hāneḥ na upapadyate tasmāt  pralaya anta tā na upapadyate iti anavasthāyām ca prati adhikaraṇam dravya avayavānām ānantyāt  parimāṇa bhedānām guru tvasya ca agrahaṇam samāna parimāṇa tvam ca avayava avayavinoḥ paramāṇu avayava vibhāgāt ūrdhvam iti yad idam bhavān buddhiḥ āśritya abuddhi viṣayāḥ santi iti manyate mithyā buddhaya etāḥ yadi hi tattva buddhayaḥ syuḥ buddhyā vivecane kriyamāṇe yathātmyam buddhi viṣayāṇām upalabhyeta yathā aayam tantuḥ ayam tantuḥ iti pratyekam tantuṣu vivicyamāneṣu na artha antaram kiñcid upalabhyate yad  paṭa buddheḥ viṣayaḥ syāt  yāthātmya anupalabdheḥ asati viṣaye paṭa buddhiḥ bhavantī mithyā buddhiḥ bhavati evam sarvatra iti yadi buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām na sarva bhāvānām yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ atha sarva bhāvānām yāthātmya anupalabdhiḥ na buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām buddhyā vivecanam ca yāthātmyānupalabdhiḥ ca iti vyāhanyate tad uktam avayava avayava prasaṅgaḥ ca evam āpralayāt  iti kārya dravyam kāraṇa dravya āśritam tad kāraṇebhyaḥ pṛthak  na upalabhyate viparyaye pṛthak  grahaṇāt  yatra āśraya āśrita bhāvaḥ  na asti tatra pṛthak  grahaṇam iti buddhyā vivecanāt tu bhāvānām pṛthak  grahaṇam atīndriyeṣu aṇuṣu yad indriyeṇa gṛhyate tad etayā buddhyā vivicyamānam anyat iti buddhyā vivecanāt  bhāvānām yāthātmya upalabdhiḥ yad asti yathā ca yad na asti yathā ca tad sarvam pramāṇata upalabdhyā sidhyati yā ca pramāṇata upalabdhiḥ tad  buddhyā vivecanam bhāvānām tena sarva śāstrāṇi sarva karmāṇi sarve ca śarīriṇām vyavahārā vyāptāḥ parīkṣamāṇaḥ  hi buddhyā adhyavasyati aidam asti idam na asti iti tatra ca na sarva bhāva anupapattiḥ evam ca sati sarvam na asti iti na upapadyate kasmāt  pramāṇa anupapatti upapattibhyām yadi sarvam na asti iti pramāṇam upapadyate sarvam na asti iti etad  vyāhanyate atha pramāṇam na upapadyate sarvam na asti iti asya katham siddhiḥ atha pramāṇam antareṇa siddhiḥ sarvam asti iti asya katham na siddhiḥ yathā svapne na viṣayāḥ santi atha ca abhimānaḥ  bhavati evam na pramāṇāni prameyāṇi ca santi atha ca pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ  bhavati asvapna ante viṣaya abhimānavat pramāṇa prameya abhimānaḥ  na punar jāgarita ante viṣaya upalabdhivat iti atra hetuḥ na asti hetu abhāvāt asiddhiḥ svapna ante ca asantaḥ  viṣayā upalabhyante iti atra api hetu abhāvaḥ pratibodhe anupalambhāt iticed  pratibodha viṣaya upalambhāt apratiṣedhaḥ yadi pratibodhe anupalambhāt  svapne viṣayā na santi iti tarhi ye ime pratibuddhena viṣayā upalabhyante te upalambhāt  santi iti viparyaye hi hetu sāmarthyam upalambha abhāve sati anupalambhāt abhāvaḥ sidhyati ubhayathā tu abhāve na anupalambhasya sāmarthyam asti yathā pradīpasya abhāvāt  rūpasya adarśanam iti tatra bhāvena abhāvaḥ samarthyate iti svapna anta vikalpe ca hetu vacanam svapna viṣaya abhimānavat iti bruvatā svapna anta vikalpe hetuḥ vācyaḥ kaścid svapnaḥ  bhaya upasaṃhitaḥ kaścid  pramoda upasaṃhitaḥ kaścid ubhaya viparītaḥ kadācid  svapnam eva na paśyati iti nimittavataḥ tu svapna viṣaya abhimānasya nimitta vikalpāt  vikalpa upapattiḥ pūrva upalabdha viṣayaḥ yathā smṛtiḥ ca saṃkalpaḥ ca pūrva upalabdha viṣayau na tasya pratyākhyānāya kalpete tathā svapne viṣaya grahaṇam pūrva upalabdha viṣayam na tasya pratyākhyāna avaya kalpate iti evam dṛṣṭa viṣayaḥ ca svapna antaḥ  jāgarita antena yaḥ suptaḥ svapnam paśyati sa eva jāgrat  svapna darśanāni pratisaṃdhatte aidam adrākṣam iti tatra jāgrat buddhi vṛtti vaśāt  svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ  mithyā iti vyavasāyaḥ usati ca pratisaṃdhāne yā jāgrataḥ  buddhi vṛttiḥ tad vaśa ādayam vyavasāyaḥ svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ  mithyā iti ubhaya aviśeṣe tu sādhana ānarthakyam yasya svapna anta jāgarita antayoḥ aviśeṣaḥ tasya svapna viṣaya abhimānavat iti sādhanam anarthakam tad āśraya pratayā ākhyānāt atasmin  tad iti ca vyavasāyaḥ pradhāna āśrayaḥ apuruṣe sthāṇau puruṣa iti yaḥ vyavasāyaḥ sa pradhāna āśrayaḥ na khalu puruṣe anupalabdhe puruṣa iti  apuruṣe vyavasāyaḥ  bhavati evam svapna viṣayasya vyavasāyaḥ ahastinam adrākṣam aparvatam adrākṣam iti pradhāna āśrayaḥ  bhavitum arhati evam ca sati sthāṇau apuruṣoyam iti vyavasāyaḥ  mithyā upalabdhiḥ atasmin  tad iti jñānam sthāṇau asthāṇuḥ iti vyavasāyaḥ tattva jñānam tattva jñānena ca mithyā upalabdhiḥ nivartyate na arthaḥ sthāṇu puruṣa sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ yathā pratibodhe yā jñāna vṛttiḥ tayā svapna viṣaya abhimānaḥ  nivartyate na arthaḥ  viṣaya sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ tathā māya gandharvanagara mṛgatṛṣṇikāṇām api yā buddhayaḥ tāḥ etasmin  tad iti vyavasāyāḥ tatra api anena eva kalpena mitya upalabdhi vināśaḥ tattva jñānāt  na artha pratiṣedha iti upādānavat ca māyā ādiṣu mithyājñānam prajñāpanīya sarūpam ca dravyam upādāvaya sādhanavān parasya mithyā adhyavasāyam karoti sā māyā nīhāra prabhatīnām naga ra sarūpa saṃniveśe dūrāt  nagara buddhiḥ utpadyate viparyaye tad abhāvāt sūrya marīciṣu bhaumena ūṣmaṇā saṃsṛṣṭeṣu spandamāneṣu udaka buddhiḥ bhavati sāmānya grahaṇāt antika sthasya viparyaye tad abhāvāt kvacid  kadācid  kasyacid ca bhāvāt  na animittam mithyājñānam dṛṣṭam ca buddhi dvaitam māyā prayoktuḥ parasya cadūra antika sthayoḥ gandharvanagara mṛgatṛṣṇikāsu supta pratibuddha yoḥ ca svapna viṣaye tad etad sarvasya abhāve nirupākhya tāyām nirātmaka tve na upapadyate iti mityābuddheḥ ca arthavat  apratiṣedhaḥ kasmāt  nimitta upalambhāt  sadbhāva upalambhāt ca upalabhyate mithyā buddhi nimittam mithyābuddhiḥ ca pratyātmam utpanna gṛhyate saṃvedya tvāt  tasmāt  mithyā buddhiḥ api asti iti tattvam sthāṇuḥ iti pradhānam puruṣa iti tattva pradhānayoḥ alopāt bhedāt  sthāṇau puruṣa iti mithyā buddhiḥ utpadyate sāmānya grahaṇāt evam patākāyām balākā iti loṣṭe kapota iti na tu  asamāne viṣaye mithyā buddhīnām samāveśaḥ sāmānya grahaṇa vyavasthānāt yasya tu nirātmakam nirupākhyam sarva tasya samāveśaḥ prasajyate gandha ādau ca prameye gandha ādi buddhayaḥ mithyā abhimatāḥ tattva pradhānayoḥ sāmānya grahaṇasya ca abhāvāt  tattva buddhaya eva bhavanti tasmāt ayuktam etad  apramāṇam apreya buddhayaḥ mithyā iti doṣa nimittānām tattva jñānāt ahaṅkāra nivṛttiḥ iti uktam atha katham tadtva jñānam utpadyate iti sa tu pratyāhṛtasya indriya arthebhyaḥ  manasaḥ  dhārakeṇa prayatnena dhāryamāṇasya ātmanā saṃyogaḥ tatva bubhutsā viśiṣṭaḥ sati hi tasmin  indriya artheṣu buddhayaḥ  na utpadyante tad abhyāsa vaśāt tattva buddhiḥ utpadyate anicchatā upi buddhi utpatteḥ na etad  yuktam kasmāt  artha viśeṣa prābalyāt  abubhutsamānasya api buddhi utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā yathā stanayitnu śabda prabhṛtiṣu tatra samādhi viśeṣaḥ  na upapadyate kṣudh pipāsābhyām śīta uṣṇābhyām vyādhibhiḥ ca anicchatā upi buddhayaḥ pravartante tasmāt aikāgryā nupapattiḥ iti astu etad  samādhi vyutthāna nimittam samādhi pratyanīkam ca sati tu etasmin pūrva kṛtaḥ janma antara upacitaḥ tattva jñāna hetuḥ dharma pravivekaḥ phala anubandhaḥ yoga abhyāsam āmarthya niṣphale hi abhyāse na abhyāsam ādriyeran dṛṣṭam hi laukikeṣu karmasu  abhyāsa sāmarthyam pratyanīka parihāra artham ca yoga abhyāsa janitaḥ  dharmaḥ  janmāntare ḥpi anuvartate pracaya kāṣṭhā gate tattva jñāna hetau dharme prakṛṣṭāyām samādhi bhāvanāyām tattva jñānam utpadyate iti dṛṣṭaḥ ca samādhinā artha viśeṣa prābalya abhibhavaḥ anāham etad aśrauṣam na aham etad ajñāsiṣam anyatra me manaḥ  abhūt iti āha laukika iti yadi artha viśeṣa prābalyāt anicchata upi buddhi utpattiḥ anujñāyate muktasya api bāhya artha sāmarthyāt  buddhaya utpadyeran  iti karma vaśāt niṣpanne śarīre ceṣṭa indriya artha āśraye nimitta bhāvāt avaśyambhāvī buddhīnām utpādaḥ na ca prabalopi san bāhyaḥ  artha  ātmanaḥ  buddhi utpāde samarthaḥ  bhavati tasya indriyeṇa saṃyogāt  buddhi utpāde sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam iti tasya buddhi nimitta āśrayasya śarīra indriyasya dharma adharma abhāvāt abhāvaḥ  apavarge tatra yad uktam aṇvargepi evam prasaṅgaḥ iti tad ayuktam tasmāt  sarva duḥkha vimokṣa upavargaḥ yasmāt  sarva duḥkha bījam sarva duḥkha āyatanam ca apavarge vicchidyate tasmāt  sarveṇa duḥkhena vimuktiḥ apavargaḥ na nirbījam nirāyatanam ca duḥkham utpadyate iti tasya apavargasya adhigamāya yama niyamābhyām ātma saṃskāraḥ yamaḥ usamānam āśramiṇām dharma sādhanam niyamaḥ tu viśiṣṭam dva ātma saṃskāraḥ punar adharma hānam dharma upacayaḥ ca yoga śāstrāt ca adhyātma vidhiḥ pratipattavyaḥ sa punar  tapaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ pratyāhāraḥ  dhyānam dhāraṇa iti indriya viṣayeṣu prasaṃkhyāna abhyāsaḥ  rāga dveṣa prahāṇa arthaḥ upāyaḥ tu yoga ācāra vidhānam iti tad artham iti prakṛtam jñāyate anena iti jñānam ātma vidyā śāstram tasya grahaṇam adhyayana dhāraṇe abhyāsaḥ satata kriyā adhyayana śravaṇa cintanāni tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvāda iti prajñā paripāka artham paripākaḥ tu saṃśaya  chedanam avijñāta artha bodhaḥ adhyavasita abhyanujñānam iti samāpavādaḥ saṃvādaḥ tad vidyaiḥ ca saha saṃvādaḥ iti avibhakta artham vacanam vibhajyate etad nigadena eva nīta artham iti yadi manyeta pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahaḥ pratikūlaḥ parasya iti tam abhyupeyāt  itivartate paratas  prajñām upāditsamānaḥ tattva bubhutsa aprakāśanena sva pakṣam anavasthāpayan sva darśanam pariśodhayet iti anyonya pratyanīkāni ca prāvādukānām darśanāni sva pakṣa rāgeṇa ca eke nyāyam ativartante tatra anutpanna tattva jñānānām aprahīṇa doṣāṇām tad artham ghaṭamānānām etad iti vidyā nirveda ādibhiḥ ca pareṇa avajñāyamānasya vigṛhya iti vijigīṣayā na tattva bubhutsayā iti tad ā idat vidyā pālana artham na lābha pūjā ākhyātyartham iti iti śrīvātsyāyana viracite nyāya bhāṣye caturthodhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ #################################################################### atha saṭīke nyāya bhāṣye pañcama adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam sādharmya vaidharmyābhyām pratyavasthānasya vikalpāt jāti bahutvam iti saṃkṣepeṇa uktam tad vistareṇa vibhajate tāḥ khalu imā jātayaḥ sthāpana ahetau prayukte caturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣedha hetavaḥ sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthān aviśiṣyamāṇam syāpanā hetutaḥ sādharmya samaḥ viśeṣam tatra tatra udāhariṣyāmi aḥ evam vaidharmya sama prabhṛtayā upi nirvaktavyāḥ lakṣaṇam tu sādharmyeṇa upasaṃkāre sādhya dharmviparyaya upapatteḥ sādharmyeṇa eva pratyavasthānam aviśiṣyamāṇam sthāpanā hetutaḥ sādharmya samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ nidarśanam akriyāvān ātmā dravyasya kriyaḥ hetu guṇa yogāt dravyam loṣṭaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yukta kriyāvān tathā ca ātmā tasamāt  kriyāvān iti evam upasaṃhṛte paraḥ sādharmyeṇa eva pratyavatiṣṭhate aniṣkriya ātmā vibhunaḥ  dravyasya niṣkriya tvāt  vibhu ca ākāśam niṣkriyam ca tathā ca ātmā tasmāt  niṣkriyaḥ iti na ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat sādharmyāt  kriyāvatā bhavitavyam na pura kriya sādharmyāt  niṣkriyeṇa iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvān sādharmya samāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ  bhavati atha vaidharmya samaḥ akriyā hetu guṇa yuktaḥ  loṣṭaḥ paricchinnaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  na tathā ātmā tasmāt na loṣṭavat  kriyāvān iti na na asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat sādharmyāt  kriyāvatā bhavitavyam na punar  kriyāvat vaidharmyāt kiyeṇa iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt  vaidharmya samaḥ vaidharmyeṇa ca upasaṃhāre aniṣkriya ātmā vibhu tvāt  kriyāvat  dravyam avibhu dṛṣṭam yathā loṣṭaḥ na ca tathā ātmā tasmāt  niṣkriyaḥ iti vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam aniṣkriyam dravyam ākāśam kriyā hetu guṇa rahitam dṛṣṭam na tathā ātmā tasmāt na niṣkriyaḥ iti ni ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat vaidharmyāt  niṣkriyeṇa bhavitavyam na punar akriya vaidharmyāt  kriyāvatā iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt  vaidharmya samaḥ atha punar  sādharmya samaḥ akriyāvān loṣṭaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yuktaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ tathā ca ātmā tasmāt pava kriyāvān iti na ca asti viśeṣa hetuḥ kriyāvat vaidharmyāt  niṣkriyaḥ  na punar  kriyāvat sādharmyāt  kriyāvān iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt sādharmya samaḥ anayoḥ uttaram sādharmya mātreṇa vaidharmya mātreṇa ca sādhya sādhane pratijñāyamāne syāt avyavasthā sā tu dharma viśeṣe na upapadyate gaḥ sādharmyāt  gaḥ tvāt jāti viśeṣāt  gauḥ sidhyati na tu sāsnādi saṃbandhāt aśva ādi vaidharmyāt  gaḥ tvāt eva gauḥ sidhyati na guṇa ādi bhedāt  tad ca etad  kṛta vyākhyānam avayava prakaraṇe pramāṇānām abhisaṃbandhāt ca eka artha kāri tvam samānam vākye iti hetvābhāsa āśrayā khalu  iyam avyavasthā iti dṛṣṭānta dharma sādhye samāsajata utkarṣa samaḥ yadi kriyā hetu guṇa yogat loṣṭavat  kriyāvān ātmā tadā loṣṭavat eva sparśavān api prāpnoti atha na sparśavān loṣṭavat  kriyāvān api na prāpnoti viparyaye vā viśeṣaḥ  vaktavya iti sādhye dharma abhāvam dṛṣṭāntāt  prasajataḥ  apakarṣa samaḥ loṣṭaḥ khalu kriyāvān avibhuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kāmam ātmā api kriyā vān avibhuḥ aḥ tu viparyaye vā viśeṣaḥ  vaktavya iti khyāpanīyaḥ  varṇyaḥ  viparyayāt avarṇyaḥ tau  etau sādhya dṛṣṭānta dharma om viparyasyataḥ  varṇyāvarṇya samau bhavataḥ sādhana dharma yukte dṛṣṭānte dharma antara vikalpāt  sādhya dharma vikalpam prasajataḥ  vikalpa samaḥ kriyā guṇa hetu yuktam kiñcid  guru yathā loṣṭaḥ kiñcid ca laghu yathā vāyuḥ evam kriyā hetu guṇa yuktam kiñcat  kriyāvat  syāt  yathā loṣṭaḥ kiñcid akriyam yathā ātmā viśeṣaḥ  vā vācya iti hetu ādi iva yava sāmarthya yogī dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tam dṛṣṭānte prasajataḥ sādhya samaḥ yadi ayathā loṣṭaḥ tathā ātmā prāptaḥ tarhi ayathā ātmā tathā loṣṭaḥ iti sādhyaḥ ca ayam ātmā kriyāvān iti kāmam loṣṭopi sādhyaḥ atha na evam na tarhi ayathā loṣṭaḥ tathā ātmā iti eteṣām uttaram alabhyaḥ siddhasya nihnavaḥ siddham ca kiñcid sādharmyāt upamānam ayathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti tatra na labhyaḥ  gaḥ gavayayoḥ dharma vikalpaḥ codayitum evam sādhake dharme dṛṣṭānta ādi sāmarthya yukte na labhyaḥ sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma vikalpāt vaidharmyāt  pratiṣedhaḥ  vaktum iti yatra laukika parīkṣakāṇām buddhi sāmyam tena aviparītaḥ  arthaḥ  atidiśyate prajñāpana artham evam sādhya atideśāt  dṛṣṭānte upapadyamāne sādhya tvam anupapannam iti hetuḥ prāpya vā sādhyam sādhayet aprāpya vā na tāvat  prāpya prāptyām aviśiṣṭa tvāt  asādhakaḥu dvayoḥ vidyamānayoḥ prāptau satyām kim kasya sādhakam sādhyam vā aprāpya sādhakam na bhavati na aprāptaḥ pradīpaḥ prakāśayati iti prāptyā pratyavasthānam prāpti samaḥ aprāptyā pratyavasthānam aprāpti samaḥ ubhayathā khalva yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kartṛ karaṇa adhikaraṇāni prāpya mṛdam ghaṭa ādi kāryam viṣpādayanti abhicārāt ca pīḍane sati dṛṣṭam aprāpya sādhaka tvam iti sādhanasya api sādhanam vaktavyam iti prasaṅgena pratyavasthānam prasaṅga samaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyā hetu guṇa yogī kriyāvān loṣṭa iti hetuḥ na apadiśyate na ca hetum antareṇa siddhiḥ asti iti pratidṛṣṭāntena pratyavasthānam pratidṛṣṭānta samaḥ akriyāvān ātmā kriyā hetu guṇa yogāt loṣṭavat iti ukte pratidṛṣṭānta upādīyate akriyā hetu guṇa yuktam ākāśam niṣkriyam dṛṣṭam iti kaḥ punar ākāśasya kriyā hetuḥ guṇaḥ vāyunā saṃyogaḥ saṃskāra apekṣaḥ vāyu vanaspati saṃyogavat iti amayoḥ uttaram idam tāvat ayam pṛṣṭaḥ  vaktum arhati atha ke pradīpam upādadate kimartham ca iti didṛkṣamāṇā dṛśya darśana artham iti atha pradīpam didṛkṣamāṇāḥ pradīpa antaram kasmāt na upādadate antareṇa api pradīpa antaram dṛśyate pradīpaḥ tatra pradīpa darśana artham pradīpa upādānam nirarthakam atha dṛṣṭāntaḥ kimartham ucyate iti aprajñātasya jñāpana artham iti atha dṛṣṭānte kāraṇa ādeśaḥ kimartham mṛgyate yadi prajñāpana artham prajñātaḥ  dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa khalu laukika parīkṣakāṇām yasmin  arthe buddhi sāmyam sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti tad prajñāpana arthaḥ kāraṇa apadeśaḥ  nirarthaka iti prasaṅga samasya uttaram atha pratidṛṣṭānta samasya uttaram pratidṛṣṭāntam bruvatā na viśeṣa hetuḥ apadiśyate anena prakāreṇa pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhakaḥ  na dṛṣṭānta iti evam pratidṛṣṭānta hetu tve na ahetuḥ dṛṣṭānta iti upapadyate sa ca katham hetuḥ nasyāt  yadi apratiṣiddhaḥ sādhakaḥ syāt iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt  ghaṭavat iti ukte apara āha prāk utpatteḥ anutpanne śabde prayatna anantarīyaka tvam anityatva kāraṇam na asti tad abhāvāt  nitya tvam prāptam nityasya ca utpattiḥ na asti anutpattyā pratyavasthānam anutpatti samaḥ asya uttaram tathā abhāvāt utpannasya iti utpannaḥ khalu ayam śabda iti bhavati prāk utpatteḥ śabda eva na asti utpannasya śabda bhāvāt  śabdasya sataḥ prayatna ānantarīyaka tvam anityatva kāraṇam upapadyate kāraṇa upapatteḥ ayuktoyam doṣaḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāraṇa abhāvāt iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt  ghaṭavat iti ukte hetau saṃśayena pratyavatiṣṭhate sati prayatnānāntarīyaka tve asti eva asya nityena sāmānyena sādharmyam aindriyaka tvam asti ca ghaṭena anityena atas  nitya anitya sādharmyāt anivṛttaḥ saṃśaya iti asya uttaram viśeṣāt  vaidharmyāt avadhāryamāṇe arthe apuruṣaḥ iti na sthāṇu puruṣa sādharmyāt  saṃśayaḥ  avakāśam labhate evam vaidharmyāt  viśeṣāt  prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt avadhāryamāṇe śabdasya anitya tve nitya anitya sādharmyāt saṃśayaḥ  avakāśam na labhate yadi vai labheta tatas  sthāṇu puruṣa sādharmya anucchedāt atyantam saṃśayaḥ syāt  gṛhyamāṇe ca viśeṣe nitya sādharmyam saṃśaya hetuḥ iti na abhyupagamyate na hi gṛhyamāṇe puruṣasya viśeṣe sthāṇu puruṣa sādharmyam saṃśaya hetuḥ bhavati ubhayena aunityena ca anityena sādharmyāt  pakṣa pratipakṣayoḥ pravṛttiḥ prakriyā aanityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt  ghaṭavat iti ekaḥ pakṣam pravartayati dvitīyaḥ ca nitya sādharmyāt  evam ca sati aprayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti hetuḥ anitya sādharmyeṇa ucyamānaḥ  na prakaraṇam ativartate prakaraṇa anati vṛtteḥ nirṇayāna nivartanam samānam ca etad nitya sādharmyeṇa ucyamāne hetau tad idam prakaraṇa anativṛttyā pratyavasthānam prakaraṇa samaḥ samānam ca etad vaidharmye api ubhaya vaidharmyāt  prakriyā siddheḥ prakaraṇa sama iti asya uttaram ubhaya sādharmyāt  prakriyā siddhim bruvatā pratipakṣāt  prakriyā siddhiḥ uktā bhavati yadi ubhya sādharmyam tatra ekataraḥ pratipakṣa iti evam sati upapannaḥ pratipakṣaḥ  bhavati pratipakṣa upapatteḥ anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ yatas  pratipakṣa upapattiḥ pratiṣedha upapattiḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham iti tattva anavadhāraṇāt ca prakriyā siddhiḥ viparyaye prakaraṇa avasānātu tattva avadhāraṇe hi avasitam prakaraṇam bhavati iti hetuḥusādhanam tad  sādhyāt  pūrvam paścāt  saha vā bhavet  yadi pūrvam sādhanam asati sādhye kasya sādhanam atha paścāt  asati sādhane kasya idam sādhyam atha yugapad  sādhya sādhate dvayoḥ vidyamānayoḥ kim kasya sādhanam kim kasya sādhyam iti hetuḥ ahetunā na viśiṣyate ahetunā sādharmyāt  pratyavasthānam ahetu samaḥ asya uttaram na traikālya asiddhiḥ kasmāt  hetutaḥ sādhya siddheḥ nirvatainīyasya nirvṛttiḥ vijñeyasya vijñānam ubhayam kāraṇataḥ dṛśyate soyam mahān pratyakṣa viṣaya udāharaṇam iti yad tu khalu uktam asati sādhye kasya sādhanam iti yad tu nirvartyate yad ca vijñāpyate tasya iti apūrvam paścāt  yugapad vā pratiṣedha iti na upapadyate pratiṣedha anupapatteḥ sthāpanā hetuḥ siddha iti aanityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt  ghaṭavat iti sthāpite pakṣe arthāpattyā pratipakṣam sādhayataḥ  arthāpatti samaḥ yadi prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt anitya sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabda iti tadā arthāt āpadyate nitya sādharmyāt nitya iti asti tu asya nityena sādharmyam asparśa tvam iti asya uttaram anupapādya sāmarthyam anuktam arthāt āpadyate itibruvataḥ pakṣa hāneḥ upapattiḥ anukta tvāt  anitya pakṣa siddhau arthāt āpannam nitya pakṣasya hāniḥ iti aneka antika tvāt ca arthāpatteḥ ubhaya pakṣa samā ca iyam arthāpattiḥ yadi nitya sādharmyāt asparśa tvāt ākāśavat ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ tadā arthāt āpannam anitya sādharmyāt  prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt anitya iti na ca iyam viparyaya mātrāt ekāntena arthāpattiḥ na khalu vai dhanasya grāvṇaḥ patanam iti arthāt āpadyate dravāṇām apām patana abhāva iti ekaḥ  dharmaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvam śabda ghaṭayoḥ upapadyate iti aviśeṣe ubhayoḥ anitaya tve sarvasya aviśeṣaḥ prasajyate katham sadbhāva upapatteḥ ekaḥ  dharmaḥ sadbhāvaḥ sarvasya upapadyate sadbhāva upapatteḥ sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt  pratyavasthānam aviśeṣa samaḥ asya uttaram yathā sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ eka dharmasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya upapatteḥ anitya tvam dharma antaram aviśeṣaḥ  na evam sarva bhāvānām sadbhāva upapatti nimittam dharma antaram asti yena aviśeṣaḥ syāt  atha matam anitya tvam eva dharma antaram sadbhāva upapatti nimittam bhāvānām sarvatra syāt iti evam khalu vai kalpyamāne aanityāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ sadbhāva upapatteḥ iti pakṣaḥ prāpnoti tatra pratijñā artha vyatiriktam anyat udāharaṇam na asti anudāharaṇaḥ ca hetuḥ na asti iti pratijña eka deśasya ca udāharaṇa tvam anupapannam na hi sādhyam udāharaṇam bhavati sataḥ ca nitya anityabhāvāt anityatva anupapattiḥ tasmāt  asadbhāva upapatteḥ sarva aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti nirabhidhā iyam etad vākyam iti asarva bhāvānām sadbhāva upapatteḥ anitya tvam iti bruvata anujñātam śabdasya anitya tvam tatra anupapannaḥ pratiṣedha iti yadi  anityatva kāraṇam upapadyate śabdasya iti  anityaḥ śabdaḥ nityatva kāraṇam api upapadyate asya asparśa tvam iti nitya tvam api upapadyate ubhayasya anitya tvasya nitya tvasya ca kāraṇa upapattyā pratyavasthānam upapatti samaḥ asya uttaram ubhaya kāraṇa upapatteḥ itibruvatā na anityatva kāraṇa upapatteḥ anitya tvam pratiṣidhyate yadi pratiṣidhyate na ubhaya kāraṇa upapattiḥ syāt  ubhaya kāraṇa upapatti vacanāt anityatva kāraṇa upapattiḥ abhyanujñāyate abhyanujñānāt anupapannaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ vyāghātāt  pratiṣedha iti ced  samānaḥ  vyāghātaḥ ekasya nityatva anityatva prasaṅgam vyāhatam bruvatā uktaḥ pratiṣedha iti ced  spapakṣa para pakṣayoḥ samānaḥ  vyāghātaḥ sa ca na ekatarasya sādhaka iti nirdiṣṭasya prayatna ānantarīyaka tvasya anityatva kāraṇasya abhāvepi vāyunodanāt  vṛkṣa śākhā bhaṅga jasya śabdasya anitya tvam upalabhyate nirdiṣṭasya sādhanasya abhāvepi sādhya dharma upalabdhyā pratyavasthānam upalabdhi samaḥ asya uttaram prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti bruvatā kāraṇata utpattiḥ abhidhīyate na tu kāryasya kāraṇa niyamaḥ yida ca kāraṇa antarāt api upapadyamānasya śabdasya tad  anitya tvam upapadyate kim atra pratiṣidhyate iti na prāk uccāraṇāt  vidyamānasya śabdasya anupalabdhiḥ kasmāt  āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥuyathā vidyamānasya udaka ādeḥ arthasya avāraṇa ādeḥ anupalabdhiḥ na evam śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇena āvaraṇa ādinā anupalabdhiḥugṛhyeta ca etad asya agrahaṇa kāraṇam udaka ādivat  na ca gṛhyate tasmāt udaka ādi viparītaḥ śabdaḥ  anupalabhyamāna iti teṣām āvaraṇa ādīnām anupalabdhiḥ na upalabhyate anupalambhāt na asti iti  abhāvaḥ  asyāḥ sidhyati abhāva siddhau hetu abhāvāt  tad viparītam astitvam āvaraṇa ādīnām avadhāryate tad viparīta upapatteḥ yad  pratijñātam ana prāk uccāraṇāt vidyamānasya śabdasya anupalabdhiḥ iti etad na sidhyati saḥ  ayam hetuḥ āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ iti āvaraṇa ādiṣu ca āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhau ca samataya anupaladhyā pratyavasthitaḥ  anupalabdhi samaḥ  bhavati asya uttaram aāvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ na asti anupalambhāt iti ahetuḥ kasmāt  anupalambha ātmaka tvāt anupalabdheḥ upalambha abhāva mātra tvāt anupalabdheḥ yad asti tad upalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ upalabdhyā tad asti iti pratijñāyate yad na asti tad anupalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ anupalabhyamānam na asti iti pratijñāyate soyam āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdheḥ anupalambhaḥ  anupalabdhau sva viṣaye pravartamānaḥ  na sva viṣayam pratiṣedhati apratiṣiddhā ca āvaraṇa ādi anupalabdhiḥ hetu tvāya kalpayate āvaraṇa ādīni tu vidyamāna tvāt upalabdheḥ viṣayāḥ teṣām upalabdhyā bhavitavyam yattāni na upalabhyante tad  upalabdheḥ sva viṣaya pratipādikāyāḥ  abhāvāt  anuṣa lambhāt anupalabdheḥ viṣayaḥ  gamyate ana santi āvaraṇa ādīni śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇāni iti anupalambhāt anupalabdhiḥ sidhyati viṣayaḥ sa tasya iti ahetuḥ iti vartate śarīre śarīriṇām jñāna vikalpānām bhāva abhāvau saṃvedanīyau aasti me saṃśaya jñānam na asti me saṃśaya jñānam iti evam pratyakṣa anumāna āgama smṛti jñāneṣu sā iyam āvaraṇa ādi  anupalabdhiḥ upalabdhi abhāvaḥ sva saṃvedyaḥ na asti me śabdasya āvaraṇa ādi upalabdhiḥ iti na upalabhyante śabdasya agrahaṇa kāraṇāni āvaraṇa ādīni iti tatra yad uktam atad anupalabdheḥ anupalambhāt abhāva siddhiḥ iti etad na upapadyate aanityena ghaṭena sādharmyāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ itibruvataḥ asti ghaṭena anityena sarva bhāvānām sādharmyam iti sarvasya anitya tvam aniṣṭam saṃpadyate soyam anitya tvena pratyavasthānāt anitya sama iti asya uttaram pratijña ādi ava yava yuktam vākyam pakṣa nivartakam pratipakṣa lakṣaṇam pratiṣedhaḥ tasya pakṣeṇa pratiṣedhyena sādharmyam pratijña ādi yogaḥ tad  yadi anitya sādharmyāt anitya tvasya asiddhiḥ sādharmyāt asiddheḥ pratiṣedhasya api asiddhiḥ pratiṣedhyena sādharmyāt iti dṛṣṭānte yaḥ khalu dharmaḥ sādhya sādhana bhāvena prajñāyate sa hetu tvena abhidhīyate sa ca ubhayathā bhavati kena cit samānaḥ kutaścid viśiṣṭaḥ sāmānyāt  sādharmya viśeṣāt ca vaidharmyam ekam sādharmya viśeṣaḥ  hetuḥ na aviśeṣeṇa sādharmya mātram vaidharmya mātram vā sādharmya mātram vaidharmya mātram ca āśritya bhāvān āha sādharmyāt tulya dharma upapatteḥ sarva anityatva prasaṅgāt anitya samaḥ iti etad ayuktam iti aviśeṣa sama pratiṣedhe ca yad uktam tad api veditavyam aanityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñāyate tad anitya tvam kim śabde nityam atha anityam yadi tāvat  sarvadā bhavati dharmasya sadā bhāvāt  dharmiṇā upi sadā bhāva iti anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti atha na sarvadā bhavati anitya tvasya abhāvāt  nityaḥ śabdaḥ evam nitya tvena pratyavasthrānāt nitya samaḥ asya uttaram pratiṣedhye śabde anityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt iti ucyamāne anujñātam śabdasya anitya tvam anityatva upapatteḥ ca anānityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratiṣedhaḥ  na upapadyate atha na abhyupagamyate anityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt iti hetuḥ na bhavati iti hetu abhāvāt  pratiṣedha anupapattiḥ iti utpannasya nirodhāt  abhāvaḥ śabdasya anitya tvam tatra paripraśna anupapattiḥ soyam praśnaḥ atat anitya tvam kim śabde sarvadā bhavati atha na iti anupapannaḥ kasmāt  utpannasyayaḥ nirodhāt  abhāvaḥ śabdasya tad  anitya tvam evam ca sati  adhikaraṇa ādheya vibhāgaḥ  vyāghātāt na asti iti nitya anityatva virodhāt ca nitya tvam anitya tvam ca ekasya dharmiṇaḥ  dharmau  iti virudhyete na saṃbhavataḥ tatra yad uktam anityam anitya tvasya bhāvāt  nitya eva tad  avartamāna artham uktam iti aprayatna ānantarīyaka tavāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti yasya prayatna anantaram ātma lābhaḥ tad khalu abhūtvā bhavati yathā ghaṭa ādi kāryam anityam iti ca abhūtvā na bhavati iti etad vijñāyate evam avasthite prayatna kārya aneka tvāt  iti pratiṣedha ucyate prayatna anantaram ātma lābhaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ  ghaṭa ādīnām vyavadhāna apohāt ca abhivyaktiḥ vyavahitānām tad  kim prayatna anantaram ātma alābhaḥ śabdasya āhaḥ abhivyaktiḥ iti viśeṣaḥ  na asti kāryā viśeṣeṇa pratyavasthānam kārya samaḥ asya uttaram sati kārya anya tve anupalabdhi kāraṇa anupapatteḥ prayatnasya ahetu tvam śabdasya abhivyaktau yatra prayatna anantaram abhivyaktiḥ tatra anupalabdhi kāraṇam vyavadhānam upapadyate vyavadhāna apohāt ca prayatna anantara bhāvinaḥ  artha saya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti na tu śabdasya anupalabdhi kāraṇam kim cit upapadyate yasya prayatna anantaram apohāt  śabdasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti tasmāt utpadyate śabdaḥ  na abhivyajyate iti hetoḥ ced anaikāntika tvam upapādyate anaikāntika tvāt asādhakaḥ syāt iti yadi ca anaikāntika tvāt asādhaktvam pratiṣedha upyana ekāntikaḥ kiñcid  pratiṣedhati kiñcinnā iti anaikāntika tvāt  asādhaka iti atha vā śabdasya anitya tvapekṣe prayatna anantaram utpādaḥ  na abhi vyaktiḥ iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ nityatva pakṣepi prayatna anantaram abhivyaktiḥ na utpāda iti viśeṣa hetu abhāvaḥ soyam ubhaya pakṣa samoviśeṣa hetu abhāva iti ubhayam api anaikāntikam iti sarveṣu sādharmya prabhatiṣu pratiṣedha hetuṣu yatra yatra aviśeṣaḥ  dṛśyate tatra ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ samaḥ prasajyate iti yaḥ  ayam pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ  doṣaḥ anaikāntika tvam āpādyate saḥ  ayam pratiṣedhasya pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ na aanityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti sādhana vādinaḥ sthāpanā prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ prayatna kārya aneka tvāt  kārya samaḥ iti dūṣaṇa vādinaḥ pratiṣedha hetunā dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ sa ca pratiṣedha iti ucyate tasya asya pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ  doṣa iti tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ sa ca vipratiṣedha ucyate tasmin pratiṣedha vipratiṣedha īpi samānaḥ  doṣaḥ anaikāntika tvam caturthaḥ pakṣaḥ pratiṣedham dvitīyam pakṣam sa doṣam abhyupetya tad uddhāram anuktvā anujñāya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe tṛtīya pakṣe samānam anaikāntika tvam iti samānam dūṣaṇam prasajataḥ  dūṣaṇa vādinaḥ  mata anujñā prasajyate iti pañcamaḥ pakṣaḥ sthāpana apekṣe prayatna kārya aneka tvāt  iti doṣaḥ pratiṣedha hetu vādinaḥ sva pakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ  bhavati kasmāt  sva pakṣa samuttha tvāt  soyam sva pakṣa lakṣaṇam doṣam apekṣamāṇaḥ  anuddhṛtya anujñāya pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ  doṣaḥ iti upapadyamānam doṣam para pakṣe upasaṃharati ittham ca anaikāntikaḥ pratiṣedha iti hetum nirdiśati tatra sva pakṣa lakṣaṇa apekṣayā upapadyamāna doṣa upasaṃhāre hetu nirdeśe ca sati anena para pakṣaḥ  abhyupagataḥ  bhavati katham kṛtvā yaḥ pareṇa prayatna kārya aneka tvāt  ityādinā anaikāntikatva doṣa  uktaḥ tam anuddhṛtya pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ  doṣaḥ iti āha evam sthāpanām sa doṣām abhyupetya pratiṣedhepi samānam doṣam prasajataḥ para pakṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ  doṣaḥ  bhavati yathā parasya pratiṣedham sa doṣam abhyupetya pratiṣedha vipratiṣedha īpi samānaḥ  doṣa prasaṅgaḥ  mata anujñā prasajyate iti tathā asya api sthāpanām sa doṣām abhyupetya pratiṣedhepi samānam doṣam prasajataḥ  mata anujñā prasajyate iti sa khalu ayam ṣaṣṭhaḥ pakṣaḥ tatra khalu sthāpanā hetu vādinaḥ prathama tṛtīya pañcama pakṣāḥ pratiṣedha hetu vādinaḥ dvitīya caturtha ṣaṣṭha pakṣāḥ teṣām sādhv asādhu tāyām mīmāṃsyamānāyām caturtha ṣaṣṭhayoḥ aviśeṣāt punarukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ caturtha pakṣe samāna doṣa tvam parasya ucyate pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe pratiṣedha doṣavat  doṣaḥ iti ṣaṣṭhepi para pakṣa abhyupagamāt samānaḥ  doṣaḥ itisamāna doṣa tvam eva ucyate na artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid asti samānaḥ tṛtīya pañcamayoḥ punarukta doṣa prasaṅga tṛtīya pakṣepi pratiṣedhepi samānaḥ  doṣaḥ iti samāna tvam abhyupagamyate pañcama pakṣepi pratiṣedha vipratiṣedhe samānaḥ  doṣa prasaṅgaḥ  abhyupagamyate na artha viśeṣaḥ kaścid ucyate iti tatra pañcama ṣaṣṭha pakṣayoḥ artha aviśeṣāt punarukta doṣaḥ tṛtīya caturthayoḥ mata anujñā prathama dvitīyayoḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāva iti ṣaṣ pakṣyām ubhayoḥ asiddhiḥ kadā ṣaṣ pakṣī yadā pratiṣedhepi sāmānaḥ  doṣaḥ iti evam pravartate tad ā ubhayoḥ pakṣayoḥ asiddhiḥ yadā tu kārya anyatva īprayatna ahetu tvam anupalabdhi kāraṇa upapatteḥ iti anena tṛtīya pakṣaḥ  yujyate tadā viśeṣa hetu vacanāt  prayatna anantaram āramala ābhaḥ śabdasya na abhi vyaktiḥ iti siddhaḥ prathama pakṣaḥ  na ṣaṣ pakṣī pravartate iti iti vātsyāyana viracite nyāya bhāṣye pañcama adhyāyasya prathamam āhnikam samāptam #################################################################### atha nyāya bhāṣya pañcama adhyāyasya dvitīyam āhnikam vipratipatti apratipattyoḥ vikalpāt nigraha sthāna bahutvam iti saṃkṣepeṇa uktam tad idānīm virbhajanīyam nigraha sthānāni khalu parājaya vastūni  aparādha adhikaraṇāni prāyeṇa pratijña ādi avayava āśrayāṇi tattva vādinam atattva vādinam ca abhisaṃplavante teṣām vibhāgaḥ tāni imāni dvāviśatidhā vibhajya lakṣyante sādhya dharma pratyanīkena dharmeṇa pratyavasthite pratidṛṣṭānta dharmam sva dṛṣṭānte abhyanujānan pratijñām jahāti iti pratijñāhāniḥ nidarśanam aaindriyaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ  ghaṭavat iti kṛte apara āha adṛṣṭam aindriyaka tvam sāmānye nitye kasmāt na tathā śabdaḥ iti evam pratyavasthite idam āha ayat ya aindriyakam sāmānyam nityam kāmam ghaṭaḥ  nityoḥ tu iti sa khalu ayam sādhakasya dṛṣṭāntasya nitya tvam prasañjayan nigamana antam eva pakṣam jahāti pakṣam jahat  pratijñā jahāti iti ucyate pratijña āśraya tvāt  pakṣasya iti pratijñāta arthaḥ aanityaḥ śabda aindriyaka tvāt  ghaṭavat iti ukte yaḥ  asya pratiṣedhaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntena hetu vyabhicāraḥ asāmānyam aindriyakam nityam iti tasmin  ca pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt iti dṛṣṭānta pratidṛṣṭāntayoḥ sādharmya yoge dharma bhedāt  sāmānyam aindriyakam sarva gatam aindriyakaḥ tu  asarva gataḥ  ghaṭa iti dharma vikalpāt  tad artham nirdeśa iti sādhya siddhi artham katham yathā ghaṭaḥ  asarvagata evam śabda upya sarva gataḥ  ghaṭavat eva anitya iti tatra aanityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pūrvā pratijñā aasarva gataḥ iti dvitīyā pratijñā pratijñāntaram tad  katham nigraha sthānam iti na pratijñāyāḥ sādhanam pratijñā antaram kim tu hetu dṛṣṭāntau sādhanam pratijñāyāḥ tad etad  asādhana upādānam anarthakam iti ānarthakyāt nigraha sthānam iti aguṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti pratijñā arūpāditaḥ  artha antarasya anupalabdheḥ iti hetuḥ soyam pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ katham yadi guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam rūpa ādibhyaḥ  artha antarasya anupalabdheḥ iti na upapadyate atha rūpa ādibhyortha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti na upapadyate guṇa vyatiriktam ca dravyam rūpa ādibhyortha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ iti virudhyate vyāhanyate na saṃbhavati iti aanityaḥ śabda aindriyaka tvāt iti ukte paraḥ  brūyāt  asāmānyam aindriyakam na ca anityam evam śabda upyaindriya kaḥ  na ca anityaḥ iti evam pratiṣiddhe pakṣe yadi brūyāt  akaḥ punar āha anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti iti soyam pratijñāta artha nihnavaḥ pratijñā saṃnyāsa iti nidarśanam aeka prakṛti idam vyaktam iti pratijñā kasmāt  hetoḥ aeka prakṛtīnām vikārāṇām parimāṇāt amṛd pūrva kāṇām śarāva ādīnām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam yāvān prakṛteḥ vyūhaḥ  bhavati tāvān vikāraḥ iti dṛṣṭam ca prativikāram parimāṇam asti ca idam parimāṇam prativyaktam tad eka prakṛtīnām vikārāṇām parimāṇāt  paśyāmaḥ  vyaktam idam eka prakṛti iti asya vyabhicāreṇa pratyavasthānam nānā prakṛtīnām eka prakṛtīnām ca vikārāṇām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam iti evam pratayava sthite āha eka prakṛti samanvaye sati śarāva ādi vikārāṇām parimāṇa darśanāt  sukha duḥkha moha samanvitam hi idam vyaktam parimitam gṛhyate tatra prakṛti antara rūpa samanvaya abhāve sati eka prakṛti tvam iti tad idam aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam bruvataḥ  hetu antaram bhavati sati ca hetu antara bhāve pūrvasya hetoḥ asādhaka tvāt nigaha sthānam hetu antara vacane sati yadi hetu artha nidarśanaḥ  dṛṣṭānta upādīyate na idam vyaktam eka prakṛti bhavati prakṛti antara upādānāt atha na upādīyate dṛṣṭānte hetu arthasya anidarśitasya sādhaka bhāva anupapatteḥ ānarthakyāt  hetoḥ anivṛttam nigraha sthānam iti yathā ukta lakṣaṇe pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahe hetutaḥ sādhya siddhau prakṛtāyām brūyāt  anityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ hetuḥ nāma hinoteḥ dhātoḥ tuni pratyaye kṛdanta padam padam ca nāma ākhyāta upasarga nipātāḥ abhidheyasya kriyā antara yogāt  viśiṣyamāṇa rūpaḥ śabdaḥ  nāma kriyā kāraka samudāyaḥ kāraka saṃkhyā viśiṣṭa kriyā kāla yoga abhidhāyi ākhyātam dhātu artha mātram ca kāla abhidhāna viśiṣṭam prayogeṣu arthāt abhidyamāna rūpā nipātāḥ upasṛjyamānāḥ kriyā avadyotakā upasargāḥ iti evamādi tad artha antaram veditavyam yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kacaṭata pānām jabagaḍa daśa tvāt  jhabhan ghaḍha dhaṣavat iti evaṃprakāram nirarthakam abhidhāna abhidheya bhāva anupapattau artha gateḥ abhāvāt  varṇāḥ krameṇa nirdiśyante iti yad  vākyam pariṣadā prativādinā ca tris abhihitam api na vijñāyate śliṣṭa śabdam apratīta prayogam atidruta uccāritam iti evamādinā kāraṇena tad avijñāta artham avijñāta artham asāmarthya saṃvaraṇāya prayuktam iti nigraha sthānam iti yatra anekasya padasya vākyasya vā paurvāpayeṇa anvaya yogaḥ  na asti iti  asaṃbaddha artha tvam gṛhyate tad samudāya arthasya apāyāt apārthakam yathā adaśa dāḍimāni ṣaṣ apūpāḥ kuṇḍamaja ajinam palala piṇḍaḥ adharaurukam etad  kumāryāḥ prāyyam tasyāḥ pitā apratiśīnaḥ iti pratijñā ādīnāmakyavānām yathālakṣaṇam artha vaśāt  kramaḥ tatra avayava viparyāsena vacanam aprāpta kālam asaṃbaddha artham nigraha sthānam iti pratijña ādīnām avayavānām anyatam eva api avayavena hīnam nyūnam nigraha sthānam sādhana abhāve sādhya asiddhiḥ iti ekena kṛta tvāt anyatarasya ānarthakyam iti tad etad niyama abhyupagame veditavyam iti anyatra anuvādāt  śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam vā anityaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabda punaruktam artha punaruktam aanityaḥ śabdaḥ nirodha dharma kaḥ dhvānaḥ iti anuvāde tu  apunaruktam śabda abhyāsāt artha viśeṣa upapatteḥ yathā hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam iti punaruktam iti prakṛtam nidarśanam autpatti dharmaka tvāt anityam iti aktvā arthāt āpannasya yaḥ  abhidhāyakaḥ śabdaḥ tena sva śabdena brūyāt  aanutpatti dharmakam nityam iti tad ca punaruktam veditavyam artha saṃpratyaya arthe śabda prayoge pratītaḥ saḥ  arthaḥ  arthāpattyā iti vijñātasya vākya arthasya pariṣadā prativādinā tris abhihitasya yad  apratyuccāraṇam tad  ananubhāṣaṇam nāma nigraha sthānām iti apratyuccārayan kim āśrayam para pakṣa pratiṣedham brūyāt  vijñāta arthasya pariṣadā prativādinā tris abhihitasya yad avijñāna tad  ajñānam nigraha sthānam iti ayam khalu avijñāya kasya pratiṣedham brūyāt iti para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ uttaram tad  yadā na pratipadyate tadā nigṛhītaḥ  bhavati yatra kartavyam vyāsajya kathām vyavacchinatti aidam me karaṇīyam vidyate tasmin   avasite paścāt  kathayiṣyāmi iti tad  vikṣepaḥ  nāma nigraha sthānam eka nigraha avasānāyām kathāyām svayam eva kathā antaram pratipadyate iti yaḥ pareṇa coditam doṣam sva pakṣe abhyupagamya anuddhṛtya vadati abhavat pakṣepi samānaḥ  doṣaḥ iti sa sva pakṣe doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣe doṣam prasañjayan para matam anujānāti iti mata anujñānām nigraha sthānam āpadyate iti paryanuyojyaḥ  nāma nigraha upapattyā codanīyaḥ tasya upekṣaṇam anigraha sthānam prāptaḥ  asi iti  ananuyogaḥ etad ca akasya parājayaḥ iti anuktayā pariṣadā vacanīyam na khalu nigraham prāptaḥ sva kaupīnam vivṛṇuyāt iti nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇasya mithyā adhyavasāyāt  anigraha sthāne anigṛhītosi iti param bruvan niravanu gojya anuyogāt  niranugojya anuyogāt  nigṛhītaḥ  veditavya iti kasyacid arthasya tathā abhāvam pratijñāya pratijñāta artha viparyayāt aniyamāt  kathām prasañjayataḥ  apasiddhāntaḥ  veditavyaḥ  yathā ana sat  ātmānam jahāti na sataḥ  vināśaḥ na asat  ātmānam labhate na asat utpadyate iti siddhāntam abhyupetya sva pakṣam vyavasthāpayati eka prakṛti idam vyaktam vikārāṇām anvaya darśanāt  mṛd anvitānām śarāva ādīnām dṛṣṭam eka prakṛti tvam tathā ca ayam vyakta bhedaḥ sukha duḥkha moha samanvitaḥ dṛśyate tasmāt  samanvaya darśanāt  sukha ādibhiḥ eka prakṛti idam viśvam iti evam uktavān anuyujyate atha prakṛtiḥ vikāra iti katham lakṣitavyam iti yasya avasthitasya dharma antara nivṛttau dharma antaram pravartate sā prakṛtiḥ yad ca dharma antaram pravartate sa vikāra iti saḥ  ayam pratijñāta artha viparyayāt aniyamāt  kathām prasañjayati pratijñātam khalu anena na asat āvirbhavati na sattiraḥ bhavati iti sat asatoḥ ca tirobhāva āvirbhāvam antareṇa na kasyacid  pravṛttiḥ pravṛtti uparamaḥ ca bhavati mṛdi khalva sthitāyām bhaviṣyati śarāva ādi lakṣaṇam dharma antaram iti pravṛttiḥ bhavati abhūt iti ca pravṛtti uparamaḥ tad etad  mṛd dharmāṇām api na syāt  evam pratyavasthitaḥ  yadi sataḥ ca ātma hānam asataḥ ca ātma lābham abhyupaiti tad asya apasiddhāntaḥ  nigraha sthānam bhavati atha na abhyupaiti prakṣaḥ  asya na sidhyati hetvābhāsāḥ ca nigraha sthānāni kim punar lakṣaṇa antara yogāt  hetvābhāsā nigraha sthāna tvam āpannāḥ yathā pramāṇāni prameya tvam iti ata āha yathā uktā iti hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇena eva nigraha sthāna bhāva iti te ime pramāṇa ādayaḥ padārthā uddiṣṭā lakṣitāḥ parīkṣitāḥ ca iti yaḥ  akṣa pādam ṛṣim nyāyaḥ pratyabhāt vadatām varam tasya vātsyāyana idam bhāṣya jātam avartayat  iti vidvat varavātsyāyana viracite nyāya bhāṣye pañcamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ nyāya darśanam ca idam samāptam
